Ayssi comensan las paraulas de Albucasim .	The opening words of the treatise begin: "Thus begins the words of Albucaisem."
O, filhs, pus yeu he a vos complit aquest libre, le qual es le derier de la sciencia de medicina, per le compliment de lu so consequit la fi en lu, e per las exposicios de lu, e per las declaracios de lu, es a mi vist que yeu complesca aquel a vos am aquest tractat, le qual es partida de la operacio am ma, so es cyrurgia.	Oh children, now I have completed this book for you, which is the last part of the science of medicine, because it has been concluded by its own result, and through its explanations, and through its declarations, it seems to me that you will be able to grasp that which belongs to you in this treatise, which is divided from my operation, namely surgery.
Quar la operacio am ma es prostrada en nostre regio e en nostre temps de tot privada, entro que fort leu peric la sciencia de lu, e le vistigi de lu es ostat; e no romasero de lu sino alcunas petitas descripcios en les libres dels Antics, les quals mudero las mas e endevenc ad aquels error e heyssitacio entro que son clausas las entencios de lu e es elonguada la forsa de lu e l’art.	For my operation is abolished in our region and at our time, entirely private, except that little light remains of it, and the remnants of it are left; and there remain no more than some small descriptions in the books of the Ancients, which have been modified by most errors and misunderstandings, until the intentions of it are sealed and its force and art are lengthened.
E es vist a mi que yeu vivifique aquela am ordenacio de aquest tractat en aquela segon la via de exposicio e de declaracio e de abreviacio; e per que vengua am las formas dels ferramentz de cautheri e dels autres instrumentz de la obra cum sia per addicio de la declaracio, e per preparacio de lu, la qual causa es necessaria.	And it seems to me that you will revitalize that same order of this treatise according to the way of exposition and declaration and abbreviation; and so that you may be familiar with the forms of the cauterizing instruments and other tools of the craft, as is necessary for addition to the declaration, and preparation for the work, which cause is necessary.
Mays la causa per la qual no es atrobat bo artifex am la sieua ma en aquest nostre temps, es quar la art de medicina es longua, e que cove le sieu actor denant aquo esser excercitat en la sciencia de anotomia la qual recontec Gualia entro que sapia les juvament dels membres e las formas de aquels, e la conjunctio e la separacio de lor; e haia la conoyssensa dels osses, dels nervis e dels lacertz, e·l nombre de aquels, e la egrecio de lor; e de las venas pulsatils e de las quietas, e dels locs del eyssiment de lor.	But the reason why no good craftsman can be found in our time who has his own hand is because the art of medicine is long-winded, and it requires its own practitioner to have been exercised in the science of anatomy, which Galen knew, so that he could know the joints of the members and their forms, and their conjunction and separation; and having knowledge of bones, nerves, and ligaments, and their number, and the arrangement of them; and of the pulsating veins and quiet ones, and the places where they are inserted.
E per aquo ditz Ypocras que am u nom es mot, mays en l’obra petit, e majorment en la art de la ma.	And therefore Hippocrates says that a name is not much, but in the small work, and most of all in the art of surgery.
Mays nos ja avem dit de aquel en l’introit de aquest libre; quar qui no es scient aquo que li avem dit de anotomia, no es evacuat que no caia en error per la qual siran mortz les homes, ayssi cum yeu he vist trops de aquels, quar alscus son formatz en esta sciencia e gettan se de aquela ses sciencia e ses experiment.	But we have already spoken of that in the introduction to this book; for whoever is not knowledgeable about what we have said about anatomy, will not be freed from error by which men will die, just as I have seen many of them, since some are formed in this science and fall short of its science and experience.
Quar yeu vi un metge folh e enperit aver incidit un apostema escrophilos en le colh de una femna, e incidic alcunas arterias del colh per que fluic gran sanc entro que la femna cazec morta entre las mas de lu.	For you saw a foolish doctor and ignorant cut open the esophagus of a woman, and cut through some arteries of the neck, so that a great deal of blood flowed until the woman died between her hands.
E vi un autre metge que pres que el traguera una peyra d’un home le qual avia procesit en sa etat, e la peyra era gran, e venguet a lu e trayssec aquela peyra am un tros de la vesiqua, per que aquel home al tertz dia es mort.	And I saw another doctor who insisted that he pull out an abscess from a man's body which had progressed in his condition, and the abscess was large, and it came to him and tore open that abscess with a piece of the intestines, so that that man died three days later.
E yeu ja apelat fuy a estrayre aquela, e vi que per la grandesa de la peyra e per la disposicio del malaute conogui subre lu que morira.	And you had already been asked to pull it out, and I saw that due to the size of the abscess and the condition of the patient, I knew that he would die.
E vi un autre metge le qual prenia stipendic de un duc de nostra terra per cyrurgia, e endeven a un crastrat negre le qual era deves lu fractura en la coyssa de lu; e perparec le metge am la sua ignorancia, estrayssec la fractura, sobre la plagua, am pulvinas e astelas am forta strectura, e no layssec a la plagua espiracio.	And I saw another doctor who was receiving a stipend from a duke in our land for surgery, and he applied himself to a blacksmith's apprentice who had a fracture on his thigh; and the doctor, with his ignorance, pulled out the fracture, above the wound, with pulleys and astals with strong tension, and did not allow the wound to breathe.
E aprop le desliet segons los sieus desiriers, e aprop le relieg, e aprop le leyssec per alcus jorns e comandec que nos deslies le liament; e estec ayssi entro que la coyssa e·l pe foro apostematz, e pervenguet a perdicio.	And the doctor untied it according to his desires, and then he re-wound it, and then he left it for some days and ordered that we should not loosen the bandage; and so it was that the thigh and leg became gangrenous, and ultimately led to perdition.
E yeu fuy apelat a lu, e aparelhegui a desliar le liament, e conseguida es tranquilitat e enayssi amermet de sas dolors.	And you were called to him, and I prepared to loosen the bandage, and consequently he found relief and began to forget his pains.
Mays empero ja corrupcio era confermada en le membre, per que no pogui refrenar aquela, e no cessec perambular la corrupcio en le membre entro que·l malaute peric.	But meanwhile corruption was confirmed in the limb, so that I could not restrain it, and it did not cease to corrupt the limb until the patient perished.
E vi un autre metge le qual perforec un apostema cancros, e fo ulcerat aprop alscus dias, entro que foc magnificada la malicia de lu am lo senhor de lu.	And I saw another doctor who pierced a cancerous abscess and had it ulcerated about three days later, so that the magnitude of his evil was revealed to him by the lord of him.
La qual causa es quar le cranc caut es pur de humor melencolic, lahoras no cove que pervengua a lu am ferr de tot, sino que sia an membre le qual suffertes que de tot fos hostat.	Which is because the cancerous boil is pure of melancholic humor, whereas it is not necessary that it should spread to him entirely, but rather be in a member which suffers as if it were being hosted by it.
E per aquo, filhs, necessari es a vos que la operacio am ma sia devisada en dos devesios: so es en operacio a lu qual es associada salut, e en obra am la qual es perilh en las majors disposicios.	And therefore, children, it is necessary for you that the operation with me be divided into two parts: one is the operation which is associated with health, and the other is the work in which there is peril in the major dispositions.
E yeu ja he exsitat aquo en tot loc de aquest libre en le qual venc opperacio en la qual es error e temor; per que necessari es a vos que guardetz aquo e layssetz aquel, per que les folhs no atrobo via a parlar e a vos desonestar.	And you have already existed here in every place of this book where the operation is in which there is error and fear; therefore it is necessary for you to keep this in mind and avoid that, so that the foolish ones do not take away the way to speak and to disown you.
E donc prenetz las vostras armas am sollicitut e am proteccio de Dieu , e les vostres malautes am falicitat e am fermetat.	And therefore take up your arms with solicitude and protection of God, and your patients with felicity and firmness.
E usatz de la milhor via per la gracia de Dieu perdusent a salut e a lausabla successio, e laysatz las malautias terriblas de difficil sanacio, e ostatz las vostras armas de aquo que vos fa temer, per so que ysitatio en vostra fe e en le vostre nom no vos evasisca: quar mays es remanent a la vostra gloria, e pus aut en le mon e en derier a las vostras sanctitatz.	And use the best way with the grace of God to obtain salvation and noble succession, and avoid the terrible diseases that are difficult to cure, and keep your arms at bay from this which makes you afraid, so that your situation in your faith and in your name does not escape you: for it is more remaining for your glory, and then again in the world and finally in your sanctity.
Gualia ja diyssec en alcunas sieuas monicios:	Galen already said in some of his own sayings:
“No mediquetz malautia mala, per so que mals metges no siatz nompnatz”.	"Do not heal bad illnesses, lest you become a bad doctor."
E yeu ja he devesit aquest libre segontz tres capitols.	And I have divided this book into three chapters.
Comensa la divisio del libre, e primier de la primieyra partida.	The division of the book begins, and the first part is on...
Le primier capitol ordenat del cap entro·s pes, en las formas dels instrumentz e en les ferrementz dels cauteris, e de aquo que necessari es en la opperacio.	The first chapter ordered from head to foot, in the forms of instruments and ironwork of cauterizers, and what is necessary for the operation.
La divisio de la segonda partida.	The division of the second part.
Le segon capitol, de siccio e perforacio, e de ventosas, e de plaguas, e de extractio de sagetas e de semblantz ad aquelas, tot capitolat e ordenat de las formas dels instrumentz.	The second chapter, on incision and puncture, and on cupping, wounds, and extraction of splinters and similar matters, all organized and ordered according to the forms of instruments.
Divisio de la tersa partida.	Division of the third part.
Le tertz capitol, de restauracio e de dislocacio, e de curacio de torcio e de semblantz ad aquels; capitol ordenat del cap entro·s pes, e de las formas dels instrumentz.	The third chapter, on restoration and re-location, and on curing of torticollis and similar matters; a chapter organized from head to foot, and according to the forms of instruments.
De cauteri am foc e am medicina aguda e rememoracio de la opperacio.	On cauterization with fire and sharp medicine, and on remembering the operation.
Am aquel comensa le tractat de tot le libre.	In this, begins the treatise of the entire book.
Cove que yeu digua la qualitat dels juvamentz de aquel cauteri e dels noccumentz de lu, e en qual compleccio sia prohibit cauteri.	You should know the quality of the joints of that cauterizer and its inconveniences, and in what condition it is prohibited to cauterize.
Donc dic que·l sermo de la qualitat del juvament de cauteri e del noccument de lu es sermo lonc e prolixs, e subtil per sciensa, e secret amaguat; e ja de lu a parlat gran multitut de savis, e de lu se son desacordatz, et a mi abasta un petit dels sermons de lor, temen perlonguacio.	Therefore I say that the discourse on the quality of the joints of the cauterizer and its inconveniences is a long and prolix sermon, subtle by science, and secret and hidden; and already many wise men have spoken about it, and they are in disagreement among themselves, and I myself am afraid to prolong the sermons of theirs.
E donc dic que cauteri comfereys a tota compleccio universalment la qual es am materia o ses materia, exceptat dos compleccios, las quals son compleccios caudas ses materia .	And therefore I say that cauterization is contrary to the entire universal complexion which is in matter or its materials, except for two complexions which are caudal with respect to their materials.
En la compleccio cauda e secca am materia se desecordero; quar alcus dyssero que cauteri es juvatiu ad aquela, e les autres dyssero le contrari de aquel, que cauteri no es convenient en malautia la qual es per qualiditat e per siccitat, quar natura del foc es qualiditat e siccitat, e enconvenient es que malautia cauda e secca am aquo que es caut e sec sia sanada.	In the dry and scorching complexion with respect to material, it will desiccate; for some people say that cauterization is beneficial in this case, while others say the opposite, namely that cauterization is not suitable in a disease which is caused by quality and dryness, because the nature of fire is quality and dryness, and it is inconvenient that a scorching and dry disease with water that is hot and dry should be healed.
E diysec aquel que ditz le contrari de aquel, que per cauteri es fayt juvament en tota malautia cauda e secca que ve en les cors dels homes, quar quan tu comparas le cors de home e las humiditatz de lu a la compleccio del foc, atrobas le cors de home freg.	And he who says the opposite, that through cauterization the joints are made healthy in all scorching and dry diseases that occur in the bodies of men, for when you compare the body of man and its moistures to the complexion of fire, you find the body of man cold.
E yeu dic per le sermo de aquel, que esperiment aquo ja a mi alscunas vetz a descubert.	And I say by the sermon of that, that experiment is this too already known to me several times to discover.
Mays empero no cove que vengua sobre aquo aquel que ja es exproat e excersitat en le capitol de cauteri per derier exercici, e a conogut la diversitat de la compleccio dels homes e la disposicio de las malautias en lor meteyssas, e las causas de aquelas, e·ls accidentz de lor, e l’espasi del temps de aquelas.	But I do not think that it is necessary to bring this forward again, as it has already been explained and exercised in the chapter on cauterization, and to understand the diversity of the complexions of men and the disposition of diseases in their respective bodies, and the causes of those, and their accidents, and the space of time for those.
Mays en las autras compleccios, no es sobre vos temor, e majorment en las malautias fregas e humidas, quar ja totz les metges se son acordatz sobre aquels, e no so desecordatz en le juvament am cauteri en aquelas.	But in other complexions, it is not for you to be afraid, and most especially in cold and humid diseases, for all doctors have agreed on these, and there is no disagreement among them about the joints being cauterized in those.
E sapiatz, filhs, que del secret de curacio per cauteri am foc e de la bontat de lu, so sobre cauteri am medicina comburent, es quar le foc es simple, la accio del qual no perven sino al membre le qual es cauterizat e no notz al autre membre am lu ajustat sino am petit nocument.	And understand, children, that from the secret of healing by cauterization with fire and its goodness, it is clear that those who burn with medicine are contrary to cauterization with fire, for the fire is simple, the action of which only reaches the member that is being cauterized and does not harm another member adjusted to it except with a small injury.
Mays la accio de medicina comburent perven ad aquel en les membres le qual de lu alunhat, e fort leu fa venir en le membre malautia de dificil sanacio e fort leu ausit.	But the action of medicine that is contrary to cauterization reaches those members which are distant from it, and very easily brings disease into a member with difficult healing and very easily leads to pus.
Mays le foc, per la sua sublimitat e de la sua substancia bontat, no fa aquo sino que superfluisca E ja es a nos conogut per experiment e per longitut de servitut de studi am l’art sobre le veritat de las causas; e per aquo yeu so excusat de la longitut del sermo E si no fos que no es legut al mieu libre en aquest pausero a vos secret amaguat am le foc, e la qualitat de la operacio de lu en les cors e de la sieua expulcio per la qual expellis las malautias, am sermo philosophic demostratiu, le qual siria acuit en las vostras pessas.	But the fire, because of its sublimity and good substance, does nothing but superfluous things. And it is already known to us through experiment and long duration of service in studying the art on the truth of causes; and therefore I am excused from the length of this sermon. And if it were not that it is not read at a better free time in this pause to you, a secret hidden by fire, and the quality of the operation of it in bodies and its expulsion by which it drives out diseases, with a philosophical demonstration sermon, which would be keenly felt in your souls.
E sapiatz, filhs, que els se desacordan del temps en le qual es convenient far cauteri e pausan le milhor temps de primaveyra.	And understand, children, that the time of year is not harmonious for making a cauterization and the best time of early spring.
E yeu dic que cauteri es convenient en tot temps, per so que le nocument per le temps accident es submergit en le juvament de aquo que am le cauteri es atirat, e majorment si le cauteri es per dolors o de dolors necessaries, fortz e fistinas, las quals no suffertan tarditat per so que es temut de aquelas que vengua malicia, que es major que petit nocument entrant per lo temps.	And I say that cauterization is suitable at any time, because the harm caused by the accidental timing is submerged in the joint of what is attracted to the cauterization, and most especially if it is for necessary pains or painful necessities, which do not tolerate delay because they are feared by those who come with malice, which is greater than small harm entering through the timing.
E aysso no catz en vostras pessas, o, filhs, aquo no estiman sino le poble vulguar e les fols metges, so es que ad aquela malautia que es sanada per cauteri no es redicio tot temps, e pausan aquel consequen.	And thus it is not considered in your souls, or, children, this is not esteemed except by the common people and foolish doctors, so that to that disease which is healed by cauterization, it is not reduced at all times, and pause is made after that consequence.
E la causa no es ges ayssi quo els cuydan per aquo, quar cauteri no es sino en loc de medicina la qual altera la compleccio e esicca las humiditatz las quals son causa per que veno las dolors.	And the cause is not thus as they say because of this, for cauterization is nothing but in a place of medicine which alters the complexion and dries out the humors that are the cause why pains come.
Mays empero cauteri superflueys sobre la medicina per volicitat de la sua valitut e vertut de la sua operacio e grandesa del sieu senhor.	But nevertheless, cauterization is superfluous over medicine due to the desire for its value and virtue of its operation and greatness of its lord.
E es possible que la sua malautia retorne en alcuna hora del temps, segon la compleccio del malaute e la locacio de la sua malautia, e la vertut de lu, e aquo que es preparat en le cors de lu de la agreguacio de las superfluitatz en lu, e aquo que es pervengut a lu en la sua acquisicio en viandas e semblantz de aquelas causas; sino que la malautia en la qual sia aministrat cauteri sia malautia subtil en membre de paucas superfluitatz e humiditatz, ayssi cum cauteri de dent per dolor e semblantz ad aquel, possible es que en lu no retorne aquela dolor, mays aquo se fa en petitz.	And it is possible that its disease will return at some hour of time, according to the complexion of the patient and the location of their disease, and the virtue of it, and what is prepared in the body of it by the accumulation of superfluities there, and what is brought forth in its acquisition through food and similar causes; but if the disease in which cauterization is administered is a subtle one in a member with few superfluities and humors, just as cauterization for toothache and similar pains, it is possible that in that case the pain will not return, but rather it will be reduced to smallness.
E mays sermo vulgar es que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, e es sermo dreyturier, no ad aquo que els entendo en lu, quar els crezo que no es curacio que aprofieyta am medicina ni am autra causa aprop cauteri.	And in addition, the common saying is that cauterization is the last resort of medicine, and it is a despairing word, not because I understand what they mean by it, for I think it is not healing that profits through medicine or any other cause approaching cauterization.
E la causa es en contrari de aquo; e la entencio que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina no es sino quan administram las manieyras de curacio en alcunas malautias, e aquelas medicinas no conferieysso, e aprop en la fi de la causa aministra hom cauteri, e aprofieyta ad aquela.	And the cause is contrary to this; and I understand that cauterization is the last resort of medicine only when we administer the methods of healing in certain diseases, and those medicines do not conduce, and approaching the end of the cause, one administers cauterization, and it profits at that.
E lahoras de aqui cat16 que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, no segon la entencio la qual entendo les vulgars e trops dels fols metges.	And from here on I want to make it clear that cauterization is the last resort of medicine, not according to my understanding which is different from that of the common people and foolish doctors.
E diyssero les antics que cauteri am aur es milhor que cauteri am ferr, e no diyssero aquo sino per la equalitat del aur e sublimitat de la sua sustancia.	And they said that cauterization with gold is better than cauterization with iron, and they did not say this except for the equality of gold and the sublimity of its substance.
E diyssero que le loc de cauteri no fa brac, cum aquo no sia absolutament vertat, quar yeu ja he aquo proat e he atrobat que aquel no fa aquo sino en alcus cors ses les autres, e cauteri am aquel es bo e milhor que am ferr ayssi quo els diyssero; mays empero quan tu fas cauteri am foc am de aur, no es a tu declarat, quar es egnit segon la quantitat que tu vols per la rugor de l’aur, e quar prepara a recebre freg; e si ajustas sobre lu ignicio se fon l’aur per le foc, e caso en le foc alcunas laminas per que le artifex catz per la occupacio de aquel.	And they said that the place of cauterization does not make a difference, as long as it is absolutely true, because you have already proved and experimented that it does not matter in some bodies except for others, and cauterization with gold is good and better than with iron just as they say; but on the other hand when you do cauterization with fire using gold, it is not to be declared, because it is hidden according to the quantity you want by the roughness of the gold, and how it prepares to receive heat; and if you adjust the ignition above it so that the gold melts in the fire, and case some plates are formed from which the artist can observe through the occupation of that.
E per aquo es fayt cauteri am ferr deves nos pus leugerament e pus propdanament a rectitut de operacio.	And therefore it is made necessary to do cauterization with iron, for us to proceed more lightly and more properly towards the rectitude of operation.
E yeu ja he ordenat aquest capitol en le cauteri segon capitols, et he ordenat aquels del cap entro les pes, per so que aleugo le demandant aquo que vol de lu.	And I have already arranged this chapter on cauterization according to chapters, and I have arranged those from head to foot, so that the one demanding it may easily find what they want in it.
De cauteri de dolor de cap per frigiditat e humiditat.	On Cauterization of Headache due to Coldness and Humidity.
Le capitol primier.	The First Chapter.
Aquesta cauterizacio confereys a la humiditat e frigiditat sobre le servel accident de la qual so doas causas, so es causa de soda e multitut de flux raumatic, apelat corissa, del cap a las partidas dels huelhs e de las aurelhas fluent, e multitut de dormir, e de dolor de dentz e del guolayro, e universalment de tota malautia que ve per fregiditat, ayssi cum paraliticament, sodo e apoplexio, e semblantz en aquelas malautias.	This cauterization brings relief to the humidity and coldness above the severest accident of which there are two causes, namely the cause of soda and the multitude of raumatic fluxes, called corissa, from the head to the partitions of the eyes and ears, fluent, and the multitude of sleepiness, and toothaches and the gout, and universally all disease that comes through coldness, just as paralysis, sodality, apoplexy, and similar diseases in those illnesses.
La forma de aquesta cauterizacio es aquesta, que primieyrament comandes al malaute que sia evacuat am medicina lacsativa le cap mondificant, per tres o per quatre nueytz, segon que exhigeys la vertut del malaute e la edat de lu e la sua costuma.	The form of this cauterization is this: first, I command the patient to be purged with lactative medicine in the head, clarifying it, for three or four nights, according to what the virtue of the patient and their age and habit demands.
E aprop comanda li que raza le sieu cap am razor, e aprop fay aquel sezer entre las tuas mas sobre una banca cayrada e que pause las suas mas sobre le pietz sieu.	And then I command him to shave his head with a razor, and after that, to make a circle between his temples on a well-crafted bench, and to place his hands on the pie-shaped pieces.
E aprop pausa la razit de la tua palma aprop le pous sobre la razit del nas entre les huels sieus.	And then I command him to pause the razor's stroke at the edge of his palm, right above the nose between his eyes.
Mays empero, cum le tieu dit del mieg loc es pervengut, signa aquel loc am tenta, e aprop igneys le cauteri olivar del qual aquesta es la forma:	But when the said place is reached, mark that place with a tent, and then ignite the olive cauterization of which this is the form:
E aprop pausa aquel sobre le loc senhat am tenta, a manieyra que descent, am la qual la tieua ma sia constrengida petit a petit, e tu revolveys aquel.	And then pause that cauterization on the marked place with a tent, in a way that it descends, as your hand is gradually constrained, and you rotate that.
E aprop leva la tua ma leugerament e reguarda le loc, e si veses ja del os esser descubert alcuna quantitat del cap, ayssi cum la quantitat de gra de errs, lahoras eleva la tua ma, e si no torno la tua ma am aquel ferr, am autre de aquel, si es enfrigidat, entro que sia vist del os aquo que yeu he dit a tu.	And then raise your hand slightly and look at the place, and if you see even a small amount of bone being uncovered, such as the size of a grain of error, immediately lift your hand, and if not, return your hand with that iron, or another like it, until what I have told you is seen by the bone.
E aprop pren un petit de sal e disolveys aquel sobre le loc e leyssa aquel per tres jorns.	And then take a small amount of salt and dissolve it on the place and let it sit for three days.
E aprop pausa sobre lu coto enbegut en boder e leyssa aquel sobre lu entro que sia destrusida la scara del foc.	And then pause above that spot, surrounded by border and let it sit on top until the scar of the fire is destroyed.
E aprop cura le loc am anguent tetrafarmacon entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the place with gentle quadriform medicine until it is healed.
E ja diyssero que quant la plagua roman uberta, tant mielhs geta le brac, per que es milhor e mays juvatiu.	And they said that as long as the wound remains open, so much the better it gets, because it is better and more healing.
E diyssero alcus de lor que sia cauterizada la codena entro al os, e sia tengut le cauteri entro que sia adhurida alcuna partida de la specitut del os.	And some of them said that the cuneiform should be cauterized into the bone, and the cauterization should be kept until some part of the specificity of the bone is consumed.
E aprop sia ras aquo que es adhust del os, e aprop sia curat.	And then that which has been adjusted to the bone will be removed, and then it will be cured.
E diyssero autres que am lo cauteri pervengua al derier, entro que enprema en le os forta enprecio entro que le os caga, e aquesta es la forma de alphecati petit:	And others said that with the cauterization, it will come to the end, and then it will press into the bone a strong impression until the bone cracks, and this is the form of little alpha.
E estiman de aquel loc expiran la vapors del cap.	And they think that from that place, the vapors of the head will evaporate.
E sia tenguda la plagua uberta per lonc temps, e aprop sia curada entro que sia consolidada.	And the open wound should be kept for a long time, and then it should be cured until it is consolidated.
Mays a mi no so vistas aquestas doas specias de cauteri de tot, sino en alcus homes segon via de temor; e layssa aquel, deves mi, milhor es am salut, quan es; quar le cap es develitat per solucio de continuitat de lu ayssi cum havem testificat en les autres membres, e majorment quan le cap del malaute es de freul natura.	But I do not see these two species of cauterization in general, but only in certain men according to the way of fear; and leaving that aside, as you should know, it is better for health when it is so; because the head is revealed by solution of continuity like we have testified in other members, and especially when the patient's head is of a frivolous nature.
E la specia de cauteri primieyra es mays salva e milhor deves mi; e de aquela husi e am aquela obra am salut.	And the first species of cauterization is more saved and better for me; and from that house and with that work, I have health.
Capitol segon.	Second Chapter.
Del cauteri del cap.	On Cauterization of the Head.
Quan en tot le cap accideys dolor cronica e longua e aquo es en le malaute prolonguat, e usa de gerras e de cochias e de capipurges e de emplaustres e de guatz e de cadels e de gualinas e de semblantz, e majorment si ja es cauterizat am un cautere le qual recontam e no aprofieyta a lu deguna de aquelas causas, lahoras considera quar si le cap del malaute es de fort creacio en la sua natura; e no es freul et atroba mot gran freg, lahoras aquel cauterisa am autra cauteri dejos aquel un pauc.	When in the entire head chronic and long-lasting pain occurs and this is prolonged in the patient's suffering, and they use remedies such as warships, comb-like things, poultices, plasters, wads, cauls, and gualinas, and especially if it has already been cauterized with one cauterization which relieves but does not benefit at all from those causes, then consider whether the patient's head is of strong creation in their nature; and if it is not frivolous and finds a great cold, then that cauterizes another cauterization, leaving it for a little while.
E aprop cauterisa aquel sobre le corn del sieu cap am cauteri entro que la codena es partida.	And then cauterize that on the crown of the patient's head with a cauterization until the cuneiform is divided.
Incisa la codena e sia descuberta del os la quantitat la qual havem recontat e cauteriza aquel am un cauteri en la partida deriera del cap en le loc le qual es apelat vas, — e es aquel loc en le qual es pausada ventosa.	Cut the cuneiform and uncover the quantity of bone which we have recounted, and cauterize that with a cauterization in the posterior part of the head in the location called "vas" - and it is that location where the wind pipe is paused.
Et alleuja la tua ma en aysso, e no descobras le os, quar le malaute per aquo atroba mot gran dolor diversa de la dolor de totz les autres cauteris del cap.	And lift up your hand in this way, and do not uncover the bone, because the patient by this will experience great and diverse pain unlike any other pains from all the other cauterizations of the head.
E yeu diyre aquest cauteri en son loc, quar cove que·l cauteri am le qual so cauterisatz les corns del cap e le occiput es pus subtil cauteri que aquel am le qual es cauterisat le mieg loc del cap; e aquesta es la forma de lu.	And you will say this cauterization in its place, because it is necessary that the cauterization with which we cauterize the horns of the head and the occiput is more subtle than that with which the middle part of the head is cauterized; and this is the form of it.
Capitol ters.	Fourth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de emigranea no-antiqua.	On Cauterization of Migraine Non-Antique.
Quan endeve en la partida del cap dolor sodo, o es stenduda dolor entro al uelh, sia evacuat am medicinas le cap mondificantz, e sia aministrada l’autra curacio, la qual yeu he dita en las devesios de las malautias; e tot no aprofieyta, lahoras cauterisacio en lu es en dos manieyras: o cauterisacio am medicina acuta comburent, o am ferr.	When it is necessary to evacuate the head clarifying medicine, and another cure is administered as I have said in the descriptions of diseases; and if none of these benefit, then cauterization takes place in two ways: either with acute medicine that is contrary, or with iron.
Mays cauteri am medicina comburent es que tu prenguas una dolsa de alh, e escorgas aquela e abcindas las extremitatz de lu de amdos les caps.	But the cauterization with medicine that is contrary is when you take a lump of aloes, and scrape it off, and cut off the extremities of both ends.
E aprop incideys le loc de la dolor en la templa am una lanceta lada entro que sia en lu feyt loc dejos la codena, entro que sia occultada.	And then incise the location of the pain on the temple with a sharp lancet, until it makes a spot below the cuneiform, so that it is hidden.
E aprop strenh sobre lu am stopada per descent constreccio, e layssa aquel per le spazi de tres horas; e aprop deslia le e tratz le alh, e laysa la plagua per dos o per tres jorn, e aprop pausa sobre lu coto submergit en boder entro que le loc fassa brac.	And then apply pressure to it with a stopper, so that the constriction descends gradually, and leave it for the space of three hours; and then remove the alum and treat the wound for two or three days, and then pause above it surrounded by border until the spot becomes hard.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with gentle quadriform medicine until it is healed.
E si tu voys, fe aquo am alcunas medicinas comburentz las quals yeu he scriutas en le douse tractat de medicinas comburentz.	And if you wish, do this with some contrary medicines which I have written in the two treatises on contrary medicines.
Mays la cauterisacio am ferr segon aquesta manieyra: igneys per cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma:	But the cauterization with iron according to this manner: ignite by cauterization of which this is the form:
e es apelat claus clavilhs, quar le cap de lu es ayssi cum forma de clavel en le qual es alcuna curvitat, e·n le mieg loc de lu es eminensia petita.	and it is called "claus clavilhs", because the head of it is like a form of claw in which there is some curvature, and in the middle part of it there is a small prominence.
E aprop pausa sobre loc de la dolor, e rete la tua ma — per que no sia adhurida la arceria la qual es dejos — e revol le ferr petit a petit am velocitat.	And then pause above the spot of pain, and keep your hand - so that the archery which is left behind is not consumed - and rotate the small iron piece by piece with speed.
E si la quantitat de lu que es adhurida per la specitut de la codena ayssi quo la maytat de lu, e elava la tua ma per so que la arteria no sia adhurida la qual es dejos, per so que no vengua flux de sanc.	And if the quantity of it that is consumed by the specificity of the cuneiform is as much as half of it, and lift up your hand to prevent the artery from being consumed which is left behind, in order that no flow of blood may come.
E aprop enbibeys coto en aygua de sal e pausa aquel sobre le loc, e layssa aquel per tres dias; e aprop pausa coto mulhat am boder, e aprop cura am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then pour the spot with saltwater and pause it above the location, and leave it for three days; and then pause the spot with a border, and cure it with gentle quadriform medicine until it is healed.
E si voys, cauterisa am la extremitat del cutellari segon cauteri, e guarda te de incisio de arteria en aquesta emigranea propriament no-antiqua.	And if you wish, cauterize with the edge of the cimeter according to the cauterization, and be careful not to cut into the artery in this non-antique migraine.
Capitol quart.	Fourth Chapter.
De cauterizacio d’emigranea antiqua.	On Cauterization of Ancient Migraine.
Quan tu curas emigranea am aquo que havem dit de la curacio precedent, e aquo que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias, e no aprofieyta la curacio, e vezes per la malautia que no abasta a lu aquo que havem dit del primier cauteri am medicina o del cauteri am foc, lahoras cove que tu igniscas le cauteri cutellar entro que sia albificat, pus que significas sobre le loc de la dolor am linha de longuesa de la qual sia la maytat del dit, o quays aquel; e depausa la tua ma per una veguada e strenh aquela entro incidiscas la arceria e pervengua entro al os.	When you cure migraine with what we have said about the previous cure, and what we have said in the divisions of diseases, and if the cure does not benefit, and sometimes by the disease it is not enough to apply what we have said about the first cauterization with medicine or with fire, then it is necessary that you ignite the cimeter cauterization until it is albified, since you indicate above the spot of pain with a line of length which is most of the digit or whatever; and place your hand for one moment and strengthen it so that the artery is incised and penetrates into the bone.
Empero necessari es a tu que guardes de la continuacio de la mandibula, la qual es mauguda deves la masticacio, e que le lacert no sia adhurit e le nervi le qual mau aquela, e que no s’endevengua espasme.	However, it is necessary for you to be careful not to damage the mandible's continuity, which is affected by mastication, and that the lacert is not consumed and the nerves which are related to it are not damaged, and that there is no spasmodic spasm.
E si es sobre la custodia e cautela de flux de sanc de l’arteria que es abciza, quar en la abcizio de lu es temor, e majorment ad aquel le qual ignora aquo que fa e no es studios e esproat; e layssa la operacio en lu al comensament.	And if it is about the custody and caution of the flow of blood from the artery that is cut, for in its cutting there is fear, and especially at that which ignores what it does and is not studied or practiced; and leave the operation in place at the beginning.
E yeu vindre am rememoracio del regiment de flux de sanc accident de la arceria segon la sieua manieyra, en le sieu loc de aquest libre.	And you will find it as a reminder of the regulation of blood flow by accident of the artery according to its own manner, in your own location of this book.
E si veses de aquesta malautia que no abaste aquest cauteri e veses le cors del malaute tollerable, cauteriza aquel en le mieg loc del cap ayssi cum havem recontat, e cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	And if you see that this disease does not respond to this cauterization and you see the patient's body is tolerant, then cauterize it in the middle part of the head as we have recounted, and cure the wound until it is healed.
E si voys, aministra le cauteri le qual havem dit en le capitol de streccio de arceria am cauteri havent dos cotels, e es milhor cauterizacio aquesta e mays conferent.	And if you wish, administer the cauterization which we have said in the chapter on strengthening of artery with two cauterizations, and it is better cauterization this one and more conformable.
Capitol .v.	Fifth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de las dolors de aurelhas.	On Cauterization of Earaches.
Quan en la aurelha ve dolor per freg e es curat am causas lacsativas e am l’autra curacio la qual he dita en la divisio, e no es remauguda la dolor, lahoras igneys le cauteri, e es aquest le qual ha nom puncta, del qual aquesta es la forma:	When in the earache there is pain due to cold and it is cured by lacrosse causes and another cure which I have said in the division, and if the pain does not subside, then ignite the cauterization point, and this is the one called "puncta", of which this is the form:
E aprop puncta aprop la ignicio, e sia menat al enviro de tota la aurelha ayssi cum roda es revolguda, o en le circuit de quascuna essemps si la dolor es en quascuna.	And then pierce the puncta and ignite it, and bring it around the entire ear as a wheel is revolved, or in the circle of each example if the pain is in each one.
Alonga te am le cauteri de la razit de la aurelha pauc a pauc pus que aias senhat le loc am tenta.	Along with the cauterization, go slowly and gradually with the razor of the ear, as you have marked the location with a tent.
E si le cauteri de detz puntz en tota aurelha, e quays aquela, e aprop cura les locz entro que sian sanatz.	And if the cauterization of all those points in the entire ear is done, and whichever one you want, and then cure the locations until they are healed.
Capitol .vi.	Sixth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de turtura.	On Cauterization of Torture.
Turtura la qual es curada e am cauterizacio no es sino de las specias las quals veno per flecma, segon que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias.	Torture which is cured and with cauterization is not but of the species that come through flux, according to what we have said in the divisions of diseases.
Esquiva cauterizacio de la specia que endeve per siccacio o per spasme del nervi.	Avoid cauterization of the species that develops due to dryness or spasm of the nerve.
Quan tu curas aquela specia de turtura am jerras e capipurgi e guarguarismes, e no comfereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas le malaute am tres cauteris: la i deves la razit de la aurelha, e·l segon un petit dejos le sieu templar, e le ters deves la conjunccio de doas labias.	When you cure that species of torture with herbs and capipurgi and guarguarismes, and your cure does not conduce, then it is necessary for you to cauterize the patient with three cauterizations: the first is a little bit of the razor of the ear, the second is a small spot on the temple, and the third is the conjunction of two lips.
E pausa lo tieu cauteri per le contrari de la partida malauta, quar mollificacio no ve sino en la partida que apar sana.	And pause your cauterization at the opposite side of the unhealthy part, for softening only appears on the part that seems to be healing.
E la forma de cauterisacio es que cauterizas aquel am le cauteri en le dreyt de la extremitat de la aurelha pus sobirana un petit sobre le corn del cap, e en le templar autre, la longuesa del qual sia segon la longitut del dit pous, e depausa la tua ma am cauteri entro que sia comburida la quantitat de la maytat de la specitut de la codena.	And the form of cauterization is that you cauterize it with the cauterizer at the right extremity of the ear, a little bit above the crown of the head, and on the temple another one, the length of which is according to the length of the thumb's tip, and place your hand with the cauterizer until the quantity of the majority of the specificity of the cuneiform is consumed.
E aquesta es la forma del cauteri, e es specia del cutellari, la forma del qual es denant mesa.	And this is the form of the cauterization, and it is a species of the cimeter, the form of which is before us.
Mays empero pus subtil es que aquel un pauc ayssi co vesas; e cove que cotel en lu de superflua groceza un pauc.	But however subtle it may be, you should see that a little bit of it is so; and it is necessary to cut away the excess flesh a little bit.
E aprop cura le loc am aquo que es denant procezit entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the location with what we have said before, until it is healed.
Capitol .vii.	Seventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio de apoplextia antiqua.	On Cauterization of Ancient Apoplexy.
Quan apoplextia es antiquada e curas aquela am aquo que havem dit e no confereys la tua medicacio e le malaute no ha febre, lahoras cauteriza aquel am quatre cauteris: sobre totz les corn del sieu cap; e am cauteri e le mieg loc del cap, ayssi cum havem dit; e am cauteri en le coguot.	When apoplexy is ancient and you cure it with what we have said and your medication does not conduce, and the patient has no fever, then cauterize that with four cauterizations: on all the horns of his head; and with a cauterization in the middle part of the head, just as we have said; and with a cauterization in the nape.
E la manieyra del cauteri es fayta segon que es desus dit.	And the manner of the cauterization is made according to what has been said above.
E ja es cauterizat sobre la boca del estomac; e es mays derier; e aprop sia curat am aquo que procezeys.	And it is already cauterized on the mouth of the stomach, and it is even later; and then be cured with what proceeds.
Capitol .viii.	Eighth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de obblivio fayta per flacma.	On Cauterization of Oblivion caused by Flux.
Cove que sian donatz al malaute en le comensament jerras grans e pilulas le servel mondificantz.	It is necessary to give the patient in the beginning large herbs and pills that serve as a clarifying medicine.
E aprop ras le cap tot del malaute e pausa sus le coguot de lu emplaustre de cetre descrit en le tractat dels emplastres.	And then take off the patient's head and pause on the back of the neck an ointment as described in the treatise on ointments.
E pausa aquel alcunas veguadas, quar aquel es manieyra de cauteri.	And pause that for several times, because it is a manner of cauterization.
E fay aquo segon aquel meteys orde le qual ja he dit.	And do so according to the method which I have already said.
E donc si per aqueles sanat bo es; e sino, lahoras fay a lu tres cauteris en la deriera partida de sieu cap, les quals sian deysendentz de la partida pus sobirana del cap entro a la partida pus dejos del col.	And therefore if by those it is well healed; and otherwise, then do so to the three cauterizations in the posterior part of his head, which are descendants of the upper part of the head down to the lower part of the neck.
E pausa entre quascun cauteri la grossetut del dit, e aprop cura lo cauteri am aquo que es procedit.	And pause between each cauterization the thickness of the finger, and then cure the cauterization with what has proceeded.
Mays si tu vos addicio e le malaute es aquo tollerant, lahoras fay a lu cauteri en le mieg loc; e si voys major addicio, lahora cauteriza aquel sobre les dos corns.	But if you wish to add more and the patient is so tolerant, then do so to the middle part; and if you wish even greater addition, then immediately cauterize that on both horns.
Aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat; e sia le cauteri olivar segon la forma denant donat.	And then cure it until it is healed; and be the cauterization olive-shaped according to the form given before.
Capitol .ix.	Ninth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de parazili e de mollificacio de tot le cors.	On Cauterization of Paresis and Softening of the Entire Body.
Cove que tu procesiscas en mondificacio del cap am jerras e am aquo que havem dit; e aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap, e am cauteri sobre totz les corns del cap, e am cauteri sobre la deriera partida de lu, e am tres cauteris sobre les spondils del col.	It is necessary for you to process in softening of the head with herbs and with what we have said; and then take off the patient's head, and then cauterize that with three cauterizations: one in the middle part of the head, one on all the horns of the head, and one on the posterior part of the neck, and three cauterizations on the vertebrae of the neck.
E si es necessari en la malautia de mollificacio del cors de trops aquel e les malautes tollerantz e la malautia es fort, lahoras cauteriza aquel am quatre cauteris sobre les spondils del dos, e dererament am cauteri entro que sia comborit de la codena mot de lu, e aleva la tieua ma.	And if it is necessary in the disease of softening of the body for many and tolerating patients, and the disease is strong, then cauterize that with four cauterizations on the vertebrae of the back, and gradually with cauterization until it is consumed by the cuneiform of the back, and lift up your hand.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat, e aquest sia cauteri olivar.	And then cure it until it is healed, and this be olive-shaped cauterization.
Capitol .x.	Tenth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de epilemcia.	On Cauterization of Epilepsy.
No es cauterizat le epilemtic sino aquella epilemcia es per flecma.	No, the epilepsy is not cauterized, but that epilepsy is caused by flux.
E donc cove que mondifiques le cervel de lu al comensament de lu am yeras e am l’autra curacio la qual havem dicta en la divisio quan le malaute es gran e es tollerant la exceperacio de las medicinas.	And therefore it is necessary to clarify the brain of him at the beginning with herbs and with the other cure which we have said in the division when the patient's disease is great and is tolerant, except for medicines.
E si es enfant le qual no sufferte las medicinas, lahoras aministra guarguarissmes e mastiguatoris le servel mondifican, denant aquo per motz dias, am bonifficacio de las viandas.	And if the child who does not tolerate medicines, then administer guarguarismes and mastiguateurs which serve as clarifying medicine, before that for several days, with good nutrition.
E aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop cauteriza aquel am un cauteri en le mieg loc del cap segon la manieyra precedent, e am autre cauteri en le occiput de lu, e sobre quascun corn del cap sieu cauterisa.	And then take off the patient's head, and then cauterize that with one cauterization in the middle part of the head according to the previous manner, and another cauterization on the back of the neck, and cauterize each horn of the head.
E si le malaute es fort e es tollerant, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteris les quals he ditz, en havent paraliticament e mollificacio del cors sobre les spondils del col e les spondils del dos.	And if the patient is strong and tolerating, then cauterize that with the cauterizations which I say, having paralyzed and softened the body on the vertebrae of the neck and the vertebrae of the back.
E sia cauteri olivar segon qu’es precedit.	And be olive-shaped according to what has preceded.
Mays si le malaute es enfant, lahoras pausa cauteri subtil segon aquesta manieyra.	But if the patient is an infant, then pause subtle cauterization according to this manner.
Capitol .xi.	Eleventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio de melencolia.	On Cauterization of Melancholy.
Quan las causas de melencolia so humiditatz corrompudas e flacma gros, lahoras cauteriza aquel am les cauteris les quals havem ditz en le havent paralisi.	When the causes of melancholy are moist and corrupted and flux is gross, then cauterize that with the cauterizations which we have said in having paralyzed.
E si la causa de melencolia es superfluitat declinant a melencolia, e le cors del malaute es humit, lahoras da ha beure aquo que mundifica le cervel de lu segon aquo que ha precedut en la divisio.	And if the cause of melancholy is superfluity declining into melancholy, and the patient's body is moist, then give him to drink that which clarifies the brain of him according to what has preceded in the division.
E aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop fay tortora decentment fayta de li sobre le cercle, e aprop depausa aquela en le mieg loc del cap.	And then take off the patient's head, and then do a torture decently done to him on the circle, and then pause that in the middle part of the head.
E le malaute sia sesent cayrat, e sia tengut de tota partida.	And the patient should be seated comfortably, and held from all sides.
E aprop pausa liniment; et es pus digne de boder antic de ovelhas.	And then pause with a liniment; and it is more worthy of ancient border of sheep's wool.
E escalfa aquel sobre le foc per calefaccio temprada per mesura, le qual le dit sufferta quan es mes en lu.	And warm that over the fire with a tempered heat by measure, which the patient suffers when it is in him.
E aprop vuo’ aquel en le mieg loc del cap de lu en le cercle, e leysa lu entro que sia enfregidat.	And then place that in the middle part of the head on the circle, and leave it until it is heated up.
E fay aquo am le malaute en tota semmana una veguada, am le autre regiment de lu bo entro que sia sanat; o si vols, cauteriza aquel fazen petitz puntz segon lo mays de lu, sino que tenguas la ma am un cauteri ayssi ordenat: aquesta es specia de cauteri la qual humecta le cervel am equalitat.	And do so with the patient in one week's time, with another regimen of it good until it is healed; or if you wish, cauterize that by making small points according to what is most suitable for him, unless you hold your hand with a cauterizer thus ordered: this is a species of cauterization which moistens the brain with equality.
E aprop pausa aquel coto enbegut en boder o en grays de gualina.	And then pause that in a cloth wrapped around it in linen or gray wool.
Capitol .xii.	Twelfth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de aygua descendent en le huel.	On Cauterization of Water Descending into the Vein.
Quan a tu es declarat le comensament de aygua en le huel per les senhals les quals yeu he ditz en la divisio, lahoras comensa e dona en beure al malaute aquo que mondifique le cap de lu, e guarda aquel de totas humiditatz.	When you have declared the beginning of water in the vein by the signs which I have said in the division, then begin and give to drink to the patient that which clarifies the head of him, and guard against all moisture.
E fay aquel suzar en banh en degu per alcus jorns.	And make that sweat in a bath for several days.
E aprop comanda a lu que raza le sieu cap, e cauteriza aquel am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap; e aprop cauteriza aquel am dos cauteris sobre dos templas si es le comensament de ysement de aygua en dos huels, o de la un latz si es comensamen de l’aygua en un huel.	And then command him to shave his head, and cauterize that with a cauterizer in the middle part of the head; and then cauterize that with two cauterizations on both temples if it is the beginning of water in two veins, or from one side if it is the beginning of water in one vein.
Incideys am cauteri totas las venas e arcerias las quals so dejos la codena; e sian les cauteris en aquela lonh en la latitut de las templas.	Cut with a cauterizer all the veins and arteries that are below the cuneiform; and be the cauterizations in that length on the latitude of the temples.
E guarda te de fluxs de sanc quan es cauterizat; e si veses de lu fluxs de sanc, osta le am alcuna medicina, la qual es a tu possible.	And beware of blood flux when it is cauterized; and if you see any blood flux from him, stop it with some medicine which is at your disposal.
E yeu vindre am savieza la qual es en extraccio de arcerias e am abscizio de aquelas e cautela de fluxs de sanc.	And you will find wisdom in the extraction of arteries and in the excision of those and caution against blood flux.
E alcunas vetz es cauterizat en le cervitz dejos dos osses am dos cauteris dererament produzitz.	And sometimes it is cauterized in the vertebral bone below two bones with two cauterizations produced gradually.
Capitol .xiii.	Thirteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de lacrimas antiquas.	On Cauterization of Ancient Tears.
Quan lacrimas dels huels so antiquas assuduament e per las venas e arterias las quals so en le loc manifest del cap defora e es verificat que aquo es superfluitatz frejas flecmatiquas, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteri le qual havem recontat en le capitol de comensament de aygua cazent en les huels, e am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap e am dos cauteris en la cervitz dejos dos templas, e am dos cauteris en la cervitz dejos dos osses.	When the tears of the eyes are ancient and by the veins and arteries which are in the manifest location on the outside of the head and it is verified that this is superfluous frozen flux, then cauterize that with a cauterizer which we have recounted in the chapter on beginning of water flowing into the veins, and with a cauterization in the middle part of the head and two cauterizations in the vertebral bone below two temples, and with two cauterizations in the vertebral bone below two bones.
E si indigeyses de addicio, lahoras cauteriza aquel en tot latz de la coa del huel sobre la extremitat del sobrecilh am petit cauteri.	And if you need to add more, then cauterize that on the entire length of the cuneiform bone over the extremity of the forehead with a small cauterizer.
Capitol .xiiii.	Fourteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fetor de nas.	On Cauterization of Foul Smell from the Nose.
Quan tu medicas aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no aprofieyta la tua medicacio, lahoras tu aparelha e dona en beure al malaute las cochias per tres noytz; e aprop ras le cap de lu, e cauteriza le am cauteri migier am cauteri olivar.	When you treat him with the water which we have said in the division and your treatment does not produce the desired effect, then prepare yourself and give to drink to the patient those concoctions for three nights; and then take off his head, and cauterize it with a middle-shaped cauterizer and an olive-shaped cauterizer.
E aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri clavelh am dos cauteris sobre les dos sobrecilhs dejos les cabels un petit.	And then cauterize that with a clove-shaped cauterizer and two cauterizations on both foreheads below the hair, a little bit.
E guarda te de la arceria que no incindas aquela.	And beware of the artery so that you do not cut it.
E del cauteri clavilh aquesta es la forma.	And with the clove-shaped cauterizer, this is the form.
Capitol .xv.	Fifteenth Chapter.
De cauteri de mollificacio de palpebras dels huels.	On Cauterization of Softening of Eyelids of the Eyes.
Quan la palpebra del huel es mollificada per malautia o per humiditat, lahoras cauteriza aquela palpebre1 am un cauteri am aquest cauteri lunar; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	When the eyelid of the eye is softened by disease or humidity, then cauterize that eyelid with a cauterizer having this lunar-shaped cauterization; and this is its form:
E si vos, cauteriza aquel sobre les dos sobrecils un petit am dos cauteris en tota partida, e sian elonguatz de las timporas.	And if you wish, cauterize that on both foreheads a little bit with two cauterizations all around, and be extended from the temples.
E sia la longitut de quascun cauteri segon la quantitat del sobrecil.	And be the length of each cauterization according to the quantity of the forehead.
E no premas trop la tua ma am le cauteri, mays segon la quantitat que la tersa partida de la palpebre sia adhurida.	And do not press too hard with your hand on the cauterizer, but according to the quantity that the third part of the eyelid is absorbed.
Capitol .xvi.	Sixteenth Chapter.
De cauteri de la palpebre del huel quan les pels so convertitz a las partidas dedintz e punho le huel.	On Cauterization of the Eyelid of the Eye when the hairs are converted to the inner parts and push the eye.
Quan les pels del huel son convertitz a las partidas dedintz ayssi que pungo le huel, cauteri en aquels es segon dos manieyras, quar cauteri o es am fer o es am medicina comburent.	When the hairs of the eye are converted to the inner parts thus that push the eye, cauterize them in those places according to two manners, either by fire or by medicine which is concomitant.
Si am cauteri de lu am foc, comanda al malaute denant aquo que leyse les sieus pels ayssi cum aquels les quals les mundan, entro que sian prolonguatz e engualhatz; e si punho aquel deves le lor naysement, lahoras tu strenh les huels de lu am una benda per so que no sia maugut entro que·ls pels sian nascutz.	If with cauterization of fire, command the patient before that he looks at his hairs thus as those which clarify them, until they are prolonged and equalized; and if push that you should not let it be, then stretch the eyes of him with a bandage so that no harm comes to them until the hairs are born.
Donc cum siran nascutz e engualhatz, lahoras pausa le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop senha sobre la palpebre dels huels de lu am tenta, am senhal le qual sia segon la figura de fulha de merta, e sia le comensament del senhal prop dels pels.	Then when they are born and equalized, pause the patient's head in your seat, and then seal over the eyelid of his eyes with a tent, with a sign which is according to the figure of a leaf of mercury, and be the beginning of the sign near the hairs.
E aprop pausa coto enbegut en album de huou o en mucillatge de ptilli sobre le huel.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped in albumen of hen or in mucilage of papyrus over the eye.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu.	And then ignite the cauterizer, whose form is this:
E aprop cauteriza sobre la figura la qual as senhada, petit a petit, em motas veguadas, entro que sia comburida la superficia de la codena la qual es ayssi cum fuelha de mirta, tota aparent propriament.	And then cauterize on the figure which has been sealed, little by little, in many times, until the surface of the cuneiform bone which is thus like a leaf of myrtle, appears properly.
E senhal de sanetat de la tieua obra es que tu vegus la palpebre de l’huel ja esser contrayta e·ls pels de lu esser elevatz deves la punctura del huel.	And the sign of health in this work is that you see the eyelid of the eye already contracted and the hairs of him raised above the puncture of the eye.
E donc eleva la tua ma e laysa aquel per tres jorns, e aprop pausa sobre lu coto am boder entro que sia eredicada la scara.	And then raise your hand and leave that for three days, and then pause with a cloth wrapped around it until the scar is elevated.
E aprop cura aquela am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with an ointment until it is healed.
Mays si retorna per les pels alcuna causa aprop lor naysement e la palpebra es mollificada, lahoras fay autra vetz le cauteri sobre aquel tot ayssi cum avias fayt primieyrament.	But if some cause returns to the hairs and the eyelid is softened again, then do another time the cauterization on that just as you did originally.
Mays si les pels so en la palpebra dejos, lahoras cauterisa aquela entro que sia elevada al sieu loc natural e sia engualhat e que les pels no punhan le huelh.	But if the hairs are in the eyelid below, then cauterize that until it is elevated to its natural place and equalized so that the hairs do not push into the eye.
Mays le cauteri am medicina comburent aquest es que comandes al malaute que leyse les pels entro que sian prolonguatz e engualhatz, e aprop sia fayta de carta de drap la forma de fuelha de mirtra.	But the cauterizer with concomitant medicine is this: you command the patient to look at his hairs until they are prolonged and equalized, and then make a chart on cloth in the shape of a leaf of myrtle.
E aprop pren de sabo conogut e de caus viva ana unc. .i., o quays aquo, e aprop mescle3 aquelas causas be, e fay aquo am festinacio per so que no sia enfregidat; e aprop expandeys de aquo sobre la carta la qual es fayta ayssi cum forma de fulha de mirtra, e pausa aquel sobre la un huel od amdos; e pausa dejos le huel coto enbegut en album de huou, e el cap del malaute sia en le tieu se.	And then take from known salt and living cause one ounce. The end! And then what is here, and mix those causes well, and make this with a festival so that it is not heated up; and then spread that water on the chart which is made like the shape of a leaf of myrtle, and pause that over one eye or both eyes; and pause below the eyelid wrapped in albumen of hen, and the patient's head be in your seat.
E pausa le dit sobre le medicina e prem aquela un petit e no la mauguas entro que lo malaute senta la mordicacio de la medicina, quar mordicacio es en lu ayssi cum de foc.	And then pause the said thing on the medicine and press that a little bit, but do not harm it until the patient feels the sting of the medicine, for sting is in him like fire.
E donc cum percevera aquo que el atrobo mordicacio, lahoras leyssa la medicina e mau aquela am le tieu dit; donc cum cessa la mordicacio, lahoras remau la medicina he lava le huel am aygua; e lahoras considera si vezes la palpebra ja es levada ayssi cum es lavada deves la costriccio am foc o am incisio, quar lahoras esta be; e si no torna sobre aquela de la medicina sobre le loc en le qual no ha empremut la medicina e no se denigra entro que sia engualhada la tua operacio e sia contrayt le huel.	And then when you see that he has received the sting, pause and let the medicine be as it is; therefore when the stinging ceases, rinse the eye with water; and then consider if the eyelid is already lifted thus as it has been washed away by fire or incision, for it is well; and if not, return to that place of the medicine where you have not yet applied it and do not neglect until your operation is equalized and the eye is contracted.
E aprop pausa sobre lu coto am boder entro que sia eradicada la codena de la adhustio, e aprop cura aquel am enguent deafinicon o am autre entro que sia sanat.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped around it until the scar of adjustment is eradicated; and then cure that with an ointment or another until it is healed.
E es necessari a tu, deves la tua operacio que guardes am pervigil diligencia que en le huel no caia re de la medicina, e si la palpebre aprop alscus dias es mollificada e alcuna causa dels pels punh en le huel, lahoras itera la tua medicina sobre aquel loc le qual de la palpebre es mollificat, e propriamen ayssi quo as fayt al comensament, e aprop enaviro lu entro que sia sanat.	And it is necessary for you to be vigilant and diligent in your operation so that the medicine does not fall into the eye; and if the eyelid becomes softened after some days and some cause of the hairs pushes into the eye, then repeat your medicine on that location where the eyelid is softened, and do just as you did at the beginning, and apply it to that place until it is healed.
E aquesta es la forma de fuelha de mirtra.	And this is the shape of a leaf of myrtle.
E sapias que les huels dels homes son diversificatz segon la magnitut e la parvitat, e donc segon aquo es fayta la tua contraccio.	And know that the eyes of men are diversified according to greatness and smallness, and therefore according to this is made your contraction.
E no sira amaguada la via de rectetut ad aquel al qual es studi en aquesta art.	And let not the way of rectitude be hidden from him who studies in this art.
Capitol .xvii.	Seventeenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistula que es en le lacrimal de l’huel.	On Cauterization of Fistula that is in the Lachrymal of the Eye.
Quan tu curas fistula am aquo que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas aquela segon aquesta manieyra: comanda al malaute que pause le cap sieu en le tieu se, e tengua le cap de lu alcun ministre entre las tieuas mas en tal manieyra que no sia maugut ni agitat am le sieu cap.	When you cure fistula with the water which we have said in the divisions of diseases and do not confirm your cure, then it is necessary that you cauterize that according to this manner: command the patient to pause his head on the seat, and hold the head of him by some minister between the seats in such a way that he is not harmed or agitated with his own head.
E aprop pausa coto enfus en album de huou o en mucellage de ptilli sobre le huel de lu.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped in albumen of hen or in mucilage of papyrus over the eye of him.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma:	And then ignite the cauterizer, whose form is this:
le qual sia conquau, ayssi cum es forma de cana o de pena de voltor, de la una extremitat am la qual es fayta lo cauteri.	the shape of which is a crescent, like the form of a cane or a pen nib of a vulture, from one extremity to which the cauterizer has been made.
E si voys, sia penetrant entro a la autra extremitat.	And if you wish, it should penetrate into the other extremity.
E si vols sia sort ayssi cum tenta.	And if you wish, let it come out like a tent.
Mays empero aquel que es concau es milhor a la tieua obra.	But meanwhile that which is concave is better for the operation.
E aprop prem la fistula si es uberta, e tra de lu sania et exsicca aquela.	And then press the fistula if it is open, and draw out the pus and dry it up.
E si no es uberta, lahoras obre aquela e extratz la poyredura de lu.	And if it is not open, then work on it and extract the pus from it.
E aprop pausa sobre lu le cauteri le qual sia be ignit, e te am aquel la tieua ma un petit deves le cauteri del huel a la partida del nas, per so que no erre la tua ma o le malaute sia enquietat, e lahoras pausa le cauteri en le grays del huel e corrompas aquel.	And then pause with the cauterizer which is well ignited, and take a little bit of that to the corner of the eye at the edge of the nose, so that your hand or the patient may not be disturbed; and then pause the cauterizer on the gray of the eye and corrupt that.
E donc si al comensament del tieu cauteri perve entro al os, bo es; e sino, lahoras itera le cauteri una veguada o dos, si mestiers era; e layssa aquel ayssi per tres jorns, e aprop pausa sobre aquel coto am boder e enviro lu am enguent exsiccatiu entro que sia sanat.	And then if at the beginning of your cauterizer you see it go into the bone, that is good; and if not, then repeat the cauterizer once or twice as needed; and leave that so for three days, and then pause with a cloth wrapped around it and surrounding it with a drying ointment until it is healed.
Mays si eran passatz xi dias e no es sanat, lahoras pausa sobre lu medicina aguda corrosiva entro que l’os sia descubert e sia ras segon que conveneys en le sieu capitol.	But if it has passed 11 days and is not healed, then pause with the sharp corrosive medicine so that the bone is uncovered and is scraped according to what is convenient in your own chapter.
E es autra manieyra de cauteri de fistula la qual alscus primiers diysero: enten al loc de la fistula e fen aquela e aprop pausa en aquela fissura camaen subtil del qual es la forma de lu: E fon en aquela la quantitat de i unc de plom fundut; e te la tua ma am camaem am bona retencio, e no sia maugut le malaute per so que le plom fundut no pervengua al huel de aquel; e cove que pausas sobre le huel del malaute coto enfus en album de huou o en aygua, quar plom adhureys le loc de la fistula e sana aquela per sanacio meravilhora.	And there is another manner of cauterizing a fistula which some earlier doctors said: take the place of the fistula and fill it with a sharp corrosive medicine, and then pause in that fissure so subtle that its shape is this: Pour into that the quantity of one ounce of melted lead; and take your hand with a small spatula having good retention, and do not let the patient be harmed because the melted lead will reach the eye of him; and it is necessary to pause over the eye of the patient wrapped in albumen of hen or water, for lead adheres to the place of the fistula and cures that by marvelous healing.
E si la fistula es sanada am aquo que havem dit del cauteri e de la curacio, bo es; e sino, lahoras es necessari aministrar trauc del nas e reduzir la fistula al cors del nas segon que vindra en son loc propri.	And if the fistula is healed with the water which we have said for cauterization and cure, that is good; and otherwise, it is necessary to make a cut of the nose and reduce the fistula to the body of the nose according to what will come in its own place.
Capitol .xviii.	Eighteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la fendedura des potz.	On Cauterization of the Wounds of the Pots.
Motas veguadas accideysso fissuras en las labias, e majorment en las labias dels enfantz.	Many times accidental fissures occur in the lips, and especially in the lips of children.
Donc cum tu curas aquelas fissuras am aquo que nos havem dit en las divisios e no aprofieyta la tua cura, lahoras igneys le cauteri petit cutellar segon aquesta forma que s’ensiec:	Therefore, when you cure those fissures with the water which we have said in the divisions and your cure does not take effect, then ignite the small cauterizer like a cutlery according to this shape that is shown:
E sia la conquavitat de lu segon la subtilitat de cotella.	And be the concavity of it according to the subtlety of a cutlery.
Aprop pausa aquel init cuytadament en aquelas fissuras entro que·l cauteri pervengua al preon de las fissuras.	And then pause that initial application cautiously in those fissures until the cauterizer reaches the bottom of the fissures.
E aprop cura aquel am cerotz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with an ointment until it is healed.
Capitol .xix.	Nineteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistula en la boca.	On Cauterization of Fistula in the Mouth.
Quan en la razit de uvula o en le paladar o en las razitz de las dentz endeve apostema e aprop fa brac, e aprop es rompuda, e aprop es antiquada, e corr brac e es fayta fistula, e aprop tu curas aquela e no aprofieyta a curacio, lahoras cove que tu igniscas cauteri segon la quantitat que sia receubuda en la fistula, e aprop met aquel ignit en le trauc de la fistola, e te la tua ma entro que pervengua le ferr ignit al preon de lu, e al derier de lu fazen aysso una veguada o dos; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que nos havem dit de la curacio entro que sia sanat.	When in the root of the uvula or on the palate or on the roots of the teeth an abscess forms and bursts, and then is softened, and then is corrupted, and a fistula forms, and then you cure that and your cure does not take effect, it is necessary to ignite the cauterizer according to the quantity received in the fistula; and then put that ignited cauterizer into the track of the fistula, and take your hand so that the hot iron reaches the bottom of it, and at the end of it make it thus once or twice; and then cure that with the water which we have said for curing until it is healed.
E donc si la sania es abscindita e es sanat, bo es; e sino, lahoras es necessari de descubrir le loc e hostar le os corrumput segon que vindra en son capitol.	And then if the pus is extracted and healed, that is good; and otherwise, it is necessary to discover the location and expose the corrupted bone according to what will come in its own chapter.
Capitol .xx.	Twentieth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de las dentz e de mollificacio de las angivas.	On Cauterization of the Teeth and Softening of the Gums.
Quan las angivas son mollificadas per humiditat e las dentz son maugudas, e curas aquelas am medicinas e no confereys, lahoras pausa le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop igneys le cauteri la forma del qual vindra aprop aysso, enayssi que tu pauses la quanula sobre la dent e entromet en aquela le cauteri ignit festinantment, e te la tieua ma un petit entro que·l malaute cente la calor del foc a la razit de la dent esser pervenguda.	When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth are decayed, and you cure those with medicines and do not confirm, then pause the patient's head on the seat, and ignite the cauterizer in the form which will come thus, so that you pause the quill over the tooth and insert into that the ignited cauterizer hastefully, and take your hand a little bit until the patient feels the heat of the fire at the root of the tooth being reached.
E aprop leva la tua ma, e aprop itera le cauteri alcunas veguadas segon que vols.	And then lift your hand, and repeat the cauterizer several times according to what you wish.
E aprop le malaute huompla la sua boca de aygua de sal e tengua aquela per una hora, e pueys stupa aquela, quar la dent mauguda es fermada e la gengiva mollificada es strenguda e la humiditat corrompuda es exsiccada.	And then the patient should fill his mouth with water of salt and hold it for an hour, and afterwards stop that, because the decayed tooth is closed and the softened gum is strengthened and the corrupted moisture is dried.
Capitol .xxi.	Twenty-First Chapter.
De cauterisacio de dolor de dent.	On Cauterization of Toothache.
Quan dolor de dent es per fregiditat, o en lu es freg o verm, o no comfereys la curacio am medicina, lahoras cauteri en aquela es segon dos manieyras: o cauteri am boder de vacas, o cauteri am foc.	When toothache is due to coldness, or in it is cold or warm, and your cure with medicine does not take effect, then cauterize that in two manners: either by border of cows, or by fire.
Cauteri am boder es que tu prenguas boder de vacas e bulhas aquel en culhe de ferr , e aprop pren coto e envolopa le sobre la extremitat de la tenta, e aprop enmergeys aquel am boder bulhit, e pausa aquel sobre la dent dolorosa festinantment entro que sia enfregidat.	Cauteri by border is that you take the border of cows and boil it in a cow's hide, and then take a cloth and wrap it around the end of the tent, and immerse that in boiling border, and pause that over the painful tooth hastily until it is cooled.
E aprop itera aquela alcunas veguadas entro que la vertut del foc pervengua a la razit de la dentz.	And then repeat that several times until the virtue of fire reaches the root of the teeth.
E si voys, submergeys lana o coto en le boder desus dit, e pausa aquel sobre la dent dolent, e pausa sobre aquel ferr ignit entro que·l ferr pervengua al preon de la conquavitat de la dent.	And if you wish, immerse wool or cloth in the border as said above, and pause that over the painful tooth, and pause on top of it with hot iron until the iron reaches the bottom of the concavity of the tooth.
Mays empero la cauterizacio am foc es que tu atendas a la quannula de eram o de ferr, e sia en le cor de lu alcuna grocesa e la acuitat del foc no pervengua a la boca del malaute.	But meanwhile the cauterization by fire is that you attend to the quill of iron or steel, and it should be in the core of it some graveness, and the sharpness of the fire not reach the mouth of the patient.
E aprop igneys le cauteri la forma del qual vindra, e pausa aquel sobre la dent e te la tua ma entro que·l cauteri sia enfregidat; e fay aquo alcunas veguadas quar la dolor sira remauguda o en aquel dia o en l’autre dia.	And then ignite the cauterizer in the shape which will come, and pause that over the tooth and take your hand until the cauterizer is cooled; and do this several times because the pain has been alleviated or on that day or the next day.
