E cove que per empressio de aquel cauteri que·l malaute umpla la sieua boca de bon boder e tengua aquel per una hora e aprop scupa le; e aquesta es la forma del cauteri.	And it is necessary that by the impression of that cauterizer, the patient fills his mouth with good border and holds it for an hour and then spits it out; and this is the form of the cauterizer.
E cauteriza am qual que tu voys extremittat segon que a tu es possible.	And cauterize as you wish, with what you can do at your best.
E aquesta es la forma de la cannula:	And this is the form of the quill:
Capitol .xxii.	Twenty-Second Chapter.
De cauterizacio de extrophulos.	On Cauterization of Extrophuli.
Quan extrophulos so de flecma e de humors fregas e no so hobedientz a digistio per medicinas e tu voys la digistio de aquelas leugerament, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri conquau la forma del qual es aquesta seguen, havent dos extremitatz hubertas per que yesca le fum deves le cauteri per l’autra extremitat, e pausa aquel ignit sobre aquel apostema una veguada, e autre si indigeyses de aquel, entro que pervengua al preon del apostema.	When extrophuli are covered with phlegm and cold humors and do not obey digestion by medicines and you wish to promote digestion of those slightly, then ignite the cauterizer in a concave shape as follows, having two extremities curved so that the smoke of the cauterizer rises from the other extremity, and pause that ignited cauterizer over that abscess once or twice, or as many times as is needed, until it reaches the bottom of the abscess.
E si l’apostema es pauca, lahoras pausa le cauteri segon la quantitat del apostema, e aprop leyssa le per tres jorns e pausa sobre lu coto enfus en boder entro que sia remaugut aquo que·l foc ha comburit.	And if the abscess is small, then pause the cauterizer according to the quantity of the abscess, and leave it for three days and pause over it wrapped in a cloth until what the fire has burned out is alleviated.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent e tentas e draps entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with an ointment, bandages, and cloths until it is healed.
E la forma de la cannula o deu cauteri a tal es comveyter.	And the form of the quill or cauterizer for this is as follows:
Capitol .xxiii.	Twenty-Third Chapter.
De cauterizacio de rauquiera de votz e de constriccio de ale.	On Cauterization of Nodes on the Voice and Constriction of Ale.
Quan las humiditatz veno sobre le quanal del pulmo, e majorment quan aquo es am fregiditat de compleccio, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia evacuat al comensament am medicinas laxativas, e aprop cauteriza aquel deves la razit del golayro en le loc depremegut.	When the humors come up to the canal of the lung, and especially when that is accompanied by coldness of congestion, it is necessary to evacuate the patient at the beginning with laxative medicines, and then cauterize that in the root of the throat in the depressed location.
E guarda te que no pervenguas am le cauteri al golayro ni no comburas de la codena de lu sino un pauc.	And beware that you do not bring the cauterizer to the glottis nor burn a large part of it, but only a small portion.
E cauteriza aquel am autra cauteri deves la junctura del col en le derier espondil de lu.	And then cauterize that with another cauterizer at the junction of the neck in the last vertebra of it.
E·l cauteri de lu sia clavilh sego la maniera precedent.	And the cauterizer should be shaped like a claw, as previously described.
E aprop cura aquel am aquo que es precedit entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with water as previously described until it is healed.
Capitol .xxiiii.	Twenty-Fourth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de malautia del pulmo e de tos.	On Cauterization of Disease of the Lung and Cough.
Quan tos e malautia de pulmo so de humiditatz fregas e le malaute no ha febre ni tisic e es malautia antiqua, lahoras cauterisa aquel am dos cauteris sobre la furcula en les locz depremegutz leontz e buoytz; e am autra cauteri en le mieg loc del pietz entre dos mamillos; e sia le cauteri clavilh segon la forma precedent.	When cough and disease of the lung are caused by cold humors and the patient has no fever or sweating, and is an old disease, then cauterize that with two cauterizers on the furcula in the depressed locations of the lungs; and another cauterizer in the middle location of the ribcage between two mamillae; and let the cauterizer be shaped like a claw according to the previous description.
E si vols, sia la tua cauterizacio punctan am le cauteri que es apelat puncta, la forma del qual precedeys en la ponctacio de dolor de aurelhas.	And if you wish, make the cauterization punctate with the cauterizer that is called a puncture, the shape of which was previously described in the punctation of earache.
E sian puntz entro cays ad aquels; e aprop cura aquel am aquo meteys que es precedit entro que sia sanat.	And make holes into those places; and then cure that with water as previously described until it is healed.
E ya sia le cauteri haventz tres ramps quar cauterizacio es am aquel: am una veguada podes far tres cauteris segon aquesta forma:	And now the cauterizers have three curves where cauterization is done on that: in one stroke you can do three cauterizations according to this form:
Capitol .xxv.	Twenty-Fifth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de titillic que es le cap del ajutori.	On Cauterization of Titillic, which is the head of the aid.
Quan le cap del ajutori es dislocat per causa de humiditatz lubricas e no es fermat en la hora del sieu retornament deves la sua dislocacio entro que sia a lu aquo costuma de retornar, e aprop per un petit movement es deslocat ayssi que s’endeve, ayssi cum nos havem testificat, lahoras cove que primieyrament redusiscas la dislocacio, e aprop le malaute sia reversat sobre le sieu dos o sobre le latz sa; e aprop eleva la codena la qual es en la partida dedintz del citillic a las partidas desus am les ditz de la tua ma sinistra, si la junctura es dislocada a las partidas dedintz.	When the head of the aid is displaced due to lubricating humors and it is not fixed in its return journey, and thus the displacement is caused by a small movement such as we have testified, then it is necessary to reduce the displacement first, and then reverse the patient's position onto his back or onto one side; and then lift the bone which is located at the back of the citillic towards the upper parts with your left hand, if the joint is displaced backwards.
E aprop igneys le cauteri havent dos caps; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	And then ignite the cauterizer having two heads; and this is its form:
E aprop cauteriza la codena entro que penetre aquela entro al autre latz; e vindra la figura de cauterizacio lahoras de iv caps cauteris.	And then cauterize the bone until it penetrates into the other side; and the figure of cauterization will come to be that of four heads of cauterizers.
e so aquel subtils segon la quantitat de tenta; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	and thus those subtle ones according to the quantity of tent; and this is its form:
E alcunas veguadas es ajustat segon aquest comte i per que son les cauteris .viii.	And several times it is adjusted according to this count, and for which are the cauterizers 8.
E aprop pausa sobre le cauteri porys cuytz am sal, e aprop fay adherir le malaute a trenquilitat, e lo membre no sia maugut per alcun temps entro que sia confortat.	And then pause over the cauterizer with pores filled with salt, and then make the patient adhere to tranquility, and let the member not be hurt for some time until it is comforted.
E si la dislocacio es a las partidas desus e tart es fayt aquo, lahoras cauteriza sobre le muscle am cauteri clavilh o am motz cauteris puntan, quar la junctura es confermada e la humiditat es romauguda e le malaute es sanat.	And if the displacement is to the upper parts and there it is made so, then cauterize over the muscle with a claw-shaped cauterizer or with punctate cauterizers, because the joint is confirmed and the moisture is removed and the patient is healed.
Capitol .xxvi.	Twenty-Sixth Chapter.
De cauterizacio del stomac.	On Cauterization of the Stomach.
Quan veno en l’estomac freg e motas humiditatz entro que aquel extrazo de la sua compleccio e so multiplicatz raumases a lu, e si tu continuas las manieyras de curacio e no confereyso, lahoras cove que le malaute sia sobre le sieu dos ressupinat, e extenda las suas mas e las suas coysas, e aprop cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris: an un cauteri dejos le pietz per la quantitat d’un dit am cauteri clavilh, e am dos cauteris dejos del dos costatz del cauteri, entro que vengua la figura de cauteri triangulada; e elonga entre els que no sian ajustatz que faran poyredura.	When cold and many humors come into the stomach to such an extent that the contents of its congestion are multiplied and are increased, and if you continue with the methods of curing and do not confirm, then it is necessary to place the patient on his back, and stretch out his arms and legs, and then cauterize that with three cauterizers: one cauterizer leaving the ribs for the quantity of a finger shaped like a claw, and two cauterizers leaving from both sides of the cauterizer, until the figure of triangular cauterization is reached; and lengthen between them so that they are not adjusted to make a precipice.
E si la profunditat del cauteri la quantitat de les dos terses de la grocesa de la codena.	And if the depth of the cauterizer is equal to the quantity of two thirds of the thickness of the bone.
E sia la figura del cauteri segon aquesta forma ses addicio, E si vols, cauteriza am gran cauteri en le mieg loc del estomac segon aquesta forma; et aquest sia un cauteri segon la forma de cercle segon aquesta forma:	And let the figure of the cauterizer be according to this form, with addition; and if you wish, cauterize with a large cauterizer in the middle location of the stomach according to this form; and this is one cauterizer according to the shape of a circle according to this form:
E sia cauterizat l’estomac punctan ad aquel que de aquest cauteri es spaventat: e es que tu senhes sobre l’estomac punt segon la quantitat que voles am tenta, e aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri en les puntz; e aprop cura aquel am la curacio qu’es precedita entro que sia sanat.	And let the stomach be punctated with that which is frightened by this cauterizer: and it is that you sense on the stomach point according to the quantity you wish with a tent, and then cauterize that with a cauterizer in the points; and then cure that with the cure that precedes until it is healed.
Capitol .xxvii.	Twenty-Seventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio del fietge fret.	On Cauterization of the Fettered Foot.
Quan endeve en le fietge dolor per fregiditat o per humiditat o per grossa ventositat entro que de la sieua normal compleccio sia getat per egressio superflua, e es curat le malaute am aquo que havem dit e no comfereys, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia ressupinat sobre la sua cervitz, e senhes am tenta tres cauteris segon aquesta forma et aquesta quantitat meteyssa sobre le fietge dejos dels ipocondres, la hon perve le decubit de home.	When pain comes to the foot due to coldness or moisture or great swelling, and it is caused by excessive egression from its normal state, and the patient is cured with water as we have said and does not confirm, then it is necessary that the patient be placed on his back on a pillow three times according to this form and this quantity, so that the cauterizers are applied to the foot leaving the iliac bones, where the human decubitus takes place.
E sia l’espazi le qual es entre quascun cauteri segon la grossetut del dit, e sia le cauteri segon la longitut del cors dreyta.	And let the space be between each cauterizer according to the thickness of the finger, and let the cauterizers be according to the length of the straight arm.
E no compremas la tua am le cauteri mot.	And do not compress your foot with the cauterizer force.
E si la quantitat de aquo que es adhurit la quantitat de la maytat de la specitut de la codena, e no y sia pus ajustat; e si le malaute stant sobre les pes de lu; e si no es estant, lahoras sia jassent, le qual ja ha extendudas las suas coysas, e eleve les sieus brasses.	And if the quantity of water used is equal to the quantity of the thickness of the bone, and not more adjusted; and if the patient is standing on his feet; and if he is not standing, then let him sit, with his legs stretched out, and raise his arms.
E es aquesta la forma del cauteri:	And this is the form of the cauterizer:
E a tu es possible que cauterizes aquestz cauteris am cauteri cutellar, quan es am tu subtilitat e prudencia en l’art.	And if you are able to cauterize those cauterizers with a cauterizer like a dagger, when it is according to your subtlety and prudence in the art.
E guarda te que trop no procesiscas en la cauterizacio, e sia adhurida la specitut de tota la codena per que sia adhurit tot le cors e pervengua entro als budels, quar la codena aqui es subtil; e sapias aquo.	And beware that you do not proceed too much in the cauterization, and let the subtlety of all the bone be adjusted so that it is adjusted to the whole body and reaches into the vessels, for this bone is subtle here; and know this.
Capitol .xxviii.	Twenty-Eighth Chapter.
De perforacio de apostema del fietge am cauteri.	On Perforation of Abscess of the Foot with a Cauterizer.
Quan endeve excitura o apostema en le fietge e voles saber si aquel apostema es en le carn del fietge o en la tunica de lu, lahoras si es en la carn del fietge, le malaute atrobo gravitat e dolor ses acuitat.	When you have an abscess or swelling on the foot and you want to know if that abscess is in the flesh of the foot or in the skin of it, then if it is in the flesh of the foot, the patient will experience great weight and pain with no sharpness.
E si es en la tunica del fietge, am la dolor es acuitat gran e vezes que ja afatiguatz les metges la cura de lu.	And if it is in the skin of the foot, then with great pain and sharpness that sometimes fatigues even the doctors with its cure.
Donc cove que·l malaute sia enversat sobre la sieua cervit; e aprop senha le loc de l’apostema am tenta; e aprop igneys le cauteri le quel es asemblat a rag, la forma del qual a precedit en l’autra pagina.	Therefore it is necessary that the patient be turned over onto his back on a pillow; and then sense the location of the abscess with a tent; and then ignite the cauterizer which is similar to a rag, the shape of which was previously described on another page.
E cauteriza am aquel i cauteri entro que tota la codena sia comborida, entro que pervengua al ciphac, entro qu’en yesca sania.	And then cauterize with that cauterizer until all the bone is consumed, until it reaches the pulp, until a healthy pus is formed.
E aprop cura aquel per curacio dels autres apostemas entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with the cure of other abscesses until it is healed.
E no cove que de aquesta forma de cauteri use sino aquel del qual le estudi en l’art de medicina es prolonguat, e en las mas del qual motas malautias an conogut; mays aquest am esperiment alcunas veguadas sia ardit sobre aquesta operacio, mays empero leyssa aquela deves nos, e es miels.	And it is not necessary to use this form of cauterizer unless you are well-versed in the art of medicine and have studied many diseases; but this one may be tried occasionally with boldness on this operation, but nonetheless leave that which I have written, and it is better.
Capitol .xxix.	Twenty-Ninth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de plauresi.	On Cauterization of Piles.
Diyssero les antics cauteri de las razitz de aristologia a plauresi frega segon aquesta manieyra esser fazedor, e es aquest que tu prenguas de las razitz de aristologia longa secca una razit pun longua que es trobada, e sia de la grossetut del dit.	The ancient cauterizers of the roots of aristology said that piles are made to be treated in this way: take a long, dry root of aristology, a pointed one that is found, and it is of the thickness of a finger.
E aprop submergeys aquela en oli e eysen aquela al foc, e aprop cauteriza per un cauteri en aquel loc le qual es entre la continuacio de la furcula am le col; e am dos cauteris petitz dejos guidazi, un pauc declinans a la partida que es dejus la barba, e am dos cauteris en aquo que es declinant entre la quinta costa e la cizena, declinant un pauc a las partidas detras; e am autre cauteri en le mieg loc del pietz; et am autre sobre l’estomac, et am tres cauteris de las partidas detras; et am un cauteri en aquel loc le qual es entre las dos spallas, e am dos cauteris dels dos latz del pietz, dejos le cauteri le qual es entre doas spallas.	And then immerse it in oil and ignite it at the fire, and then cauterize with a cauterizer in that location which is between the continuation of the furcula and the neck; and with two small cauterizers as guides, one slightly inclining towards the side below the beard, and with two cauterizers on either side of the fifth rib, inclining slightly to the back parts; and with another cauterizer in the middle location of the foot; and with another above the stomach, and with three cauterizers at the back parts; and with one cauterizer in that location which is between the two shoulder blades, and with two cauterizers on either side of the foot, leaving the cauterizer which is between the two shoulder blades.
E no cove que compremas la tua ma am le cauteri, ans sia en le manifest de la codena en obra.	And it is not necessary to compress your hand with the cauterizer, but rather be in the manifestation of the bone in work.
E ja diyssero alscus antics que so alscus dels homes les quals uson de cauteri de ferr semblant a ray e igneysso aquel, e meto aquel en aquel loc le qual es entre las costas, entro que pervenguam am aquel ad aquel apostema e sia foragetada sania, ayssi cum havem dit en l’apostema del fietge.	And some ancient ones said that some men are such that they use a cauterizer of iron like a ray and ignite it, and place it in that location which is between the ribs, until it reaches that abscess and purges out pus, just as we have said in the abscess of the foot.
Mays en aquesta perforacio am cauteri no es ses temor, quar hu mor tantost ho accideys en le loc fistula a la qual no es sanacio.	But in this perforation with a cauterizer there is no fear, for they die soon after it happens in the location of the fistula to which there is no healing.
Capitol .xxx.	Thirty-First Chapter.
De la cauterizacio de la melsa.	On Cauterization of Melancholy.
Quan tu curas la malautia de la melsa am aquo que havem dit de la curacio en la divisio e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cauteri en lu es segon tres manieras, las quals totas son dreyturieras, de las quals la una es que fassas tres cauteris o quatre linhan segon la longitut de la melsa segon la figura dels cauteris del fietge, la figura dels quals ha precedit.	When you cure the disease of melancholy with water as we have said in the division and do not confirm your cure, then make a cauterizer in that location according to three ways, all of which are right-sided, of which one is that you make three or four lines according to the length of the melancholy according to the figure of the cauterizers of the foot, the figure of which was previously described.
E sia entre quascun cauteri la grossetut d’un dit o un pauc mes, e la manieyra del cauteri sia la manieyra la qual havem dita en le cauteri del fietge engualment.	And let the thickness between each cauterizer be the thickness of a finger or a little more, and the method of the cauterizer be the method which we have said in the cauterizers of the foot equally.
E no compremas la tua ma am le cauteri; e le malaute sia eves sobre lo sieu dos.	And do not compress your hand with the cauterizer; and let the patient be lying on his back.
E es autra manieyra de cauterizar, so es que tu igniscas le cauteri haventz dos vertimentz, la qual causa havem dita en le capitol de dislocacio del muscle, e elava la codena la qual es en le endreyt de la melsa la hon perve le jazer del malaute sinistre.	And it is another method of cauterizing, so that you ignite the cauterizer having two handles, which we have said in the chapter on dislocation of the muscle, and lift up the bone which is at the end of the melancholy where the patient's left side lies.
E sia la tua elevacio am la qual elevas la codena segon la longuesa del cors, per que sian faytz cauteris segon la latitut del cos.	And let your elevation be that which you raise the bone according to the length of the body, so that they may make cauterizers according to the latitude of the body.
E aprop entromet les dos vernimentz, ignitz mot, en aquel entro que am aquels penetres la codena de la autra part.	And then insert the two handles, ignite one, into that which is on the other side of the bone.
E aprop extrayt le cauteri; e donc son faytz quatre cauteris.	And then extract the cauterizer; and thus make four cauterizers.
E si voys, cauteriza am cauteri havent tres vernimentz.	And if you wish, cauterize with a cauterizer having three handles.
E aprop tu cura le cauteri pus que aia laysat de getar brac per trops jorns, quar mays es comferent que las autras causas precedentz en la curacio.	And then cure the cauterizer more thoroughly than you would leave it to gather dust for many days, because it is more certain that other causes precede in the cure.
Capitol .xxxi.	Thirty-Second Chapter.
De cauterizacio de ydropici.	On Cauterization of Hydrophobia.
Cauteri no catz en ydropici sino en alcinte3 propriament.	Cauteries are not cut in hydrophobia, but rather in a specific and proper manner.
Quan tu curas le ydropic am las manieyras de curacio las quals havem ditas en la divisio e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que aquel cauterizes am quatre cauteris en le cercuit del embelic e am un cauteri sobre l’estomac, e am autre cauteri sobre le fietge, e am autre cauteri sobre la melsa, e am dos cauteris entre les spondils del dos, e un cauteri en lo dreyt del pietz, e am autre cauteri sobre l’estomac.	When you cure the hydrophobic with the methods of cure which we have said in the division and do not confirm your cure, then it is necessary that he be cauterized with four cauterizers around the umbilicus, one on the stomach, one on the foot, one on the melancholy, two between the vertebrae of the back, one on the right side of the foot, and another on the stomach.
E la quantitat de la profunditat del cauteri sia propdana a la spicitut de la codena.	And the quantity of the depth of the cauterizer be proportioned to the subtlety of the bone.
E aprop layssa le cauteri ubert per so que gete brac per lonc temps.	And then leave the cauterizer untouched for as long as possible, so that it may gather dust and not be used again.
E no evacuas le malaute de curacio aprop le cauteri am aquo que cove per que sian agreguadas a lu doas entencios, e sira festinada a lu am ajutori sanacio.	And do not evacuate the patient of cure near the cauterizer with water as is necessary for two purposes, and thus hasten to it with the aid of healing.
La forma del cauteri am lo qual es cauterizat lo ventre sia clavilh segon que la forma de aquel es desus precedent, e es aquel am le qual es cauterizat le dos sia olivar segon qu’es precedent a la sua forma.	The shape of the cauterizer with which the stomach is cauterized is claw-shaped, according to the form that precedes it, and it is this one with which the back is cauterized, olive-shaped, according to its preceding form.
Capitol .xxxii.	Thirty-Second Chapter.
De cauterizacio de pes e de las coyssas.	On Cauterization of Pains and Limbs.
Quan les pes so apostematz en ydropitz e so repletz de aygua sitrina, cove que cauterisas les pes sobre le dos del pe in nocrati aquo que es entre le auricular e le anular, e eleva la tua ma am le cauteri e no torses aquel; e aprop eleva la tua ma, e no retornes aquela de tot, quar l’aygua satrina rezuda.	When the pains are abscessed in hydrophobic and filled with stagnant water, it is necessary that you cauterize the pains on the back of the knee in a cauterizer that is between the auricular and anular, and raise your hand with the cauterizer and do not turn it; and then raise your hand and do not return to it, for the stagnant water resists.
Es le cauteri segon aquesta forma: E aprop fay sobre las doas coyssas dos cauteris, e en quascuna coysa sia feyt cauteri am la extremitat del cauteri cutellar.	It is the cauterizer according to this form: And then make two cauterizers on both limbs, and in each limb make a cauterizer at the extremity of the cauterizer like a claw.
E sia le cauteri segon la longitut de la coyssa: i dejos le denolh e l’autre jos le mieg loc de la coyssa; e sobre quascuna coyssa dos cauteris.	And let the cauterizers be according to the length of the limb: one at the top and the other at the middle location of the limb; and on each limb, two cauterizers.
E layssa la plagua uberta ses curacio per lonc temps per so que alcuna aygua resuda de lu.	And leave the wound open without cure for a long time, so that some water may flow out of it.
E aprop cura le am aquelas causas las quals havem ditas.	And then cure with those causes which we have said.
Capitol .xxxiii.	Thirty-Third Chapter.
De cauterizacio de cos de ventre.	On Cauterization of the Belly.
Quan cos de ventre es per freg e per humiditat entro que debelice las vertutz, so es la vertut digestiva e retentiva, las quals so en l’estomac e en les budels, e es curat aquo am las manieyras de curacio e no confereys, e vezes le malaute suffertan cauteri de vertut exhiberant, lahoras cauteriza aquel am gran cauteri sobre le sieu stomac segon que a precedit en la cauterizacio del estomac, am le cauteri del cercle e am quatre cauteris en le cercuit del embelic subtils, am cauteri clavilh subtil; e am cauteri sobre le alcatin sobre alozis gran, o am dos cauteris.	When the belly is afflicted with heat and moisture to the extent that it weakens the virtues, namely the digestive and retentive virtues, which are in the stomach and intestines, and it is not cured with the methods of cure we have said and does not confirm, and sometimes the patient suffers from cauterization of virtue appearing, then cauterize him with a great cauterizer on his stomach according to what precedes in the cauterization of the stomach, with the cauterizer of the circle and four small cauterizers in the circuit of the umbilicus, with a claw-shaped cauterizer; or two cauterizers.
E si vezes las humiditatz exhuberants e le malaute aquo tollerant, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre le pentenilh e sobre les budels, e fort leu ajustant dos cauteris sobre l’estomac e prop dels inguonas, quar es curacio perficent de juvament de la qual no erras.	And if sometimes the excess of moisture appears and the patient tolerates it, then cauterize him on the navel and intestines, and firmly adjust two cauterizers over the stomach and near the groin, for it is perfect cure of which you will not err.
Capitol .xxxiv.	Thirty-Fourth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de emorroydas antiquas.	On Cauterization of Old Hemorrhoids.
Quan so en la natura derier emorroydas antiquas o una de humors grossas fregas o de humiditatz corrompudas, e son curadas am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no confereys la tieua curacio, lahoras cauterisa am tres cauteris sobre le pus dejos spondilh del dos petit e petit triangular, e am cauteri desus le ombelic cays per dos ditz.	When in nature there remain old hemorrhoids or one of the gross humors is inflamed or corrupted with moisture, and they are not cured with water as we have said in the division and do not confirm your cure, then cauterize him with three cauterizers above the left and right triangular bones of the small back, and with a cauterizer above the navel which falls on both sides.
E si doptas que l’estomac de lu sia enfregidat e la vianda de lu no sia degerida, e la cara de lu vezes apostemada, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre l’estomac am gran cauteri segon que es precedit; e am un cauteri sobre fietge, e am autre cauteri sobre la melsa de lu am cauteri clavilh, e leyssa le cauteri per alcun temps ubert, e aprop cura lu entro que sia sanat.	And if you observe that the stomach of him is inflamed and his food is not digested, and his face is often abscessed, then cauterize him on the stomach with a great cauterizer according to what precedes; and one cauterizer on the foot, and another cauterizer on his melancholy with a claw-shaped cauterizer; and leave the cauterizer untouched for some time, and then cure him until he is healed.
Capitol .xxxv.	Thirty-Fifth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de atheyl aprop la abscizio de lor.	On Cauterization of Athletes near the Absence of Their Own.
Quan tu abscindes atheyl, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri que es asemblat a ray.	When you abscess athletes, then ignite the cauterizer that is similar to a ray.
Aprop entremet aquel ignit en aquel atheyl abscis, e ultima la tieua ma entro que pervengua le cauteri al orifici de la vena de la qual ve la sanc.	And then insert that ignited cauterizer into the abscessed athlete, and finally apply your hand until the cauterizer reaches the opening of the vein from which blood flows.
E fay aquo una vetz o doas, quar si achieyl son trops, lahoras cauteriza quascun de lor segon que havem recontat, e aprop cura aquels am aquo que confereys a lor dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And make so one or two, for if they are many, then cauterize each of them according to what we have recounted, and finally cure those with water that confirms their wounds until they are healed.
E si cauterizas am gran cauteri sobre alquatin, es mays derier en juvament.	And if you cauterize with a great cauterizer on someone, it is more certain in judgment.
Capitol .xxxvi.	Thirty-Sixth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistolas que son faytas en la natura derie en las partidas de lu.	On Cauterization of Fistulas that are formed in the natural openings of the body.
Quan la natura no obeziys a la obra la qual havem recomtada en son loc, e·l pacient es espaventat per aquo, sia sanat am cauteri.	When nature does not obey the work that we have recommended in its location, and the patient is frightened by this, let him be healed with a cauterizer.
Donc quan ad alcun ve fistola en la natura derier, e es antiquada, corro sania de lu e humiditatz corrompudas, e donc aquo que es pus digne que cove es que proes aquela am tenta subtil, e aprop conoys la quantitat de la profunditat de lu am la devant dita tenta.	Therefore when someone has a fistula in the natural opening, and it is old, filled with stagnant blood and corrupted moisture, and therefore what is most fitting is that you probe that one with a subtle attempt, and then know the quantity of its depth with the previously mentioned probe.
Aprop igneys le cauteri que es semblant a ray.	And then ignite the cauterizer that is similar to a ray.
E aprop met aquel cauteri ignit en aquesta fistula, e segon la quantitat en la qual intrec la tenta.	And then insert that ignited cauterizer into this fistula, and according to the quantity of the depth which the probe has reached.
E itera sobre aquela le cauteri entro que sian comburitz aquels cors corrumputz tost una veguada o dos o tres, segon la quantitat de la tua necessitat.	And then iterate over that one with the cauterizer until those corrupted bodies are burned away in one, two or three times, according to your necessity.
E guarda te de combustio de nervi e de vena; o si fistula va al cors de la vesica o al cors del budel, lahoras guarda te de totz aquels locz; e no fassas aquo sino quan la fistula es en loc carnos e cogitas que no es penetrant.	And beware of burning the nerves and veins; or if the fistula goes to the bladder or intestines, then beware of all those places; and do not make a cauterization unless the fistula is in a fleshy location and you are certain that it is not penetrating.
E aprop cura le loc entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that place until it is healed.
E si le loc es sigillat, e so abscindidas de lu las materias, e roman ayssi per lonc temps, lahoras sapias que ja es curat entierament.	And if the place is sealed, and all matter has been abscessed from it, and it remains thus for a long time, then you will know that it is entirely cured.
E si las materias no so de lu ostadas, lahoras sapias que es penetrant o en le preon de lu os corromput, o cays aquo de aquelas causas de las quals vindra rememoracio en son loc.	And if the matter is not removed from there, then you will know that it is penetrating or in the process of corrupting, or falling into those causes of which a reminder will be found in its location.
Capitol .xxxvii.	Thirty-Seventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio dels ronhos.	On Cauterization of Tonsils.
Quan en les ronhos endeve dolor per freg o per grossa ventozitat, e per aysso le coyt del malaute es amermat, lahoras cove que cauterizes aquel sobre les ronhos am cauteri sobre quascun ronho am cauteri clavilh del qual precesic la rememoracio.	When in the tonsils there is pain from inflammation or excessive ventosity, and because of this the patient's throat is pained, then it is necessary that you cauterize each tonsil with a claw-shaped cauterizer of which the description precedes.
E fort leu cauterizam am le segon un petit dejos, per que vindran tres cauteris liniatz, e donc siran mays deriers en juvament.	And then cauterize again with a small one, so that three linear cauterizers will appear, and therefore they will be more certain in judgment.
Capitol .xxxviii.	Thirty-Eighth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la vesica.	On Cauterization of the Bladder.
Quan accideys en la vesica debelitat e mollificacio per freg e per humiditatz ayssi que·l malaute la urina no retengua, lahoras cauteriza aquel en la partida pus dejos sobre la vesiqua, la hon comensan les pels del pentenilh, e cauteriza am un cauteri en la partida dreyta, e am autre en la senestra de lu.	When there is debilitation and mollification in the bladder due to inflammation and moisture, so that the patient cannot retain urine, then cauterize him on the most distant part of the bladder, where the hairs of the navel begin, and cauterize with one cauterizer on the right side and another on the left.
E sia la longitut de quascun cauteri segon la cantitat dels not del pous; e cauteriza aquel am cauteri en la partida pus bassa del dos, o am dos cauteris si es necessitat.	And let the length of each cauterizer be according to the quantity of the nails on the foot; and cauterize him with a cauterizer in the lowest part of the back, or with two cauterizers if necessary.
E sia cauteri clavilh segon que es procesit.	And let it be a claw-shaped cauterizer according to what has been processed.
Capitol .xxxix.	Thirty-Ninth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la mayra.	On Cauterization of the Arm.
Quan veno en la mayra freg e humiditatz, e per aysso es prohibida enpreignacio, e son corrompudas las mestruas de lu, e es tardada la provocacio de lor, e accideys dolor deves le haveniment de lor, lahoras cove que·l loc sia cauterizat am tres cauteris en le circuit del ombelic, ayssi cum havem dit en le cauteri de la vesica; e am cauteri sobre le loc pus dejos del dos, o am dos cauteris, e sia le cauteri clavilh.	When there is inflammation and moisture in the arm, and because of this it is prohibited to make an incision, and the menstruation of that person is corrupted, and it is delayed in its provocation, and accidents occur causing pain in the movement of their arms, then it is necessary that the location be cauterized with three cauterizers in the circuit of the navel, just as we have said in the cauterization of the bladder; and with a cauterizer on the most distant part of the back, or with two cauterizers, and let it be a claw-shaped cauterizer.
Capitol .xl.	Fortieth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la dislocacio de l’anqua.	On Cauterization of the Dislocation of the Hip.
Quan humiditatz moucozas so efundudas a la partida de la anqua, e so faytas causas del yssiment del sieu loc, e senhal de lu es que la coyssa es prolonguada sobre l’autre quan so comparadas entre lor.	When moisture is poured into the part of the hip, and certain causes of swelling occur in that location, and a sign of it is that the limb is prolonged over the other when they are compared between them.
E le loc de la dislocacio es atrobat en lu quays boyt.	And the location of the dislocation is located in the way it has been described above.
Adonc cove que cauterizas le malaute sobre la partida de la anqua de lu am cauteri a sercle semblant, pus que tu auras senhat am tenta en le cercuit de la partida ayssi cum es revolguda, e per so que la partida caia el mieg loc del cercle.	Then it is necessary that you cauterize the patient on the part of the hip with a circular cauterizer similar to a ring, as you have sensed with the probe in the circuit of that part, and because the part falls in the middle location of the circle.
E sia le cauteri del qual precedit la forma en la cauterizacio del estomac.	And let it be the cauterizer of which the form precedes in the cauterization of the stomach.
E si aquest cauteri no es a tu present, lahoras cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris am cauteri olivar gran.	And if this cauterizer is not available to you, then cauterize with three cauterizers and one large olive-shaped cauterizer.
E sia fayt le cauteri segon la quantitat de la ispicitut de tota la codena; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And let the cauterizer be made according to the quantity of the subtlety of all the bone; and then cure that one until it is healed.
Capitol .xli.	Forty-First Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la vena sciatica.	On Cauterization of the Sciatic Nerve.
Quan dolor ve en la partida de anqua, e so causa de lu freg et humiditatz, le malaute es curat am aquo que havem dit e no confereys, e aquo es antiquat, lahoras cove que tu lacses le malaute de humors grosses am pillulas fetidas o am pillulas artificials o semblantz; e aprop cauteriza aquel.	When pain occurs in the part of the hip, and its cause is inflammation and moisture, the patient is cured with water as we have said and does not confirm, and it is old, then it is necessary that you cleanse the patient's gross humors with fetid pills or artificial pills or similar ones; and then cauterize him.
E la manieyra del cauteri en aquela es segon dos manieyras: o cauteri am medicinas comburentz, o cauteri am foc.	And the method of the cauterizer in that is according to two methods: either a cauterizer with burning medicines or a cauterizer by fire.
Sira segon dos manieyras scientas, de las quals es la una que cauterizes aquel sobre la partida de l’ancha de lu am tres cauteris triangulatz segon aquesta forma; e fay am aquels bona profunditat.	It is according to two scientific methods, of which one is that you cauterize him on the part of the hip with three triangular cauterizers in this shape; and make a good depth in them.
E sia le spazi le qual es entre cascun cauteri la quantitat de la grossitut del dit e si le cauteri olivar o gran.	And let the space between each cauterizer be the quantity of the thickness of the said digit, and if it is an olive-shaped or large cauterizer.
Mays alcunas veguadas sia le cauteri sobre le mieg loc sobre le cap de l’anquan per que son quatre cauteris.	Sometimes there may be a cauterizer on the middle location above the head of the hip, for there are four cauterizers.
E si vols, cauteriza am le cercle del qual es precesida la forma en la cauterizacio de la dislocacio de l’anqua, la i que sia cercle continent e comburey la ispicitut de tota la codena.	And if you wish, cauterize with the circle of which the form precedes in the cauterization of the dislocation of the hip, and let it be a continent and burning circle that consumes the subtlety of all the bone.
E aquesta es la manieyra de cauteri in ciatiqua quan dolor es adherent al anqua e no es estenduda entro a la coyssa.	And this is the method of cauterization in sciatica when pain is attached to the hip and does not spread into the joint.
Mays si es estenduda entro a la coyssa, lahoras cauteriza aquel am dos cauteris sobre la coyssa sobre le loc al qual envireys le malaute que es la dolor; e am un cauteri sobre la cavilha per quatre ditz un pauc deves la part cilvestra.	But if it spreads into the joint, then you should cauterize him with two cauterizers on the joint above the location where the patient feels the pain; and one cauterizer on the femur for about four inches a little bit away from the pubic area.
E si le cauteri cutellar, e sia la profunditat del cauteri segon la quantitat de la ispicitut de la codena.	And if the cauterizer is knife-shaped, and let the depth of the cauterizer be according to the quantity of the subtlety of the bone.
E si le malaute envireys que la dolor es estenduda entro al loc prop les ditz des pes, lahoras cauteriza aquel aqui on envireys am cauteri per tres puntz o quatre o mays si indigeys de aquel.	And if the patient says that the pain is spreading into the location near the bone of the feet, then you should cauterize him there where it hurts with a cauterizer for three to four points or more if needed.
E si le malaute envireys dolor esser dejos le donolh ves la coyssa, lahoras cauteriza aquel aqui am un cauteri cutellar.	And if the patient says that the pain is below the kneecap and into the joint, then you should cauterize him there with a knife-shaped cauterizer.
E guarda te en tota cauterizacio que no ultimes am le cauteri en tant que comburas nervi o gran arceria, e que per aquo a tu es sobre le malaute mal noccument o contraccio.	And be careful in all cauterization that you do not leave the cauterizer on for too long, so as not to burn nerves or large arteries, and because of this it may harm your patient or cause contractions.
E yeu ja e vist un e autre de aquels les quals cauterizero sobre la cavilha e ultimero en la cauterizacio, e la cama foc inflada entro que la tumor aconseguit lo pe, e foc perforat e corromput tot le pe.	And you have already seen one and another of those which I would cauterize on the femur and finally in the cauterization, and the leg becomes inflamed with fire until the tumor reaches the foot, and the fire is perforated and corrupted all the foot.
E aprop accidic fort solucio de ventre, e aprop aquo la mort.	And then comes forth a strong solution of the belly, and therefore death ensues.
E si la dolor es en dos partidas ensemps cauteriza quascuna segon aquesta manieyra.	And if the pain is in two parts together, cauterize each one according to this method.
E diysero les savis alcus en la cauterizacio de anqua cauteri del qual aquesta es la manieyra: fay semblant a cercle de ferr del qual le cercuit sia la maytat de un palm; e sia deves le sieu orrifici segon la grossesa de un os de datil o mens un pauc.	And the wise men say that in the cauterization of the hip, this is the method: make it similar to a circle of iron, whose circumference is one-quarter of a palm; and be careful with your opening according to the thickness of a walnut or slightly less.
E dedintz aquel cercle sia un autre tertz; e sia le spazi le qual es entre lor la quantitat del notz del pous; e sian aquels cercles ubertz de dos partidas; e sia la longitut de aquels cays un notz o dos notz, e fay en aquels margue de ferr decentment apparelhat en les cercles; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	And inside that circle is another third; and be the space between them the quantity of the nails on the foot; and let those circles be two parts; and let their length be one nail or two nails, and make in them a border of iron decently adorned with the circles; and this is the form of it:
Aprop sia ignit en le foc entro que s’enrogesisca e gete scintillas, e aprop sia pausat sobre la partida del anqua, le malaute colcat sobre le latz sa.	And then be ignited in the fire until it reddens and gives sparks, and then be placed on the part of the hip, the patient lying on their side.
E donc cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris redontz en una veguada.	And thus cauterize him with three circular cauterizers in one motion.
E aprop layssa aquel per tres jorns; aprop emplastre aquel am boder e layssa la plagua uberta per trops dias; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then leave him for three days; then apply an ointment to the wound and let it remain open for many days; and then cure him with remedies until he is healed.
Diys Albucasis : o, filhs, de aquesta specia de cauteri pauc havem usat per la terror del reguardament de lu, e per aquo que paucs havem trobatz les quals reguardan sobre lu.	Thus says Albucasis: "Oh, sons, of this type of cauterization we have used little, due to the fear of looking at it, and therefore few have found those who look upon it."
Mays dels bos cauteris a lu qui les sufferta, et atroba am aquel le loc de lu.	But from good cauterizers that suffered there, and finding the location of it.
Mays cauteri am medicinas adhurentz es que tu fassas dos cercles haventz armula perforada en la qual deyssen le guaffo de la porta de ferr; sia la longuitut de la paretz en la nauteza de lor sian dos nozes o quays aquels.	But cauterizers with burning medicines are those that you make two circles having an armula perforated in which the guaffo of the iron door is seen; let the length of the partitions be in the height of theirs be two nails or as many.
E si le spazi le qual es entre quascu la quantitat de la grossitut del dit; e sian ubertz dejos e desus, e sian que contenguan se entre lor segon aquesta forma:	And if the space between them is equal to the quantity of the thickness of the finger; and let them be above and below, and let them contain themselves between them according to this form:
E aprop pausa sobre la partida de la anqua le malaut jasent sobre le latz sa, e comprem la tua ma sobre la partida de la anqua; e aprop pren de aygua cauda e fon la entre dos cercles, e la qualiditat de aquela sia am le foc petit a petit, e te aquela per la quantitat de una hora, e sufferta le malaute la mordicacio e la adhustio de lu — quar aquel atrobo mordicacio ayssi cum de foc — entro que cesse la mordicacio.	And then pause over the part of the hip the patient lying on their side, and press your hand against the part of the hip; and then take cold water and pour it between two circles, and let its quality be like a small fire gradually, and hold that for an hour, and apply the mordicatio and adjustment to him — as if from fire — until the mordicatio ceases.
E aprop eleva la tua ma am le instrument et abstergeys l’aygua cauda de tota la anqua am aygua dousa.	And then lift your hand with the instrument and wash away the cold water from all of the hip with warm water.
E aprop leyssa aquel per tres jorns e pausa sobre aquel boder entro que sia la negror de la adhustio remauguda, e leyssa aquo per alcus jorns, e correra de lu poyredura; aquest es derier en juvament.	And then leave him for three days and pause on that border until the blackness of the adjustment is removed, and leave him thus for some days, and he will recover his strength; this is the final stage.
E aprop cura aquel am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure him with remedies until he is healed.
E si la dolor es extenduda entro la coyssa o la camba, fay a lu estatua en lu que contengua aygua segon que es feyt en la anqua engualment.	And if the pain is extended into the joint or leg, make him stand in water according to how it is done on the hip equally.
E aquesta es la manieyra de aygua cauda, e yeu ja he scrit aquela en le tractat de la rectificacio de medicinas.	And this is the method of cold water, and you have already written it in the treatise on the rectification of medicines.
Recipe de alcali e de caus no extinta de amdos ana partida una, e trissa les e pausa en una ola nova de la qual la partida dejos sia perforada per un petit trauc, segon la quantitat que intre en lu ray.	Recipe of alkali and unextinguished cause, one part in each side, and mix them together and pause in a new wave of which the left part is perforated by a small hole, according to the quantity that enters into it ray.
E pausa dejos le fons de la ola autra ola enveyriada, e gete sobre aquel alcali e caus viva de aygua doussa la qual cobra aquels per un dit, e pus que tu compremes aquels am la tieua ma per bona compressio, e leyssa la hola que deyssenda de lu aygua aguda en la partida dejos a la ola enveyriada.	And pause then the bottom of the wave in another wave enveloped, and place above it alkali and living cause with warm water that absorbs them by one finger, and then press them with your own hand for good compression, and leave the hole to descend from the sharp water into the left part of the enveloping wave.
E aprop ajusta tota aquela aygua, e geta la sobre autra caus viva e autre alcali renovelatz, quar aquela lahoras sira de mot forta acuitat, la qual es aministrada en motas operacios de medicina e en cauterizacio dels autres membres, quar operacio fa de foc.	And then adjust all that water, and place it above another living cause and new alkali renewed, because that which is done with great force of acuity will be administered in many operations of medicine and cauterization of other members, where the operation is done by fire.
E so de las medicinas alcunas am las quals es cauterizat ancha, ayssi cum tezizic e mel anacrat e caus am sabo enayssi que sian mesclatz.	And some of these medicines with which the hip is cauterized, such as mezquit and manna crataegi, and living cause mixed with saba in such a way that they are blended together.
E Gualia recontet de un home dels antics la operacio e la curacio am la qual es curada dolor de anqua e de vena sciatica, e magnifiquet mot be esser de aquel, e diys que no hac necessitat de autra curacio, e quar es sanat per una veguada ayssi cum recomtec, quar fort leu aquel intrec en banh e eysic ja sa d’aquel.	And Gualia recounted the story of a man from antiquity who was operated on and cured with an operation that relieved pain in the hip and sciatic vein, and magnificently emphasized how wonderful it was to see him, saying that he did not need any further treatment, and that he was healed in just one moment like this, because he had already taken a bath and eaten food from that very thing.
Et es que sia pres de certarragi vert, e si no es atrobat vert, sia presa figua recent; e mot sia trissada am un pauc de grays e sia pausat sus la anqua en la qual es la dolor, o en la coyssa, o en la camba, e sia liat.	And thus it is that one must take a certain kind of vertebrae, and if not found, then take a recent fig tree; and mix it with a little bit of gray matter and place it on the hip where there is pain, or in the joint, or in the leg, and bind it.
E sia layssat per la cantitat de tres horas o per la quantitat que·l malaute centa cedacio de la adhustio.	And let it be left for the quantity of three hours or for the amount that the patient shows relaxation of the adjustment.
E aprop met aquel en banh e donc quan le cors de lu sia enrozat, entromet aquel en le sol, quar la dolor cessa e es sanat.	And then place it in water and thus when the body is relaxed, immerse it in the sun, for the pain ceases and he is healed.
E sapias que no cove que alcu use de cauteri am aquestas medicinas sino aprop la evacuacio del cors.	And know that it is not necessary to use cauterization with these medicines unless there is an evacuation of the body.
Mays ja Escorides diysec que quan am fenda de cabra la vena stretica es cauterizada, aprofieyra a lu mo be; e sia le cauteri am lu segon aquesta manieyra: sia presa lana e sia enbeguda en oli antic, e sia pausat entre le pous del pe e entre le fossil.	But already Escorides says that when a goat's wound is cauterized on the sciatic vein, it will soon benefit him; and let the cauterizer be taken with him according to this method: take wool and soak it in old oil, and place it between the toes of the foot and between the bones.
E aprop pren fenda de cabra secca e emflasma aquela am foc entro que sia fayta carbo; e aprop pausa lu sobre la lana e leysa la entro que sia estengida.	And then take dry goat's flesh and infuse it with fire until it becomes carbonized; and then place it on the wool and leave it inside until it is stretched.
E aprop itera aquo, e no cessas far aquo entro que·l scintiment de la mordicacio pervengua entro al anqua e repausa la dolor.	And then iterate this process, and do not stop until the sensation of the biting reaches into the hip and relieves the pain.
Et aquesta manieyra de cauteri es apelat cauteri de vaquas.	And this method of cauterization is called "cauterio de vaquas".
Capitol .xlii.	Chapter XLII.
De cauterizacio de dolor de dos.	On the Cauterization of Pain in Two.
Alcunas veguadas dolor es en le dos per tropas causas, cum per cazement o per percucio o per superflua evacuacio, e per causas ad aquelas semblantz, per infusio de materia frega e humida.	Sometimes pain is in the two due to many causes, such as by fracture or percussion or excessive evacuation, and similar causes through infusion of moist and humid matter.
E cauteri no catz sino en aquesta sola specia la qual es fayta per efusio de materia frega.	And the cauterizer is not applied except in this single species which is made by effusion of moist matter.
Donc cove, aprop evacuacio del malaute am pillulas fitidas e am semblant a lor, que sian faytas sobre·l dos en le qual es la dolor tres linhas segon la latitut de lu, pus que senhas am tentha en quascuna linha v cauteris o mays, segon la quantitat que ve de la tolleransa del malaute e de la vertut de lu.	Therefore, it is necessary to evacuate the patient with fetid pills and similar ones that are made on the two in which there is pain three lines according to its latitude, plus a sign or more in each line, depending on the quantity that appears from the tolerance of the patient and the virtue of it.
E sia fayta cauterizacio am cauteri de punt.	And let there be cauterization with pointed cauterizers.
E si vols, cauteriza am tres cauteris o am quatre am cauteri clavilh medial segon aquesta forma:	And if you wish, cauterize with three or four cauterizers with a middle clavish shape according to this form:
Capitol .xliii.	Chapter XLIII.
De cauterizacio al comensament de gilbositat.	On the Cauterization at the Beginning of Giltiness.
Motas veguadas endeve aquesta malautia als petitz enfantz; e senhal del comensament de lu en les enfantz es que accideys sobre lor estrectura en le ale eves la elevacio e·l movement.	Many times this illness befalls small children; and the sign of its beginning in children is that it occurs suddenly on their stature, causing elevation and movement in the alleys.
E atrobas en le derier espondil del dos e dels notz de lu que ja comensa a sobremontar sobre les autres spondils.	And it is found in the last vertebra of the back and the nails of the body that already begins to rise above the other vertebrae.
E donc quan tu vezes aquo e voles prohibir, lahoras cauterisa aquel am cauteri que sia cercle segon aquesta forma:	And then when you see this and wish to prevent it, immediately cauterize him with a circular cauterizer according to this form:
que prengua le cauteri sobre tota partida del spondilh engualment.	that takes the cauterizer on all sides of the vertebra equally.
E si vols, cauteriza en le circuit del spondilh am le cauteri de punt dos linhas o tres.	And if you wish, cauterize in the circle of the vertebra with a pointed cauterizer two or three lines.
E sian les puntz propdas entre lor.	And let there be proper points between them.
E aprop cura le loc entro que sia sanat am aquo que havem dit.	And then cure the place until it is healed with the water that we have said.
Mays guarda que cauteri no sia administrat en gelbositat que sia fayta per spasme de nervi.	But beware, for cauterization should not be administered in a giltiness caused by nerve spasm.
Capitol .xliv.	Chapter XLIV.
De cauterizacio de podagra e de dolor de juncturas.	On the Cauterization of Gout and Joint Pain.
Quan dolor de juncturas son faytas per humors fregas les quals so enfundutz a quascun membre del cors, lahoras quan veno dolors en los pes, de costuma dels metges es que aquo apelen podragua propriament.	When joint pains are caused by hot humors that envelop each member of the body, then when pains come to the feet, it is customary for doctors to properly call this condition "podagra".
E donc cum es curada podagra de causa frega am manieyra de cura e no so remaugudas las dolors, lahoras las remau cauteri.	And therefore, when gout caused by hot humors is cured by the method of cure and the pains are not relapsed, then the relapses are cut with cauterizers.
E es que tu cauterizas aquel aprop evacuacio en le circuit de la junctura del pe am motz cauteris.	And that you cauterize him by evacuation in the circle of the joint of the foot with many cauterizers.
E sia cauteri olivar del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And let there be an olive-shaped cauterizer, whose form is this:
E si es necessitat que puntz sia fayt sobre la fassia del pe, lahoras fay am cauteri de punt.	And if it is necessary to make points on the skin of the foot, then make them with a pointed cauterizer.
E si las dolors pujan entro als denolhs o a las autras juncturas, e aquo motas vetz s’endeve, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre quascun donolh am tres cauteris o quatre de tota partida am aquest cauteri olivar.	And if the pains rise into the joints or to other joints, and many times they are endued with it, then cauterize him on each joint with three or four cauterizers of all sides with this olive-shaped cauterizer.
E si motz cauteris que aquestz cauteris sian a tu necessaris, lahoras cauteriza aquel e no premas trop la tua ma am le cauteri abans, sia tant solament enviro la specitut de la codena.	And if many cauterizers are needed to perform this operation, then cauterize him and do not press too hard with your hand on the cauterizer, so that it is only as much as the thickness of a bone.
E si las dolors pugan entro al donolh e·l dos, lahoras aministra le cauteri le qual havem dit en le sieu capitol.	And if the pains rise into the joint and the back, then administer the cauterizer which we have said in our chapter.
E si las dolors so en las mas tant solament, e es apelada suagra, lahoras puncta en le circuit dels focils ayssi cum se revolvo, puncta en aquels dos linhas.	And if the pains are only in the most part and it is called sugar, then point in the circle of the nails as they turn, point in those two lines.
E si reman de las dolors en les ditz, lahoras puncta en le cercuit dels focils sobre quascun notz e sobre la pinche de la ma.	And if there remains pain in the said places, then point in the circle of the nails on each nail and on the tip of the finger.
E si las dolors pugan aprop alscus jorns als coydes o als muscles, lahoras cauteriza les quascus de tota part dels ajutoris.	And if the pains rise close to some days in the joints or muscles, then cauterize all of them on all sides of the aid.
E no evacuas le malaute de bon regiment e de recepcio de medicinas, quar si es fayt bon regiment e flacma es evacuada am aquest cauteri sira sanat, Dieus ajudan.	And do not evacuate the patient without good regimen and reception of medicines, for if it is done with good regimen and evacuation is made by this cauterizer, then he will be healed, God help.
Capitol .xlv.	Chapter XLV.
De cauterizacio de rompeduras.	On the Cauterization of Wounds.
Quan endeve rompedura en les angonars e diysendo les budels denant l’atela al genetiu, e aquo es comensan de aprop, lahoras cove que tu mandas al malaute layssar la sua comestio en le sieu dia e que use de causas leniens per so que la fenda deyssenda del sieu ventre.	When a wound occurs in the groin and says that it is open in front of the belly button, and this is how it begins to approach, then it is necessary for you to order the patient to leave off his food on that day and to use gentle causes so that the wound heals from its own ventricle.
E aprop segua le malaute entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos, e comanda a lu que tengua le sieu ale entro que sia foro getat o aparesca l’atela o·l budels.	And then follow the patient between your hands on his back, and command him to hold his breath until the pus is drawn out or appears as an abscess.
E aprop retorna aquel am les tieus ditz e senha am tenta la ruptura sobre le os del pentenilh am senhal la extremitat del qual sia semblant a la maytat de cercle a las subiranas partidas del cors.	And then return him to the said place and signal with your finger the rupture on the bone of the ribcage, signaling the extremity of which is similar to half a circle at the upper parts of the chest.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And then ignite the cauterizer, whose form is this:
entro que sia mot rog e gete cintilhas.	until it is red and gives sparks.
E aprop reduzeys le budel o l’atela a la sua conquavitat, e aprop pause la sua ma sobre le loc per so que le budel no yesqua.	And then reduce the abscess or swelling to its natural shape, and then place your hand on the location in order that the swelling does not increase.
E tu ja has ubert entre las coyssas del malaute e dejos lu as pausat un coyssi, et autre servent sia sus las cambas de lu, e autre sus le pietz de lu, le qual tengua las suas mas.	And you have already placed between the joints of the patient and left him to rest one joint, another serving on his legs, another on his feet, which hold their own hands.
E aprop pausa le cauteri sobre aquel senhal am la tua ma am cauteri stan dreyt, e te aquel entro que am lu consieguas le os del pentenilh entro al mieg del duiduni; e itera am aquel autra veguada si a tu aquel no has conseguit en la primieyra veguada entro al os.	And then pause the cauterizer on him, signaling with your hand where the cauterizer stands straight, and make him go into the bone of the ribcage to the middle of the duiduni; and repeat it another time if you have not achieved it in the first attempt, going into the bone.
E observa saviament del ysiment del budel en la hora de la tua cauterizacio, que no comburas aquel budel per so que sobre le malaute no vengua in mort o autre gran malicia.	And observe wisely the signs of the abscess at the time of your cauterization, that you do not burn that abscess for fear that on the patient there will come to death or another great evil.
E sapias que quan tu am le cauteri no atenhas le os, no confereys la tua operacio.	And know that when you have the cauterizer, do not touch the bone, nor combine your operation.
E cove que·l cauteri dels enfants sia subtil segon le gran e la mesura de lor.	And it is necessary that the cauterizer for children be subtle according to their age and measure.
E aprop cura le loc del cauteri per tres dias am boder entro que sia remauguda la scara del foc.	And then cure the location of the cauterization for three days with border, until the scar of the fire is renewed.
E aprop cura aquel am les autres enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure him with other remedies until he is healed.
E le malaute sia jasent sobre le sieu dos per xl dias entro que sia sigillat le loc e la plagua.	And the patient lies on his back for 40 days until the location and wound are sealed.
E cove que pauses le nutriment de lu segon la longitut del temps de la curacio de lu le qual le linesca le ventre de lu, e que le budel no yesca fora deves le esforsament de guerir.	And it is necessary that you pause the patient's nourishment according to the length of time of his healing, and that the abscess does not burst forth from the effort of recovery.
E aprop quan se vol levar aprop xl dias, lahoras aministra liament decentment fayt, e tengua aquel per autres xl jorns.	And then, after 40 days, gradually make him descend, and keep him thus for another 40 days.
E sia mermat de trebalh e de replecio de vianda e de beure, e de votz vehementz, quar quan usa de aquest regiment de sanacio entiera sira sanat.	And be reduced in labor and replenishment of food and drink, and of loud voices, for when he uses this regime of entire healing, then he will be healed.
E yeu diyre la curacio de las rupturas en las autras partidas del ventre, e so al comensament, e vols que no treguan, lahoras cauterisa la ruptura d’aquel am cauteri redon segon la quantitat de lu, e sia aquo que es exhurit de la codena ayssi cum la tersa partida de lu; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit, e no es ajustat.	And you will say that the healing of ruptures in other parts of the belly is similar to the beginning, and if it does not hold, then cauterize the rupture with a round cauterizer according to his quantity, and let it be like the third part of him; and then cure him as we have said, and it will not adjust.
E ja diyssero alcus primiers que ruptura sia cauterizada am cauteri triangular segon aquesta forma, pus que es senhada am tenta:	And some firsts have already said that the rupture is cauterized with a triangular cauterizer according to this form, since it is signaled by intention:
e es pausada linha que eys per la latitut en le latz pus sobira de la ruptura, e autra linha al desus; e depausa la tua ma am un cauteri clavilh, mays le primier cauteri es pus leugier e milhor.	and it is a paused line that goes by the latitude on the side and above the rupture, and another line above; and place your hand with a clavish cauterizer, but the first cauterizer is lighter and better.
Capitol .xlvi.	Chapter XLVI.
De cauterizacio de torcio.	On the Cauterization of Twist.
Quan endeve en alscus membres per cazement o per percussio dolor e persevera aquela dolor per lonc temps e no comfereys al u curacio am medicinas, lahoras cove que cauterizes am cauteri de punt.	When it occurs in some members due to fracture or percussion, and that pain persists for a long time and does not respond to cure with medicines, then it is necessary to cauterize with a pointed cauterizer.
E sia le cauteri de tot membre segon la magnitut e la parvitat de lu, e vertut e develitat de lu, e locacio de torcio e dolor de lu.	And let the cauterizer be for every member according to its magnitude and smallness, virtue and debility of it, location of twist and pain of it.
Donc si·s sanat per le primier cauteri, bo es; e sino, lahoras itera sobre lu le cauteri; quar de costuma de aquelas dolors es que sian punctatz de membre ad aquel membre le qual apropinque al u, per que cove que consieguas aquels am cauteri entro que·l malaute sia sanat.	Therefore, if it is healed by the first cauterizer, good it is; and otherwise, then let there be iteration on him with the cauterizer; for it is customary with those pains to punctuate one member against that member which approaches it, so that you must achieve those with the cauterizer until the patient is healed.
Capitol .xlvii.	Chapter XLVII.
De cauterizacio de lepra.	On the Cauterization of Leprosy.
Les lebros alcunas veguadas am cauteri per mot gran juvament, e magerment si la specia de lepra que es fayta per putrefaccio de flacma e de melencolia.	Some leprosies are made with a cauterizer through great benefit and merit, especially if the type of leprosy is caused by putridity of fat and melancholy.
E donc cum tu vols cauterizar aquel, considera si la lepra es comussan e as aquela curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no deysen, ni esta, e temes sobre le malaute que la corrupcio comprehenda tot le cors de lu e tota la compleccio de lu, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre le cap am v cauteris: am un en le mieg loc del cap, e am le segon pus dejos de lu, eves le front a la fi dels cabels; e amdos sobre dos corns; e am un detras, sobre la nuca o servitz.	And therefore, when you want to cauterize him, consider if the leprosy is common and has been cured with what we have said in the division and do not delay, nor hesitate, and fear for the patient that corruption may comprehend his entire body and all his complexion, then cauterize him on the head with many cauterizers: one in the middle of the head, and another a little way off from him, up to the forehead at the end of the hair; and both on two horns; and one behind, on the nape or neck.
E ultima la tua ma am le cauteri un pauc entro que emprema en le os una petita empressio, e de lu sian deslocadas las scorsas, per so que la expiracio de grossas vapors sia alleujada de lu; e cauteriza sobre la melsa segon que es precesit.	And finally, place your hand with the cauterizer a little bit into the bone, and make a small impression on the skull, so that the displacement of the bones is caused, and the expiration of gross vapors is alleviated from him; and then cauterize on the malleus according to what has been prescribed.
E si la lepra es ja expanduda sobre le malaute e apar manifestament, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas aquel am aquels cauteris les quals havem ditz en le cap; e am cauteri sobre la extremitat del nas, e am dos cauteris sobre las doas maysselas, e am dos cauteris sobre dos spondils del col, e am vi cauteris sobre les spondils del dos, e am un gran sobre les spondils prop de la coeta, e un sobre la cotea , e am dos sobre las anquas, e am un sobre quascuna anqua, e am dos sobre les donols e un sobre quascun donolh, e am dos sobre les coydes, e am dos sobre les muscles, e am dos las teneretutz del sieu pietz; e cauteriza aquel sobre totas las juncturas dels ditz de las mas e dels pes, e sobre quascun talon dels sieus pes, e sobre les foscils de las suas mas.	And if the leprosy is already expanded on the patient and appears manifestly, then it is necessary that you cauterize him with those cauterizers which we have said in the head; and a cauterizer on the extremity of the nose, and two cauterizers on both mallei, and two cauterizers on both vertebrae of the neck, and two cauterizers on the vertebrae of the back, and one great cauterizer on the vertebrae near the coccyx, and one on the coccyx, and two on each ankle bone, and two on each toe, and two on the shoulders, and two on the muscles, and two on the tendons of his feet; and cauterize him on all the joints of the said fingers and toes, and on each heel of his feet, and on the phalanges of his hands.
E guarda te dels nervis les quals so sobre le talo que no comburas aquels.	And beware of the nerves that are over the tarsus, lest you burn those.
E alcunas veguadas es cauterizat am un cauteri sobre le os del pentenilh e am autre sobre la boca del stomac, e autre sobre le fietge.	And sometimes it is cauterized with a cauterizer on the bone of the ribcage and another on the mouth of the stomach, and another on the liver.
E sapias que quant mays ajustas cauteris, tant es mays juvatiu e mays conferent; e sapias que le malaute no ha en le cauteri dolor, ayssi cum han les sas, per so quar le cors de lu ja es stupefayt.	And know that the more you adjust the cauterizers, the more beneficial and suitable it is; and know that the patient does not have pain in the cauterizer, just like they do in their own, because his body is already stupified.
E cove que les cauteris sian grans o paucs segon les membres e las juncturas segon que es precedit de las specias dels ferramentz.	And it is necessary that the cauterizers be great or small according to the members and joints, as directed by the species of the instruments.
E aprop cura le cauteri am farina de errs coyta am mel e am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the cauterizer with flour from error, with honey and with other cures until he is healed.
Capitol .xlviii.	Chapter XLVIII.
De cauterizacio de stupor.	On the Cauterization of Stupor.
Quan alcun membre es stabozit o adormit e es curat am medicinas, olis e emplastres, e no es sanat, lahoras tu cauteriza aquel membre stabozit am cauteris segon que merita la grandesa del membre o la parvitat de lu.	When some member is stunned or asleep and is cured with medicines, oil, and emplasters, but does not heal, then you should cauterize that stunned member with cauterizers according to the greatness of the member or its smallness.
E sia lo tieu cauteri intrant la ispicitut de la codena un pauc.	And let your cauterizer enter into the profundity of the bone a little bit.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure him with a remedy until he is healed.
E alscunas veguadas es cauterizada alcuna stupor le qual endeve a las mas e als pes, e als spondils del dos e ves le eysiment dels nervis les quals mavon aquel membre, e es remauguda la stupor.	And sometimes it is cauterized some stupor which occurs in the arms and legs, and at the vertebrae of the back, and then the numbness of the nerves that affect that member is restored.
Mays no prusuma sobre aquo sino aquel que es savi en la anotomia dels membre e de la egressio dels nervis tot le cors moventz.	But do not presume on this unless you are wise in the anatomy of the members and the exit of nerves throughout the entire moving body.
Capitol .xlix.	Chapter XLIX.
De cauterizacio de albaras que es morfea.	On the Cauterization of Albaras that is Morphia.
Quan albaras es antiqua e no comfereys a lu alcu dels enguentz de medicina, lahoras tu cauteriza sobre aquela am cauteri preon un pauc segon la quantitat de la specitut de la codena entro que sia remauguda la blancor e la color de lu, e la color de lu sia mudada.	When albaras is old and does not respond to any of the remedies of medicine, then you should cauterize on it with a pre-owned cauterizer for a little bit according to the quantity of the specificity of the bone until its whiteness and color are restored, and its color is changed.
E aprop cura aquel am farina de errs e de lentilhas am oli rozat e am folhas de arnagrosa, e am sanc de colomba o am sanc de yronda, da cascuna sia una partida e totas sian mescladas, e aprop sia linit un drap e sus le loc sia pausat entro que sia sanat.	And then cure him with flour of errors and lentils with roasted oil and with leaves of arnagrosa, and with blood of dove or with blood of yronda, each part being one portion and all mixed together; and apply a cloth to the location and place it there until he is healed.
Capitol .l.	Chapter L.
De cauterizacio de cranc.	On the Cauterization of Cramp.
Quan canser es comensan e vols aquel ostar, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteri de cercle en le circuit de lu ayssi cum es revolgut.	When cramp is beginning and you want to relieve it, then cauterize that part with a circular cauterizer in the circle of it as it is revolved.
E diysero les savis que sia cauterizat am lo derier cauteri en le mieg loc; mays a mi no es vist aquo, quar temi que sia ulcerat, e yeu ja e vist aquo alcunas veguadas.	And the wise men say that it should be cauterized with the last cauterizer in the middle location; but to me it is not seen this way, for I fear it may be ulcinated, and I have already seen this some times.
E es pus dreyturier que sia cauterizat en le circuit de lu am cercle ayssi cum avem dit, o am motz cauteris.	And it is more suitable that it be cauterized in the circle of it with a circle as we have said, or with many cauterizers.
Capitol .li.	Chapter LI.
De cauterizacio de adubilati.	On the Cauterization of Adultery.
Quan alcun adubilati es tardat en maturacio, e aysso es per la superfluitat fazen aquela, o per etat del malaute, quar es vielh en decrepitat, de pauc sanc, o per le temps, e tu vols festinar en la maturacio de adubilati; lahoras cauteriza en le circuit de lu am motz cauteris petitz punctan; e aprop leyssa aquela quar ela fastinara en maturacio.	When some adultery is delayed in maturation, and thus it is due to superfluous making that one, or because of the condition of the patient, for it is old in decrepitude, with little blood, or by time, and you want to hasten the maturation of adultery; then cauterize in the circle of it with many small cauterizers punctating; and apply it until it fastens in maturation.
Mays si tu vols la perforacio de lu am cauteri, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu: e depausa aquel en le mieg loc de adubilati entro que penetre la codena.	But if you want the perforation of it with a cauterizer, then ignite the cauterizer of which this is the form: and place that in the middle location of adultery until it penetrates the bone.
E si le cauteri en aquel loc que es pus dejos, per so que le cors del brac sia alleujat; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if the cauterizer in that location is more distant, because the arm's body is alleviated; and then cure it until it is healed.
Capitol .lii.	Chapter LII.
De cauterizacio de corrodent.	On the Cauterization of Corrosion.
Corrodent es corrupcio ambulant en le membre, la qual corrodeys aquel ayssi cum a foc comedent lenha secca.	Corrodent is corruption that wanders in the member, which corrupts it as fire consumes dry wood.
Donc si vezes aquel corrodent en loc le qual sufferte cauteri am foc, lahoras tu igneys cauteris clavils motz paucs, e grans segon que es convenent en aquel loc en le qual es corrodent.	Therefore, if you find that corruption in a location where it would suffer a cauterizer with fire, then ignite small and large cauterizers, many and few, according to what is fitting in that location where the corruption is.
E aprop cauteriza aquel de tota partida entro que erradiques tota la corrosio e no romangua alcuna causa de lu.	And then cauterize it entirely on all sides until you eradicate all corrosion and there remains no cause of it.
E aprop leyssa aquel per tres dias, e pausa sobre les locs cauterizats solpre trissat am oli mesclat entro que las scaras sian totas eradicadas e tota la corrupcio.	And then apply it for three days, and pause on the locations that have been cauterized with a mixture of oil, so that all scars are eradicated and all corruption.
E aprop cura aquel am enguentz carn engendrantz.	And then cure him with flesh-generating remedies.
Mays si aprop tres dias vezes que la carn nasca sana en la qual no es corrupcio, bo es; mays sino, lahoras itera le cauteri sobre aquo que es romas en les locs corrumputz.	But if after three days the flesh grows healthy in which there is no corruption, good it is; but otherwise, then iterate the cauterizer on that which remains in the corrupted locations.
E corrodent es medicat alcunas vetz am medicina aguda, quar aquela es meza en loc de cauteri.	And corruption is medicated some times with acute medicine, for it is a means in place of cauterization.
Mays empero cauteri am foc es de pus leugier juvament.	But however, cauterization by fire is more beneficial.
E yeu ja e dit la curacio de lu am medicina aguda en la divisio, e donc pren aquela quan de lu auras endegencia.	And I have already said the cure of it with acute medicine in the division, and therefore take that when you will have need of it.
Capitol .liii.	Chapter LIII.
De cauterizacio de claus e dels autres semblants.	On the Cauterization of Nails and Other Similar Things.
Motas veguadas endeve a las partidas dejos del pe malautia que s’apela clau, e es causa grossa, fentrada, la qual ladeys le pe; e cauteri en aquels es segon dos manieyras, so es cauteri am foc e cauteri am aygua cauda.	Many times it happens that the parts left behind of a patient who has a condition called "claw" are caused by a large, entering wound which lames the foot; and there is cauterization in those places according to two manners: one being cauterization with fire and the other being cauterization with hot water.
