Mays cauteri am foc es que igniscas le cauteri concau semblant a pena de voltor, le qual sia feyt de ferr segon la quantitat la qual contengua le clau de tota partida, e sia de subtils marguas.	But the cauterization with fire is that you ignite the concave-like cauterizer resembling a vulture's beak, which is made of iron according to the quantity that contains the claw of all parts, and it is of subtle margins.
E aprop pausa aquel ignit sobre le clau, e aprop revolveys la tua ma am le cauteri en le circuit del clau entro que·l cauteri pervengua a la profunditat del clau.	And then pause that ignited cauterizer on the claw, and then revolve your hand with the cauterizer in the circle of the claw until the cauterizer penetrates to the depth of the claw.
E leyssa aquel per tres dias entro que comense getar brac.	And then leave it for three days until you begin to see a bruise.
E aprop emplastre aquel am malvas salvatges trissadas am sal, e leyssa le emplastre sobre aquel per una nuoyt, quar aquel sira eradicat de las suas razitz.	And then apply that with wild mallow leaves trampled with salt, and leave the plaster on it for one night, so that it may be eradicated from its roots.
E aprop cura le loc am enguent de carn generatiu entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the location with flesh-generating remedies until it is healed.
E si so no-convertitz, e motas veguadas accideysso en la superficia del cors, majorment en las mas e les pes, lahoras cove que tu aministres en aquels cauteri am aygua, e es que prenguas una quannula de eram o de ferr o de pena de voltor, e pausa aquela sobre le clau; e aprop geta en la quanula de aygua cauda pauca cantitat, e rete la tua ma, e tu revolveys aquela am compressio de la tua ma de tot, e sia enpremut le marge de la canula en la razit del clau, e atrobara la aygua cauda via al preon de la razit del cau; e espera le malaute un pauc la mordicacio de l’aygua cauda per una hora, e aprop remau aquela, quar le clau am las suas razitz sira erredicat.	And if it does not convert, and many times it happens in the surface of the body, especially on the arms and legs, then you must administer in those places cauterizers with water; and this is that you take a quill made of reed or iron or vulture's beak, and place it on the claw; and then pour into the quill some quantity of hot water, and grasp your hand, and you revolve it with compression from all sides, so that the margin of the quill presses against the root of the claw, and the hot water flows through to the front of the root; and let the patient endure for a little while the burning sensation of the hot water for one hour, and then remove it, because the claw along with its roots will be eradicated.
E ayssi fe am aquels la i aprop l’autre entro que venguas sobre totz les quals de lor so en le cors.	And thus do this to those places where you have applied the other, until you come upon all of them in their place on the body.
E aprop cura aquels pus que las razitz dels claus so erradicadas am aquo dels enguentz les quals la carn ve engenran.	And then cure those places where the roots of the claws have been eradicated with this same flesh-generating remedies which cause the skin to regenerate.
Capitol .liiii.	Chapter LIV.
De cauterizacio de tremor.	On the Cauterization of Trembling.
Quan endeve ad alcu tremor per freg en le nervi o per febre de causa frega, o per autra causa semblant, lahoras cove que tu cauterises aquel am quatre cauteris o am v sobre les spondils del dos, entre quascun spondilh am un cauteri; e am cauteri en le pietz de lu, e sobre l‘estomac de lu, am cauteri olivar.	When it happens to anyone that they have trembling due to a strain on the nerves or because of a fever caused by a strain, or for any similar reason, then you must cauterize that place with four cauterizers or five on the vertebrae of the back, between each vertebra with one cauterizer; and with a cauterizer in the feet of it, and over the stomach of it, with an olive cauterizer.
E la tremor de lu se repausa e festina la sanetat de la malautia frega.	And the trembling of him subsides and hastens the recovery from the strain-caused illness.
Capitol .lv.	Chapter LV.
De cauterizacio de albati accidentz al cors.	On the Cauterization of Accidental Bruises on the Body.
Quan en le cors so espellitz albati, e so pustulas fendas las quals so feytas de materias grossas corruptas; donc cove al comensament cum apareyso, que sia cauterizat sobre tot cap de la fistola am cauteri subtil am fustz de mirt, la extremitat del qual es estenduda am foc; o am razitz de erestologia longua; o am cauteri lentecular.	When on the body there are accidental bruises that burst forth pustules which are caused by gross corrupted matter; therefore it is necessary at first to appear as if so, that the whole head of the fistula be cauterized with a subtle cauterizer made of myrtle wood, the extremity of which is extended by fire; or with roots of long-ago-dried estrogia; or with a lentecular cauterizer.
E alscunas veguadas es cauteri ademamil al comensament de la sua expulcio segon aquesta manieyra; e no so cregudas, e es disrumpuda la superfluitat fazens aquels, et sana de aquels.	And sometimes it is necessary to cauterize beforehand at the beginning of its expulsion according to this manner; and do not believe, and it is disrupted by the superfluity which forms those, and cures from those.
Mays empero cove que aquo sia fayt aprop evacuacio am fleubotomia.	But however, it is necessary that this be done properly with evacuation through phlebotomy.
Capitol lvi.	Chapter LVI.
De cauterizacio de fluex de sanc accident per incisio de arceria.	On the Cauterization of Blood Flux Accidentally Caused by Arrow Wounds.
Tropas veguadas endeve fluex de arceria que es inciza deves la plagua la qual endeve deforo, o deves la incizio de apostemas o cauteri del membre, e alor semblantz, e es dificil remaura aquel.	Many times it happens that blood fluxes of arrow wounds are caused by the incision of the wound itself, or from the opening of apostemes or cauterizers on the member, and thus it resembles, and it is difficult to heal that.
Donc cum accideys ad alcu aquo, lahoras tu·t coyta am la tua ma a l’orrifici de la arceria, e pausa sobre aquel le tieu dit endic estrenh aquel motas veguadas entro que sia ostat le fluex del sanc dejos le tieu dit, e que non yesqua.	Therefore, as it happens to anyone in this case, then you must take the cauterizer made of your own hand and put it on the wound, and place it firmly upon that, many times, until the blood flux is stopped by the aforementioned cauterizer, and there is no more bleeding.
E aprop pausa en le foc les cauteris olivars paucs e grantz, per nombre motz, e exsuffla sobre aquels entro que sian mot ignitz.	And then pause in the fire the olive cauterizers, small and large, for many times, and exhale upon them until they are thoroughly ignited.
E aprop pren de aquels un petit o un gran segon le loc e la plagua en la qual es rompuda la arteria, sobre aquela vena festinantment pus que auras remaugut le tieu dit, e te le cauteri entro que sia abcindit e restreyt aquel sanc.	And then take from those one small or large one according to the location and wound in which the artery has been broken, over that vein more quickly than you would have removed the aforementioned, and place the cauterizer on it until the blood is stopped and constricted.
E si le sanc es expellit de l’orrifici de la arteria quan tu remaues le tieu dit e extringeys le cauteri, lahoras pren la un autre cauteri coytadament dels cauteris les quals en le foc son preparatz, e donc no cesses fer aquo un aprop autre entro que le sanc sia restrengit.	And if the blood is expelled from the wound of the artery when you remove the aforementioned and extinguish the cauterizer, then take another cauterizer, carefully selected from those which are prepared in the fire, and do not stop doing this until the blood is constricted.
E guarda te que no comburas le nervi que aqui es, e que vengua sobre le malaute autra malicia.	And take care that you do not burn the nerves which are here, and that you bring over the patient another harm.
E sapias que quan de l’arteria flueys sanc, lahoras no es possible en aquels restrenge la sanc, e majorment quan l’arteria es gran, si no am una de quatre manieyras: o am cauteri ayssi quo dit havem, o am extraccio quan no es extrayta, quar quan es extrayta las extremitatz de lu miels son comburidas e es restreyt le sanc, o que sia liat am fiel o am liament per fort strectura, o que sian pausadas sobre lu medicinas de las quals la vertut es restringir la sanc; e sian strengudas am pulvinar am costriccio decent.	And know that when blood flows from the artery, it is not possible to constrict the blood in those places, and especially when the artery is large, unless through one of four methods: or with a cauterizer as we have said, or by extraction when it is not extracted, for when it is extracted, the extremities are burned and the blood is constricted; or that it be bound with thread or ligament through strong traction, or that medicinal applications are made upon him which virtue is to constrict the blood; and be strengthened with a pillow and constriction decent.
Mays aquel que aministra restriccio decent de lu am liament e am strictura am draps o per posicio de causas comburentz e de semblantz, no comfereys sino tart.	But he who administers constriction decently by ligature and binding with threads or through the position of constricting causes and similar ones, does not come to fruition until late.
Mays si aquo endeve ad alcu e no sia le metge present ni medicina, lahoras obre am pausament del dit indic sobre le orrifici de aquela vena ayssi cum havem dit, e entenda a la gran costreccio de lu entro que le sanc sia ostat de la sobirana partida de la plagua, e sobre la arceria le dit no sia remaugut; e de sobre la arceria sia aspergit am aygua frega de mot gran fregiditat entro que·l sanc sia congilat e engrossat; e mays cossire en que ha de cauteri o de medicina necessitat.	But if this happens to someone and there is no doctor present or medicine, then work with patience on the indication given above over the wound of that vein just as we have said, and understand the great constriction of it until the blood is stopped from the superior part of the wound, and on the artery let what has been removed not be; and on top of the artery be sprinkled with cold water of great coolness so that the blood is congealed and thickened; and more carefully in that there is need for cauterization or medicine.
Comensa la segonda partida.	Starts the second part.
De incisio e perforacio e ventozas e de fleubotomia e de plaguas e de lor semblants.	On the Incision and Perforation, Wounds, Bleeding, and their Similarities.
Aquestas son paraulas de Albucazis.	These are words of Albucasis.
Ja havem dit en le primier capitol tota malautia en la qual cauteri am foc es convenient e am medicina comburent, e las occasios e las causas de lu, e les instrumentz en aquels necessaris am las formas dels cauteris; e he ordenatz les capitols de la subiranetat del cap entro als pes.	We have already said in the first chapter about all illness in which cauterization with fire is suitable and with medicine that constrains, and the occasions and causes of it, and the instruments needed in those places, and we have organized the chapters from the highest part of the head to the feet.
E yeu procesire en aquest capitol per aquela meteysa guisa, per que sia alliujat lo querent aquo, lahoras sobre aquo que aura demandat.	And you will proceed in this chapter by that same manner, so that whoever wants to know about it may be illuminated on what has been requested.
E denant que yeu comense aquo, cove, fils, que aprenguatz que en aquest capitol es per terror aquo que es en le capitol primier de cauterizacio.	And before you begin this, dear son, take note that in this chapter it is about the same terror as in the first chapter of cauterization.
E per aquo que cove que sia en lu gran cautela, quar en la operacio la qual es en aquest capitol motas veguadas catz evacuacio la qual es am sanc am le qual esta la vida deves la aspersio de la vena o incisio sobre l’apostema o apercio de exsitura o puracio de la plagua o extraccio de sageta o incizio de peyra e a lor semblantz.	And for this reason, it is necessary to be in great caution, because in the operation which is in this chapter, many times blood evacuation occurs, which contains the life-giving substance that flows through the veins or incision upon an apostema or warning of exit or purging of a wound or extraction of an arrow or incision of a boil and their similar ones.
E de totz aquels so acompanhatz temor e tremor e en le mas de lor catz la mort.	And among all those, accompanied by fear and trembling, and in most of them, death.
E yeu amonesti vos que sobre vos no caia aquo en le qual es esitacio, quar alcunas veguadas cazo deves vos manieyras de homes am manieyras motas de malautias.	And I admonish you that upon yourself do not fall what is written here, for sometimes you will have to use the ways of men with many mannerisms of illnesses.
E de lor es alcu que s’irays am la sua malautia e es leugiera deves lu la mort, e aysso per la vehemensia de aquo que troba de sa malautia, e per longuesa de la malautia de lu, e am la malautia es paor la qual significa mort.	And among those are some who will flee from their illness and it is easy for them to meet death, and thus because of the vehemence of what they find in their illness, and because of the length of their illness, and with illness there is fear which means death.
E de aquels es le qual dona a tu son aver e ditta, tu esperant am aquel sanetat, e la sieua malautia es perniciosa.	And among those is one who gives you his word and promise, you hoping for his health, and his illness is deadly.
E donc no cove que tu consentas en aquel que ve a vos del qual es aquesta manieyra; e la vostra cautela sia major que covesitat e la vostra rapacitat; e no presumatz alcuna causa sobre aquo sino aprop sciencia certa la qual virifica aquo deves vos, e al qual perve successio lausabla.	And therefore it is not necessary that you consent to one who comes to you with this manner; and your caution be greater than covetousness and rapacity; and do not assume any cause without aprop certain science which verifies what you see, and which leads to blameless succession.
E usatz en la curacio de totz vostres malautes de pronosticacio e indicacio de lu al qual es salut convertida, quar en aquel es a vos ajutori sobre adquisicio de fama e de memoria, de lausor e de gloria.	And use in the cure of all your illnesses the prophecy and indication of that which is converted into health, for in that is aid to you on the acquisition of fame and memory, praise and glory.
O, filhs, Dieus en vos spire le sieu entendement e no oste a vos direccio e proteccio, quar aquo es en la sua ma.	Oh, sons, God inspires His understanding in you, and does not withhold direction and protection from you, for this is in His hands.
E yeu e ordenat aquest capitol distingent per capitols segon que precedit en le capitol de cauteris, de la cura del cap entro als pes, per que sia a vos alleujat aquo que demandatz de aquo e del qual havetz necessitat.	And I have ordered this chapter distinct by chapters according to what preceded in the chapter of cauterization, from the cure of the head to the feet, so that it may be illuminated for you about what you request and which you need.
Capitol primier.	Chapter One.
De la curacio de aygua la qual es contenguda en le cap dels enfantz.	On the Cure of Water Contained in the Head of Children.
Sapias que aquesta malautia motas veguadas endeve als enfantz deves le enfantament e quan la noyrissa estrenh le cap del enfant ses livitat.	Know that this illness often occurs in children during the period of childhood and when the fontanelle is still open on the child's head.
E alcunas veguadas endeve per causa amaguada la qual no es saubuda.	And sometimes it occurs due to a hidden cause that is not known.
Mays yeu no vi aquesta malautia sino en les enfantz; e a totz aquels les quals yeu vi se coytec la mort, e per ayssi es a mi vist layssada obra en aquels.	But I have only seen this illness in children; and of all those whom I have seen, death has claimed them, and thus it is what I have witnessed in them.
E yeu e vist que un enfant le cap del qual era d’aygua omplit, e·l cap de lu era totjorn ayssi magnificat entro que ceser no podia sobre si meteys per la grandesa del sieu cap, e mays que la humiditat fe aucmentada entro que foc mort.	And I have seen that one child whose head was filled with water and the top of it was always magnificently expanded until he could not contain himself anymore due to the greatness of his head, and more than the humidity increased to the point of mortal fire.
E aquesta humiditat o es agreguada entre la codena e l’os, o es agreguada dejos le os sobre le ciphac.	And this humidity either accumulates between the vertebrae and bone, or accumulates behind the bone above the skull.
Quar la operacio en aquel si la humiditat es entre la codena e l’os e le apostema es pauc, lahoras cove que tu fendas en le mieg loc del cap am una fissura en la latitut, e sia la longitut de la fissura cays dos notz entro que corra la humiditat, e aquesta es la forma del spatum:	Therefore, the operation in that case is to make an incision on the middle part of the skull with a fissure in the latitude, and the length of the fissure should be about two fingers deep until the humidity flows out, and this is the form of the spatula:
E donc si la humiditat es mays augmentada e l’apostema es major, lahoras son aqui dos fissuras segon aquesta manieyra:	And therefore, if the humidity is more increased and the apostema is greater, then two incisions are made in this way:
E si la humiditat es dejos le os, senhal de lu es que tu vezes la comissuras del cap ubertas de tota partida e l’aygua es spremuda quan tu compremes aquela am la tieua ma a las partidas dedintz e no es aquo a tu amaguat.	And if the humidity is behind the bone, then it is signified that you must open up the commissures of the skull all around and squeeze out the water when you compress that with your hand on both sides, and there will be no more hiddenness.
Cove que tu fendas en le mieg loc del cap am tres fissuras segon aquesta manieyra:	It is necessary to make an incision in the middle part of the skull with three fissures in this manner:
e aprop la inscizio extratz ne tota la humiditat; e aprop strenh las fissuras am draps e plumassols; e aprop enbroca aquo de sobre am vi e oli entro al quint dia, e aprop deslia le liament e cura la plagua am tentas e enguentz, e strenh le cap am equalitat; e mange le malaute am vianda secca de pauca humiditat entro que·l membre sia confortat e sanat.	And immediately after the incision, extract all the humidity; and immediately strengthen the fissures with cloths and poultices; and immediately immerse that part above in vinegar and oil for five days, and then loosen the ligament and cure the wound with tents and bandages, and strengthen the head with equality; and feed the patient with dry food with little moisture until the member is comforted and healed.
E es autra manieyra de incisio, que consideras hon apar la magnitut del apostema e la colleccio de l’aygua, quar alcunas veguadas es mays en le occipicii, o en la partida denant, o en la destra, o en la sinistra; e donc aten am la incizio on appar le apostema e la replecio de l’aygua, e fen aquo segon que a tu es miels possible.	And there is another manner of incision that considers the magnitude of the apostema and the collection of water, for sometimes it is more in the occipital region, or on the anterior part, or on the right side, or on the left side; and therefore, attend to the incision where the apostema appears and the accumulation of water, and make it as best you can according to your skill.
Et observa que no inscindas la arteria e endevengua flueys de sanc e mora le malaute per aquel flux de sanc am evacuacio de humiditat.	And observe that you do not incise the artery and thus avoid bleeding of blood and death of the patient due to that flow of blood with evacuation of humidity.
Capitol .ii.	Chapter II.
De inscisio de las arterias las quals so aprop las aurelhas, apeladas hilasseysse.	On the Incision of the Arteries which are near the Ears, called Hilasseysse.
Capitol segon.	Chapter Third.
Quan endeveno ad alcu catars o raumas als huelhs o al pietz, e es antiquat aquo, e no confereys en aquo la curacio de las medicinas, lahoras la deriera curacio en aquest es incizio de aquelas dos arterias.	When there is catarrh or rheumatism in the eyes or feet and it is chronic, and there is no agreement on that with medical treatment, then the last resort is to make an incision on those two arteries.
E donc cove quan tu vols inscidir aquelas que le malaute raza lo sieu cap, e aprop fregua le loc am drap aspre per so que aparan las arcerias, e aprop sia strengut le col del malaute am alcu drap; e aprop considera on polsa la vena; e les locs de quascuna sobre les locs les quals so aprop las aurelhas depremutz, e tant se occultan sino en alcus homes.	And therefore, when you want to incise those which the patient's head is filled with, and immediately freshen up the place with an asperous cloth so that the arteries appear, and immediately strengthen the neck of the patient with a few cloths; and consider on what pulse the vein is; and the places of each one over the places which are near the ears, depressed, and only in some men.
E aprop senha sobre la arceria am tenta, e aprop inscideys quascuna am le spatum de quascuna partida agut am inscizio pervenient entro al os, e sia aquo per la latitut del cap.	And immediately sign over the artery with a tent, and immediately incise each one with the spatula of each side going up to the incision which penetrates into the bone, and that is so by the latitude of the head.
E si vols, entromet le spatum dejos la arteria e trenqua aquala a las inciden a las partidas desus.	And if you wish, insert the spatula below the artery and cut it at the incision on the upper parts.
E sia la longitut de la inscizio cays dos ditz ajustatz, quar quan alcuna vena es inscizida le sanc es eyssit am egressio pulsatil, le qual saut deforo per saut frequent.	And the length of the incision should be about two finger-widths, for when some vein is cut, the blood flows out with pulsatile emission, which jumps forth repeatedly.
Mays si la arceria no apareys al cintiment, lahoras cove que tu mesures de la aurelha la quantitat del spazi de tres ditz, e aprop senha am tenta, e fen entro al os.	But if the artery does not appear at the incision, then it is necessary that you measure from the ear the quantity of space equal to three finger-widths, and immediately sign with a tent, and go into the bone.
E aquo que cove getar del sanc es quantitat de vi unc., e fort leu ne geta de lu mays o mens, e tot aquo es segon la quantitat la qual appareys de la vertut del malaute e de la replecio de la arceria de lu.	And as much blood as flows out is equal to about one quarter of an ounce. and not too much or too little flows out from it, and all this is according to the quantity which appears of the virtue of the disease and the accumulation of the artery in it.
E aprop considera la plagua, e donc si reman sobre le os alcuna causa del ciphac, lahoras inscindys aquo per so que no endevengua apostema caut.	And immediately consider the wound, and therefore if there remains on the bone some cause of the skull, then incise it in order that no hidden apostema may occur.
E aprop strenh la plagua am plumassols e am liamentz de drap de li, e aprop cura aquela am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And immediately strengthen the wound with poultices and bandages of linen cloth, and immediately cure it with dressings until it is healed.
Capitol .iii.	Chapter III.
De extraccio de las arcerias las quals so en las templas.	On the Extraction of the Arteries which are in the Temples.
Quan ad alcu accideys emigranea antiqua o catertz agutz, per humiditatz agrimonials e per qualiditat en les lacertz des templas, o sodo antiqua vehement e semblantz ad aquels, e es medicat am las manieyras de curacio de medicina e aquo no comfereys, lahoras nos hem sproatz en aquestas malautias extraccio de las arcerias en les templas, o cauterizacio de aquelas ayssi cum havem mostrat.	When some ancient or chronic disease migrates to the temples, due to humid and aggravating conditions, and by the quality of the lacertae in the temples, or an old and violent sores and similar ones, and it is medicated with the methods of medical cure, but this does not help, then we have resorted to extracting the arteries in the temples, or cauterizing those just as we have shown.
E la manieyra de la operacio e extracio de aquelas es que·l malaute raza les pels les quals son en les templas; e entenda a la arceria apparent en le templar quar ela es a tu mostrada per le sieu pols, e·s occultada sino en paucs homes per vehemencia de freg.	And the method of the operation and extraction of those is that the patient has boils on the temples; and understand that the artery appears in the temple, for it is shown to you by its pulse, and is hidden from most people due to the intensity of heat.
E si a tu es occultada, lahoras le col del malaute sia strengut am alcun drap; e aprop fregua le loc am un drap aspre o evapora le loc am aygua cauda entro que aparesca a tu la arceria manifestament.	And if it is hidden from you, then strengthen the neck of the patient with some cloth; and immediately freshen up the place with a rough cloth or evaporate the place with hot water until the artery appears manifestly to you.
E lahoras tu pren le spatum del qual aquesta es la forma:	And then take the spatula, the shape of which is:
E aprop tu scorja la codena am aquel am facilitat entro que pervenguas a la arceria; e aprop geta en lu onti e extratz aquela a las partidas sobiranas entro que extraguas aquela de la codena e descobras aquela de las tunicas las quals so dejos aquela, de tota partida.	And immediately cut the vertebra with that [spatula] with ease until you reach the artery; and immediately get into it and extract that from the upper parts until you extract that from the vertebra and uncover those tunics which are below it, of all sides.
Mays si la arteria es subtil, lahoras envolveys aquela am la extremitat del oncii, e aprop inscindeys de aquela una partida segon la quantitat per la qual sian alonguadas las extremitatz de lu e sian contraytas, e no endevindra flux de sanc, quar si no so inscididas no pujara le sanc de tot.	But if the artery is subtle, then immediately envelop it with the tip of the spatula, and immediately incise one part of that according to the quantity by which the extensions of it are lengthened and contracted, and there will be no flow of blood, for if they are not incised, the blood will not rise from all.
E aprop evacua del sanc de vi unc. entro a tres.	And immediately evacuate about one quarter ounce of blood. until three [ounces]
E si la arceria es gran, lahoras cove que tu lies aquela en dos locs am fiel dopble fort de ceda o am cordas a lonc, e no coyte a lu putrefaccio denant la consolidacio de la plagua e endevengua flux de sanc.	And if the artery is large, then it is necessary that you divide it into two parts with a double fold of cedarn or cordage to a length, and not fear putrefaction before the consolidation of the wound and impending flow of blood.
E aprop incideys la superfluitat la qual es entre dos liamentz; e fay aquo en aquela hora o aprop autra ora.	And immediately incise the superfluity which is between two ligaments; and do this at that hour or at another nearby.
E si vols, cauteriza aquela am cauteri entro al os am cauteri cutellar entro que sian incididas las extramitatz de lu, e stara en loc de aquela meteyssa obra.	And if you wish, cauterize that with a cauterizer into the bone and a cauterizer like a scalpel until the extensions of it are incised, and remain in that same place.
E es milhor obra sino que·l malaute aia febre o es de escalfada compleccio; quar cauteri es de aquelas causas que ajudan a las humiditatz finidoras, e donc es milhor en juvament.	And it is better work if the patient has fever or is in a state of scalding complexity; for cauterization is one of those causes that helps to finish off the humidity, and therefore it is better in judgment.
E cove aprop la extraccio de las arcerias que huomplas le loc de coto antic, e sian pausatz sobre lu polvils decentement fayt, e aprop sia curat am medicinas seccas fazen naysser la carn e am calguas entro que sia sanat.	And it is necessary to immediately extract the arteries that fill the place with old blood, and let them rest on decently made powders, and be cured with dry medicines that make the flesh appear and with some remedies until it is healed.
E si mentre obres autra veguada endeventa flux de sanc de la arceria, lahora tu te coyta a restrenger aquel sanc, o am cauteri, o que omplas le loc de coto, e strenh la tua ma entro que sia restreyt le sanc.	And if while you are working another vein suddenly bleeds from the artery, then immediately take care to stop that bleeding, either with a cauterizer or by filling the place with old blood, and strengthen your hand until the bleeding is stopped.
E si deguna causa de aquelas no es a tu present, lahoras pausa le tieu dit sobre le loc entro que·l sanc sia congilat, e enbroca le loc am aygua de vehement fregiditat entro que la acuitat repausa, e sia strengut segon que cove.	And if any of these causes are not present to you, then immediately pause your touch on the place until the blood is coagulated, and immerse the place in hot water with vehement heat until the acute pain subsides, and strengthen it as needed.
E aquo que es pus leugier en extraccio de arceria es que tu cauterizes la vena am aquest cauteri haventz dos cotels, pus que tu has senhat les dos locs am tenta, e depausa quascus, mot ignitz, entro que pervenguan al os e inscindan la vena en dos locs, per so que sia elonguat aquo que es entre las extremitatz de lu, quar no son consolidadas de tot am aquest cauteri.	And what is easier in the extraction of an artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cauterizer having two blades, since you have marked out the two places with a tent, and each one is motionless, until they reach the bone and incise the vein into two parts, so that what is between the extensions of it may be elongated, for it is not fully consolidated by this cauterization.
E aquesta es la forma del cauteri:	And this is the shape of the cauterizer:
E sia la acuitat dels dos cotels esemps.	And the sharpness of the two blades is exemplary.
Mays empero si so mendres acuitat que dos cotels es milhor, quar si so agudas cum dos cotels propera a quascuna freg, e no enscideysso la carn am velocitat.	But even if there is less sharpness than two blades, it is better, for if they are sharp like two blades close to each part of the flesh, and do not cut through the flesh with velocity.
Donc cum en aquels es alcuna grossitut, es tenguda la calor del foc en aquels e la carn es abscindida leugierament.	So when there is some thickness in those [blades], it is kept that the heat of the fire is applied to those and the flesh is cut away slightly.
E aquesta obra es milhor en tota obra e pus leugiera.	And this work is better than all other works and easier.
E sia le spazi le qual es entre dos cotels la quantitat de la grossesa del dit.	And the space which is between two blades is equal to the thickness of a digit.
Capitol quart.	Chapter Fourth.
De la cura de cors de lagremas agudas e aciduas dels huels.	On the Cure of Eyes with Acute and Acid Lachrymation.
Quan so lagremas aciduas, e es le cors de aquelas venas las quals so sobre le test del cap deforo, e no comfereys en aquo alcuna causa de la curacio de medicina, e vezes la cara del malaute ja enrogesir e sent en le sieu front deambulacio ayssi cum si era deambulacio de formiguas, e·ls huels de aquel so extenuatz, humitz enayssi que ja les pels de lor son conodutz, e las parpelas so scalfadas per la acuitat de las lacrimas, les antics agro mesties en la curacio de aquelas de aquesta operacio, e nompnero aquela curacio am spassa.	When the eyes have acid lachrymation, and it is the core of those veins which are above the forehead of the head, and does not agree with any cause for medical cure, and the face of the patient becomes red and there is wandering in his forehead like a march of ants, and the eyes of that person are exhausted, wet as if they were crying, and their eyelids are scaled off by the acidity of the tears, the ancient agrimenes mixed into the cure of those with this operation, and named it "spassa".
E es que tu comandas al malaute rayre les pels les quals son en le sieu front, e aprop inscideys en le front tres fissuras engualment distans segon la longitut del front.	And it is that you command the patient to scratch the skin which is on his forehead, and immediately incise in the forehead three fissures equally distant according to the length of the forehead.
E si’ la longitut de la fissura cays dos ditz: la una fissura sia engualment distant a la longitut del nas en le mieg loc del front, e la segonda segon la longitut un petit del movement dels lacertz les quals so en le lacrimal, e la tersa del autre part.	And if the length of the fissure is two finger-widths: one fissure should be equally distant from the nose in the middle part of the forehead, and the second according to the length of a small movement of the lashes which are in the lacrimal, and the third on the other side.
E guarda te de la incizio de las arcerias las quals so en dos latz, e elongua la tua ma de la continuacio de amdos las mandibulas.	And be careful of the incision of the arteries which are in two sides, and stretch your hand from the continuation of both jawbones.
E si’ l’espazi de quascuna inscizio la quantitat de tres ditz ajustatz.	And if the space of each incision is the quantity of three finger-widths adjusted.
E si’ a tu una pessa d’espongua apparelhada o draps seccatz motz am les quals exsiccas le sanc.	And if you have a sponge or cloth with dry fibers which absorb the blood.
E aprop entremet le spatum de dos agudas extremitatz, del qual aquesta es la forma de la inscisio de lu:	And immediately insert the spatula of two sharp extensions, the shape of which is:
que es de la partida des templas entro a la segonda inscizio.	which is from the part of the temples to the second incision.
Exxcorja am aquel tota la codena la qual es entre dos incizios am le ciphac le qual es sobre le os, e aprop fay aquo de la inscizio migera entro a la segonda inscisio.	Excoriate with that the entire vertebra which is between two incisions on the skull which is above the bone, and immediately make it migrate into the second incision.
E aprop stratz ne aquest spatum e entromet en la primieyra inscizio autra vetz un autre instrument le qual es apelat cutellar, agut de una part e del autre no agut.	And immediately take this spatula and insert it into the first incision another time with a different instrument called a scalpel, sharp on one side and not sharp on the other.
E pausa le latz de aquel agut deves la carn annexa deves la codena, e le latz de lu leon dintz le os, e empelley aquel entro que pervengua a la fissura migera, e abscindeys am aquel totz les vaysels que descendo del cap als huels.	And pause the blade of that scalpel so that it touches the flesh annexed to the vertebra, and the edge of it is inserted into the bone, and push it in until it reaches the mid fissure, and cut away with it all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes.
Mays que sia continuada la inscizio ad aquo appar de la codena, e aprop fay aquo en la fissura migana entro al autra fissura.	But continue the incision up to where it appears on the vertebra, and immediately make it in the mid fissure into another fissure.
E pus que corr del sanc quantitat engual, exprem les locs de las pessas del sanc congilat.	And since there is a quantity of blood equal to that which has coagulated, express the places of the sponge with coagulated blood.
E aprop pausa en quascuna fissura calgua de coto vielh, e pausa sobre aquels polvils enbegutz en vi e oli e vi agre, e vegas que no endevengua apostema caut.	And immediately pause in each fissure with old blood, and pause over those powders made with vinegar, oil, and vinegar mixed together, so that there is no hidden apostema.
E en le tertz dia deslia le liament e aministra gran enfusio de aygua cauda o tebeza, e aprop cura aquo am enguent bazilicon am oli rozat e autres entro que las plaguas sian sanadas.	And on the third day loosen the bandage and administer great effusion of hot water or tepid water, and immediately cure with ointment basilicon made with rose oil and other remedies until the wounds are healed.
Capitol .v.	Chapter Five.
De la cura de lagramas per catartz e als huels descendentz de las partidas dedintz del cap.	On the Cure of Lachrymation by Cataracts and Eyes Descending from the Parts Behind the Head.
Quan ad alcu veno catartz agutz e continuantz, e vezes les huels del malaute extenuatz petitz, e ja le reguardament de lor es debelitat, e las palpebras ulceradas e de lor cazo les pels, e en le preon del cap es dolor aguda ledent e extrenutacio consequent, lahoras sapias per aquestz accidentz que las materias e catartz no veno sino de motas venas de las partidas dedintz procedent.	When there are acute and continuous cataracts in some veins and they continue, and the patient's eyes are exhausted and small, and the regard of their pupils is debilitated, and the eyelids ulcerated and their skin dry, and in the forehead of the head there is sharp pain and subsequent exhaustion, then know by these accidents that the matters and cataracts come only from many veins proceeding from the parts behind.
E la milhor curacio en aquels es aquesta: que comandes al malaute que raza lo sieu front, e aprop inscideys en aquel una fissura al mieg loc del front, un petit per la latitut (e comensa am la fissura del templar senestre entro al dextre templar; e sia inscisio entro al os; e eslongua la tua ma dels lacertz del templas lesquals son maugutz deves la mastigacio), entro que sia le os descubert.	And the best cure in those is this: that you command the patient to scratch his forehead, and immediately incise a fissure in the middle of the forehead, about as long as the width of a finger (and begin with the fissure of the left temple and extend it into the right temple; and the incision should be made into the bone; and stretch your hand over the lashes of the temples which are above the mastoid process), until the bone is uncovered.
Exsicca tot le sanc am espongua o am drap secc e aprop repleys entre las doas labias de la fissura am coto vielh o am draps de li.	Dry up all the blood with a sponge or a dry cloth and immediately fill between the two lips of the fissure with old blood or dry cloths.
E aprop estrenh desus am polvils enbegutz en vi e oli per so que no endevengua apostema caut.	And immediately strengthen above with powders made with vinegar and oil, so that there is no hidden apostema.
E quan deslias aquo e veses que l’apostema ja es diminuit, lahoras cove que fregua le os entro que comensa en lu nayser carn, e aprop cura aquel am regiment exsiccatiu le qual fassa neysser la carn, ayssi cum si tu prenes de farina de froment dos partidas e de colofania quatre partidas e mescla o, e de lor sia fayt emplastre e sia aministrat en aquestas plaguas a de la carn nativitat.	And when you see that the apostema has diminished, then it is necessary to freshen up the bone until it begins to show flesh, and immediately cure with an emollient regimen which will make the flesh appear, just as if you take two parts of wheat flour and four parts of colophony, mix them together, and from them make a poultice, and administer it to these wounds in the natural state of the skin.
Capitol .vi.	Chapter Six.
De la cura de aquo que catz en las aurelhas.	On the Cure of That Which Causes Humors in the Ears.
Tota causa que catz en las aurelhas es una de quatre specias, quar o es peyra mineral o causa semblant a peyra, ayssi cum ferr e veyre, o es de planta ayssi cum ceze o fava, o es causa fluxtibla ayssi cum aygua e vi agre e a lor semblantz, o alcuna bestia.	All causes that occur in the ears are one of four species, for either it is a mineral peyra or a similar cause, such as iron and lead, or it is from a plant, such as cumin or fava, or it is a fluidic cause, such as water and vinegar and their like, or some animal.
E donc quan peyra catz en l’aurelha o autra causa semblant de aquelas causas que no ajustan ne creysso en l’aurelha, e pausa la aurelha al solelh, e si vezes la peyra, lahoras distilla en aquela alcuna causa de oli violat o sizami, e aprop aministra la extraccio de lu, e fay le stornudar am condizi, e oppila las nars deve le aveniment de stornutacio.	And therefore when peyra occurs in the ear or some other similar cause that does not agree with the ear, and pauses the ear at the sun, and if the peyra times it, then immediately distill into that some cause of violet oil or sassafras, and properly administer the extraction of it, and make the stornutacio to come out in condition, and stop up the nose against the occurrence of stornutacio.
E aprop pausa en le circuit de la aurelha alscunas pessas de drap o lana, e dextendas la aurelha a las partidas desus, quar motas veguadas es foro-getada am aquestas causas.	And immediately pause in the circuit of the ear some pieces of cloth or wool, and stretch the ear to the parts above, because many times it is forgotten about these causes.
E si no n’es getada, lahoras aministra extraccio de lu am le instrument apelat gesti epicicarios subtil del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if not, then immediately administer the extraction of it with the instrument called "epicaricatic gestures" which are subtle and have this shape:
E si es foro-getada am gesti, bo es; e sino, lahoras aministra la extraccio de lu am onci subtil de pauca duplicacio.	And if forgotten about the gestures, it is better so; and if not, then immediately administer the extraction of it with a subtle instrument of slight duplication.
E donc si no es foro-getada per aquo, lahoras fay una canula de aram e entromet la extremitat de la canula en le trauc de la aurelha e claus a l’enviro de la canula am cera e am oli mollificada per so que no sia ubert sino la canula.	And therefore if not forgotten about this, then immediately make a canal of iron and insert the end of the canal into the opening of the ear and close around the canal with wax and softened oil so that it is only open to the canal.
E aprop extratz am le tieu vent am fort atraccio, quar tropas veguadas cum aquo que havem recontat.	And immediately extract with your breath strong attraction, because many times as we have recounted.
Mays si no es foro-getada en aquesta manieyra, lahoras pren de halka alumbat o de vecz aparelhat am le qual son preses les ausels una patita quantitat, e pausa aquel en la extremitat de ray, e aprop envolopa sobre aquel coto decentment pausat.	But if not forgotten in this manner, then immediately take from the candlelight or the prepared wax with which birds are caught and taken a small quantity, and pause that on the extremity of the ray, and immediately wrap around that spot decently paused.
E aprop entromet aquel en le trauc de la aurelha am facilitat, e aprop excicca la aurelha de la humiditat.	And immediately insert that into the opening of the ear with ease, and immediately dry out the ear from its humidity.
E donc si no es foro-getada am totas las causas las quals havem recontadas, lahoras tu coyta a talhar aquela denant que endevengua apostema caut o espasme.	And therefore if not forgotten about all the causes which we have recounted, then immediately take care to cut off that before it becomes a hidden apostema or spasm.
E la manieyra de talhar aquela es que tu al comensament sancnes le malaute de la vena sephasica e extratz del sanc segon la mannieyra de la vertut de lu, e aprop fay aquel cezer entre las tuas mas e converteys l’aurelha a las partidas desus, e fen am petita fissura en la razit de la aurelha deves lo greys de lu en le loc be premegut de lu.	And the method of cutting off that is to first bleed the patient from the sephasic vein and extract blood according to the virtue of it, and immediately make that cease between your hands and convert the ear to the parts above, and then close with a small fissure in the root of the ear over the grey matter in the location previously prepared.
E sia la fissura de figura lunar entro que pervengua a la peyra, e, la peyra atrobada, osta aquela si podes am instrumentz apropriatz; e aprop cos la fissura en aquela hora am velocitat, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And let the fissure be of a lunar shape until it reaches the peyra, and when the peyra is atrophied, stop that if possible with appropriate instruments; and immediately close the fissure in that hour with velocity, and cure that until it is healed.
E si la causa cazent en la aurelha es un dels gras que creysso e so inflatz, lahoras aministra la curacio e la extraccio de lu; mays si no obezeys a tu ad eyssiment, lahoras tu pren spatum teune subtil segon aquesta forma:	And if the cause is in the ear is one of the fat that you consider and which swells, then immediately administer the cure and extraction of it; but if it does not obey your sight, then immediately take a subtle spatula according to this shape:
e aministra am aquel la abscizio de aquel gra lo qual es cazut en l’aurelha.	and administer with that the removal of that fat which has fallen into the ear.
E no fassas aquo quan cogitas que aquel ja es humectat per la vapor del aurelha, e pausa aquel en motas pessas, e prop extratz ne aquelas am les oncis o am gesti subtil, o ab inscizio ayssi co dit havem, quar es alleujada la extraccio de lu.	And do not do this when you think that it is already moistened by the vapor of the ear, and pause in many pieces, and immediately extract those from them with onces or subtle gestures, or with incision as we have said, for it is facilitated the extraction of it.
Mays en l’aygua la qual es intrada en l’aurelha cove que·l malaute use de sternutacio am condizi al comensament, e omple la sieua aurelha am alcu coto vielh, e jagua sobre aquela aurelha en la qual es l’aygua, e si per aquo es foro-getada, bo es; e sino, lahoras pren tropas peyras teunas e leons segon la longitut del dit, e calfa aquelas en le foc un pauc, e le pacient entrometa una de aquelas en le trauc de la sua aurelha e saute sobre la un pe sieu de aquela partida e percussia am una autra peyra sobre la peyra la qual es dintz la aurelha.	But in the water that has entered the ear, it is necessary for the patient to use stornutacio in condition at first, and fill his own ear with some old blood, and pour over that ear where the water is, and if forgotten, good; but if not, then take many sharp peyres and lemons according to the length of a finger, heat those in the fire for a little while, and have the patient insert one of them into the opening of his own ear and strike with another peyra on the peyra that is behind the ear.
Donc no cesse aquo am peyra entro que tota l’aygua sia foro-getada.	Therefore do not stop until all the water has been forgotten.
E ja l’aygua sira foro-getada enayssi que tu prenguas de papier o de gonc .i., e met la una extremetat de lu en l’aurelha e estendas l’autre extremitat am foc entro que sia comburit le may de lu.	And then the water will be forgotten, just as you take paper or parchment and... and place one end of it in the ear and stretch the other end with fire until the wax is burnt.
E prop met i autre gonc e fay aquo tantas veguadas entro que tota l’aygua sia foro-getada, e stratz aquel am canula ayssi co desus es dit de la peyra extrasadora.	And then take another piece of parchment and do this many times until all the water is forgotten, and extract that with a cannula just as described above.
Mays en la extraccio de bestia intrant en aquela aurelha, si es a petit cos, ayssi piussa e a lu semblant, cura aquel ayssi cum havem dit en la divisio; mays si es de gran cos la qual causa apar al sen del vezement, lahoras aministra la extraccio de lu am gesti e oncis, e la causa de lu es pus leugiera de totas las autras causas que cazo en l’aurelha.	But if an animal enters into that ear, whether it is small or great, and the cause appears to the sense of smell, then immediately administer the extraction of it with gestures and onces, and the cause of it is easier than all other causes that occur in the ear.
Mays en la extraccio de verm engendrat en la aurelha, quan tu curas aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e en le tractat de distillacios e no comfereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu reguardes la aurelha al solelh.	But if there is a worm generated in the ear, when you cure that with water as we have said in the division and treatise on distillations, and your cure does not agree, then it is necessary to gaze at the ear towards the sun.
E donc si apar aqui alcuna causa dels verms, lahoras extratz aquel am gesti o am onci subtils, mays si no apar deguna causa, lahoras pren una canula dejos streyta e desus ampla de la qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And therefore if any cause of worms appears here, then immediately extract that with gestures or subtle onces, but if no cause appears, then take a cannula made of straw and expanded above, which is shaped like this:
E entromet la extremitat subtil en la aurelha segon la quantitat la qual suffertar puesca le malaute; e aprop sucgeys am aquela per succio fort, e fay aquo motas veguadas, entro que totz les verms sian foro-gitatz.	And insert the subtle end of it into the ear according to the quantity that the patient can tolerate; and immediately suck with force through it, and do this many times, until all the worms are forgotten.
Mays si no obezeysso a tu al ayssiment, lahoras tu opila e claus en le circuit de la canula am cera ayssi cum havem dit; lahoras aministre distillacios las quals han ja esproadas les antics en la curacio dels verms, e atrobaras aquo en le tractat de distillacios.	But if it does not obey you in this way, then immediately stop and close the circuit of the cannula with wax as we have said; then administer distillations which the ancients have already tried in the cure of worms, and find this in the treatise on distillations.
E sia la tua efusio am la qual efundas les olis medicinas en la aurelha am aquest strument del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And be your effusion with which you pour the medicinal oils into the ear with this instrument, the shape of which is:
E fay aquela de argent o de eram, dejos streyt, en le qual sia un petit trauc, e am pla desus.	And make that of silver or iron, made from straw, with a small hole in it and a plate on top.
E donc sia cum empellent a que es en la conquavitat de la canula de continent aqui on sira necessari.	And therefore be as they are driven to what is in the convergence of the cannula of content here where it will be necessary.
E si vols, pren le ray e envolveys en la extremitat de lu decentment coto, e aprop gieta oli en la concavitat del auziment, o suc de alcuna herba, o aquo que vols de aquestas medicinas en la canula — e aquela es en la aurelha —, e aprop entromet le ray am coto desus e exprem am la tua ma aquel am compressio temprada de lu entro que l’oli sia expellit en la concavitat del auziment e le malaute senta le oli dedintz.	And if you want, take the ray and wrap it around the end of it decently cut off, and immediately pour oil into the convergence of the ascent, or juice of some herb, or whatever you want from these medicines in the cannula -- and that is in the ear --, and immediately insert the ray with a cut-off end and press gently with your hand on that with a mild compression so that the oil is expelled into the convergence of the ascent and the patient feels the oil outside.
E aquo que sia enfundut en la aurelha sia ja scalfat am foc un petit.	And what is inserted in the ear is already scarified with fire, a little bit.
E guarda te que la causa la qual distillaras en l’aurelha no sia trop frega, quar las medicinas de aurelha no suffertan aquo.	And beware that the cause which you are about to distill in the ear is not too hot, for the medicines of the ear cannot withstand it.
Capitol .vii.	Chapter VII.
De curacio de opilacio de aurelhas.	On the Cure of Earwax.
Alcunas veguadas alcus enfantz yeysso dels ventres de lors mayres no-perforatz, e aquo ja accideys en alcus homes, opilacio en le meat de la aurelha per plagua o per carn nada en aquela; e aquesta opilacio alcunas veguadas es fayta en le preon del trau de la aurelha la qual no consiec le vezement, e alcunas veguadas es en las partidas defora.	Some times, some children are born with the vents of their mothers unperforated, and this already occurs in some men, opilacio in the meatus of the ear due to a wound or flesh not perforating in that place; and this opilacio sometimes is made in the prominence of the tract of the ear which does not allow the sense of smell, and sometimes it is in the outer parts.
E aquela que accideys en le preon de lu, la qual no comprehen le vezement, es en las majors disposicios de dificil sanacio.	And that which occurs in the prominence of it, which does not comprehend the sense of smell, is in the greater difficulties of difficult healing.
E en aquela en qual consegueys le vezement, cove que tu pauses la aurelha del malaute al solelh e reguarda en aquela.	And in that which comprehends the sense of smell, it is necessary to pause the ear of the patient towards the sun and gaze at it.
E donc si vezes oppulacio apparent, obre aquela am espatum subtil del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And therefore if there appears an apparent obstruction, open that with a subtle spatula of which this is the shape:
Si’ la extremitat de lu en la qual sia petita la latitut, del qual la una partida sia aguda e l’autra no; e le spatum sia de dos latz leon per so que no fassa lizio al aurelha.	If the end of it is in the ear where there is a small width, with one side sharp and the other not; and the spatula has two lion's claws to prevent any harm to the ear.
E donc si la opilacio es per carn nascuda en la aurelha o en le meat de lu, lahoras te aquela am oncis subtils e incidiys aquela vehement facilitat entro que sia ostada tota la carn.	And therefore if the obstruction is due to flesh born in the ear or in the meatus, then immediately take that with subtle onces and cut into it with a vehement ease until all the flesh is removed.
E si opilacio es en le preon de la aurelha, lahoras pren ray subtil leon e escalfa aquel am foc un pauc, e aprop met aquel en le meat de l’aurelha.	And if the obstruction is in the prominence of the ear, then immediately take a subtle iron rod and heat it with fire for a little while, and then insert that into the meatus of the ear.
E donc si as scentit oppulacio am aquo que le malaute atroba am facilitat, per gravetat de ausir, esforsa la oppressio de lu am facilitat; e guarda te que no plagues les nervis del aurelha.	And therefore if you have sensed obstruction with what the patient feels with ease, due to the gravity of having it, force the oppression of it with ease; and beware that you do not harm the nerves of the ear.
E aprop pausa en l’aurelha drap de li segon la quantitat del ample del trauc lo qual tu as envolvutz en l’enguent egipciac; e fay aquo per alcus jorns entro que sias segur de la consolidacio de la plagua; o que prenguas qualgua e enfon aquela en ayguaros e pulveriza sobre lu segi trissat e usa de lu; e si vezes la aurelha ja esser apostemada, lahoras cove que tu estraguas la qualgua e permutes aquela am autra qualgua la qual tu envoloparas en cerot que sia fayt am oli rozat, entro que sia le apostema caut cedat; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And immediately apply a cloth soaked with the liquid according to the quantity of the width of the channel which you have wrapped in Egyptian bandages; and do this for some days until you are sure of the consolidation of the wound; or take some powder and pour it into water and pulverize over it as it is sown, and use it; and if the ear has already become apostemated, then immediately extract the liquid and replace it with another liquid which you have wrapped in wax that has been made with rose oil, until the apostema is calm; and immediately cure that until it is healed.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc, lahoras submergeys esponga o drap en aygua frega e pausa sobre la aurelha, e usa del autra curacio la qual restrengeys le flux del sanc, la qual es dita en le tractat de distillacio.	But if bleeding occurs, then immediately submerge a sponge or cloth in hot water and pause it over the ear, and use another cure that restricts the flow of blood, which is described in the treatise on distillation.
Capitol .viii.	Chapter VIII.
De cura de athezil le qual endeveno a las palpebras.	On the Cure of Athazil, which afflicts the eyelids.
Athezil les quals endeveno a las paupebras dels huels alcuna veguada so humitz, alscunas veguadas son secs.	Athazil, which afflicts the eyelids of some people sometimes moistens them, and at other times makes them dry.
Donc cove que tu tenguas aquels am tenhalhas o am onci, e inscindas aquels am espatum de las suas razitz, e aprop pausa sobre les locs segi trissat.	Therefore, take those with tenacious or onces, and cut them with a spatula of their own roots, and immediately apply it to the places as sown.
Mays si dolor am flux de sanc veno, lahoras tu cauteriza aquels am cauteri lanticular subtil.	But if pain with bleeding occurs, then immediately cauterize those with a subtle lunar cauterizer.
E la milhor cauterizacio es aprop las inscizios e tropas veguadas retornam quan reman alcuna causa de sas razitz; e quan so cauterizadas am foc, aquelas razitz son comburidas e no retornan.	And the best cauterization is to do it near the incisions and many times when there remains some cause of their roots; and when they are cauterized with fire, those roots are burnt and do not return.
Capitol .ix.	Chapter IX.
Cura de grandeyssa que veno a las palpebras dels huels.	On the Cure of Grandiness which comes to the eyelids of humans.
Motas veguadas endeve en las palpebras dels huels alcuna causa la qual es asemblada a grandissa en sa fortalicia e duricia, e per so grandissia es apelada.	Many times, something develops in the eyelids of humans due to some cause which is related to grandiness in its strength and hardness, and because of this grandness it is called.
E es agreguacio de humiditat grossa en la palpebra dejos e desus.	And it is an accumulation of thick moisture on the eyelid below and above.
Donc la opperacio en lor es que consideras lahoras si la grandissia es procedent en lu en aquo que apar de la palpebra e es mauguda a tota partida; e la causa de lu es leugiera.	Therefore, the operation in them is that you should immediately consider whether the grandiness is proceeding from there to the eyelid and is spreading to all parts; and the cause of it is light.
Donc fen sobre aquela am fissura per la latitut, e aprop escorga aquela de tota partida am facilitat entro que evasesca, e aprop suspen aquela am onci e abscindeys aquela.	Therefore, make an incision on it with a fine fissure by the width, and immediately examine that of all parts with ease until it evaporates, and then suspend it with onces and cut off.
Mays si a tu no es apparelhada la incizio de lu si no pus que penetras la palpebra am inscizio pauc a pauc, lahoras aquo no notz en deguna causa.	But if the incision of it is not well-apprehended by you, and only pushes to penetrate the eyelid with a slow and gradual incision, then immediately this will not come into any cause.
E si la figura es gran, lahoras tu l’ajusta am sutura; e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	And if the figure is great, then you should adjust it with a suture; and cure that until it is healed.
E si es pauca, a tu no sobrevindra mal per aquela quar l’anguent de lu restaura aquela e encarna.	And if it is small, you will not suffer harm from it, because the humor of it restores that and fleshifies.
E si la grandissia es declinant a las partidas dedintz de la palpebra deves la superficia dedintz, lahoras evesa la palpebra e suspen la grandissia am onci, otra que tu indigescas de incizio, e prem aquela de tota part, e si la palpebra per inscizio es alonguada, aquo no notz en deguna causa.	And if the grandiness is declining to the outer parts of the eyelid, you must smooth the surface outwardly; then immediately elevate the eyelid and suspend the grandiness with onces, unless you need an incision, and press that from all sides, and if the eyelid by incision becomes lengthened, this will not come into any cause.
E aprop la incizio, lava le huel am aygua salada; e cura le loc am aquo que encarna entro que sia sanat.	And immediately after the incision, wash the eyes with salted water; and cure the place with that which fleshifies until it is healed.
Capitol .x.	Chapter X.
De la cura axcirnah en la palpebra desus del huel.	On the Cure of Axirna in the eyelid above the eye.
Axcirnath es grays le qual es engendrat en las tunicas de la palpebra desus, e majorment endeve als enfantz, agrava les huels de aquels et accideyso a lor catartz le mayti; e no podon reguardar la claror del solelh per aquo quar lagremas se coytan ad aquels.	Axirna is a grayish substance which is generated in the tunic of the eyelid above, and most often develops in children, aggravates their eyes, and causes great pain to them; and they cannot look at the brightness of the sun because of it, for tears are shed upon them.
E per so tu vezes aquels jaser sobre les lors caras tot temps, e sobre les lors caras dormen; e so a las palpebras de lor dejos les sobrecils humidas, las quals ja ha cuberta imflacio, e iminencia de accernac apparent es en l’uelh; e que quant tu premes le loc am les tieus ditz, tu centes accernac entro aquels.	And therefore you should often wash their faces with water at all times, and on their faces they sleep; and thus the eyelids of theirs below are covered with humidified lids, which have already been inflated, and a visible approach to swelling is in the eye; and when you press the location with those things I said, you will bring forth swelling into it.
E alcuna manieyra de opperacio es en aquel que le malaute pausa le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop pausa drap de li e de lu fay calgua, e fay de lu cercle segon la quantitat la qual contena arthernach de tota partida, e aprop pausa aquel sobre aquela e prem am les tieus ditz de tota per que sia agreguat arcernac en le mieg del cercle, e aprop fen en le mieg de aquela humiditat am spatum inscident am fissura per la latitut, e la fissura no sia major que la fissura que es fayta en flaubotomia.	And some method of operation is in that which the patient places his own head on the edge of the bed, and immediately pauses a cloth of linen and of wool, and makes of it a ball; then immediately makes a circle according to the quantity which contains arthernach of all parts, and immediately pauses that upon that and presses with those things I said from all sides so that swelling may be aggregated in the middle of the circle, and immediately ends in the middle of that humidification with a spatula incised by a fissure by the width, and the fissure is not greater than the one made in phlebotomy.
Mays en le preon cove que tu fendas la codena tota entro que pervenguas ad arcernach, quar en las mays desposicios proceseys arcernach per fissura segon la forma de grayseza blanca.	But in the prominence it is necessary to cut through the cord completely until you reach the swelling, because in the greatest difficulties process of swelling by fissure according to the form of white greasiness.
Donc extratz aquela am draps los quals tu as envolopatz entre les tieus ditz a las partidas deforo e revolv entre la ma dextra e sinistre entro que sia dispargut.	Therefore, extract that with cloths which you have wrapped between the said ties and the outer parts and revolve between the right hand and left hand until it is dispersed.
E guarda te que no ajustes en la fissura per so que am le spatum no pervenguas al huel e ladescas aquel.	And beware that you do not adjust in the fissure because with the spatula you will not reach the eye and thus cause damage to it.
Mays si no apar a tu arternach en le comensament de la fissura, mays que tu ajustes en la fissura un petit am fecilitat entro que procesisca arternach; e aprop extratz aquela ayssi quo havem dit; e aprop submargeys draps de li en aygua e vi agre e pausa les sobre le loc e estrenh aquels am polvils.	But if you do not find swelling at the beginning of the fissure, but that you adjust in the fissure a little with ease until swelling processes; and immediately extract it as we have said; and immediately submerge cloths of linen in water and vinegar, and pour them over the place and strengthen those with powders.
E so alcus que trissan sal e pausan aquel en la conquavitat de la fissura per so que aquo que es remas de aquela humiditat.	And thus all that remains of that moisture is salted and poured into the convergence of the fissure, so that this which remains of that moisture.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And immediately cure it until it is healed.
Mays si accideys en le loc apostema caut, lahoras cura aquel am emplastres cedatils entro que sia sanat.	But if an apostema occurs in the place, then immediately cure it with caustic poultices until it is healed.
Capitol .xi.	Chapter XI.
De manieyras de tactimi del huel.	On Methods of Touching the Eye.
Quan en las palpebras dels huels so natz pels ajustatz dejos les pels naturals e so antiquatz, lahoras aquels noso al huel e fan endevenir manieras de malautias ayssi cum lacrimas assiduas e mollificacio de palpebras e tela entro que aquo sia causa de destruccio del huel que s’apela tactinir del huel, e cura se en quatre manieyras: o per cauteri am foc; o am medicina acuta segon que denant es dit en le capitol de cauteri; o es fayt atactini per inscizio e sutura; o per cannas segon que yeu diyre.	When in the eyelids of humans there are noted by the adjustments below the natural skin and are becoming old, then immediately those things do not belong to the eye and make ways for bad diseases such as constant tears and softening of eyelids and tissue until that is a cause of destruction of the eye which is called touching the eye; and cure it in four ways: or by cauterization with fire; or by sharp medicine according to what was said before in the chapter on cauterization; or made into an atactini by incision and suture; or by canals as you will say.
E donc cove que tu pauses le cap del malaute en le tieu se; aprop converteys la palpebra del uelh am la tua ma sinistra, e si es convertida, bo es; e sino, entromet agulha en aquela en la qual sia fiel de la partida pus dejos de la palpebra, e fay penetrar la agulha am fiel desus, e aquo sia — prop del marge de la palpebra en le qual naysso les pels — prop dels pels, e tira le fiel a las partidas desus am la palpebra, e converteys aquela am le ray.	And therefore it is necessary that you pause the head of the patient on the edge; immediately convert the eyelid of the eye with your left hand, and if it is converted, so be it; and if not, then insert a needle into that which has felt of the part below the eyelid, and make the needle penetrate the felt above, and thus - right next to the margin of the eyelid where the skin is - next to the skin, and pull the felt upwards towards the eyelid, and convert it with the ray.
E aprop fen en la partida dedintz de la palpebra dejos les pels ajustatz am spatum inscidentz del lacrimal major entro al lacrimal mendre; e aprop extratz le fiel e pausa dejos la palpebra polvilhs petitz de coto o de drap, e aprop senha sobre la palpebra am tenta, e sia ayssi cum figura de fuelha de mirt.	And immediately end at the outer part of the eyelid below the skin adjusted with spatula incised from the lacrimal major into the lacrimal minor; and immediately extract the needle and pause below the eyelid with small powders of coto or cloth, and immediately send over the eyelid with tentation, and it will be thus as a figure of myrtle fuel.
Mays empero cove que sia la figura segon la quantitat de helevacio de la palpebra, quar aquo ja es diversificat en les homes, quar de aquels es le quals indigeys que sia inscidit de la palpebra gran quantitat segon la quantitat per la qual la palpebra es mollificada.	But in any case it is necessary that the figure be according to the quantity of elevation of the eyelid, for this is already diversified among humans, for some of them are those who need to have a large quantity incised from the eyelid according to the quantity by which the eyelid is softened.
E aprop fen am le spatum sobre las doas linhas las quals has senhadas, e comensa del lacrimal major entro al lacrimal menor.	And immediately end with the spatula on both lines which you have marked, and begin from the lacrimal major to the lacrimal minor.
E si’ la tua fissura prop dels pels naturals ayssi cum es la grossetut del rey.	And if your fissure is right next to the natural skin, just as it is the widest part of a king.
E aprop met le onci en un dels dos angles de la codena, e aprop excoria aquela tota, e aprop ajusta am la scitura las doas labias am gula o fiel de lana subtil, e abstergeys le sanc, e fay adherir aquo que superflueys dels fiels sobre dos sobrecils am alcunas causas enviscans, si voles far aquo, e sino, non cures.	And immediately insert the onces into one of the two angles of the cord, and immediately extract it all, and immediately adjust with a stitch the two lips or fine wool thread, and wash away the blood, and make adhere what is superfluous from the threads over two eyelids with some visible causes, if you want to do so, and otherwise, do not cure.
E aprop leyssa la sutura dels fiels entro a tres dias o quatre, e aprop cura aquo.	And immediately loosen the stitch of the threads within three or four days, and immediately cure it.
E si vols, layssa la plagua ses sutura, e cura aquela am aquo que exsicca e constrenh, quar la palpebra es alevada deves la sigillacio de la plagua e la agreguacio de lu; mays sutura es milor E donc aysso diysso les antics de taxanir.	And if you wish, leave the wound open without stitching and cure it with that which dries and strengthens, for the eyelid is raised by the sealing of the wound and the accumulation of humors; but stitching is better. And thus I say to the ancients who taught to taxinate.
Mays empero en lu sia sollicitut sobre le malaute, e es de bona operacio, e no es en lu temor.	But in this case there is solicitude over the patient, and it is of good operation, and not from fear.
E es autra manieyra en taxmir, e es que senhes sobre la palpebra figura ayssi cum fuelha de mirt, e aprop eleva la palpebra am tres uncis segreguatz e congreguatz segon aquesta forma:	And there is another method in taxinating, and it is that you mark on the eyelid a figure such as myrtle leaves, and immediately elevate the eyelid with three separate and gathered threads according to this form:
Mays si no es possible aquo, tener les uncis, e aquo no es engualhat, lahoras pren una agula en la qual haia fil e met aquela en le mieg de la figura, e entromet le autre fiel prop le lacrimal major, e·l fiel segon prop le lacrimal mendre, e ajusta entre les tieus ditz les fiels am equalitat, e aprop am aquels eleva la tua ma am elevacio engual, eleva tota la codena sobre la qual es senhat ayssi cum havem recomtat.	But if it is not possible to take the threads, and this is not adjusted, then immediately take a needle with thread and insert it into the middle of the figure, and enter the other thread next to the lacrimal major, and the second thread next to the lacrimal minor, and adjust between the said ties the threads in equality, and immediately raise your hand with equal elevation, raise all the cord above which is marked as we have recounted.
E aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am sutura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And immediately adjust the two lips of the wound with a stitch, and cure it until it is healed.
Mays si accideys apostema deves la tua inscizio o la tua fissura, seda aquel apostema am cerot e a lu semblantz, e am enguentz.	But if an apostema occurs due to your incision or your fissure, calm that apostema with cerote and like it, and with gentle motions.
E alcunas veguadas endeve a la palpebra que·ls sieus pels sian convertitz, adonc cove que tu uses en aquela de aquo que havem dit de inscizio; mays sutura en quascus es mays artificial.	And sometimes it is necessary to touch the eyelid which its own skin is converted, then it is necessary that you use in it what we have said about incision; but stitching in each case is more artificial.
Ataxinir am cannas es segon aquesta forma:	Atactinating with canals is according to this form:
e es que tu convertas la palpebra e scindas la figura qu’es dedintz segon que he recontat; e aprop per art fay doas cannas o doas astelas subtils de las quals longitut sia segon la longitut de la palpebra e la latitut de lor sia mendra de la latitut del spatum.	and it is that you convert the eyelid and divide the figure which is below according to what I have recounted; and immediately by art make two canals or two thin tubes, of which the length is according to the length of the eyelid and the width is smaller than the width of the spatula.
E tu ja has inscidit en las extremitatz de quascunas partidas, la on tenes les fils.	And you have already incised at the extremities of each part, where you have the threads.
Aprop agregua quascuna am subtilitat subre aquo que superflueys de la palpebra del huel, e constres las cannas de quascunas partidas am fort strictura, e layssa aquela per alcus jorns, quar la codena per la strictura morira e sira denegada e se poyrira entro que per si meteyssa cayra.	And immediately add each one with subtlety over that which is superfluous of the eyelid of the eye, and compress the canals of each part with a strong constriction, and leave it for some days, because the cord will die and become denigrated and will sink in until it comes back.
Mays si es tardat, lahoras trenca la am las toroyras, e aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanat.	But if it is delayed, then immediately cut the cord with scissors, and immediately cure the wound until it is healed.
Donc cum es solidada, la palpebra es elevada e les pels no pungo.	Therefore, when it is solidified, the eyelid is elevated and the skin does not hurt.
E aquesta es la forma de doas cannas las quals faras segon aquesta forma:	And this is the form of two canals which you will make according to this form:
e haia la quantitat de la longitut e de la latitut ni mays ni mens.	and has the quantity of length and width neither more nor less.
Capitol .xii.	Chapter XII.
De elevacio de pels pungentz en le huel am agula quan le pel es dur.	On Elevating Painful Skin in the Eye with a Needle when the Skin is Hard.
Quan son pels no-naturals, durs e aspres e pungentz les huels, lahoras la operacio en lu es que tu prenguas agula subtil e pauses en aquela fiel de ceda subtil e leon, e aprop que tu ajustes las extremitatz de lu e nozes quascu en manieyra mot subtil.	When the skin is non-natural, hard and rough, and painful to the eyes, the operation in this case is that you take a fine needle and insert it into that subtle thread of cedron and linen, and immediately adjust the extremities of it and notice what each one does in a very subtle manner.
E sia la longitut dels fiels de quantitat de una palma.	And let the length of the threads be equal to the quantity of one palm.
E aprop tu compon2 autre fiel subtil dejos lu en breu, e nuza las extremitatz de aquel si tu·t vols.	And immediately compose another fine thread below it in brief, and tie the extremities of that one if you wish.
E aprop pause le malaute le sieu cap en le tieu se, e sia prop del solelh per que la tua obra sia declarada, quar es operacio subtil e menuda.	And immediately place the patient's head on the edge, and be right next to the sun so that your work may be declared, for it is a subtle and minute operation.
E aprop intromet la agulha en la razit del pel ajustat la qual ha necessitat de engen, e fay aquela penetrar en la palpebra festinantment entro que extraguas aquela desus le pel natural.	And immediately insert the needle into the root of the skin adjusted which has required an engineer, and make that thread penetrate the eyelid quickly until you extract it above the natural skin.
E aprop tire le pel entro desus e intromet aquel en alixati, e sian les pels un o dos o tres e no mays.	And immediately pull the skin up and insert it into its place, and be the number of skins one, two, or three, but not more.
E aprop tira la tua ma am aquel entro que·l pel sia fora-gitat am alixolati en la palpebra am le pel natural.	And immediately pull your hand with that until the skin is outside-put and in its place in the eyelid with the natural skin.
Mays si es atirat alixalati e non es gitat le pel, atiraras alixati a las partidas dejos am le fiel le qual tu has compost am aquela, entro qu’en sia gitat alixalati del trau sobira.	But if it is pulled out of its place and the skin is not put outside, pull it to the parts below with the thread which you have composed in that, until it is put outside above the uppermost part.
E vegas aquela am la visio del huel, quar lahoras tu gitaras alixati e lo fiel, e grotan quascu e clautz le huel, e laysse le claus per dos dias o tres, entro que·l pel adheresca al sieu loc e nasque sobre aquel bona carn.	And look at that with the vision of the eye, for you will take out the thread and the skin, and grate some and clean the eye, and leave the closure for two or three days, until the skin adheres to its place and grows above it good flesh.
E si es mays breu le pel, lahoras tu ajusta un pel lonc dels pels naturals, e es elevat am aquel, o que·l leysses entro que sia alonguat aprop alcu spazi, e lehoras tu eleva aquel.	And if the skin is too short, then you adjust one long piece of natural skin, and elevate it with that, or leave it so that it will be lengthened to its proper space, and then you elevate that.
Capitol .xiii.	Chapter XIII.
De la cura de ehacratir la qual ve en la palpebra desus.	On the Cure of Echachatry which appears in the Eyelid above.
Quan ve en le huel ehacratir, e es contraccio de la palpebra quan es contrayta en sus, o a dextra o a sinistra partida, per mala consolidacio de plagua o de seccio o de cauteri, e es apelada leporina, e aquesta ahercrati o es natural o accidental, e es fayta per consolidacio de plagua o de seccios o de cauteri, o per semblantz a lor malcuratz.	When it appears in the eye echachatry, and it is a contraction of the eyelid when it is contracted upwards or sideways, to the right or left part, due to bad consolidation of wound or section or cauterization, and it is called leporina, and this echachatry either is natural or accidental, and is made by consolidation of wound or sections or cauterizations, or by resemblance to their maladies.
