May la manieyra de la operacio en lu es que tu fendas aquela consolidacio e que separes las labias de lu, e pauses en lu en aquo que es entre aquelas una meca de drap de li, e ligues aquelas entro que sian sanadas.	The method of the operation in this case is that you open up that consolidation and separate the lips of it, and place a piece of linen cloth between them, and tie those together until they are healed.
E no cove que tu uses de curacio de lu de las causas las quals exsiccan, constrenho; quar si tu fas aquo retorna alixacratir pus mal que nulh temps no foc habantz.	And it is not necessary that you use a cure for this condition from the causes which dry and constrict; for if you do so, it will return to echachatry even worse than before, having no time at all.
Usa en aquela de causas que mollifico ayssi cum es fenugrec, e embroca am la aygua en la qual son coytz altea e semensa de li, o enguent dyaquilon, le qual sia liquefayt am alcu dels olis, e submergeys en aquel la meca, e cura am aquel.	Use in that condition causes which soften, such as fenugreek, and mix it with the water in which are steeped high-quality seeds of linen or yarrow, or a gentle poultice made from aquilon, which is liquefied with some oil, and submerge the cloth in that mixture, and cure it with that.
E lo tesaur de la tua curacio es que tu perforsses am tot engen que no sia consolidat segon la forma que foc al comensament.	And the treasure of your cure is that you perforate with all skill and art, not allowing anything to be consolidated in its place, according to the form that was present at the beginning.
E aquesta operacio la qual havem dita, no es sino alcuna rectificacio de ehalixacrati que no retorna la forma del loc segon que foc denant.	And this operation which we have described is nothing but some correction of echachatry that does not return to its original form as it was before.
Capitol .xiiii.	Chapter XIV.
De la cura de ehacrati le qual es fayt en la palpebra dejos.	On the Cure of Echachatry which is made in the Eyelid below.
Aquesta alxacrati la qual es fayta en la palpebra dejos, la qual es nompnada vertadierament alxacrati; e es de lu alcuna natural, autra accidental.	This echachatry which is made in the Eyelid below, which is truly named echachatry; and it is either of a natural or an accidental cause.
Mays accidental es fayta per plagua o per scissura o per cauteri o per autres semblantz.	But accidental is caused by wound, section, cauterization, or other similar things.
E la via de la operacio de lu es que tu prenguas una agula en la qual haga fil doble, e fiques aquela en la carn, e que la fassas passar del lacrimal de senestre entro al lacrimal dextre, entro que·l fil pervengua en las doas extremitatz de la carn.	And the method of the operation is that you take a needle with double thread, and insert it into the flesh, and make it pass from the lacrimal canal on the left to the lacrimal canal on the right, until the thread reaches both ends of the flesh.
E aprop exten la carn a las partidas desus am la agula e cus aquela am la agula, e inscideys am spatum ample.	And immediately extend the flesh to the upper parts with the needle and cut it with the needle, and incise with a spatula of good width.
E donc si retorne la figura de la palpebre segon que cove, bo es; e sino, pren le ray e pausa aquel en la figura fenduda, e am aquel converteys la palpebra, e fen las doas fissuras en le latz de la palpebra dejos.	And therefore if the figure of the eyelid returns to its natural shape as it should, that is good; and otherwise, take the thread and pause it in the cleft figure, and with it convert the eyelid, and close the two fissures on the side of the eyelid below.
E sian las extremitatz de las doas fissuras de dos angles de la inscizio, la qual has fayta entro que concurren, e sia de lor fayt angle entro que quan se congreguan sia fayta figura de lor.	And the extremities of the two fissures be at two angles of the incision, which you have made so that they converge, and be of their own making angle, such that when they come together, it forms a figure of its own.
E aquesta figura es letra greca: la landa.	And this figure is a Greek letter: the lambda.
E aprop osta la carn aquela per la quantitat que es le latz de lu agut dejos de lu, aquo que siec la palpebra.	And immediately stop the flesh at that point, for the quantity is the thickness of the eyelid below, which is the natural shape.
E aprop ajusta las partz seperadas e cos aquelas am le fil de lana; e aprop cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit de las medicinas mollificativas e de las calguas entro que sia sanat.	And immediately adjust the separated parts and sew them together with wool thread; and immediately cure those with what we have said about softening medicines and poultices until it is healed.
E si alxacrati endeve per fissura o sutura o cauteri, lahoras cove que tu fendas am fissura plana sobre les pels de la palpebra segon que es precedit.	And if echachatry occurs due to fissure or suture or cauterization, then it is necessary that you open a flat fissure on the skin of the eyelid, as was previously described.
E aprop separa am la calgua entre doas labias segon que havem dit.	And immediately separate with a poultice between two lips, according to what we have said.
En la suma del sermo de la cura de alxacrati quan es desus o dejos, que corra en lu operacio, segon que es preparat de la forma de alxacrati, e aquela es en forma de motas diversitatz.	In the summary of this sermon on the cure of echachatry when it is above or below, which flows into the operation, according to what is prepared in the form of echachatry, and that is in the form of diverse manners.
E le artifexs savi totz temps prepara engen en quascuna manieyra la qual es possibla a lu entro que fassa retornar la figura a la forma natural, o prop de aquela, e aquel malaute segon que a lu conveneys de la operacio e dels strumentz en las majors disposicios.	And the skilled artisans always prepare skillfully in each possible manner, so that they may return the figure to its natural form or nearly so, and that malady according to what is convenient for the operation and the instruments in the greatest dispositions.
Capitol .xv.	Chapter XV.
De la adherencia de la palpebra am la conjunctiva o am la cornea.	On the Adhesion of the Eyelid to the Conjunctiva or to the Cornea.
Quan accideys aquesta consolidacio a motz homes enayssi que sia solidada la palpebra pus desus am le album del huel, e sia prohibida de la facilitat del movement e de las suas obras naturals, donc cove que tu entrometas la extramitat del ray dejos la palpebra, e eleva en sus aquela, o exten aquela am le unci.	When this consolidation occurs in many people, it is solidified above the eyelid to the point where the album of the eye, and it hinders the facility of movement and its natural works, therefore it is necessary that you intervene at the end of the ray below the eyelid, and elevate it upwards or extend it with a thread.
E aprop tu inscideys la adherencia am spatum subtil, le qual no sia am acuitat de las inscisios, habantz obtus un petit per so que·l malaute no sia inquietat deves la operacio, e remau le spatum que no ledesca le huel am la sua acuitat.	And immediately you incise the adhesion with a subtle spatula, which is not sharp like the incisions, having only a small obtuseness so that the malady is not disturbed during the operation, and then remove the spatula so as not to disturb the eye with its sharpness.
E sia la tua inscizio quays excorjan aquela adherencia am facilitat entro que sia retornada la palpebra segon la sua forma natural e que sia sanada tota la adherencia.	And may your incision be such that it easily excises that adhesion, so that the eyelid is returned to its natural form and all the adhesion is healed.
E aprop tu met en le huel aygua salada am la qual tu laves; o distilla en lu de zunia dissolvut en l’aygua.	And immediately put into the eye salt water with which you wash it; or distill on it in a gentle manner, dissolved in water.
E aprop separa entre la palpebra e l’huel am calgua de li, e pausa sobre le huel lana infuza en album de huou, e aprop le tertz jorn usa de causas consolidativas entro que sia sanat.	And immediately separate between the eyelid and the eye with a poultice of linen, and place it on the eye infused in albumen of egg, and then use for three days causes that consolidate, until it is healed.
Capitol .xvi.	Chapter XVI.
De inscizio de ungla e de eminencia de carn dels lacrimals.	On the Incision of the Eyelid and the Eminence of Flesh of the Lacrimal Canal.
Sapias que ungla es segon dos manieyras, quar o es nervosa, e es semblant a ciphac dur subtil; o es no-nervosa, semblant a humiditat blanca congilada, la qual quan ferr la toca, o es forsat aquela prendre am onci, es abscindida e le onci no es ficat en lu.	Know that an eyelid is according to two ways, for either it is nervous, and resembles a hard, thin ciphac; or it is non-nervous, resembling white humidity congealed, which when iron touches it, becomes hardened and the needle cannot be inserted into it.
E amdos las specias no comensan sino del lacrimal major entro que va petit a petit que cobre la vista e prohibeys le lum e·l movement de huel.	And both species do not begin until the lacrimal major, and then gradually cover the eye, prohibiting light and movement.
Mays la manieyra del obrar en la inscizio de lu es que·l malaute pause le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop obre les huels de lu, e eleva la palpebra am la tua ma, e aprop colligeys la ungla am onci de pauca duplicacio e exten aquela a las partidas desus.	But the method of working in this incision is that the malady puts its head in its place, and immediately opens the eyes of it, and elevates the eyelid with your hand, and immediately collects the eyelid with a needle of slight duplication and extends it to the upper parts.
E aprop pren una agula e entromet en aquela un pel de cavalh o de buou o de vaqua, o de semblantz, o de fiel fort, o duplica la extremitat de la agulha petit a petit e fica aquela en le mieg de la ungla, e penetra aquela am la agulha, e lia am fiel la ungla; e exten aquela a las partidas desus, e excorja am le pel le latz de la ungla lo qual siec la pupilla.	And immediately take a needle and insert into it a piece of horse, ox, or cow hide, or something similar, or a strong thread, or duplicate the extremity of the needle little by little and place it in the middle of the eyelid, and penetrate it with the needle, and tie it with thread the eyelid; and extend it to the upper parts, and excise on the edge of the eyelid which sees the pupil.
E ayssi tu sieguas aquela am le pel entro al derier de lu.	And thus you will follow that with the hide until the very end of it.
E aprop tu inscideys le romanent en la razitz del lacrimal am spatum subtil o am petitas forfexs, e leysa la carn del lacrimal natural per so que per inscizio de aquela no endevengua fluxs de lagremas continuabla.	And immediately you incise the remainder in the root of the lacrimal canal with a subtle spatula or small forceps, and remove the natural flesh of the lacrimal canal so that through the incision of it no continuous flow of tears may ensue.
E alscunas vetz la ungla am le sol onci estenduda o am fiel, ayssi co havem dit, e aprop sia excurjat am spatum leon del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And some days later the eyelid with the extended needle or thread, as we have said, and immediately excise it with a lion's spatula whose form is this:
E guarda te que am le spatum no toques la tunica cornea e que avengua en lu ruptura, e que la pupilla sia perforada.	And be careful not to touch the corneal tunic with the spatula and avoid a rupture in that place, lest the pupil be perforated.
Aprop la inscizio geta en le huel un pauc de sal trissa o di cief fayt de siniar, e leyssa aquel entro al autre dia; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove entro que sia sanat.	And immediately the incision gets in the eye a little bit of salt or the juice made from sinew, and leave it until the next day; and then cure that with water as needed, until it is healed.
E si la ungla no es nervoza e no podes metre la agulha, ni es ficada en aquela le onci, lahoras motas veguadas aquesta specia de ungla es curada am medicinas, e es sanada ayssi cum yeu e recomtat en la divisio.	And if the eyelid is not nervous and you cannot insert the needle, nor is it taken in that place by the thread, then many times this type of eyelid is cured with medicines, and is healed thus as I have said and recounted in the division.
E si tu vols inscindir aquela, lahoras tu obre le huel del malaute e pren spatum subtil leon de freul acuitat segon aquesta forma:	And if you want to incise it, then you will work on the eye of the malady and take a subtle spatula lion with sharpness according to this form:
am subtilitat.	with subtlety.
E si vezes que aquela es rarificada e es confugida e empren en aquela razit, lahoras distilla de la tua ora en le huel de cief fayt de siniar o am cief rog o am sal trissat, e opila le huel entro a l’autre dia.	And if at times that is rarefied and is confused and enters into the root of it, then you will distill from your hand in the eye juice made from sinew or with raw onion or with salt crushed, and cover the eye until the next day.
E aprop itera sobre aquela la operacio entro que sia remaugut tot aquo que es de lu, sino que·l contrari apostema caut sia en le huel, quar lahoras tu leyssa aquela, e cura al comensament la apostema entro que sia sanat.	And immediately repeat the operation on that until all that is of it is removed, except for the contrary apostema which is in the eye, because then you will leave it, and cure the apostema at first until it is healed.
E aprop itera la tua operacio sobre aquela am razo entro que sia sanat.	And immediately repeat your operation on that with reason until it is healed.
La emenencia de la carn lacrimal, si notz en le huel per gran nocument, sia suspendut am onci; e inscideys aquela de aquela una partida, e no ultimes la inscizio per so que no inscidesqua fluxs de lagremas.	The eminence of the lacrimal flesh, if noticed in the eye with great harm, is suspended with a thread; and incise that part of it, and do not finish the incision for fear of continuous flow of tears.
E aprop distilla en le lacrimal cief rog e fayt de siniar entro que sia sanat.	And immediately distill in the lacrimal juice made from onion and sinew until it is healed.
Capitol .xvii.	Chapter XVII.
De inscizio de alguazardenic e de aquo que es nascut de carn ajustada en le huel.	On the Incision of Algae-like growths and of Water that is born from flesh adjusted in the Eye.
Alcunas veguadas en les huels de alcus es nascuda carn roga, e es sobre-pausada entro que cobre la pupilla, o apropinqua o estrenh sobre las palpebras e fort leu comprem las palpebras a las partidas deforo e es assemblada a roza de balaustra.	Some times in the eyes of some people is born red flesh, and it is superimposed until it covers the pupil, or approaches or strengthens on the eyelids and lightly presses them against the parts above and is assembled like a rose window.
Mays la operacio en lu es que·l malaute pausa le sieu cap en le tieu se; e aprop obre les huels de aquel e colligeys tota aquela carn am oncis convenientz ad aquo, e te aquo am una forcep o am cesti; e aprop inscindiys la carn el comensament entro que tot sia finit am le encisori, e guarda te del huel que no ledescas aquel deves la tua operacio.	But the operation in this case is that the malady puts its head in its place; and immediately opens the eyes of that and collects all that flesh with suitable thread, and tie it with a forceps or with a basket; and immediately incises the flesh at first until all is finished with the needle, and be careful not to disturb the eye lest you spoil your operation.
E sia la tua inscizio am la qual inscides aquelas o am espatum le qual nos havem recomtat en la inscizio de la ungla, o am petitas forfexs am las quals es colligit ascebel segon que vindra la forma de lu aprop aquest capitol.	And be the incision with which you incise those or with a spatula which we have recounted in the incision of the eyelid, or with small forceps with which it is collected according to the form that comes closest to this chapter.
Donc cum es complida la tua inscizio e es remauguda tota aquela carn, lahoras omple le huel de sal trissa, o destilla en lu polvera roga e semblantz a lu de las medicinas corrossivas, e pausa sobre le huel deforo coto am album de huou entro que sia asegurat de apostema caut.	And thus when your incision is complete and all that flesh is removed, then fill the eye with crushed salt, or distill in it a red powder resembling that of corrosive medicines, and place on the eye above a thin layer of albumen of egg to ensure against apostema.
E si roman alcuna causa de alguardenici e es senhoragat sanc caut, e temes apostema caut, lahoras leyssa le huel e cura aquela apostema am aquo que ceda aquela apostema, e aprop itera sobre aquel am operacio entro que sia sanat, e semblantment fay en la carn ajustada la qual accideys en le huel de aquesta especia.	And if any cause of algae-like growths is present and is Lord of the sanguineous apostema caution, and you fear apostema caution, then leave the eye alone and cure that apostema with water which dissolves that apostema, and immediately repeat the operation on that until it is healed, and similarly do in the adjusted flesh which occurs in the eye of this species.
Mays empero tu cove que alienes tota curacio del huel freul per via natural o per via accidental, obran am ferr, e no metas la tua ma en alcuna de aquestas operacios entro que veges que aquel membre sia suffertant aquela operacio.	But however you must know that alienates all cure of the eye by way of natural or accidental means, work with iron, and do not put your hand in any of these operations until you see that member is capable of that operation.
Capitol .xviii.	Chapter XVIII.
De colleccio de sabel en le huel.	On the Collection of Sabellum in the Eye.
Sabel so venas rogas las quals son testudas sobre le huel e prohibeysso al vesement la sua operacio, e develican le huel am longitut de dias.	Sabel is a reddish-colored vein which forms knots on the eye and prevents the eyelid from performing its operation, and opens up the eye along with length of days.
Donc necessari es al comensament que tu consideres si le huel en le qual es sabel es fort e en lu no es autra malautia que sabel, lahoras tu colligeys aquel sabel.	Therefore it is necessary at the beginning that you consider whether the eye in which the sabel is present is strong and in it there is no other disease besides sabel, then you collect that sabel.
E es que tu comandes al malaute que pause le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop suspen aquelas venas am un onci o am dos segon la tua prudencia; e sia aquel onci de subtil duplicacio segon aquesta forma:	And it is that you command the malady to put its head in its place, and immediately suspend those veins with one or two threads according to your prudence; and be that thread of subtle duplication according to this form:
o so dos oncis gradantment en un cos segon aquesta forma:	or two threads gradually woven into one body according to this form:
E aprop sian colligidas aquelas venas am forses subtils, am subtilitat, e abstergeys le sanc hora aprop hora, entro que vegas aquelas venas esser remaugudas del huel e sian revolgudas.	And immediately those veins are collected with subtle forces, with subtlety, and wash away the blood hour by hour, until you see those veins being removed from the eye and turned back.
E guarda te que tu no ledes le huel am las extremitatz del spatum; e si’ la tua operacio en le miegjorn denant le solelh, e sias mot ferm en la tua operacio que no inscidas sino aquelas venas.	And be careful that you do not touch the eye with the extremities of the spatula; and if your operation is in the middle of the day before the sun, and be steadfast in your operation so as to incise only those veins.
E quan tu auras complitz, lahoras tu distilla en le huel cief vert o rog per que am sa acuitat corrodesca aquo que es remaugut del sabel.	And when you have completed, then you will distill in the eye juice of green or red onion so that with its sharpness it may corrode the water that is removed from the sabel.
Mays si aquo no es a tu possible colligeys tot en aquela hora, e lahoras tu emplastra tot am aquo que cede la dolor de lu, e leyssa lu per alcus dias entro que sia sedada la dolor de lu e que sia asegurat de apostema caut.	But if that is not possible for you, then collect all of it in that hour, and immediately apply all the water that relieves the pain of it, and leave it for some days until the pain of it is sedated and is ensured against caution.
E aprop itera sobre lu segon que la mateyssa manieyra entro que sia sanat.	And immediately repeat on it in the same manner until it is healed.
E aquesta es la forma de las forfexs:	And this is the form of forceps:
Capitol .xix.	Chapter XIX.
De reduccio de arizati al nas.	On the Reduction of Arthritis to the Nose.
Quan tu curas arisati am cauteri o am medicina aguda comburent segon que es precedida la narracio de lu e no es sanat, lahoras no es engen en lu sino que fendas sobre le apostema deves la maturitat de lu, e que extraguas tota la humiditat la qual es en lu e·l poyre entro que sia descubert le os.	When you cure arthritis with cauterization or acute medicine as it is preceded by the narrative of it and does not heal, then do not intervene in it but instead make incisions on the apostema of maturity until all the humidity that is in it is extracted and dried out so that the bone is revealed.
E donc cum es descubert le os e vezes en lu corrupcio o negror, lahoras tu ratz lu am un sturment del qual aquesta es la forma:	And therefore when the bone is exposed and times in it corruption or blackness appears, then you will scrape it with an instrument of which this is the form:
E es nompnat de aspre cap, e sia feyt de fer indi, e sia le cap redon ayssi cum asir le qual sia fayt punctat per punctacio de lima o aliskalfati per punctacio subtil (ayssi cum es en la forma seguent).	And it is called the "aspre cap", and it is made of iron, and its head is rounded like an ash which has been pointed by a lime point or sharpened to a subtle point (such as it is in this form).
E pausa aquel sobre le loc corrumput del os, e aprop revolveys aquel entre les tieus ditz, e prem la tua ma petit a petit entro que sapias que aquela corropcio es rasa.	And place that on the decayed part of the bone, and immediately turn it between those said points, and press your hand little by little until you know that that corruption is gone.
E aquo sia fayt alcunas veguadas, e aprop restaura le loc am causas exsiccativas e stipticas.	And this be done several times, and immediately restore the place with drying and purgative causes.
Donc si·l loc es consolidat e es en lu nascuda bona carn e es abscindit le cors de la sania e roman per xl dias, e no es renovat e no es apostemat e no accideys en lu accident, lahoras tu sapias que es sanat.	Therefore if the place is consolidated and good flesh has grown in it and the body of the disease has been cut off and remains for 40 days, and is not renewed and is not apostemated and there is no accident in it, then you will know that it is healed.
E sino, lahoras no es en lu engen sino reduzir la fissura a la forma del nas, e segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu descuebras de segon os am ferr o am medicina acuta, e cum sira descubert le os, lahoras tu pren tribo segon aquesta forma:	And otherwise, then do not intervene in it but rather reduce the fissure to the shape of the nose, and according to this manner: and it is that you remove a second bone with iron or acute medicine, and when the bone is exposed, then you take a thread according to this form:
Sia la extramitat de lu ferr triangulada, e·l fust de lu sia prim extenuat entro a la extremitat ayssi cum vezes assi.	Be the extremity of the iron triangular, and the handle of it be first exhausted to the tip just so that it is as if you were to bite it.
E aprop pausa aquel sobre le os, e sia aquel prop del lacrimal; e alongua la tua ma un pauc del huel, e aprop revol la tua ma am le tribo entro que penetre tot le os, e aquel sente le malaute per asso que atroba vent yssir per so quan te la sua ma.	And immediately place that on the bone, and it should be near the lacrimal; and stretch your hand a little further into the eye, and immediately turn your hand with the thread until it penetrates all the bone, and that feels the malady by which it finds vent to come out so when you pull your hand.
Donc lahoras restaura le loc am medicinas stipticas exsiccantz ayssi cum t’e eyssenhat.	Therefore then restore the place with purgative medicines that dry, just as they were applied.
Donc cum nays la carn e·l loc es endurazit, lahoras la materia la qual effundia a las partidas deforo retorna al nas, donc aquo es pus leugier sobre le malaute.	Therefore when the flesh and the place are hardened, then the material that flowed to the parts above returns to the nose, therefore this is more gentle on the malady.
Capitol .xx.	Chapter XX.
De reduccio de la eminencia del huel.	On the Reduction of the Eminence of the Eye.
Quan le huel emineys am la sua totalitat e no accideys en le vezement nocument ni diminuacio, lahoras cove que laxas le malaute, e aprop que·l segues, e aprop que pausas ventozas en le cervitz ses scarificacio e succa per bona succaccio; e aprop pausa sobre le huel liniment le qual sia fayt de acatra e aloe e enses e sarcocolla, e aprop strenh le emplaustre sobre le huel am motz polvils.	When the eye protrudes in its entirety and there is no accident or diminution in it, then you must relax the malady, and immediately follow, and immediately pause breathing on the neck without scarification and suck for good suction; and immediately place a poultice on the eye which is made of acacia, aloe, and sarsaparilla, and immediately strengthen the application on the eye with many powders.
E la manieyra dels polvils es que prenguas draps de li leons motz, e quascun drap sia duplicat en quatre plecs; e fay de aquels motz.	And the manner of the powders is that you take cloths of lion's mane, and each cloth be doubled into four folds; and make powder from those.
E aprop pausa aquels la un sobre le autre segon la quantitat de la qual ha le huel necessitat.	And immediately place one on top of the other according to the quantity which the eye requires.
E aprop strenh sobre aquels am drap dur am fort strictura; e itera las ventosas am succio ses scarificacio; e aprop osta las ventosas e leyssa le huel streyt le dia e la nueyt.	And immediately strengthen on top of those with a strong cloth, and repeat the suction without scarification; and immediately stop the suction and leave the eye straight for a day and night.
Mays si entretant le liguament es mollificat, lahoras cove que sia mot streyt.	But if in the meantime the ligament is relaxed, then you must make it tight.
E aprop osta le liament aprop le dia e la nueyt ayssi cum havem dit.	And immediately stop the ligament for a day and night just as we have said.
E si vezes le huel ja esser redusit, bo es, e sino, lahoras itera le emplastre am les polvils e la strictura e las ventosas entro que sia sanat.	And if the eye is already reduced, well it is; and otherwise, then immediately repeat the application with powders, ligament, and suction until it is healed.
Capitol .xxi.	Chapter XXI.
De la inscizio de la eminencia de la tunica uvea.	On the Incision of the Eminence of the Uveal Tunic.
Quan endeve disrupcio en la tunica uvea, e aprop es eminent e procezeys fora las palpebras ayssi cum un gra de rasim, e es orrazada la forma de home per aquo, e vols aquo inscidir, lahoras la operacio en lu es ayssi cum havem recomtat, que tu entrometas la agula en la razitz de la uvea de la partida dejos en la partida desus, e aprop met la agula autra en la qual sia fil doble de la part del lacrimal, e fay aquela penetrar e leyssa la primieyra agula segon la sua disposicio; e aprop inscideys le loc del fiel doble e leva am aquel la partida de la uvea en le circuit de la agula, e strenh aquela mot.	When the tunica uvea becomes disrupptive and protrudes forth between the eyelids like a grain of raisin, and its shape is that of a man for this reason, and you want to incise it, then the operation in it is as we have recounted, which is that you insert the needle into the root of the uvea from the left side and above, and immediately place another needle in the double thread part near the lacrimal, and make it penetrate and leave the first needle according to its disposition; and immediately incise the location of the double thread and lift up with it the part of the uvea in the circuit of the needle, and strengthen that motion.
E aprop extratz la agula e pausa sobre le huel lana infusa en album de huou e leyssa entro que cayha le fil am la uva.	And immediately extract the needle and place it on the eye lanolin infused in egg white, and leave it until the thread falls away from the uvea.
E aprop cura le huel am aquo que conforte aquel entro que la plagua sia sanada.	And immediately cure the eye with water that comforts it, until the wound is healed.
E alcunas veguadas aduna de tota partida am cercle de drap entro le huel ajuste eminencia gran, e aprop sia perforat am le spatum subtil que vengua al preon del huel, e corra la humiditat albuginea, e descen le huel e intra tantost.	And sometimes gather all the parts with a circle of cloth into the eye adjusted to the great eminence, and immediately be perforated by a subtle spatula that comes before the eye, and flow out the albigenous moisture, and descend the eye and enter soon.
E aprop strenh entro que sia sanat.	And immediately strengthen until it is healed.
Capitol .xxii.	Chapter XXII.
De curacio de alconati.	On the Cure of Alconatitis.
Aquesta malautia que es apelada alconati no es sino sania la qual es ajustada en le huel semblant a aygua dessendent e no es aquela.	This disease which is called alconatitis is nothing but inflammation that is adjusted in the eye resembling descending water and not that.
Mays la manieyra del obrar en ela es que fasses le malaute sezer sobre la sela aparelada e dreyta, e aprop pren le cap sieu en las tuas mas de doas partz e mau aquel entro que veias la sania pervenir a las partidas dejos, e aprop sia siccada e no descenda, e sia ostat le lum, e·l malaute veia las causas ayssi cum vezia.	But the manner of working on it is that you make the malady cease upon the prepared and right couch, and immediately take hold of your own head with both hands and bring it down into the part where you see the inflammation reaching, and immediately dry it up so that it does not descend, and stop the light, and the malady sees the causes just as if it saw.
E si no descendra en jos, sapias que es aygua.	And if it does not descend below, you will know that it is water.
Mays si no es preparat le descendement a la sania am aquo que havem dit, lahoras fay le malaute sezer entre las tuas mas e aprop pren spatum subtil e fen am aquel sobre le pannicol cernent un petit deves la continuacio de la conjunctiva am la tunica cornea en la corona (entro al loc vuet), entro que sia fora-getada la sania.	But if it is not prepared for the descent of the inflammation with water as we have said, then make the malady cease between your hands and immediately take a subtle spatula and place it on the panniculus cernenting a small part of the continuation of the conjunctiva with the tunic cornea in the crown (until the location is forgotten), until the inflammation is forgotten.
Donc cum es fora-getada, lahoras tu distilla en le huel aygua cauda en la qual has mesclat mel o aygua en la qual ja has bulit fenugrec e mel.	Therefore when it is forgotten, then you will distill in the eye warm water into which you have mixed honey and water in which you have boiled fenugreek and honey.
E aprop sia curat am las autras causas entro que sia sanat.	And immediately be cured by other causes until it is healed.
Capitol .xxii.	Chapter XXIII.
De la curacio de la aygua descendent del huel.	On the Cure of the Descending Water from the Eye.
Ja havem dit las specias de la aygua en la divisio e qual conveneys a perforar am sermo declarant, lahoras aquel segon la sanetat.	We have already said the species of water in the division and which is suitable to pierce according to what we declare, then that one according to health.
Lahoras cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute entre las tuas mas sobre un cayrat e lia le sieu huel sa, lu mot stringent.	Then you must make the malady cease between your hands on a cloth and tie up your own eye so that it is very tight.
E aprop pausa prop de la palpebra del sieu huel la tua ma senestra, si le huel en le qual es l’aygua es le huel senestra; o am la tua ma dreyta, si le huel es le dextre.	And immediately place your left hand near the eyelid of your own eye if the eye in which the water is flowing is the left one; or with your right hand if it is the right one.
E aprop am la tua ma dextra pren almagda, si le huel es senestre; o am la tua ma senestra, si le huel es de dreyt.	And immediately with your right hand take almond, if the eye is left; or with your left hand, if it is right.
E aprop pausa la extremitat de almagda prop de la corona per la grossesa del ray en le album del huel de part del mendre lacrimal, e aprop enpelleys almagda am vertut e revol la tua ma am aquel.	And immediately place the extremity of almond near the crown for the thickness of the ray in the album of the eye from the smaller lacrimal part, and immediately anoint with virtue and turn your hand around it.
E aprop penetre en le album del huel e sentas que almagda ja es pervenguda a causa vueda.	And immediately penetrate into the album of the eye and feel that almond has already penetrated to the desired cause.
E cove que sia la masura del cami de almagda al preon la mesura del spazi le qual es de la pupilla entro a la fi de la negror, e es la corona del huel; quar tu veyras am aquel pupilla am la visio de l’huel per la clartat de la tunica cornea.	And it must be the measure of the path of almond to reach the precursor the measure of space which is that of the pupil from the beginning of darkness, and it is the crown of the eye; because you will see with it the pupil with the vision of the eye through the clarity of the tunic cornea.
E aprop pausa almagda entro al loc en le qual es l’aygua, e aprop tu la atira en jos una veguada aprop autra, e donc si la aygua descen tantost, lahoras vetz le malaute aquo sobre le qual huebre la sua vista tantost, e almagda en le sieu huel.	And immediately place almond into the location where the water is, and immediately attract it down once or twice, and therefore if the water descends at once, then you will see the malady cured over which it had its view at once, and almond in your own eye.
E aprop repausa se un pauc; donc si la aygua es descenduda, lahoras tu depausa aquela autre veguada abantz que almagda ne sia getada.	And immediately pause for a moment; therefore if the water has descended, then you will put aside that other time before almond is exhausted.
E donc quan es sicada e no descen, lahoras tu extrat almagda am facilitat, e revol am aquel la tua ma pauc a pauc, e aprop dissolveys en l’aygua un petit de sal clara de gemma e am aquela lava le huel dedintz; e aprop pausa fora le huel coto o stopa o lana infusa en oli rozat e album de huou e ligua am aquo le huel sa.	And therefore when it is dry and no longer descends, then you will extract almond with ease, and turn around with it your hand a little at a time, and immediately dissolve in the water a small amount of clear salt from gemstone and with that wash the eye outwardly; and immediately pause outside the eye with cotton or stopper or lanolin infused in rose oil and album of egg white, and tie with water your own eye.
Mays nos e aquels que so de nostre temps pause sobre aquel comi trissat am album de huou.	But those of our time place on it a comb made of albumen of eggs.
E si no obezeys a tu almagda al intrament de l’huel per la sua duricia — quar es alcu dels homes del qual le huel es dur mot —, lahoras cove que prenguas le spatum le qual es nompnat alberid del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if it does not obey your almond at the instrument of the eye because of its hardness - for some men have eyes that are very hard - then you must take the spatula which is called alberid, and this is its form:
E donc perfora am aquel aquela conjunctura, e no ultimes la tua ma en le trauc, e no es si no que fassas via ad almagda loc subtil.	And therefore pierce with it that conjuncture, and do not leave your hand in the hole, and it is only if you make a way for almond to reach the subtle location.
E aprop entromet almagda segon que havem dit.	And immediately insert almond according to what we have said.
E deves le compliment de la tua obra, sia preparat al malaute dormitori descentment fayt en le qual dorma sobre le sieu dos en mayson tenebrosa, e sia prohibit de totz movementz .	And complete the complement of your work, be prepared for the sleeping malady to descend in which it will sleep on its own back in a dark house, and be prohibited from all movements.
E pausa en la natura de lu aquo per que sia linida la sua natura, e no maugua le sieu cap a la partida dreyta ni senestra de tot.	And pause in the nature of it so that its nature is aligned, and do not upset your head to the right or left side at all.
E sia le liament segon la sua disposicio entro al tertz dia.	And be the ligament according to its disposition for three days.
E aprop deslia aquel en aquela maysso tenebrosa e exproha la freol vista, e fay li vezer alcunas causas, e aprop retorna le liament entro al dia .vii.	And immediately release it into that darkest place and expose the most hidden view, and make it see some causes, and immediately return to the ligament on the 7th day.
E no cove que fassas aquo en la hora de las curacios o tantost aprop la infusio.	And do not make this so in the hour of the cures or almost immediately after the infusion.
Habantz cove que tu alienes aquo per so quar la aygua puega leugierament per gran e vehement de reguardament.	They have to be careful that you do not make this so because the water can flow more easily through great and violent regard.
Mays si accideys apostema caut, lahoras cove que deslias le huel denant le vii dia, e rectifica aquel am aquo que ceda apostema.	But if an apostema occurs, then you must release the eye before the 7th day and correct it with water that calms the apostema.
Lahoras tu absol la vista de lu e pausa sobre la cara de lu oral per le qual sia regit le vezement de lu dejos lu per alcus dias, lu existent en la mayszo tenebrosa.	And then you will absolve the vision of it and pause on the face of it orally so that it is guided by it for some days, existing in the darkest place.
E aprop sia gitat de aquela mayzo gradantment e conversa8 en las suas causas.	And immediately be gotten from that dark place gradually and converse with its causes.
E sapias que in alchatea no es excusat le discipol de visio alcunas veguadas, e lahoras tu sias ardit sobre la operacio.	And know that in each case, the disciple is not exempt from some vision occasionally, and then you will be bold on the operation.
E ja es pervengut a nos de alcu de aquels les quals so al Artach , e alcu disse que fayt foc en al Ayrac magdaam perforat am le qual es succada la aygua.	And now it has been reached to us from some of those who are in Artach, and some said that a fire is made in Ayrac, greatly perforated at the place where the water is sucked.
Mays empero yeu non e vist degu en la nostra terra le qual haia perfeyt aquo, ni e aquo legit en alcu dels libres dels antics; e es possible que aquo sia novel.	But however, I do not see that in our land which has perfected this, nor have I read it in any of the books of the ancients; and it is possible that this is new.
E aquestas so las formas de las specias de magdaan per que sia sobre aquelas aquel le qual ignora aquelas:	And these are the forms of the species of magdaan by which one is above those who do not know them:
E sian faytas de eram o de ferr propriament, e sian las extramitatz de lor am aquesta subtilitat triangulada, la extremitat aguda ayssi cum aquela es la forma.	And these are made of iron or of bronze properly, and they are the extremities of their own, with this subtlety triangular, the sharp end just like that is the form.
Capitol .xxiv.	Chapter XXIV.
De la curacio de carn nada en le nas.	On the Cure of Noxious Flesh in the Nose.
Quan en le nas so nascudas carns diversas ajustadas de las quals es alcuna causa la qual es assemblada a scorpio de motz pes, o a polip peys; e aquesta malautia es apelada polipus quar es a semblansa de aquel peys representat.	When in the nose there are born various fleshy growths, some of which are caused by a cause resembling Scorpio's heavy weight or Polyp's flesh; and this disease is called Polypus because it resembles that flesh represented.
E de lu es carn cancrosa, lapadea, de fusca color; e de lu es que es carn leon no de color fusca.	And of it is cancerous flesh, bluish-gray in color; and of it also is the lion's flesh not gray.
Donc en aquela que es en aquestas carns leon no fraudulenta ni cancroza, cove que fassas le malaute sezer entre las tuas mas e posat al solelh, e huebre las nars de lu, e picoys le tieu onci en aquelas carns.	Then in that which is not fraudulent nor cancerous lion's flesh, you must make the malady cease between your hands and place it in the sun, and anoint the nose with it, and pierce it once or twice in those fleshy growths.
E aprop extrat aquela a las partidas deforo, e aprop inscindeys aquo que has comprehendut de aquelas am spatum agut subtil de la una partida entro que sapias que tota la carn ja es ostada; que si roman de lu deguna causa de la qual la abscisio es possibla, lahoras tu ratz aquo am la un dels estrumentz subtils am facilitat entro que de lu romangua denguna causa.	And immediately extract it from the parts above, and immediately insert into that which you have comprehended from those with a sharp subtle spatula of one part until you know that all the flesh has been removed; for if there remains any cause by which ablation is possible, then you must ratify this with one of the subtle instruments with ease until no cause remains.
Mays si senhoreja am sanc o accida apostema caut, lahoras tu pausa a lu aquo que cove; o es dels apostemas malignes, lahoras tu coyta e cauteriza aquel entro que sia abscindit sanc e sian ostadas las cavas totas.	But if there is bleeding or an apostema occurs, then you must pause in that which is necessary; or it is one of the malignant apostemas, then you must cut and cauterize that until the bleeding ceases and all the cavities are removed.
E aprop sia getatz en le nas aprop la inscizio vi agre e aygua o vi.	And immediately be gotten in the nose with an incision, either by water or vinegar.
Mays si le nas es ubert e de lu procezeys humiditat entro al palat, lahoras sapias que ja es sanat.	But if the nose is open and moisture proceeds from it into the palate, then you will know that it is already healed.
Mays si la humiditat no penetra segon que cove, lahoras tu sapias que dedintz lu es carn nada en los pus sobiras osses de las nars als quals non es pervengut abscizio.	But if the moisture does not penetrate as it should, then you will know that behind it is noxious flesh in the sinuses of the nose which has not been removed.
Donc lahoras cove que entromitas fiel de li al qual sia alcuna grosseza, e nuza en lu motz nuzes, e pausa entre quascun nutz la quantitat del dit o mens, e engene le malaute e entromet una extremitat del fiel en le nars am lo ray o am autra causa la qual es a lu possibla.	Therefore it is necessary to introduce the point of the needle into that which has some thickness, and push it gently, and pause between each thrust the quantity of the said or more, and generate the malady and introduce one end of the needle into the nose with the ray or with another cause which is possible to it.
E pus que aquo aura fayt, que atire le sieu odorament entro que pervengua a las canals de las nars, e sia eyssit sobre le sieu golayro, quar tropas veguadas le semblant ad aquesta accio fan les enfantz a las scolas, e es leugiera causa ad aquel que ho vol far.	And after this has been done, that you draw your odorament into the nostrils so that it reaches the channels of the nose, and be exhaled over your gullet, for many times they seem to do this at school, and it is a light cause for him who wants to do.
E aprop pausa las dos extramitatz del fiel, una extremitat que iesca sobre le nas et l’autra que romangua en le nas, e aprop aministra serratura de carn am les nuzes que so en le fiel, e fay aquo entro que sapias que las carn ja so am les nuzes del fiel.	And immediately pause the two extremities of the needle, one end that comes out over the nose and the other that remains in the nose, and immediately administer a closure of flesh with the knots that are in the needle, and do this until you know that the flesh is already bound by the knots of the needle.
E aprop extratz le fiel, e pausa en le nas aprop la abstraccio del sanc una calgua , e fay aquo per tres dias o mays entro que l’enguent corrodo tot aquo que es romas de las carns.	And immediately extract the needle, and pause in the nose about the abstraction of blood one quarter, and do this for three days or more until the scab is completely formed over what remains of the flesh.
E aprop en la fi de la causa, pausa en le nas una canula de plom per alscus jorns entro que sia sanat.	And immediately in the end of the cause, pause in the nose with a leaden cannula for several days until it is healed.
Mays si endigeys de curacio que exsique, usa de aquela.	But if you degenerate from the cure that exists, use this one.
E aquesta es la forma del instrument a capipurge fazedor am le qual son distillatz olis e medicinas en le nars:	And this is the form of the instrument to make a capipurge, with which oils and medicines are distilled in the nose:
E fay aquo de argent o de eram, la qual sia semblant a una petita lampesa uberta, ayssi cum petita conqua, e le meat semblantment.	And make this of silver or bronze, which is similar to a small open lamp, just like a small shell, and the metal similarly.
E si vols, fay una canula clausa ayssi cum cana, e la cancula del estrument a capipurge fazedor e sia plana, descuberta; a la qual sia manubre en lo derier de lu, am le qual tenguas aquela quan escaufas en lu oli o aquo que tu vols dels sucs e de las causas suctiblas.	And if you wish, make a closed cannula like a reed, and the cannula of the instrument to make a capipurge maker be flat, open; to which there is a handle at the end, with which you can take that when you need it in oil or water that you want from the juices and causes suitable.
E aquestz capipurgi es precios: recipe de enforbi de castor, de balayra blanc, de giengiebre, e piletre de safra, de pebre lonc, de escafragia, de epetum de spic ana unc. vi cumfizeys am suc de bleda e de caul, e sian faytas pillulas, e sia destemprada una pillula am aygua tebeza, e sia gitat en las nars del malaute jasent envers.	And these capipurgis are precious: recipe of antimony of castor, of white balm, of gingerbread, and saffron, of long pepper, of asafoetida, of hyssop, and anaunced spices. And mix them with the juice of blueberry and of poppy, and make pills, and one pill be tempered with watered tea, and be inserted into the nostrils of the malady as it is situated.
Capitol .xxv.	Chapter XXV.
De theyls natz en las extramitatz del nas.	On the Worms in the External Parts of the Nose.
Motas veguadas es nat theyl en las extramitatz del nas, e es magnificat e omentat en alscus dias entro en que mot es leg le reguardament de lu.	Many times it is born a worm in the external parts of the nose, and it is magnificent and augmented in several days until its appearance is seen.
E per aquo cove que tu inscidas aquel en le comensament de la apparissio de lu, e erediques tot aquel.	And therefore you must introduce that into the beginning of its appearance and eradicate all of it.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc o cauteri o medicina comburent la qual estia en loc de lu.	And immediately pause over the place or cauterize with medicine which is in the location of it.
Mays si es tardada la sua inscizio entro que sia magnificat, lahoras considera si es lapificat, dur, de fusca color e de pauc sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel am ferr quar es apostema crancos; quar motas veguadas ad aquel que inscideys aquesta apostema endeve per lu granda malicia sobre aquel le qual aquel havia.	But if its insertion is delayed until it becomes magnificent, then consider whether it is calcified, hard, of dark color and little sensation, then do not touch that with iron because it is a cancerous apostema; for many times the one who inserts this apostema devolves great malice upon the one whom it had.
E si le apostema es de leon tocament e no es de fosca color, e vezes que inscizio es possibla en tot aquel, lahoras evacua le malaute e inscideys aquel senes temor, e cura le loc am aquo que exsique e costrenh entro que sia sanat.	And if the apostema is of lion's touch and not of dark color, and it is possible to insert that into all of it, then evacuate the malady and insert that without fear, and cure the location with what exists and constrains until it is healed.
Capitol .xxvi.	Chapter XXVI.
De sutura del nas e de las labias e de la aurelha quan la continuitat es dissolvuda per plagua o per semblantz.	On the Suture of the Nose, Lips, and Ears when Continuity is Dissolved by Wound or Similarness.
Sapias que quan accideys solucio de continuitat en una de aquestas cartillages, pauc confereys en aquela operacio sino en alcus homes.	Know that when dissolution of continuity occurs in one of these cartilages, few confer on that operation except among certain men.
Donc cove, quan endeve ad alcu alcuna causa de aquelas, que consideres si es plagua fresca am le sieu sanc, e lahoras tu ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am sutura, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	Therefore, when you need to treat some cause of those, you must consider whether it is fresh wound with its own blood, and then adjust the two lips of the wound with suture, and immediately cure that until it is healed.
E si las labias de solucio de continuitat so ja separadas, e quascuna es fayta sana, lahoras cove que tu excorjes quascuna partida de la sua codena apparent entro que n’iesca sanc.	And if the lips of dissolution of continuity are already separated, and each is made whole, then you must excise each part of its own codeen that appears until blood comes out.
E aprop ajusta las doas labias am sutura e strenh aquelas, e sobre aquelas pulveriza sanc de drago e enses trissat, e pausa sobre la polvera una pessa de emplaustra diafinicon, o de alcu autre dels emplastres consolidatius, e leyssa aquel liat per dos jorns o per tres, e aprop deslia aquel e permuta aquel emplaustre e leyssa aquel entro que·ls fiels per si sian abscinditz, e aprop cura am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And immediately adjust the two lips with suture and strengthen those, and on top of those sprinkle blood of dragon and well-trimmed fat, and pause over the powder one piece of emplastrum diaphanic or some other consolidative plaster, and leave that tied for two days or three, and then release that and change that plaster and leave it until the wounds are completely removed, and immediately cure with a scab until it is healed.
Mays la manieyra de la sutura es que tu agregues la solucio de continuitat o am agulhas ayssi cum havem recomtat en la sutura del ventre, o agregua la solucio de continuitat am fiel ayssi cum a tu e fayt saber.	But the method of suture is that you add the solution of continuity or with needles as we have recounted in the suture of the abdomen, or add the solution of continuity with needle and thread as I make it known.
Capitol .xxvii.	Chapter XXVII.
De extraccio de aquela causas que veno en las doas labias en las partidas dedintz.	On the Extraction of those Causes that come in the Two Lips in the Parts Behind.
Motas veguadas endeve a motz homes en las partidas dedintz de las suas labias alcus apostemas durs semblantz a gras de errs, e alscunas de lors son mendres e alcunas son majors.	Many times it happens that certain men in the Parts Behind of their Lips have some hard and stubborn apostemas resembling errors, and some are smaller and others are larger.
Donc cove que tu convertas las labias e fendas quascuna de aquelas duricias de tota part, e aprop la abscizio umpliscas le loc de sagi trissat entro que·l sanc sia restrengut, e aprop sia lavat am vi agre e sia curat le loc am aquo que es stipticitat, entro que sia sanat.	Therefore you must convert the lips and fissures each of those hardnesses of all parts, and immediately fill the location with sagacious fat until the blood is restrained, and then be washed with vinegar and be cured the location with what exists and is stiptic, until it is healed.
Capitol .xxviii.	Chapter XXVIII.
De inscizio de la carn ajustada en las gengivas.	On the Insertion of Adjusted Flesh into the Gums.
Granre de veguadas nays sobre la gengiva carn ajustada la qual les antics apelero albulus, adonc cove que tu suspendas aquela am onci o que tenguas aquela am las forfecs e inscidas aquela deves la sua razit, e leyssas la sania correr o le sanc.	Great many times they have said over the gum adjusted flesh which the ancients called albulus, therefore you must suspend that with a needle or that you take that with forceps and insert it as it should be, and let the blood flow or run.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc sagi trissat o autra polveras stipticas o excicativas.	And immediately pause over the location with sagacious fat or other powders that are stiptic or excitant.
E si aquela carn retorna, lahoras inscideys aquela segundariament, e cauterisa aquela, quar aprop le cauteri no retornara.	And if the flesh returns, then immediately reinsert it secondarily, and cauterize it, for immediately after cauterization it will not return.
Capitol .xxix.	Chapter XXIX.
De razo de dentz am ferr.	On the Reason of Teeth with Iron.
Quan en la superficia de las dentz de las partidas dedintz e de las de foro e entre las gingivas so ajustadas escorsas aspras, legas, e alcunas veguadas son de nigradas e son faytas citrinas o vertz entro que a la gingiva ve per aquo corrupcio e son faytas las dentz legas.	When on the surface of the teeth of the parts behind and those of the front and between the gums, there are adjusted rough, sharp, and some blackened, and some yellowed or greenish, so that the gum is corrupted by it, and the teeth become loosened.
E donc cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute entre las tuas mas e pausar le cap de lu en le tieu se, e ratz las dents en las quals apareysso aquelas escorsas e causas semblantz arena entro que de lor no romangua deguna causa, e aquo fay de la negror e de la citrinitat e de las autras entro que sian mondificadas.	And therefore you must make the malady cease between your hands and pause the head of it in its own place, and ratify the teeth on which those roughnesses and causes similar to sand appear, until there is no longer any cause remaining, and do this with the blackness and yellowness and other things so that they are purified.
Donc si es ostat aquo que es en aquelas del comensament de la razio, bo es; e sino, lahoras tu itera la razio sobre aquelas al autra dia e al segon e al tertz entro que vengua al derier stament en aquo que tu vols.	Therefore, if this is the beginning of the reason, good is; and if not, then you must iterate the reason on those for another day and second and third until it reaches the final statement in what you desire.
E sapias que las dentz han necessitat de motz rezoris de diversas formas e de motas figuras segon que es preparat a la tua operacio.	And know that teeth have needed many remedies of diverse forms and figures according to how it is prepared for your operation.
E per so quar le razori am le qual la dent es raza de la partida dedintz es autre del razori am le qual es ras entre las dentz segon autras formas, e aquestas formas de razoris sian deves tu preparadas las quals veyras tantost:	And therefore, because the remedies with which the tooth is rased from the part behind are different from those with which it is rasped between teeth according to other forms, and these forms of remedies must be prepared by you which you will see at once:
Capitol .xxx.	Chapter XXX.
D’eradicacio de dentz.	On the Extraction of Teeth.
Cove que tu cures la dent de la sua dolor am tot engen e tardes en tota eradicacio de lu, quar no es denguna causa que suplisqua la veguada de lu quan es eradicada, quar es sustancia sublima entro que es excusacio en la eradicacio de lu.	Therefore you must cure the tooth of its pain with all care and attention in every extraction of it, because there is no cause that surpasses the frequency of its occurrence when it is extracted, for it is a subtle substance entering into excuse in the extraction of it.
Mays cove quan le malaute es forsat aquela dent eradicar, que fermament deves tu sia certificat quala es la dent dolent, quar motas veguadas la dolor descep le malaute e cuga que sia en dent sana, e tu eradicas aquela e aprop la dolor no cessa entro que la dent malauta e dolent sia eradicada, quar nos ja havem vist aquo per operacio dels barbies.	But when the malady is firmly seated in that tooth to be extracted, then you must be certain that it is a painful tooth, because many times the pain deceives the malady and claims to be in a healthy tooth, and you extract that one and immediately the pain does not cease until the sick and painful tooth is extracted, for we have already seen this through the operation of barbers.
Donc cum deves tu es sertificat qual es la dent dolent, e que o sabes be, lahoras cove que tu scarifiques en le circuit de la dent am spatum en le qual sia alcuna vertut, entro que sia dissolvut de la dent de la gingiva de tota partida, e aprop mau aquel am les tieus ditz, o am forfexs subtils al comensament petit a petit entro que aquela concucesquas.	Therefore, since you must be certain which is the painful tooth, and when you know well, then it is necessary that you scarify in the circuit of the tooth with spatula in the place where there is some virtue, so that it dissolves from the tooth to the gum of all parts, and then immediately remove it with those said ditz, or with fine forceps little by little until it is extracted.
E aprop alogua en lu fortz tenalhas grans per bona loquacio o estuptura fort, e pausa le cap del malaute entre les tieus denolhs que be le tengues que no·s maugua, e aprop tratz la dent segon rectitut en manieyra que no trenques aquela, ni al malaute major dolor no dones.	And immediately grasp in it with great forceps for good speaking or strong extraction, and pause the head of the malady between those said ditz that hold you not to be mauled, and then extract the tooth according to rectitude in a manner that does not break it, nor give greater pain to the malady.
E donc si no es foro-getat, lahoras pren un de aquels instrumentz, e met aquel dejos lu de tota part am facilitat e esforsa la remocio de lu ayssi que es feyt al comensament.	And therefore, if it is not forgotten, then take one of those instruments and place it deep into the tooth from all parts with facility and effort the removal of it as was done at the beginning.
Mays si la dent es trauquada o corrosa, lahoras cove que tu comples de drap aquel trauc e estrenguas aquel am la extremitat de ray subtil per so que no sia trinquada en la hora de la tua constriccio sobre aquela am tenalas.	But if the tooth is bruised or corroded, then it is necessary that you wrap with cloth that bruise and strengthen it with a thin thread at the extremity of a subtle ray so that it is not torn in the hour of your constriction upon it when you take hold.
E cove que tu obres exquesitament am scarificacio en le circuit de tota part de la gingiva e guarda mot la tua fortaleza que no trenques aquela e romangua partida de lu, e retorne sobre le malaute per la malicia que sia majo que la primieyra dolor de lu.	And it is necessary that you work with great exactness with scarification in the circuit of all parts of the gum and guard your strength so that you do not break it and leave a part of it, and return to the malady for the maliciousness which is greater than the first pain of it.
E guarda te que no fassas aquo que fan alscus ignorantz barbiers en lor fistinacio e audacia sobre la eradicacio de lor, ses que no aministran aquo que nos havem recomtat; quar motas veguadas fan venir sobre les homes malautias grans las quals son pus dificils que sian trinquadas, e las razitz de lor remaugudas totas, o alcunas de aquelas, o que extrayguas aquela am alcus osses de la mandigula ayssi cum motas veguadas havem testificat.	And beware that you do not do as some ignorant barbers do in their recklessness and audacity in the extraction of their teeth, without administering what we have recommended; for many times they bring upon men great illnesses which are more difficult to be torn out, and the roots of their remaugudas all or some of those, or that you extract it with some bones from the jawbone just as many times we have testified.
E aprop la eradicacio de lu sia lavada la boca am vi caut o vi agre am sal.	And immediately after extraction, wash the mouth with vinegar or lemon juice and salt.
E si endeve fluxs de sanc per aysso, ayssi cum motas veguadas endeve, lahoras trissa alcuna quantitat de zegi e aspergeys sobre la plagua, e si no confereys aquel zegi, cauteriza.	And if there is bleeding after this, just like many times there has been, then immediately sprinkle some quantity of rose water and apply it to the wound, and if that rose water does not concur, cauterize.
La forma de las forceps e tenalas subtils am las quals es mauguda la dent al comensament sia de longua extramitat, de breu manubre e gros, per so que no sian doblatz quan am aquels deves obrar.	The form of the forceps and fine tongs with which the tooth is mauled at the beginning should be one of long extremity, short handle and thick, so that they are not doubled when you must work with them.
E sian ayssi cum vezes de gros manubre entro que quan estrenhas am aquelas no sian dobladas, sian breus extramitatz.	And should be like times of thick handle so that when you strain with those, they are not doubled, having short extremities.
E sian faytas de ferr de India descentment faytas de dreytas extramitatz, e en las extramitatz de aquelas sian dentz de las quals las unas intron en las autras e estrenhan per constriccio descent fort, e alscunas veguadas las extramitatz de aquelas sian la forma del bec d’un auzel le qual ha nom ciconia, so es guanta, e son de fort constriccio.	And should be made of Indian iron with descending shapes and right angles, and in the extremities of those, there are teeth which fit into each other and strain by construction descent strong, and some times the extremities of those are in the shape of a bird's beak called ciconia, so it is guarded, and they are of strong constriction.
Capitol .xxxi.	Chapter XXXI.
De erradicacio de dentz e d‘estraccio dels osses de las mandibulas trincadas.	On the Extraction of Teeth and Dislocation of the Bones of the Mandibles Broken.
Quan deves la eradicacio de dent le qual es trinquat roman alcuna causa, lahoras cove que tu pauses sobre le loc coto am boder per un jorn o per dos entro que·l loc sia mollificat; e aprop entromet algesti o tenalhas las extramitatz de las quals so asembladas al bec de un auzel apelat ciconia o guanta, la forma de las forceps:	When you must extract the tooth which is broken due to some cause, then it is necessary that you pause over the location with border for one day or two until the location is mollified; and immediately introduce algid or tongs into the extremities of those which are assembled at the beak of a bird called ciconia or guard, the shape of the forceps:
Las extramitatz de lor sian faytas dedintz ayssi cum lima o alfagi.	The extremities of them are made behind like a file or alfalfa.
E si no obediys a tu a eyssiment am aquestas forceps o tenalas, lahoras cove que tu caves sobre la razit e descrobas tota la carn e entrometas le instrument le qual ha nom atali, so es palanca petita del qual la forma es aquesta:	And if you do not obey your eye to these forceps or tongs, then it is necessary that you dig into the root and uncover all the flesh and introduce the instrument which has the name of atali, so it is a small lever whose form is this:
E sia de breu extremitat grossa un petit, e no sia enbegut per so que no sia trinquat.	And be short with a large extremity and a little one, and not entangled, so that it is not broken.
Donc si per aquo la razit es foro-getada, bo es; e sino, ajuda te am aquestz autres instrument dels quals aquestas son las formas: la forma del primier instrument es de triangulada extramitat en la qual sia alcuna grossesa:	Therefore, if by this the root is forgotten, good is; and otherwise, help yourself with these other instruments of which these are the forms: the form of the first instrument is a triangular extremity in which there is some thickness:
La forma del segon instrument es que sia de triangulada e de pus subtil extremitat.	The form of the second instrument is that it be triangular and with a more subtle extremity.
E ja so ajudatz am aquest instrument havent dos ramps del qual aquesta es la forma aprop la seguent:	And already help yourself with this instrument having two prongs of which this is the form approaching the next:
e am autres instrumentz les quals precidero en rasura de dentz; quar juvament es fayt am aquest instrument le qual es asemblat a onci gran, e aquesta es la forma:	and with other instruments which precede in scraping of teeth; for already it is made with this instrument which is similar to once great, and this is the form:
de la triangulada extremitat torta o curta, la qual sia alcuna grossesa, e no sia enbegut per so que no sia trinquat.	of a triangular extremity bent or short, which has some thickness, and not entangled, so that it is not broken.
E otra sapias que·ls instrumentz de las dentz motz so e semblantment les autres instruments.	And also know that the instruments of teeth many are so and similar to other instruments.
Mays le artifexs savi e subtil en l’art, atroba per si mateys segon aquo que a lu significa la operacio e las malautias diversas; quar son de las malautias a las quals les antics no diysero ni pausero propri instrument, per las formas de diversas specias.	But the skilled and subtle artisans in the art find for themselves by trial and error according to what each operation and diverse illnesses mean; for they are of illnesses to which the ancients did not say nor pause with proper instruments, due to the forms of various species.
Mays si es trinquat l’os de la mandibula o dels autres osses de la boca, o si poyreys, lahoras sia pes curat sobre aquel en son loc am aquo que es a lu convenient dels instrumentz e de las forceps las quals havem dit en la extraccio de las razitz de las dentz, e ajuda te am gesti del qual aquesta es la forma:	But if the bone of the mandible or of other bones in the mouth is broken, or if it becomes disjointed, then immediately apply gentle pressure on that place where it is convenient for instruments and forceps which we have mentioned in the extraction of tooth roots, and help yourself with gestures such as this form:
E sia en lu alcuna grosseza petit a petit, e sia instringida o tenguda am la boca per que no evasesca o fuga entro que l’os de tot sia foro-getat; e aprop restaura le loc am medicinas convenientz ad aquo.	And be in that place some thickness gradually, and be strung or held with the mouth so that it does not escape or flee until the bone of all is forgotten; and then restore the place with medicines suitable for this.
Mays si en l’os es petita poyredura, lahoras ratz aquel de aquela poyredura e de la sua negror, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	But if in the bone there is a small fracture, then immediately break that into pieces and cure it with its blackness, and heal that until it is well.
Capitol .xxxii.	Chapter XXXII.
De la cura de las dentz eminentz sobre las autras.	On the Cure of Teeth Elevated above Others.
Quan las dentz so eminentz no segon lor cors natural per aquelas la forma es laga, e majorment quan endeve a las femnas, e majorment a las piuselas venerablas; donc cove que tu consideras: si dent es nada aprop autra dent, e no es possibla sarradura ni linament de lu, lahoras radica aquela; mays que no sia annexa am autra dent, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am aquest instrument del qual aquesta es la forma; e es semblant a morr de porc, e sia feyt de ferr de India de extramitat mot aguda.	When the teeth are elevated and not according to their natural form, and more so when they involve women, and most especially venerable girls; therefore it is necessary that you consider: if a tooth is very close to another tooth, and there is no possibility of suture or ligament of it, then immediately remove that one; but if it is attached to another tooth, then you must insert it with this instrument which has the form of a pig's jawbone, made of Indian iron with an extremely sharp extremity.
E sia la tua inscizio am la qual inscideyses aquela en trops dias per la duricia de la dent, e que no sia comauguda autra de las dentz.	And be your insertion with which you insert it in many days due to the hardness of the tooth, and that it is not like another tooth.
E si es dent eminent expausat a limadura, lahoras lima aquel am lima de ferr de India del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if the elevated tooth is exposed to erosion, then immediately file it with a file made of Indian iron which has this form:
E sia tot de ferr de India e·l margua eysament; e sia de motz menutz puntz ayssi cum lima am la qual son faytas agulhas, am la qual la dent sia limada pauc a pauc en motz dias am fecilitat, per so que no sia autra dent comauguda e caga.	And be all of Indian iron and its margin well-shaped; and be with many small points like a file which is made of hairpins, by which the tooth is filed little by little in many days with ease, so that it is not another tooth deformed and spoiled.
E aprop lineys aquela en la fi, e ratz aquela am alscus razoris.	And then line it up at the end, and break it off with some rasors.
E si es dent del qual una partida es trinquada e lideys la lengua, lahoras cove que tu limescas aquel entro que l’aspretat de aquela fraccio sia ostada e engualhada, e sia aplenada per so que la lengua no ledesca ni la paraula no corrumpa.	And if a tooth is broken and the tongue lies on it, then it is necessary that you file it down until the sharpness of that fracture is removed and smoothed, and filled in so that the tongue does not lie on it nor corrupt the word.
Capitol .xxxiii.	Chapter XXXIII.
De restauracio de dentz maugudas am fiel de aur o de argent.	On the Restoration of Deformed Teeth with Gold or Silver Wire.
Quan accideys a las dentz devant concussio e remossio per percussio o per cazament, e le malaute no pot strenher sobre aquo que manga, e tu has curat aquel am medicinas stipticas, e no ha valgut la tua curacio, lahoras per so que no cagan es engen en aquelas que sian strengudas am fiel de aur e no de argent, quar argent se fa vert e aprop se poyreys aprop alscus dias, mays aur nul temps no es mudat.	When accidents happen to teeth before concussion and removal by percussion or falling, and the malady cannot be strengthened over that which remains, and you have treated it with stiptic medicines, and your treatment has not been effective, then because they do not decay immediately, it is necessary to strengthen them with a gold wire and not silver, for silver becomes green and soon becomes loose, but gold never changes.
E sia le fiel en tal subtilitat e grocesa segon la quantitat que puesca entrar entre las dentz; e la forma de la reccio es que prenguas le fiel e pren lo doble de lu entre doas dentz sanas, e aprop que cresques am doas tortuositatz del fiel entre doas maugudas, o si’ una o motas, entro que pervengua la tela a la dent sana del autra partida.	And the wire is in such subtlety and thickness according to the quantity that can enter between the teeth; and the form of the recitation is that you take the wire and take double its length between two healthy teeth, and then increase it with two turns of the wire between two deformed ones, or if only one or many, until the thread reaches the healthy tooth on the other side.
E aprop itera le teyssiment entro a la partida de la qual comenciest, e strenh la tua ma am facilitat e savieza entro que no sia mauguda.	And then repeat the treatment until you reach the part where you began, and strengthen your hand with ease and wisdom until it is not deformed.
E sia la tua striccio am la qual strenhas le fiel deves las razitz de las dentz que no evasesca.	And be your traction by which you tighten the wire on the roots of the teeth that do not decay.
E aprop inscindeys las extramitatz del fiel superfluens am las forceps o tosoyras, e agregua aquelas en quascun loc am gesti, e converteys aquelas e las occulta entre la dent sana e la dent mauguda, per so que no fassa lesio a la lengua.	And then insert the superfluous extremities of the wire with forceps or tweezers, and add them to each place with gestures, and convert them and conceal them between the healthy tooth and the deformed one, so that it does not cause injury to the tongue.
E aprop leyssa aquela ayssi streyta cum roman.	And then loosen it just as stretched tight.
Mays si es desliada o rumpuda, strenh aquela o aquelas am autra fiel en tal manieyra en tot son temps.	But if it is loosened or broken, strengthen that one or those with another wire in such a manner for all its time.
E aquesta es la forma de las dentz e la figura de la rectacio de doas dentz sanas e de doas maugudas, ayssi cum vezes aquestas liadas:	And this is the form of teeth and the figure of the recitation of two healthy teeth and two deformed ones, just as these linked:
E quan se fa que retorno una dent o doas aprop le cazement de quascuna en lors locs, e sian recrescutz ayssi cum havem recomtat, e que remauguan.	And when one returns or two nearby the falling of each in its place, and are reborn just as we have recounted, and remain.
E no fa aquo sino bo artifexs e savi.	And only skilled artisans can do this.
E alcunas veguadas es aptat alcuna causa dels osses de vaca, e es fayt de lor ayssi cum forma de dent, e es pausada en loc en le qual defayl la dent, e es strengit ayssi cum havem dit, e reman e serveys am aquel per lonc temps.	And sometimes it is suitable for some cause of cow bones, and is made from them in the form of a tooth, and is placed in a location where the tooth falls out, and is strengthened just as we have said, and remains and serves that one for a long time.
Capitol .xxxiv.	Chapter XXXIV.
De inscizio del liament le qual ve en la lengua e prohibeys loquela.	On the Insertion of the Ligament Which is in the Tongue and Prohibits Speech.
Aquest liguament le qual ve dejos la lengua alcunas veguadas o es natural am le qual hom nays, o accidental e accideys per plagua la qual ja es consolidada.	This ligament which is left behind the tongue sometimes or is natural to it and which one has not, or accidental and occurs by injury that is already consolidated.
E la operacio en lu es que huobres la boca del malaute, le sieu cap existent en le tieu se; e eleva la sieua lengua, e aprop inscideys aquel liament nervos segon la latitut entro que sia solvuda la lengua de la sua recencio.	And the operation in it is that you open the mouth of the malady, its own head being situated in your tongue; and raise your tongue, and then insert that nervous ligament according to the latitude until the tongue is freed from its recency.
Mays si en aquela es alcuna duricia o denodacio, e aquo es stat per consolidacio de plagua, lahoras tu gieta unci e scindeys aquel per la latitut entro que aias inscindit le liament e sia dissolvuda la nodacio.	But if in that there is some hardness or nodulation, and this is fixed by the consolidation of injury, then you must gently loosen it and cut through with latitude until you have dissected the ligament and dissolved the nodulation.
E guarda te que no sia fayta fissura en le preon de la carn e que scindas aqui arceria e vengua flux de sanc.	And beware that there is not a fissure made in the forehead of the flesh, and that you do not cut here archery and bring forth a flow of blood.
E aprop sia lavat le vestigi de la inscisio am ayguaros o am vi agre o am aygua frega; e aprop pausa dejos la lengua licini; so es meca la qual tengua le malaute dejos la lengua en quascuna nuoyt per so que no sia consolidat autra veguada.	And then be washed the vestige of the incision with warm water or vinegar, or with lukewarm water; and then pause for a moment after the tongue is freed; thus is the manner which holds the malady from the tongue in every night so that it will not consolidate again.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc, pausa sobre le loc vetriol trissat; mays si le sanc ventz, lahoras cauteriza le loc am cauteri lantiginos le qual conveneys ad aquo.	But if there is a flow of blood, pause over the location with a poultice made from vinegar; but if the blood flows, then immediately cauterize the location with a caustic lint which corresponds to this.
E aprop aquel cura am las autras causas entro que sia sanat.	And then treat that one with the other causes until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxv.	Chapter XXXV.
De extraccio de ranula dejos la lengua.	On the Extraction of Ranula Left Behind the Tongue.
Alcunas veguadas accideys dejos la lengua apostema asemblant a nomla petita prohibent la lengua de la sua operacio natural; e fort leu es magnificada entro que huempla la boca.	Sometimes a swelling appears behind the tongue, resembling a small tumor that prevents the tongue from performing its natural operation; and very little is magnified until it fills up the mouth.
E la operacio en lu es que huebras la boca del malaute sesent devant le solel e considera le apostema.	And the operation in it is that you open the mouth of the malady, sitting in front of the sun and considering the swelling.
E si tu le vezes de fusca color o de negra, dur, al qual le malaute no atroba sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel quar es cranc.	And if it is a dark or black, hard lump that the malady does not sense, then do not touch it because it is cancerous.
E si es declinat a blancor, en le qual es humiditat, lahoras tu met le onci en lu, e inscideys aquel am spatum subtil, e inscindeys le de tota partida; e si sanc te ventz en la hora de la tua operacio, lahoras tu pausa desus zegi trissat, so es vetriol, entro que sia restreyt le sanc.	And if it is declined to whiteness, in which there is moisture, then you must put the once into it, and insert that with a subtle spatula, and dissect all around; and if blood flows on the hour of your operation, then pause for a moment above a poultice made from vinegar, so that the blood may be restrained.
