E aprop retorna a la obra tua entro que lo haias trayt am compliment de lu, entro que sia lavat am vi agre e sal; e cura aquel am l’autra curacio ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And then return to your work until you have treated it in its entirety, so that it is washed with vinegar and salt; and cure that one with the other cure corresponding to this, until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxvi.	Chapter XXXVI.
De extraccio de apostema de doas aurelhas e de aquel que es nada en le golayro e de las autras apostemas.	On the Extraction of Swellings from Two Ears and that which is nothing in the Groin and other Swellings.
Quan endeveno en le golayro godat, so son glandulas las quals son asembladas algodat, las quals accideysso deforas e son nompnadas doas aurelhas, las quals quan tu las curas am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no es sanat, lahoras tu considera si le apostema es dur, de fusca color, de pauc sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel am ferr.	When there is a swelling in the groin, so are the glands which are assembled together, which swell up and are named two ears, which when you treat them with what we have said in the division and they do not heal, then you must consider whether the swelling is hard, of dark color, and of little sensation, then do not touch it with iron.
E si es de roga color e la razic es grossa, lahoras no toques aquela am ferr per le flux del sanc; abantz layssa aquel entro sia madurat, e lahoras o tu trauqueras aquel, o sira romput per si.	And if it is of red color and the root is thick, then do not touch it with iron for the flow of blood; before let that one ripen, and then either you will break it or it will burst on its own.
E si es de blanqua color, radon, e la razit de lu es subtil, lahoras aquel es que cove esser inscidit.	And if it is of white color, rounded, and the root of it is subtle, then that one must be dissected.
E la operacio en lu es que consideras, denant la tua operacio, si ja ha repausat le apostema de lu caut am repaus complit o si es deminuit am alcuna deminucio; e lahoras fay sezer le malaute denant le soleyl, e·l cap de lu sia en le tieu se, e huebre la boca de lu, e le servidor prenent entre las suas mas prema la lengua de lu dejos am instrument mot noble del qual aquesta es la forma:	And the operation in it is that you consider, before your operation, if the swelling of it has rested or not, and whether it has rested completely or diminished by some diminution; and then make the patient sit down before the sun, with his head in its own place, and open his mouth, and the servant takes between his hands the tongue of it, left behind an instrument very noble which is as follows:
E sia fayt de argent o de aram, e sia subtil cum cotel.	And be made of silver or iron, and be subtle like a knife.
Donc cum tu premes am aquel la lengua e es mostrat a tu la apostema, e catz sobre aquel le tieu vezement, lahoras pren onci e fica aquel en l’amenla, e tira aquel a las partidas defora tant quant podes.	Therefore, when you take the tongue and it is shown to you the swelling, and gaze upon that with your own eyesight, then take the once and place that in the amnion, and pull that out as far as you can.
Otra aquo que tiras alcuna causa de las tunicas, e aprop incideys aquela am instrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	Or else, another cause that pulls some of the tunics, and then insert it with an instrument which has this form:
e es asemblat a forceps, empero las extramitatz de lu son corvadas, ayssi que l’orrifici de quascuna de aquelas es en le endreyt del autra, mot agudas, le qual sia de ferr indi enbegut.	and is assembled like forceps, but the extremities of it are curved, so that the orifice of each one is in the end of the other, very sharp, made of Indian iron well-enough.
Mays si aquest instrument no es a tu present, lahoras inscideys aquel am spatum del qual aquesta es la forma de lu: E sia agut de la una part, no agut del autra part.	But if this instrument is not at your disposal, then insert it with a spatula which has this form of it: And be sharp on one side, not sharp on the other side.
E pus que has inscidit una mella, inscideys l’autra segon aquesta meteyssa manieyra de inscizio, e aprop la inscizio le malaute guarguarise de aygua frega	And after you have dissected one notch, then insert the other in the same manner of insertion, and immediately apply the insertion to the malady with lukewarm water.
Mays si endeve flux de sanc, guarguarise aygua de decoccio de scorsa de milgrana o de fuelha de mirtra e semblantz ad aquel de las causas stiptiquas entro que·l flux del sanc sia restreyt, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	But if there is bleeding, apply lukewarm water of decoction of scorzonera or myrtle leaves and similar to that of the stiptic causes until the flow of blood is restrained, and then cure that one until it is healed.
E alcunas veguadas naysso en le guolayro autras apostemas otra aquelas doas aurelhas, e inscideys aquelas segon que yeu e dit en la inscizio de doas mellas engualment.	And sometimes you find other swellings in the groin besides those two ears, and dissect those according to what I have said in the dissection of two notches with a spatula.
E yeu ja fu medicat una femna de apostema le qual era nat en le golayro de lu, le qual apostema tendia a color fusca, de pauc sentiment, le qual ja havia claus le golayro de lu, e la femna respirava am meat streyt, e ja havia prohibit a lu comestio e beure de aygua, e ja era pervenguda a la mort si mays agues stat per un dia o per dos.	And you have already treated a woman who had a swelling in her groin which was turning black, of little sensation, which had closed up the groin of hers, and the woman was breathing with great difficulty, and had already prohibited herself from eating and drinking water, and was on the point of death if you had not acted within a day or two.
E l’apostema ja tant havia pugat que havia mezes dos ramps entro que eyssiro per dos traucs.	And the swelling had grown so much that it had opened up two holes, through which pus was flowing through two channels.
Donc yeu me cuytegui fisturalment e fiquegui en un de lor onci, e tiregui aquel, e atirada es de lu gran porcio, e aprop yeu incidigui aquela de on comprendegui del autre trau, e aprop yeu obrigui la boca de lu, e compremegui la sua lengua, e aprop yeu fiquegui le onci en aquela apostema.	Therefore you must proceed fisturally and get stuck in one of them once, and pull that out, and as it comes forth with a great piece, and then you insert the other once into the understanding of the other channel, and then you force the mouth open, and grasp its tongue, and then you place the once in that swelling.
E aprop yeu abscizi gran partida de lu, e no corria de lu sino un pauc de sanc.	And immediately you cut off a great part of it, and there was only a little blood flowing from it.
Donc absolut es le guolayro de aquela femna, e comensec tantost beure aygua, e aprop presec vianda, donc yeu no cessegui inscidir de aquela apostema motas vetz per lonc temps, e succesia apostema en loc de aquel, le qual inscizia entro que es prolonguat aquel.	Therefore the groin of that woman was completely healed, and she began to drink water immediately, and then you prescribed food for her, so that you did not cease to dissect that swelling many times over a long period, and successive swellings occurred in the same place, which were dissected until it was prolonged.
Donc yeu engen agui e cauterizegui le guolayro de lu, donc astec de addicio; e aprop yeu perambulegui e no saubi que fec Dieus de aquela aprop mi.	Therefore I generated this and caused the groin of her to be cauterized, thus adding a new element; and then I walked away and did not know what God had done for that one with me.
Capitol .xxxvii.	Chapter XXXVII.
De inscizio de huvela quan es apostemada.	On the Dissection of an Uterus when it is Swollen.
Quan catarr deysen a la huvula, e es apostemada e es longa, lahoras ela es nompnada perpendicular; e si es en la partida dejos grossa e redonda, e lahoras ela es apelada buba.	When the catarrh settles in the uterus, and it is swollen and long, then it is called perpendicular; and if it is on the left side big and round, then it is called a bubble.
Mays quan es curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio, e no comfereys la tua curacio, e eyssament ja vezes que apostema caut ja es ostat de lu e es subtil, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquela que es agreguadas redonda; e si es ad aquela longitut, e es sanguina, de fusca color o de negre, e no es a lu centiment, lahoras cove que tu temtes la inscizio de lu, quar en aquela es temor sobre le malaute.	But when it is cured with what we have said in the division, and your cure does not agree, and if only sometimes that swelling again becomes a lump of it and is subtle, then you must dissect those which are aggregated round; and if it is as long as that, and it is sanguine, of dark color or black, and has no sensation, then you must tremble at the dissection of it, for in that there is fear over the patient.
E quan tu vezes aquela segon la manieyra que yeu he dita de la sua blancor e longuesa, que tu fassas sezer le malaute e premas la lengua de lu am instrument del qual procesic la sua forma e aprop fica le onci en la nuva, e tira aquela en jos e inscideys aquela am un de dos instrumentz les quals e ditz en la inscizio de dos mellas.	And when you take that one according to the manner which I have said of its whiteness and length, so that you make the patient sit down and press the tongue with an instrument whose form is as follows: and immediately place the once in the newness, and pull that down and dissect it with one of two instruments which are said in the dissection of two notches.
E cove que no inscidas aquela sino aquo que es ajustat sobre le terme natural ses addicio, quar si tu inscides de lu mays, lediyras le sieu parlar.	And you must not dissect that one unless it is adjusted to the natural term with an addition, for if you dissect more than that, you will deprive yourself of your own speech.
E aprop la inscizio, usa de aquo le qual havem recomtat en la inscizio de dos mellas, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And then the dissection, use what we have recommended in the dissection of two notches, and cure that one until it is healed.
Mays si era le malaute espaventat per la inscizio de lu, cove que use de engen en la cauterizacio de lu ses temor, e la manieyra del cauteri en lu no es sino am aygua aguda, e es que tu pauses le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop prem la lengua de lu am le instrument le qual havem dit, e aprop pren de l’aygua la qual havem dita en le capitol de cauterizacio, e comfeys am aquela caus viva, e pausa aquela no spessa ni subtil, e de aquela omple la concavitat de l’estrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	But if the patient is frightened by the dissection of it, then you must use cunning in the cauterization of it without fear, and the manner of the cauterizer in it is not but with sharp water, and it is that you pause the head of the patient in its own place, and immediately press the tongue of it with the instrument which we have said, and immediately take from the water which we have said in the chapter on cauterization, and confirm with it a living cause, and pause it not dense nor subtle, and fill the concavity of the instrument which has this form:
Sia la extramitat de lu conquavitat en la qual sia pausada la medicina ayssi cum la conquavitat de culher de ray, e pausa le strument am la medicina sobre la vula, e·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu latz per so que corro saliva o musellage de la boca de aquel per la intrinscequa medicina, per so que no deyssenda de aquela deguna causa sobre le golayro de lu e que ledesca aquel.	So that the extremity of it is in the concavity where the medicine is paused just as the concavity of a spoon is, and pause the instrument with the medicine over the vulva, and the patient will stretch out his hand over his own lap for so that the saliva or mastication of the mouth of that one will come forth by the intrinsic medicine, in order that it may not descend from any cause upon the groin of it and corrupt that.
E aprop te la tua ma am la medicina, e exprem aquela sobre la uvula per l’espazi de miega hora entro que vegas aquela esser denegrada e sedada per la mordicacio de la medicina.	And then take your hand and the medicine, and press that upon the uvula for the space of a quarter hour until you see it to be darkened and sedated by the biting of the medicine.
E si vols, prengues coto e envolopes aquel sobre la extremitat del ray, e submergeys le coto en la medicina, e entrometas le ray am le coto en una canula de sobre entro que·l coto adheresca en aquela canula, e fay aquo tantas vetz entro que consiegues aquo que vols de la cauterizacio de la uva, e aprop leyssa aquela quar ela se seccara e cayra aprop tres dias o quatre.	And if you wish, take a cloth and wrap that around the extremity of the ray, and submerge the cloth in the medicine, and insert the ray with the cloth into a tube on top so that the cloth adheres to that tube, and do this many times until you achieve what you want from the cauterization of the uvula, and then release it when it becomes dry and falls away three or four days later.
E si indigeysses que iteras la medicina, itera aquela, e aprop la cauterizacio abstergeys en le circuit de la uva am coto enbegut en boder, e mondifica am aquel aquo que es en le circuit de lu de la medicina, e sia lavat am aygua frega, e sia curat deforo am embrocacio, e dedintz am guarguarismes entro que sia sanat.	And if you need to repeat the medicine, repeat it, and then apply the cauterization abstergent in the circuit of the uvula with a cloth wrapped around it, and clarify with that what is in the circuit of it from the medicine, and be washed with lukewarm water, and be cured externally with embrocation, and internally with gargling until it is healed.
E aquesta especia de curacio es pus salva que inscizio e pus long de temor.	And this kind of cure is more saved than dissection and more free from fear.
Alcunas veguadas es curada la uvuola am aquo que es pus subtil que cauteri e inscizio, quar es curat am subfumigacio en aquesta manieyra: recipe calament, ysop, origua, ruda, scicados arabic, camamilla, broyda e semblant ad aquels de las erbas, e ajusta totas aquelas causas, o alcunas de lor, en una ola, e sian submergidas am vi agre, e bulhan; e la ola sia be lutada am lut decentment, e sia en le mieg loc de la ola un trauc, sobre le qual sia pausat un instrument conquau de aram segon aquesta manieyra; sia fayt de argent o de aram.	And sometimes the uvula is cured with something more subtle than cauterization and dissection, for it is cured by subfumigation in this manner: take calament, saffron, origanum, ruda, Arabic gum, camomile, and similar herbs to those, and combine all those causes or some of them into a pot, and let them be submerged in lukewarm water, and boil; and the pot is well stirred with decent stirring, and there is a hole in the middle of the pot, on which is placed an instrument made of iron or silver according to this manner.
E sia entromesa la extremitat en la boca del malaute entro que la vapor poge a la uvula sobre la quanula, entro que la uvula sia mot ofuscada.	And the extremity is inserted into the mouth of the patient until the vapor reaches the uvula on the tongue, until the uvula becomes very darkened.
E aprop itera sobre aquela motas veguadas entro qu’es secca, e guarda te que no fassas aquesta curacio al comesament de l’aveniment de apostemas, quar trop ajustaria en le apostema, e no cove que tu fassas aquo, sino deves la declaracio de apostema de lu caut.	And then repeat this many times until it is dry, and be careful not to do this cure at the beginning of the appearance of swellings, for too much would settle in the swelling, and you must not do that, but rather declare the swelling of it beforehand.
Mays si no es a tu present aquest instrument, lahoras pren una cana e compon en la extramitat de lu un clos de huou, per so que la boca del malaute sia comborida, quar le closc del huou prohibeys la vapor comburir la boca.	But if you don't have this instrument, then take a reed and shape it at the extremity of it into a stopper of wood, so that the mouth of the patient is blocked, for the stopper of wood prevents the vapor from burning the mouth.
E aquesta curacio es bona am salut.	And this cure is good for health.
Capitol .xxxviii.	Chapter XXXVIII.
De extraccio d’espinas e de aquo que adhereys en le golayro e de las autras causas.	On the Extraction of Thorns and that which adheres in the groin and other causes.
Motas veguadas adhereys en le guolayro o spina de peys o alcuna autra causa.	Many times it adheres in the groin or thorn of a pea or some other cause.
Adonc cove que tu extraguas aquo que de aquels es apparent, sobre le qual catz la vista, pus que tu premes la lengua am instrument denant solelh, per so que a tu sia declarat aquo que es en la guola.	Then it is necessary that you extract what appears from those things which are visible to the eye, for as you press the tongue with an instrument in front of the sun, so that it may be declared to you what is in the groin.
E aquo que no apar e es a tu occultat en le guolayro, cove que tu fassas vomir le malaute denant que la vianda sia degerida en l’estomac, quar fort leu la causa annexsa le golayro sira foro-getada per vomit; o que deglusia le malaute una pessa de nap o de razit de laytuga o un boci de pa sec; o prengua una pessa de sponga marina sequa leon, e lia aquela fortment am fiel, e aprop le malaute transglussia aquela, quar cum perve al loc en le qual so spinas e es extrahuda, lahoras so foro-getatz.	And what does not appear and is hidden in the groin, it is necessary that you make the patient vomit before food is digested in the stomach, because very soon the cause annexed to the groin will be forgotten by vomiting; or give the patient a piece of nap or root of lettuce or a small loaf of bread; or take a piece of marine sponge, and bind it tightly with twine, and then make the patient swallow it, so that when it reaches the place where the thorns are and is extracted, then they will be forgotten.
E mays pren una anguila e be am fiel liada, e sia dedintz mesa e soptament sia extrayta; o pren un porr e soptament le metas e soptament l’en tratz.	And then take an eel and bind it tightly with twine, and have it placed inside and slowly extracted; or take a basket and have it placed inside and slowly taken out.
Mays si no so foro-getatz am aquelas causas las quals havem ditas, lahoras husa de un instrument de plom segon aquesta forma:	But if they are not forgotten with those causes which we have said, then use an instrument of lead according to this form:
E sia pus gros que ray un petit, e en la extramitat de lu sia conquavitat la qual tu entrometas en la sua guola am facilitat.	And be more thick than a small reed, and in the extremity of it be a concavity which you insert into its groin with ease.
E el aga le sieu cap elevat en sus, e guarda te que·l tocament del sieu os de la gola, per so que endevengua a lu cos e am aquela que enpellesca le os o la spina, o que aquel le metge am la sua ma.	And it raises its head upwards and be careful that the touch of its bone in the throat, for so that it may discover the body and with that which enters into the bone or spine, or that it places itself in its own hand.
Mays empero que·l malaute aquel entrometa es miels, per la sua sciencia del loc de la causa annexa e enpellisca en jos, e tira la sua ma am le instrument en sus, tot aquo segon la quantitat la qual es a lu preparada entro que sia foro-getada.	But then the patient that inserts is honey, by its knowledge of the location of the annexed cause and enters in below, and pulls out its hand with the instrument on it, all according to the quantity which is prepared at it until it is forgotten.
Capitol .xxxix.	Chapter XXXIX.
De extraccio de sancguisugua annexsa al golayro.	On the Extraction of Blood-sucking Worms attached to the groin.
Quan es medicada sanguisugua am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la curacio am medicinas e no comfereys, considera lahoras en le guolayro del malaute al solelh, pus que tu aias compremuda la lengua de lu am instrument le qual a tu havem recomtat.	When the blood-sucking worm is medicated with what we have said in the division of cures with medicines and it does not agree, consider then in the groin of the patient to the sun, because you have grasped the tongue of it with an instrument which we have recommended.
Donc si tu vezes la sancguisugua, extratz aquela am onci petit o am gesti subtils decentment.	Therefore, if you find the blood-sucking worm, extract it with a small once or with subtle gestures decently.
E si no es a tu possible estrayre am aquel, lahoras pren una canula concava e entromet aquela en lo guolayro del malaute, e aprop pausa en la concavitat de la canula un ferr ignit, e fay aquo tantas vetz (entro que la sancguisugua sia morta e se osta del guolayro) e abstengua se le malaute tot lo jorn de aygua.	And if it is not possible to extract it, then take a concave tube and insert that into the groin of the patient, and then pause in the concavity of the tube an iron heated instrument, and do this many times (until the blood-sucking worm is dead and falls out of the groin) and abstain from giving water to the patient for all day.
E aprop prengua una veyria plena de aygua frega, e obra la boca de lu en aquela, e lava la boca am aquela; e no trasglucia de aquela alcuna causa e maugua l’aygua una hora aprop autra am la sua ma, quar la sancguisugua tantost cum sent l’aygua catz.	And then take a vial full of lukewarm water, and open the mouth of it in that, and wash the mouth with that; and do not let any cause pass through that and murmur at the water for an hour afterwards by its own hand, because the blood-sucking worm will soon come to sense the water.
Mays si no es foro-getada am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras subfumigua le malaute am cimetz o am assafetida per le instrument le qual havem recomtat en la sufumiguacio de uvula.	But if it is not forgotten with what we have recommended, then subfumigate the patient with cinnamon or with assafetida by the instrument which we have recommended in the subfumigation of the uvula.
Fay aquo, so en quar cayra.	Do this, and it will come to be so.
E es un’autra manieyra de operacio en sufumiguacio de aquela, es que tu prenguas una ola en la qual sian carbos ignitz e la ola sia cuberta am una cobertora en le mieg de la qual sia un trauc, e sia compausat en aquel trauc la extremitat del instrument; e aprop dega desus la subfumigacio; e pause le malaute la sua boca en la extremitat de la canula, e claugua la sua boca per que la subfumiguacio no sia foro-getada entro que sapias que la subfumigacio es pervenguda a la sancguisugua, quar la sancguisugua tantost cayra.	And this is another way of operation in subfumigation, that you take a pot with burning coals and the pot be covered with a cloth in the middle of which is a hole, and the extremity of the instrument be placed in that hole; and then proceed to subfumigate; and pause the patient's mouth on the extremity of the tube, and close his mouth so that the subfumigation is not forgotten until you know that the subfumigation has reached the blood-sucking worm, for the blood-sucking worm will soon fall.
E si no catz, lahoras tu itera la subfumiguacio motas vetz, e abstengua le malaute de beure, e mange causas saladas e alhs, e no begua aygua, e ayssi necessari es que am aquest regiment sia fora-getada.	And if it does not catch, then you repeat the subfumigation many times, and abstain from giving water to the patient, and give him salty causes and herbs, and do not let him drink water, and thus it is necessary that with this regimen be forgotten.
E aquesta es la forma del instrument am le qual es trayta sancguisugua del guolayro quan es vista; e es semblant a forceps ayssi cum vezes, sino quar es en lu alcuna curvitat:	And this is the form of the instrument with which blood-sucking worms are extracted from the groin when it is visible; and it resembles forceps like those, except that it has some curvature.
le qual sia mesa al guolayro, e la extremitat de lu es semblant a bec de ciconia, que es guanta, en la qual es aspretat de lima, per so quar, quan comprem alcuna causa, aquela no leyssa.	which is placed in the groin, and the extremity of it resembles the beak of a stork, which is grasped, with a lime-like point, for so that when you compress any cause, it does not let go.
Capitol .xl.	Chapter XL.
En le qual es la suma del sermo en apercio de apostemas e en seccio de lor.	In which is the summary of the sermon in warning of swellings and their section.
Les apostemas so motas specias, de motas manieyras, segon que ve rememoracio de lor, de quascuna en aquest libre.	The swellings are many species, of many manners, according to the remembrance of them, of each one in this book.
E so diversas en perforacio e seccio de lor per doas manieyras, de las quals la una es per la specia de apostemas en si meteys; e per aquo que comprem de las humiditatz.	And so diverse in their perforation and section by two manners, of which one is by the species of swellings themselves; and therefore that we compress from the humors.
E la segonda manieyra es prop les locs en les quals accideys del cos, quar le apostema accident en le cap es autra de la apostema accident en le cul; e le apostema en le loc carnos accident es autra del apostema accident en junctura; e a quascun de lor es son juguament per operacio.	And the second manner is proper to the places where accidents occur in the body, for the swelling that occurs in the head is another than the swelling that occurs in the tail; and the swelling that occurs in the fleshy part is another than the swelling that occurs at the joint; and each of them has its own judgment by operation.
E mays de apostemas so alcunas las quals cove que no sian perforadas sino aprop maturacio de la sania en aquels o compliment de lor.	And some swellings are such that they should not be perforated, but rather allowed to mature with the pus in those or its completion.
So autras apostemas les quals cove que sian traucatz quan son cruzes, e no son maturatz segon lor compliment, ayssi cum apostemas que son propdas a las juncturas, quar apostema quan ve prop junctura, lo esser de lu es prolonguat entro que·s poyreys aquo que es en le circuit de lu, e fort leu son corromputz les liamentz o les nervis de aquela junctura, per que es fayta causa de contraccio de aquel membre; o es apostema prop de membre principal, e si tu tardas la perforacio de lu entro sia madurat nosira al membre principal; o es prop le cul, donc perfora aque no-madurat; e no cove que·l perforas cru, de no-complida degestio, sino aquel que es prop del cul, per so que no poyresca le preon de lu e sia elonguat a las partidas dedintz del cul, e sia fayta fistula, o que sia fayt en le terme de lu que no sia sanat.	And other swellings are such that they should be pierced when they are crossed, and not mature according to their completion, just like swellings that are proper to joints. For a swelling that occurs near a joint, the matter of it is prolonged until it pours out what is in its circuit, and then the bonds or nerves of that joint are corrupted, causing contraction of that member; or it is a swelling proper to the main member, and if you delay perforation of it until it becomes mature on the main member; or it is near the anus, therefore pierce it unripe. Do not pierce it when it is ripe with non-completed digestion, but only that which is proper to the anus, so that it does not pour forth its contents and be elongated towards the outer parts of the anus, causing a fistula, or that it become in its term what is not healed.
Mays cove que tu sapias la hora de la perforacio de la apostema, e aysso es quan es maturat.	But you must know the hour of piercing the swelling, and that is when it is mature.
E sapias que es madurat quan es la cedacio de la dolor e la cessacio de la febre, e aprop la diminucio de la rogor e de la pulsacio, e la acuitat del cap del apostema, e les autres senhals.	And you must know that it is mature when there is the yielding of pain and the ceasing of fever, and accordingly the decrease in swelling and pulse, and the sharpness of the tip of the swelling, and the other signs.
E quar cove que sapias la perforacio cazer en le loc pus dejos del apostema e de pus venient de curacio de la eminencia.	And therefore you must know that the piercing should take place in the most distant part of the swelling and from the coming forth of the cure of the prominence.
E perforacio tostemps sia per le lonc de la carn o del cors, si las apostemas son en las partidas de las mas o dels pes, e en loc dels lacertz, de las cordas dels nervis, de las arcerias; e, al derier, en totz locs enguals en les quals no es reflecio; quar en aquels que so reflectitz, usa de perforacio segon aquel membre.	And piercing should be done through the length of the flesh or the body, if the swellings are in the parts of the muscles or of the fat, and in places of the lacertae, of the cords of the nerves, of the arteries; and finally, in all equal places where there is no reflection; for in those that are reflected, use piercing according to that member.
Mays quan le apostema es en loc carnos, lahoras miels es que leysses la perforacio de lu entro que sia confermada la digestio de lu segon compliment, ayssi quo havem dit; quar si tu perforas aquel denant aquo, es prolonguat le cors del poyre de lu e de mota sordicia, e fort leu las labias de lu so enduradas e la profunditat de lu.	But when the swelling is in a fleshy part, then it is better that you delay the piercing of it until it is confirmed by the digestion of it according to its completion, just as we have said; for if you pierce it before that, the body of the pus will be prolonged and many foul humors will be brought forth, and therefore the lips of it will become hardened and its depth.
Mays alcus apostemas so perforatz segon la latitut de la carn o del cos deves la necessitat, o segon aquo del qual lo membre indigeys.	But some swellings should be pierced according to the latitude of the flesh or body, as necessity demands, or according to that which the member requires.
E cove que administres petita perforacio , e·n les apostemas grans gran perforacio e ampla o motas seccios segon la diversitat de la grandesa dels apostemas.	And you must administer a small piercing, and in large swellings, a large piercing and wide or many sections according to the diversity of the size of the swellings.
E autras so dels apostemas en les quals cove que la codena sia conquavada e sia encidida, quan es fayta ayssi quo pan e fayta es en terme que ja stigua, ayssi cum aquel que accideys en trops de dubelec e de bubos.	And others are of swellings in which the cord should be concave and indented, when it is made thus as if bread and cheese were placed together, just like those that occur in troops of dubeclets and buboes.
E de aquels so que so insciditz am seccio havent tres angles; e de aquels es en le qual es inscidit ayssi cum figura de fuelha de mirtra, ayssi cum las apostemas dels angonars.	And of those which are indented with a section having three angles; and of those is one which is indented just like the figure of a myrtle leaf, just like the swellings of the gangrene.
E de lor so en les quals es administrada seccio redonda e seccio lunar, e semblantz ad aquels.	And of those which are indented with a round section and a lunar-shaped section, and resemble them.
Mays aquel al qual no es cap ayssi cum son apostemas leons superficials, cove que tu perforas aquel am perforacio superficial, o plana tant solament.	But that one which is not like the others, such as superficial swellings of the lion, should be pierced with a superficial or flat piercing only.
E cove quant le apostema es gros e ya ha colligit mota sania, que perfores aquel e no te coytes que extraguas tot le poyre en aquela hora; habantz extratz de aquel una partida, e aprop opila le apostema entro al autre dia, e aprop extratz una partida major, e aprop fa aquo motas veguadas segon graduacio entro que sia foro-getat.	And you should know that when the swelling is large and has collected much pus, you must pierce it and not worry about extracting all the pus at once; having extracted one part, prop up the swelling until the next day, and then extract a larger part, and do this many times according to graduation until it is forgotten.
E majorment si·l malaute es de freol vertut, o femna prens, o enfant petit, o viel en decrepitut, quar l’esperit animal motas vetz es resolvut am la egressio de la sania, e fort leu mor le malaute, e tu operte les.	And most especially if the patient is of a fragile constitution, or a woman in childbirth, or a child, or an old person in decrepitude; for the animal spirit many times is resolved with the excretion of pus, and therefore the patient dies quickly, and you must operate on them.
Don guarda aquest capitol am gran cautela, e aprop la tua perforacio en la qual perforas aquestz apostemas, cove que abstergescas las plagues e consideras donc si la plagua del apostema es pauca, o es una seccio plana, lahoras tu aministra las qualguas de li o de coto antic; e si le apostema es gran, e las fissuras de la perforacio son motas, lahoras cove que tu pauses meca en quascun trauc entro que pervenguan ensemps.	Therefore guard this chapter with great caution, and accordingly administer your piercing in which you pierce these swellings, so that you cleanse the plagues and consider then whether the plague of the swelling is slight, or it is a flat section; therefore you must administer some of old wine or vinegar; and if the swelling is large, and the fissures of the perforation are many, then you must pause in each hole until they come together.
E si en le apostema es abscindit una partida de la codena o has concavada aquela en le circuit, lahoras cove que tu la complescas de coto viel o de fil fayt de drap de li, ayssi cum quan has traytz pans o razizos, ses humiditat; e strenh aquel entro al tertz dia; e aprop proceseys aquel e cura le am aquo que cove dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And if in the swelling is abscessed a part of the cord or has concavated it in the circuit, then you must fill it with old cloth or a thread made of linen, just as when you have drained pustules or boils, with their moisture; and strengthen that within three days; and accordingly process that and cure it with what is needed from the poultices until it is healed.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc en la hora de la operacio tua, lahoras tu aministra aygua frega e vi agre en les quals mules un drap de li, e pausa aquel sobre le loc del fluxs del sanc motas veguadas.	But if bleeding occurs during the hour of your operation, then you must administer lukewarm water and vinegar to the places where a linen cloth is wrapped around it, and pause that over the place of the bleeding many times.
Mays si persevera le fluxs del sanc, lahoras cove que tu aministres regiment e curacio e polveras las quals he recomtadas en motz locs de aquest nostre libre e de divisio.	But if the bleeding persists, then you must administer a regimen and cure, and powder the ones which I have recommended in many places of this our book and division.
Mays si es en temps de hivern, e·l loc de la apostema es loc de motz nervis, lahoras cove que tu enfundas pulvils en vi e oli caut, e pauses aquels sobre les locs.	But if it is in the time of winter, and the location of the swelling is a place of many nerves, then you must envelop powders in vinegar and oil carefully, and pause them on those places.
E si es en estiu, e les locs son carnoses, lahoras cove que tu pauses pulvils enbeguts am aygua e oli o am vi e oli, e tot aquo sia freg entro que sia le ters dia, ayssi cum havem dit, e lahoras cove que tu deslies le apostema e abstergescas aquel e aministres en la curacio de lu aquo que a lu conveneys entro que sia sanat.	And if it is in summer, and the places are fleshy, then you must pause powders mixed with water and oil or vinegar and oil, and all that be hot within three days, just as we have said, and then you must loosen the swelling and cleanse that and administer to it what is needed for its cure until it is healed.
E aysso es aquo que es necessari de la cognicio de la curacio de apostemas universalment, mays segon la via de distinccio ja he dit de tot apostema en qual manieyra es via de la cura de lu per capitols singularment.	And thus is this what is necessary for the knowledge of the cure of swellings universally, but according to the way of distinction which I have said for each swelling in a particular manner by chapters.
Capitol .xli.	Chapter XLI.
De seccio de apostemas les quals veno en la codena del cap.	On the Section of Swellings which occur on the Cord of the Head.
En la codena del cap petitz apostemas, e so de specias de nodes les quals conteno tunicas que so a lor factz ; e las specias de lor so motas.	In the cord of the head, small swellings occur, and of species of nodes which contain tunics that are to their uses; and the species of these are many.
E de lor son pingas, e de aquelas so que conteno humiditat semblant a lima.	And among them are pustules, and those which contain moisture resembling lime.
E de aquelas so las quals conteno humiditat semblant a pols, et asemblantz a lor; e de aquelas so que son lapideas, durs.	And among them are those which contain moisture resembling powder, and similar to theirs; and those which are lithoid, hard.
E en la seccio de totz, e en la extraccio de aquels no es temor, cum deves la exteccio de aquels no fa contrariat arceria.	And in the section of all, and in the extraction of these, there is no fear, as you should extract them so that the extraction does not cause constriction of the artery.
E la operacio en seccio de aquels es que tu esproes aquels am instrument la forma del qual ve aprop aysso, le qual es apelat entromes, entro que sapias que contengua.	And the operation in section of these is that you express them with an instrument whose shape approaches thus, which is called "entromes", until you know what they contain.
Quar si aquo que conte es humiditat, lahoras scindeys aquel am seccio segon la longitut per seccio superficial segon aquesta forma:	Therefore, if what is contained is moisture, then you must divide it into sections according to its length, by a superficial section in this form:
E comensa en la seccio de la linha de .B. entro a la linha de .G. Donc cum la humiditat es evacuada, lahoras tu excoria aquela pel que conte aquela humiditat, e no leysses de aquela alcuna causa de tot, quar tropas veguadas retorna, si roman de aquela alcuna causa.	And begins at the section of the line .B. up to the line .G. Then, when the moisture is evacuated, you must excoriate that which contains that moisture, and not leave any cause behind, for many times it returns, if there remains some cause.
E aprop submergeys coto en enguent egipciach, si es present, e sino, en aygua e sal; e umpleys am aquel la plagua e layssa aquel entro ad autra dia, quar am aquo corrodeys tot so que es romas de aquela pellicula.	And accordingly, you must submerge it in an Egyptian poultice, if present, or else in water and salt; and fill it with that poultice and leave it until the next day, for by this, all that remains of that peel will be corroded.
E aprop itera sobre aquel coto am enguent egipciach segondament e tersament si indigeyses de lu, entro que·t comfides que no y haia romas alcuna causa de aquela pellicula; lahoras cura la plagua am enguent entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, you must iterate over that poultice with an Egyptian poultice secondly and thirdly if needed, until you are confident that there is no remaining cause of that peel; then cure the wound with a poultice until it is healed.
E si apostema conte nodi gras, lahoras tu inscideys aquel segon aquesta forma:	And if the swelling contains fatty nodes, then you must incise it in this form:
am seccio havent forma de crotz, e geta oncis entre doas labias de la seccio e scorsa aquel de tota partida, e esforsa la tua vertut en extraccio de la tunica la qual conte aquel.	by section having the form of a cross, and cut once between two lips of the section and scrape that away from all part, and exert your virtue in extracting the tunic which contains it.
Mays si a tu arceria fa contrarieta, lahoras fay aquo que yeu t’e recontat primieyrament.	But if your artery is constricted, then do what I have recounted first.
E semblantment fay en le apostema lapificat de seccio e de curacio segon que a tu havem dit; e seccio sobre apostema lapificat es pus leugiera, quar es de pauc sanc e de pauca humiditat.	And similarly do with the lithoid swelling of section and cure according to what we have said; and section over lithoid swelling is lighter, because it has little blood and little moisture.
E alcunas vetz so alcus de aquestz apostemas les quals so en le cap en alcus homes am los quals de tot no es humiditat; la qual causa es quar yeu inscindigui sobre un apostema en le cap de una femna vielha e atrobegui le apostema ayssi cum peyra sorda, aspra, blanqua, la qual no podia esser trinquada, e si a alcu fos am aquela percussit, plaguera aquel.	And sometimes there are some of these swellings which are in the head of certain old men who have little moisture; and this cause is because you incised over one swelling on the head of an old woman and afterwards struck the swelling with a sordid, asperous, white hammer that could not be bent, and if it touched any part, it would wound.
Mays en les autres apostemas accidentz en le cap otra aquest no es aquest capitol, ayssi cum les apostemas que veno als caps dels enfantz e deves las razitz de las aurelhas, mays la seccio de aquestz totz sia seccio superficial.	But in other accidental swellings on the head, this is not this chapter, as are the swellings that occur on the heads of children and in the ears, but the section of these all shall be a superficial section.
E pausa la perforacio de aquels de la partida pus bassa de lor per so que sia alleujat le cos de la sania a las partidas pus bassas.	And pause the piercing of those in the lower part of them, so that it may be alleviated the body of the pus to the lower parts.
E aprop cura aquelas am aquo que conveneys ad aquel de curacio.	And accordingly cure those with what is needed for their cure.
Capitol .xlii.	Chapter XLII.
De seccio de scrophulas las quals accideyso en le col.	On the Section of Scrofulae which occur in the Neck.
Motas veguadas endeveno aquestas apostemas en le colh e en las aysselhas e en les angonars; e alcunas veguadas accideyso en las autras partidas del cos.	Many times these swellings occur in the neck and in the armpits and in the groin; and sometimes they occur in other parts of the body.
E so aquelas que accideysso en le colh, e so motas que so engendradas entre lor, e tota scrofula de aquelas es dintz la sua tunica propria, e ayssi cum en les nodis e apostema del cap, ayssi cum havem recomtat.	And those which occur in the neck, and many that are generated between them, and all scrofula of these is dissolved into its own tunic, just like in the nodes and swellings of the head, as we have recounted.
E las specias de aquestas scrophulas son motas, quar de aquelas so alcunas lapideas, e de aquelas so que conteno humiditatz, e de aquelas so malignas las quals no obeseysso a curacio.	And the species of these scrofulae are many, for some are lithoid, and some that contain moisture, and some malignant which do not yield to cure.
Donc en aquela la qual tu vezes de bona disposicio en le Tocament, de la qual la color de aquo que es manifest es propda a la color de la codena, e es mauguda a tota partida, e no es annexsa am le nervi del colh, ni am las venas, ni am la arceria, e no es preonda, cove que tu inscidiscas aquela am siccio superficial de la partida desus a la partida dejos del cos de la linha de .G. entro la linha de .B., e scorja aquela de tota partida, e exten dos labias de la codena am onci, o am motz oncis si has necessitat de aquels, ayssi cum havem dit en las apostemas del cap, e extratz aquela petit a petit.	Therefore, in that one which you find to be of good disposition in the Tocament, whose color is manifest and is related to the color of the cord, and is spread out to all parts, and is not annexed to the nerve of the neck, nor to the veins, nor to the artery, and is not preponderant, you must incise it with a superficial section from the upper part of the body down to the lower part of the body along the line .G. up to the line .B., and scrape away that entire part, and extend two lips of the cord with an oncus or with many onci if you have need of them, just as we have said in the swellings of the head, and extract it little by little.
E es mays cautela que no sia inscidida la vena o nervi.	And it is more cautious not to incise the vein or nerve.
E sia le spatum no mot agut, que no ajuste a tu la tua ma am inscizio, o que enquiete le malaute, e que inscidas aquo que no es necessari inscidir; quar si inscideysses vena o arceria e prohibeys tu de la tua operacio, lahoras pausa en la plagua vetriol trissat o autras polveras las quals ostan fluxs de sanc, e estrenh la plagua, e layssa aquel entro que·s repausa la acuitat de la apostema e sia mollificada la plagua e comense esser poyrida.	And if the spatula is not sharp enough, that it does not adjust to your touch and inscision, or that it annoys the patient, and you incise something that is not necessary to be incised; for if you incise a vein or artery and prohibit your operation, then pause in the wound, and sprinkle vitriol or other powders which stop bleeding, and strengthen the wound, and leave it until the swelling subsides and the wound becomes soft and begins to heal.
Quan le sanc es abscindit.	When the blood is abscessed.
Donc retorna a la tua operacio entro que l’aias complida.	Therefore, return to your operation until you have completed it.
E aprop inquireys am le tieu dit indic si es romas alcuna causa de las autras petitas scrophulas, donc inscideys aquelas e munda aquelas.	And accordingly, inquire about the sign that your teacher has indicated whether there remains any cause of other small scrofulae, therefore incise those and clean them.
E si es en la razit de la scrophula gran vena, cove lahoras que no inscidas aquela scrophula de la sua razitz.	And if it is in the root of the great scrofula, then beware that you do not incise that scrofula from its roots.
Abantz cove que lies aquela am fiel doblat fort e que leysses aquela entro que caia per si ses nocument.	Beware that you leave it alone with a doubled force and let it fall of its own accord, without causing any harm.
E aprop omple la plagua de coto vielh le qual tu has ja submirgit en enguent egipciac, e aprop cura aquel.	And accordingly fill the wound with old cloth which you have already submerged in an Egyptian poultice, and accordingly cure that.
E si inscides aquela scrophula tota, lahoras cove que tu ajustes las doas labias de la plagua e cuzas2 tantost pus que no y ha romasa deguna superfluitat.	And if you incise that scrofula entirely, then beware that you adjust the two lips of the wound and close it as soon as possible so that there is no remaining superfluity.
Mays si tu vezes que haia romasa superfluitat per la grandeza de la scrofula, cove que tu entendas a inscidir la razit de aquela, e astrayra aquela e aministra sutura e aquo que es dit.	But if you see that there remains some superfluity due to the greatness of the scrofula, then beware that you understand how to incise the root of it, and extract it and administer suturing and what is said.
E aquela de las scrophulas que conteno humiditatz, perfora aquela am perforacio superficial aqui la on appar a tu le loc de maturacio de lu, e pausa perforacio de aquo que siec le pus bas del cos, ayssi cum havem dit.	And as for the scrofulae that contain moisture, pierce it with a superficial piercing at the location where you see the spot of maturation, and pause in the piercing so that the pus drains from the lower part of the body, just as we have said.
E aprop aministra perforacio, calguas am enguent e semblantz ad aquels, per so que corroda aquo que es romas de la corropcio.	And accordingly administer piercing, with poultices and similar substances to those, so that it corrodes what remains of the corruption.
E aprop quan tu vezes la plagua ja esser mundada, lahoras tu cura aquela am enguent de carn generatiu entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, when you see the wound already cleansed, then you must cure it with a poultice of generative flesh until it is healed.
Capitol .xliii.	Chapter XLIII.
De seccio del pilhot del apostema accident dintz le guolayro.	On the Section of the Pithotomy of the Accidental Swelling that occurs in the Gullet.
Diyssero les antics aquesta seccio en le epilhot, e no vist alcu hom en nostra terra que aquela aia fayta.	The ancients described this section as the "Epilhot", and it is not seen in our land that anyone has performed it.
E aquesta es la inscriptura del sermo de aquels.	And this is the inscription of the sermon of those.
Mays en les homes haventz esquinencia, cove que sia esquivada la extraccio del epilhot, cum per aquo no sia fayt juvament per so quar totas las venas e las majors del malaute so aqui.	But in men who have squintiness, it is necessary to avoid the extraction of the epilhot, because through this the veins and main arteries of the patient are all here.
Mays en aquels que han apostemas cautz en la boca o guolayro o dos aurelhas, quan la malautia no es en la cana, cove husar de la seccio de epilhot a fugir la perdicio la qual es fayta per perfocacio.	But in those who have swellings caused by caustics in the mouth or gullet or ears, when the disease is not in the canal, it is necessary to use the section of epilhot to flee from the destruction which is made by perforation.
Donc cove quan volem aquo, que inscidam le epilhot dejos tres cercles dels cercles del epilhot, o quatre am petita seccio per la latitut en aquel que es entre dos cercles per quantitat, que la seccio sia en ciphac, no en la cartillage, e aquest loc es convenent a seccio, quar es privat de carn e les vayselhs de sanc de lu son luhen.	Therefore, when we wish to do this, let us incise the epilhot below three circles of the circles of the epilhot, or four with small section by latitude in that which is between two circles for quantity, so that the section is in ciphac, not in cartilage, and this location is suitable for a section, because it is deprived of flesh and the vessels of blood are hollow.
E si le metge es pauruc, cove lahoras que extenda la codena del golayro am onci, e aprop fenda la codena entro que pervengua a la canal, mays evite les vaysels de sanc si vetz de aquelas alcuna causa.	And if the physician is hesitant, then beware that he extends the cord of the gullet with an oncus, and accordingly makes an incision in the cord until it reaches the canal, but avoid the vessels of blood if you see any cause.
E aprop inscida li ciplach segon que havem recomtat; e es significat sobre la seccio de la canal per le flacma le qual es de aquela eyssit am aquo que es de lu disromput e per la abscizio de la votz.	And accordingly incise the ciphac according to what we have recounted; and it is signified above the section of the canal by the flame which is from that very thing, mixed with water that is broken down and by the abscess of the voice.
E layssa la plagua uberta per alcun temps.	And leave the wound open for some time.
Donc cum la hora es remauguda en la qual perforacio es temuda, agregua doas labias de la codena de la plagua, e cus aquela sola ses la cartillage.	Therefore, when the hour is come in which perforation is feared, add two lips to the cord of the wound, and close it alone except for the cartilage.
E aprop administra medicinas que fan naysser la carn entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly administer medicines that make the flesh grow until it is healed.
E diyssec Albucasis que la summa del sermo le qual havem recomtat, exposicio no es sino que veias que alcus de aquetz apostemas ja han opilat lo guolayro del malaute, e le malaute es vengut entro a mort, e le ale de lu es entresecat, e alcus van a inscidir le epiglos per so que respire le malaute sobre le loc de la plagua per alcuna respiracio, e sia salvat de mort.	And let Albucasis say that the summary of the sermon which we have recounted is nothing but that you see some of those swellings have filled up the gullet of the patient, and the patient has come to death, and the voice of life is extinct, and some go to incise the epiglottis so that the patient may breathe over the location of the wound through some respiration, and be saved from death.
E per aquo comandero layssar la plagua uberta entro que sia consumida la malicia de la malautia; e es la malicia de lu per tres dias; e donc lahoras comandero cosi la plagua, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And therefore command to leave the wound open until the malice of the disease is consumed; and it is the malice of life for three days; and then command to close the wound, and cure it until it is healed.
E aquo que yeu he vist per mi meteys, es que una sirventa pres un cotel e mesec le en le sieu golayro e inscidic am aquel una partida de la cana del pulmo, e yeu fu apelat a la curacio de lu, e atrobegui la mugen ayssi cum es mugit del moridos, e descubrigui la plagua e atrobegui le sanc le qual era yssit de la plagua petit.	And this which I have seen by my own eyes is that a servant took a knife and put it in his own gullet and incised with it a part of the tube of the lung, and you were called to the cure of him, and he began to cough as the dead are coughed out, and uncovered the wound and brought forth the blood which was situated in the small part.
Donc yeu fo confessat que aquela no havia inscidit vena ni guidegi, e le vent yssia de la plagua, e curegui aquela entro que foc sanada.	Therefore you were confessed that it had not cut a vein nor an artery, and the breath was from the wound, and cured it until it was healed.
E no accidic a la sirventa si no rauquiera en la votz, e aprop alcus dias retornec ad miloracio de las suas dispozicios.	And there was not an accident with the servant, except that he became hoarse in his voice, and accordingly some days returned to improvement of his physical condition.
E ara dic yeu que en la seccio del epilhot no ha temor.	And now I say to you that in the section of the epilhot there is no fear.
Capitol .xliv.	Chapter XLIV.
De seccio sobre apostema le qual accideys en le golayro defora, e es apelat hernia del golayro.	On the Section of the Swelling which occurs in the Gullet outside, and is called Hernia of the Gullet.
Aquest apostema nompnat hernia del golayro es apostema gran segon la color del cors, e es mot en las femnas.	This swelling, named hernia of the gullet, is a great swelling according to the color of the body, and it is more common in women.
E es segon dos manieyras, quar o es natural o accidental.	And it is according to two manners, whether it be natural or accidental.
E en le natural no es engen de curar.	And in the natural one there is no need to cure.
E l’accidental es segon dos manieyras del qual la un es semblant a nodes grasses, e l’autra manieyra es semblant apostema le qual es fayt per nodacio de arteria, e en aquel es temor.	And the accidental one is according to two manners, of which one is similar to grassy nodes, and the other manner is similar to a swelling caused by constriction of an artery, and in that one there is fear.
E no cove que·s fassa presumpcio a lu cum ferr sino en aquel que es petit.	And it is not necessary to make presumptions about it except in the small one.
E tu proha aquel e investigua aquel am le dit, e si atrobas lu semblant a nodi gras, e no es suspendut am alcuna de las venas, lahoras tu inscideys aquel ayssi cum les nodes, e extratz aquel am aquo que conte lu de la pel e bursiclam; e sino, lahoras es perscrutat tot le sieu esser, e aprop cura le loc am aquo que cove de curacio entro que sia sanat.	And you proceed with that and investigate it according to what is said, and if you find it similar to grassy nodes, and it is not suspended from any of the veins, then you incise it as with the nodes, and extract it with water which contains the peel and bursicles; and otherwise, then it is thoroughly examined, and accordingly cure the location where it needs healing until it is healed.
Capitol .xlv.	Chapter XLV.
De seccio de las specias de nodes.	On the Section of the Species of Nodes.
Dels nodes so motas specias e yeu ja he dit totas las specias de lor en la divisio.	Of the nodes, many species and you have already said all the species of them in the division.
E cove que yeu recomte assi la diferencia entre node e exitura cum fassa dubitacio.	And it is necessary that you recount thus the difference between a node and an excrescence, lest there be doubt.
Donc yeu dic que am exitura es caliditat e febre e dolors vehementz entro que es sedada la ebullicio de la superfluitat; e es complida putrefaccio que lahora cessa la febre, la dolor e la calor.	Therefore you say that in an excrescence there is heat and fever and violent pains until the ebullition of the superfluity subsides; and it is completed putrefaction which then ceases the fever, pain, and heat.
Mays am node no es caliditat ni febre ni dolor, e conte aquel ciphac leon le qual es al u sac propri.	But in a node there is no heat nor fever nor pain, and it contains that cephac lion which is at the proper sac.
E es segon la color del cors, e le comensament de lu es cum un ceze e es fayt ayssi cum vace, sia major o minor, e son segon dos specias, quar o so grassas e conteno humiditat, e las colors de la humiditat son motas, segon que yeu diyssi en la divisio.	And it is according to the color of the body, and its beginning is like a cheese and it is made thus as a void, whether greater or lesser, and they are according to two species, whether they be grassy and contain moisture, and the colors of the moisture are many, as I said in the division.
Donc cove, quan pervenas a la curacio de node, que exprohes aquel e inquiras aquel al comensament am sturment le qual es apelat intromes, segon que vindra la sua forma en le capitol le qual es aprop aquest.	Therefore, when you come to the cure of a node, beware that you expose it and inquire into it at the beginning with a gentle instrument called an intro-mess, according to what its form will come in the chapter which is appropriate to this one.
E es manieyra de inquisicio de apostemas e de totz nodes, e es que tu prenguas aquest sturment e entromet aquel en le loc pus humit le qual atrobas en le apostema, e tu revolveras les tieus ditz am aquel petit a petit entro que sapias que·l sturment ja ha penetrat la codena.	And this is the manner of inquiry into swellings and all nodes, and it is that you take this instrument and introduce it into the most humid place which you find in the swelling, and you rotate those things said with it little by little until you know that the instrument has penetrated to the cord.
E aprop ultima la tua ma segon la mesura de la grandeza del apostema, e aprop extratz le entromes e considera aquo que es yssit en le vestigi de lu.	And accordingly, finally, your hand according to the measure of the greatness of the swelling, and accordingly extract the intro-mess and consider what is situated in its track.
E si es fora-getada la humiditat corrent, de qualque color sia, lahoras tu le inscideys am seccio superficial segon que he dit en les autres apostemas.	And if the humidity has flowed out, of whatever color it may be, then you will incise it with a superficial section according to what I have said in other swellings.
E si del vestigi de l’intromes no hieys humiditat, lahoras sapias que es gras.	And if from the track of the intro-mess there is no humidity, then you know that it is grass.
E secca sobre lu am seccio havent forma de crotz segon aquesta forma:	And cut above it with a section having the form of a cross according to this form:
ayssi cum t’e ensenhat, e suspen aquel am oncis, e excorja la codena de tota part am facilitat, e guarda la pel o sac, si podes, sobre aquel e extraguas aquela sania am le node.	Just as you have been taught, and suspend it with an oncus, and excoriate the cord of all parts with ease, and preserve the peel or sac, if possible, above it and extract that pus from the node.
Mays si es romput en la operacio, no es possible extrayre aquela sana, e motas veguadas endeve aquo, e lahoras tu la extratz a pessas entro que de lu no romangua denguna causa.	But if it is broken in the operation, then it is not possible to extract that pus, and many times there will be an opening above, and accordingly you will extract it by piecemeal until there is no longer any cause from it.
Quar si de lu roman denguna causa, pauc o trop, le node retorne segon le mays.	For if from it there remains no cause, little or much, the node will return to its original state.
E si tu vezes que de lu roman alcuna part petita, lahoras comple la plagua de alcunas polveras corrosivas agudas e strenh la plagua, e pausa sobre aquela que sede apostema caut, e cura aquel del autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And if you see that from it remains a small part, then fill the wound with some sharp and strong corrosive powders and strengthen the wound, and pause above it where the swelling is cautious, and cure it by another cure until it is healed.
E si es node gran, lahoras tu cus las doas labias de lu e cura aquel am aquo que encarna.	And if it is a large node, then you will close the two lips of it and cure it with water that nourishes.
Mays si vena pulsatil es a lu contraria, o no-pulsatil, lahoras tu coyta e huemple le loc de zegi trissat que es vetriol e leyssa aquel streyt per dos dias o per tres entro que·s poyresca la plagua e que repause la ebullicio del sanc; e aprop retorna a inscindir aquo que es romas del node.	But if the pulsating vein is on the contrary, or non-pulsatile, then you will cut and hollow out the location of the three-fold wound that is filled with vitriol and leave it straight for two days or three until the wound becomes putrid and the ebullition of blood subsides; and accordingly return to incise what remains of the node.
Capitol .xlvi.	Chapter XLVI.
De las formas del sturmentz necessaris en seccio e perforacio.	On the Forms of the Instruments Necessary in Section and Perforation.
De aquels so las formas dels intromesas, e so de tres specias, que de aquels es alcu gran, e de lor es migier, e de lor es petit.	Of those, the forms of intro-messes are three species, that some are great, and some medium, and some small.
La forma de intromes gran es aquesta:	The form of the great intro-mess is this:
La forma de intromes migier es aquesta:	The form of the medium-sized intro-mess is this:
La forma de intromes petit es aquesta:	The form of the small intro-mess is this:
Sian faytz de ferr, de alfulud, de extremitatz cayradas decentment, per so que festino le intrament en les apostemas.	They are made of iron, with a handle of wood or bone, and extremities curved decently, so that the instrument may be introduced into swellings.
E aquestas so las formas dels experientz, e son nompnatz albered, e un de aquels es apelat berid.	And these are the forms of the experimenters, and they are named by name, and one of them is called Berid.
E so de tres especias, quar de lor es gran, migier e pauc.	And there are three species, that some are great, some medium, and some small.
La forma de experient gran, forma de lu:	The form of the great experimenter is this:
La forma de experient migier, forma de lu:	The form of the medium-sized experimenter is this:
La forma de experient pauc, forma de lu:	The form of the small experimenter is this:
Conveneysso que sian per aquels apostemas e exituras e fistulas e bubos per so que entre aquelas so dels osses e de autras causas.	And thus it is fitting that they be for those swellings, excrescences, and fistulas, and buboes, because among them are those of bones and other causes.
E so faytz redontz, grosses, leons, ayssi cum grans agulhas am las quals son cosidas las selhas, e son faytas de eram citri, o de eram o de ferr, o de argent, E las milhors so quan so faytas de eram citri.	And thus they are made rounded, thick, and lions, just like large needles with which the scales are sewn, and they are made of terra cotta, or iron, or silver, And the best ones are when they are made of terra citta.
E son faytz les experient de plum negre, les quals se acordan que per aquels sian ubertas las fistulas en la conquavitat de las quals so reflexios, que sian reflectidas am la sua levitat am aquelas refleccios.	And they are made by experimenters of black lead, which they agree that for those, the fistulas should be opened in the convergence of the reflections, which should be reflected into their lightness with those reflections.
E so de tres specias, quar alcus de lor so loncs, e dels autres migiers, e dels autres breus, segon la quantitat del ample de la fistula e de la strictura de lu.	And there are three species, that some of them are long, and others medium-sized, and others short, according to the quantity of the width of the fistula and its constriction.
Forma del experient gran de plom:	Form of the great experimenter of lead:
Forma del experient migier de plom:	Form of the medium-sized experimenter of lead:
Forma del experient petit de plom:	Form of the small experimenter of lead:
Las formas dels oncis so de motas specias, quar de aquels so alcus simples, als quals es una curvitat solament, e so de tres specias: grans, paucs e migiers.	The forms of the onuses are many species, that some of them are simple, to which is only one curvature, and there are three species: great, small, and medium-sized.
E de lor so uncis orps, e so de tres specias.	And among them are onuses of iron, and there are three species.
E de aquels so uncis haventz doas curvaturas, e so de tres specias.	And among them are onuses that have two curvature, and there are three species.
E de lor so haventz tres curvaturas, e so de tres specias.	And among them are onuses that have three curvatures, and there are three species.
E totz aquetz so necessaris en lor loc.	And all these are necessary in their place.
Forma de unci simple gran, forma de lu:	Form of a great simple onus, form of it:
Forma de unci simple migier:	Form of a medium-sized simple onus:
Forma de unci simple pauc, forma de lu:	Form of a small simple onus, form of it:
Forma de unci orp gran:	Form of an iron great onus:
Forma de unci orp migier, forma de lu:	Form of an iron medium-sized onus, form of it:
Forma de unci orp pauc, forma de lu:	Form of an iron small onus, form of it:
Forma de unci gran havent dos curvaturas:	Form of a great onus having two curvatures:
Forma de unci migier havent dos curvatas:	Form of a medium-sized onus having two curvatures:
Forma de unci pauc havent dos curvaturas:	Form of a small onus having two curvatures:
Forma de unci gran havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a great onus having three curvatures:
Forma de unci migier havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a medium-sized onus having three curvatures:
Forma de unci pauc havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a small onus having three curvatures:
E aquestas so las formas dels scalpels am les quals son seccatz e scorjatz les nodes e le apostemas, e so de tres specias, quar de aquels es gran, migier, e pauc.	And these are the forms of scalpels with which nodes and swellings are cut and excised, and there are three species, that some are great, others medium-sized, and others small.
Forma de scapel gran:	Form of a great scalpel:
Forma del scapel migier:	Form of a medium-sized scalpel:
Forma de scapel pauc:	Form of a small scalpel:
Las extramitatz de aquels am les quals es fayta seccio so agudas e las autres extramitatz so no-agudas, e no so pausadas en tal manieyra, sino per que sia fayt juvament en la excorjacio dels nodes la temor de inscizio de vena o de nervi, e per aquels sia sanat le malaute e atrobe tranquilitat un petit per la adustio la qual atroba deves la excoriacio del apostema.	The extremities of those with which the section is made are sharp and others not sharp, and are not so paused in such a way that it may be done jointly in the excision of nodes, so as to avoid cutting into a vein or nerve, and through these the patient may be healed and restored to tranquility, somewhat for the adjustment which finds fault with the excision of the swelling.
E aquestas son las formas de almagidas, e so de tres specias: gran, migier e pauc, ayssi cum veyras.	And these are the forms of ligatures, and there are three species: great, medium-sized, and small, just like veins.
La forma de magda gran:	Form of a great ligature:
Forma de magda migier:	Form of a medium-sized ligature:
Forma de magda pauc:	Form of a small ligature:
Sian faytas de eram e so semblantz de ray am le qual e fayt alcofol.	They are made of terra cotta and resemble a ray with which alcohol is distilled.
E es en la extramitat lada punctada am spatum occultada e en aquela corr a las partidas dedintz e defora, quan tu vols, ayssi cum veses.	And it has on the extremity a pierced point with a hidden spatula and in that corner there are partitions inside and outside, when you want, just as you see.
Las formas de spatimis, les quals so amaguatz entre los ditz deves la perforacio dels apostemas e no les percebo les malautes, e so de tres specias: gran, migier e pauc.	The forms of spatulas, which are hidden between the said parts of the perforation of swellings and do not touch the patients, and there are three species: great, medium-sized, and small.
E aquestas so las formas de aquels:	And these are the forms of those:
Las formas de ventozas am las quals es abscindit le flux del sanc, e so de tres specias; gran, migiera e pauca; las formas de lu:	The forms of ventoses with which the flow of blood is drained off, and there are three species: great, medium-sized, and small; the forms are:
Sian faytas de eram citri, redondas am alcuna longitut , e sian subtils.	They are made of terra cotta, rounded with some length, and are subtle.
E cove que sian aquestas specias de ventosas deves tu grans, migieras e paucas, per so que per aquelas abscindas flux de sanc am velocitat en necessitat, e lahoras quan a tu primieyrament no es medicina.	And it is necessary that you have these species of ventoses, great, medium-sized, and small, so that through them the flow of blood may be drained off with speed in need, and thus when your patient's condition is not yet medicated.
Enpero no uses de aquelas ad abscidir sanc en tot loc del cors, e non uses sino en locs carnoses, ayssi cum en les lacertis de las cambas e de las coyssas, e en les lacertz dels brasses, e de las mamillas e del ventre e dels engonars, e semblantz a lor dels lacertz carnoses humitz.	However, you do not use those to drain blood in all parts of the body, but only in fleshy places, just like in the armpits and groins, and in the armpits of the breasts, belly, and groin, and similar to their fleshy hummocks.
E alcunas veguadas son faytz de aquels strumentz autres petitz semblantz scorsas de fisacs segon aquesta forma; per les quals lo sanc es abscindit quan es fayt per fleubotomia, o deves inscizio de vena o de arceria.	And some times they are made of those small instruments similar to scissors according to this form; through which the blood is drained when it is done by phlebotomy, or incision of vein or artery.
E alcunas veguadas son faytas redondas segon aquesta forma:	And some times they are made rounded according to this form:
Capitol .xlvii.	Chapter XLVII.
De la cura de las mamillas dels homes las quals so asembladas de femnas.	Of the cure of the breasts of men which are assembled like those of women.
Alcunas veguadas so infladas las mamillas de alcus homes deves le compliment del dormir cum comensan esser pellutz, e aprop so infladas las mamillas, e so asembladas las mamillas de las femnas, e romano apostemosas, lejas.	Sometimes the breasts of some men become inflated just as they begin to be relaxed, and accordingly the breasts are swollen, and assembled like those of women, and apostemous, distant.
E ad aquel que avoreys aquo, cove que inscidisca aquelas am seccio lunar segon aquesta forma, de la linha de .B. entro a la linha de .G., e aprop excorja la groceza tota, e aprop uempla la plagua de medicament encarnatiu, e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am cosidura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And to the one who has this condition, you should incise those with a lunar section according to this form, from the line of B to the line of G, and accordingly excise the entire hardness, and accordingly fill the wound with flesh-colored medicine, and accordingly adjust the two lips of the wound with stitching, and cure that until it is healed.
Mays si la mamilla declina a las partidas dejos e es mollificada per la sua magnitut ayssi cum endeve a las femnas, lahoras sia fendut en dos latz sieus pus sobiras, am dos seccios semblantz a figura lunar, de las quals quascuna sia contenguda en l’autra deves la fi de quascuna, entro que sia que la linha major contengua la menor segon aquesta forma de la linha de .B. e la linha de .G. E aprop excorja la codena la qual es entre dos labias de la plagua, e osta la pingueza, e aministra aquo que havem dit de la sutura e de las polveras aquo que es necessari en la curacio entro que sia sanat.	But if the breast descends to its natural parts and is softened by its own magnitude just like in women, then it should be cut into two halves with a slight surplus on each side, with two sections resembling the shape of the moon, where each one contains the end of the other, until the major line contains the minor one according to this form from the line of B to the line of G. And accordingly excise the cord which is between the two lips of the wound, and stop the swelling, and administer what we have said about suturing and the powders that are necessary for healing until it is healed.
E si tu non conpleysses la inscizio de aquo que cove inscidir per la inquietut del malaute, e per flux de sanc, lahoras cove que huemplas la plagua de coto submergit en enguent corrosiu e layssa aquel entro que aquo corroda que es romas de la grayssa, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if you do not complete the incision of that which should be cut because of the anxiety of the patient and the flow of blood, then it is necessary to fill the wound with cotton submerged in corrosive gall and leave it until the corrosion that remains from the grayish color has disappeared, and accordingly cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .xlviii.	Chapter XLVIII.
De perforacio de apostemas que veno dejos le titillic.	Of the perforation of swellings that come from left behind the titillate.
Aquetz apostemas que veno dejos le titillic so de las specias de scrophulas, durs, las quals conte una pel que es sac.	Those swellings that come from left behind the titillate are of the species of scrofulas, which contain a sack.
E de aquelas so alcunas que conteno humiditatz; e aquelas que conteno humiditatz cove que sian inscididas am seccio lunar segon aquesta figura: de la linha de .G. a la linha de .B. E cum es tot evacuat aquo que es en le apostema de la sania, lahoras tu le comple de coto viel e leysa le entro al autra dia.	And some of those contain humidity; and those that contain humidity must be incised with a lunar section according to this figure: from the line of G to the line of B. And when all the pus is evacuated from the swelling, then you must fill it with old cotton and leave it for another day.
E aprop le coto sia ostat e sia curat am enguent convenient ad aquo, entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly the cotton should be left to stay and be cured with suitable gall, until it is healed.
E si le apostema de las specias dels nodes es, e de las scrophulas, lahoras tu scindeys sobre aquel ayssi cum havem dit en la seccio sobre las scrophulas engualment.	And if the swelling is of the species of nodes or scrofulas, then you should cut into it just as we have said in the section on scrofulas, equally.
May si la plagua es extenduda en aysso que yesca poyredura, lahoras administra en lu cauteri segon que en aquo havem denant dit.	And if the wound is extended in such a way that it becomes putrid, then administer to it caustic according to what we have said before.
Capitol .xlix.	Chapter XLIX.
De seccio de apostemas que accideysso per arceria o per vena.	Of the section of swellings that occur by artery or vein.
Quan arceria es rompuda, e la codena es consolidada la qual es sobre aquela, lahoras motas veguadas accideys apostema E les senhals per les quals es conoguda que imflamacio e apostema sian per la arteria o per vena: quar quan apostema es per arceria es lonc agreguat en le preon del cors; e que quan inpelleysses le apostema am les tieus ditz, sentes en lu quays sia stridor.	When the artery is broken and the cord is consolidated which is above it, many times a swelling occurs And the signs by which it is known that inflammation and swelling are due to the artery or vein: for when the swelling is from the artery, it is long extended in the region of the chest; and when you apply pressure with those said things, you will feel in it what is called stridor.
E aquel que es per vena es redon al manifest del cors.	And that which is from the vein is rounded to the visible part of the body.
E seccio sobre aquest apostema es error, e majorment en aquel que es dejos las aysselhas, e en les angonars, e en le col, e en motz locs del cors; e es mot gran, donc cove que la sua curacio am ferr sia esquivada, e aquel que es en las extramitatz, o al cap, cove que sia evitat.	And the section on this swelling is an error, and more so in those that are left behind the armpits, and in the groin, and in the neck, and in many parts of the body; and it is very great, therefore its cure with iron should be avoided, and that which is in the extremities or at the head should be prevented.
Mays sobre aquel que es de lor per imflacio de l’orrifici de la arceria, scindeys en la codena seccio en le lonc; e aprop huebre la seccio am uncis e aprop la arceria, e deliura de las tunicas entro que sia descuberta.	But on that which is from the artery due to inflammation of the orifice of the artery, you should cut into the cord in the long section; and accordingly cut the section with scissors and accordingly open up the artery, and deliver the tunics until it is uncovered.
E aprop met sobre aquel agulha e fay aquela penetrar entro al autre latz, e estrenh la arceria am fiel doble en dos locs, — la qual causa yeu a tu eyssenhegui en extraccio de doas arcerias les quals so en les templars.	And accordingly make an incision on that aglet and cause it to penetrate into the other side, and strengthen the artery with a double thread in two places, — which is the reason why you should have your eye sight in extracting two arteries which are in the temples.
E aprop punh le loc le qual es entre dos liamentz am spatum entro que yesca le sanc tot que es en lu, e sia dissolvut le apostema.	And accordingly push the place that is between two ligaments with a spatula until all the blood that is in it is let out and the swelling is dissolved.
