E aprop administra curacio en la qual es engendrat poyre entro que caian les liamentz; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz convenientz ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly administer treatment in which pus is generated until the ligaments fall apart; and accordingly cure that with suitable gall until it is healed.
E si es apostema per seccio de vena, lahoras cove que tu tenguas am la tua ma aquo que es a tu possible del apostema am la codena, e aprop intromet la agulha dejos le loc le qual tu has tengut dejos la tua ma, e fay aquela penetrar; e sia en aquela fil doble entro que tu extraguas aquel del autre latz, e aprop ligua le apostema am bo liament segon que yeu he dit a tu en le liament de uva4 de doas partz am doas extremitatz del fil.	And if the swelling is due to section of vein, then you should take with your hand as much of the swelling and cord as possible from the swelling and cord, and accordingly introduce the aglet behind the place where you have kept your hand, and make it penetrate; and be in that file double so that you can extract what is on the other side, and accordingly bind the swelling with a single ligament just as I have told you to do with two parts and two extremities of the thread.
Mays si temes que extraguam le fil, lahoras entromet le fiel am aquela agula dejos tot le apostema deves la inscizio de la agulha primieyra, e strenh les tieus fiels en quatre locs.	But if you fear that the thread may break, then accordingly introduce the thread with that aglet behind all the swelling before making the incision of the first needle, and strengthen those threads in four places.
Aprop secca le apostema en le mieg loc de lu entro que quan es yssit aquo que es en lu, lahoras tu inscideys la superfluitat de la codena, e layssa aquo que de lu es liat.	And accordingly cut the swelling in the middle of it so that when what is there is removed, you will then incise the surplus of the cord and leave what remains tied.
E aprop pausa sobre lu pulvil le qual has submergit en vi e oli, e aprop administra la curacio la qual es fayta am calguas e enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly put on the poultice which you have soaked in vinegar and oil, and accordingly administer the treatment which is made with some and gall until it is healed.
Capitol l del apostema le qual accideys per torcio de nervis.	Chapter LX of the swelling that occurs due to twisting of nerves.
Ayssi cum accideys apostema en arceria e en vena, e semblantment accideys apostema en les nervis quan accideys en lor percussio o accideys per trebal superfluable, e per semblantz.	Just as swellings occur in the artery and vein, and similarly swellings occur in nerves when they are pierced or twisted excessively, and for similar reasons.
E es fayt le mays de lu en les locs dels adjutoris o del talo, o en tot loc en le qual so maugudas las juncturas.	And it is caused by the greatest of all in the areas of the assistants or of the tibia, or in any place where the joints are affected.
E es apostema greu, e es asemblat a la color del autre cors, e es en las majors de lu disposicios ses de lor e quan es streyt am vehementia, sent en lu le malaute semblant stupor.	And it is a grave swelling, and it is similar in color to the other body parts, and it occurs in the areas of greatest disposition for its formation and when it is stretched with great intensity, as if the patient were struck with stupor.
E no es apostema agreguat en le preon del cors, e per so es dejos la codena, e el es maugut a tota partida e no va a las partidas denant ni detras.	And it is not a swelling that is aggregated in the chest, and therefore it remains behind the cord, and it is affected to all parts and does not go to the anterior or posterior regions.
Donc aquo de aquels que es en las juncturas no cove que sia envasit am ferr, quar fort leu endevenguera contracio.	Therefore, what is in the joints should not be treated with iron, because it would cause too great a contraction.
Mays aquel que es en le cap o en le front fen la codena am spatum.	But that which is in the head or forehead can be opened up with a spatula.
Mays si es apostema pauc, lahoras te aquel am les forfecs e abscindeys aquel de razitz.	But if it is a small swelling, then you should use the forceps and cut it off at the roots.
E si es gran, lahoras tu le suspen am unci, e excorja aquel, e aprop osta aquel; e ajusta la plagua am sutura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if it is large, then you should suspend it with scissors, and excise that part, and accordingly stop the bleeding; and adjust the wound with stitches, and cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .li.	Chapter LXI.
De seccio de apostema le qual accideys de cheil que accideys al ventre.	Of the section of swelling which occurs in the cheek that occurs in the belly.
Endeveno ad alcus homes motas veguadas en les ventres de aquels e en las autras partidas del cors de aquels theils les quals son apelatz funguals per similitut de aquels am funges, dels quals la razitz es subtil e·l cap de aquel es gros; e ja las labias de aquels so conversas, e es de aquels que es petit, e es de aquels que es mot magnificat.	I have found in some men many times in their bellies and in other parts of their bodies which are called fungous by similarity to those with fungi, whose roots are subtle and the top is thick; and already the lips of these are conversed, and it is of those that is small, and it is of those that is very magnificent.
E yeu ja e vist un, e en le ventre de lu eran dos theils les quals eran mays a funges semblantz, e no era diferencia entre aquels blancs, de menuda razitz.	And I myself have seen one, and in its belly there were two theils that were more like fungi, and there was no difference between them in their white color, with very subtle roots.
E ja las labias de aquels eran enversadas e se fendian, e humiditat corria de aquel tot temps.	And already the lips of those were turned inward and split open, and moisture flowed from it at all times.
Donc yeu inscidegui aquels e atrobegui en la un en pes quays xviii unc. e l’autre quays vi unc.	Therefore, you should incise them and cut into the one in pieces of eighteen ounces. and the other piece weighs seven ounces.
E la operacio en la inscizio de lor es que consideres lahoras si·l malaute es humit, e la color de atheil es blanca, humit, de subtil razitz; lahoras tu le inscideys am spatum lat, e sian en la presencia tua cauteris en le foc, quar motas veguadas deves la seccio de lu es expellit mot sanc; e si te ventz le sanc, cauteriza aquel.	And the operation in the incision of theirs is that you consider now if the patient is humid, and the color of their theil is white, humid, with subtle roots; then you should cut them open with a spatula, and have in your presence some caustic in the fire, because many times the section of it is expelled much blood; and if you find blood, cauterize that.
E si vezes le malaute pauruc e temeros, guarda te de inscizio am ferr; mays lahoras pren fiel de plom recent fayt, e strenh am aquel atheil, la manieyra del qual es aquela que havem dita; e leyssa aquel per dos dias.	And if the patient is poor and timid, beware of incising with iron; but rather take a lead thread freshly made and strengthen it on that theil, in the manner which we have said; and leave it for two days.
E aprop ajusta en la strictura del fil de plom; donc, no cesses strenher le plom granre devetz en theil, entro que sia abscindit e cayha per se ses trebalh.	And accordingly adjust it in the constriction of the lead thread; therefore, do not cease to strengthen the lead greatly on that theil, until it is cut off and falls away from its excessive labor.
Mays si theil es de grossa razitz, lahoras en la inscizio de lu es alcuna causa de temor e de paor, e majorment en aquel que es en le ventre.	But if the theil is of great roots, then in the incision of it there is some cause for fear and dread, and even more so in that which is in the belly.
Mays possibla es que tu inscindas la maytat de lu , e aprop cauteriza aquel per que no retorne.	But possible it is that you cut out most of it, and accordingly cauterize that so that it does not return.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanada la plagua.	And accordingly cure that until the wound is healed.
E guarda te que tu no presumas inscidir theil le qual es de fusca color, de pauc sentiment, de leg reguardament, quar aquel es absi cancros.	And beware that you do not presume to cut out a theil which is of dark color, with little sensation, and having no regard, for it is absolutely cancerous.
E yeu vindre am rememoracio de cranc aprop aysso.	And I have found in my recollection a sign accordingly.
Capitol .lii.	Chapter LXII.
De curacio de eminencia del umbilic.	Of the cure of prominence of the navel.
Eminencia del umbilic es fayta per motas causas; o per fissuras del ciphac le qual es sobre le ventre, e yeys de lu la tela o budel segon que endeve en las autras rupturas; o per sanc le qual flueys de vena o de arceria segon que es denant dit, o per ventositat coarctada en lu.	Prominence of the navel is caused by many reasons; or by fissures of the cicatrix which is above the belly, and eyes of it are torn or burst forth according to what develops in other ruptures; or by blood which flows from vein or artery as has been said before, or by ventral constriction.
Mays si es per fissura del ciphac e per yssiment de la tela, lahoras la color del apostema es semblant a la color del cors; e es leon ses dolor, e aprop appar de divers situament.	But if it is due to fissure of the cicatrix and bursting forth of the skin, then the color of the swelling is similar to the color of the body; and there is no great pain, but rather an appearance of diverse situations.
E si es per egressio del budel, lahoras le situament de aquel am lu de aquo que havem recontat, de mays vehement diversitat, e cum tu premes aquel am les tieus ditz es occultat, e aprop retorna; e fort leu es am lu so, e es magnificat mot deves le introt de banh e vehement trebalh.	And if it is due to protrusion of the budel, then the situation of that with water which we have recounted, and with more violent diversity, and as you press that with the said threads it is hidden, and accordingly returns; and very soon it becomes so, and is greatly magnified by the introduction of bath and intense labor.
Mays si per humiditat, lahoras es leon e no es occultat quan premes am la tua ma, ni es constrengut, ni es cregut.	But if due to humidity, then it is so loose and not hidden when you press with your hand, nor is it constricted or creased.
E si es per sanc, lahoras am aquestz senhals apareys le apostema a negror declinant.	And if it is due to blood, then accordingly with these signs the swelling appears declining towards blackness.
Mays si es per carn nada, lahoras es apostema greu, gros e dur, e es ficat segon una quantitat.	But if it is due to nothing but flesh, then accordingly it is a great and large swelling, hard and firm, and fixed according to a quantity.
Mays si es per ventositat, lahoras le tocament de lu es leon.	But if it is due to constriction, then accordingly the touch of it is loose.
E la operacio en lu es que consideras lahoras si la eminencia de l’umbilic es per sanc de arceria, o de vena, o per ventositat; lahoras cove que sias prohibit de la curacio de lu, quar en aquela es temor e paor ayssi cum t’e ensenhat en le capitol en le qual he dit les apostemas per arceria e per vena.	And the operation in this case is that you consider now if the prominence of the navel is due to blood from an artery, or a vein, or constriction; accordingly it is necessary to prohibit the cure of it, because there is fear and dread just as I have taught you in the chapter where I said about swellings caused by arteries and veins.
E si la eminencia del umbilic es per le budel o per la tela, lahoras cove que comandes al malaute que tengua le ale sieu, e sia stant extendut; e aprop senha am tenta en le circuit de tot le umbilic, e aprop comanda a lu que stia envers entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos, e aprop circunda am spatum lat en le circuit del umbilic sobre le loc le qual has senhat am la tenta; e aprop exten la maytat del apostema a las partidas desus am unci gran; e aprop lia en le circuit am fiel fort o am ceda e la manieyra del liar decent.	And if the prominence of the navel is due to the budel or skin, then accordingly you should command the patient to hold his belly in one hand and be standing upright; and accordingly send someone with a tent in the circuit of all the navel, and accordingly command him to stand between your hands on either side of his belly, and accordingly circle with a spatula wide enough around the navel at the place you have marked with the tent; and accordingly extend most of the swelling towards the upper parts with scissors great; and accordingly tie it in the circuit with strong thread or with cord, and the manner of tying decent.
E aprop huebre le mieg del apostema extendut sobre le liament e intromet le dit tieu en aquel indic e quereys le budel; e si tu l’as atrobat ni guardat per le liament, lahoras tu extratz alxorati e impelleys le budel a las partidas dedintz del ventre.	And accordingly make an incision in the middle of the swelling extended over the ligament and introduce the said thread into that indicated and seek out the budel; and if you have not found nor guarded it by the ligament, then you should extract the thread and push the budel towards the parts behind the belly.
E si has atrobada la tela, lahoras pren aquel am unci; e inscideys las superfluitatz de lu.	And if you have found the skin, then accordingly take it with scissors; and cut out the excess parts of it.
Mays si es contraria a tu arceria o vena, lahoras circunda aquel mot, e aprop retorna a la tua operacio; e pren dos agulhas e met en aquelas dos fiels fortz e entromet dos agulhas en le circuit le qual has feyt entorn le apostema en manieyra de crotz, las quals fassas penetrar; e aprop strenh le apostema en quatre partidas sobre las agulhas.	But if it is contrary to your artery or vein, then accordingly circle around that spot, and accordingly return to your operation; and take two needles and insert them into those two strong threads and enter two needles into the circuit which you have made around the swelling in a cross-like manner, which will make them penetrate; and accordingly strengthen the swelling in four parts over the needles.
E si tu vols, osta las agulhas e leyssa le loc entro que poyresca la carn extenduda e caia per si; o inscideys aquel quan es subtiliat e se poyreys, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And if you wish, stop the needles and leave the place until the flesh extended and falls away on its own; or cut it when it is softened and becomes pliable, and accordingly cure that with water as needed until it is healed.
E si la eminencia del ombilic es de carn nada en lu o per humiditat, lahoras cove que tu conquaves le apostema ayssi cum havem dit e estraguas le sanc o la humiditat, la qual atrobas en lu, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove e que consolide le loc.	And if the prominence of the navel is due to flesh or moisture in that place, then accordingly it is necessary for you to conquer the swelling as we have said and remove the blood or moisture which you find there, and accordingly cure that with water as needed and consolidate the place.
Capitol .liii.	Chapter LXIII.
De curacio de cranc.	Of the cure of cancer.
Ja havem dit, en la divisio, de specia de cranc e en qual manieyra es via a la curacio de lu am medicinas, e que es squivador en lu la curacio am ferr per so que no sia ulcerat; e havem dit cranc engendrat en la mayra e cautela de la curacio de lu.	We have already said in the division, about the kind of cancer and how it is to be cured with medicines, and that it is advisable not to use iron for its cure so as not to ulcerate; and we have also said that cancer is generated in the majority of cases through carelessness and caution in its treatment.
E diyssero les antics que alcunas veguadas cranc es en loc on es possibla la eradicacio de lu, ayssi cum de cran le qual es en las mamillas o en la coyssa e a lor semblantz dels membres allocat a estrayre tot aquel, e majorment quan es comensant petit.	And the ancients said that sometimes cancer is in a place where it is possible to eradicate it, just like the cancer which is on the nipples or in the armpits and similar to those members allocated to remove all that, and most of all when it is beginning small.
Mays quan es antiquat e es gra, no cove que te propries a lu, quar yeu non pogui sanar de aquel alcu ni no he vist autre, ni que sia pervengut ad aquo.	But when it is old and great, it is not possible for you to take ownership of it, because you cannot heal from that place or disease, nor have I seen another way, nor one that has reached its end.
E la operacio en lu es quan es allocat ayssi cum havem dit, es que tu precedescas e laysses le malaute e purgues de colera negra alcunas veguadas, e aprop sagna aquel, si es atrobada replecio manifesta.	And the operation in this case is when it is allocated as we have said, which is that you precede and leave the patient and purge with black cholera several times, and accordingly bind up that part if it is found to be manifestly full.
E aprop prepara le malaute am preparacio en le qual sia locat am operacio, e aprop prohiceys en le trauc uncis les quals cove ad aquel; e aprop concava de tota part am la codena sego bona perexcrutacio entro que no romangua alcuna causa de las razitz de lu.	And accordingly prepare the patient with preparation for the operation, and accordingly prohibit from entering the wound with scissors that are needed for that; and accordingly excavate all parts with a cord so good as possible excision, until there remains no cause for the roots of it.
E layssa correr le sanc, e no abscidas aquel leugierament, e exprem les locs, e abstergeys le sanc gros tot am la tua ma o am instrument am le qual es a tu possible dels instruments.	And let the blood flow, and do not cut too deeply, and remove the clots, and wash away the great deal of blood with your hand or with an instrument at your disposal among the instruments.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat de sanc gros inscizio de vena o de arceria, lahoras cauterisa aquela entro que·l flux del sanc sia cessat, e aprop cura aquel am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	But if you find great opposition from the blood flow in an incision of a vein or artery, then accordingly cauterize that place until the bleeding has ceased, and accordingly cure that with another cure until it is healed.
Capitol .liv.	Chapter LXIV.
De curacio de ydropici.	Of the cure of dropsy.
Nos ja havem recomtat, en la divisio, de las specias de ydropici de l’aygua, e les senhals de quascuna especia, de la curacio de lu am medicinas.	We have already recounted, in the division, about the kinds of dropsy caused by water, and the signs of each kind, as well as the cure of it with medicines.
E aquela la qual es curada am ferr no es sino la specia de althitas sola, e no es aproximat am ferr a la specia de timpanistres ni a la especia de yposarcha, quar aquo es mortal.	And that which is cured with iron is not but the species of althitis alone, and it is not approached by iron to the species of timpanists nor to the species of hypoarchae, for this is mortal.
E quan tu ja has medicat aquesta especia de ydropici timpanistre am medicinas e no comfereys la tua medicacio, lahoras considera, quar si al malaute ja es conseguida debelitat, o es am aquel autra malautia otra ydropici, ayssi cum si es en lu tos o cos de ventre e semblant ad aquels, lahoras guarda te que no le mediques am ferr, quar temor es sobre aquo.	And when you have already medicated this species of dropsy timpanistre with medicines and your treatment has not been effective, then accordingly consider, for if the patient is already weakened or has another disease, such as in the lungs or belly and similar to those, then beware that you do not treat it with iron, for fear is great over this.
Mays si tu vezes le malaute de vertut exuberant, e am lu no es autra malautia sino ydropici tant solament, e no enfant ni vielh, lahoras la manieyra de la operacio de lu es que tu eleves le malaute entre las tuas mas, e le ministre aprop lu exprema le ventre de lu am la sua ma, enpellen la aygua a la partida dejos del pentenilh, e aprop pren spatum spinos segon aquesta forma:	But if you find the patient to be in good health, with no other disease but dropsy alone, and not young or old, then accordingly the manner of the operation is that you raise the patient between your hands, and give them appropriate medicine, and empty the belly of water with their own hand, filling the partition next to the pentenilh, and accordingly take a spatula with spines in this form:
sia de dos partz agudas lonc, de aguda extremitat ayssi cum spatum; mays empero sia en lu alcuna brevitat petit a petit, per so que en la operacio am aquel no passes entro al budel, e que ledas aquel.	to be of two sharp parts long, with an acute extremity just like a spatula; but however it should have some brief smallness little by little, in order that in the operation on that part you do not go too far into the belly and leave it there.
E aprop considera si la generacio de ydropici es de part dels budels, quar lahoras cove que tu am la seccio te alonhes del ombelic per la quantitat de tres ditz a las partidas dejos, en le dreyt de lu sobre le pentenilh.	And accordingly consider if the generation of dropsy is from one of the bellies, for then it is necessary that you with the section go away from the navel by three times this distance to the parts left behind, on the right side of the belly over the pentenilh.
Mays si la generacio de hydropici es per malautia del fietge, lahoras la tua seccio sia sinistra del ombilic per tres ditz.	But if the generation of dropsy is due to disease of the liver, then accordingly your section should be on the left side of the navel by three times this distance.
E si la generacio de lu es per la melsa, lahoras la tua seccio sia en le las dreyt.	And if the generation of it is due to the kidneys, then accordingly your section should be on the right side.
E no cove que la tua seccio sia sobre le costat sobre le qual vol jaser le malaute per que no corron las superfluitatz ad aquel loc freul.	And it is not necessary that your section be on the side opposite to which the patient wishes to lie down, so that the superfluous fluids do not flow to that location.
E aprop perfora am le instrument tota la codena, e aprop entromet en aquela seccio, e eleva la tua ma am le spatum entre la codena e·l siphac, e tu excorja aquel; e si’ la quantitat de una ungla o enviro.	And accordingly pierce the entire cord with an instrument, and accordingly enter into that section, and lift your hand with a spatula between the cord and the sphincter, and you excise that part; and if it is about the length of a fingernail or thereabout.
E aprop perforo le ciphac entro que pervengua le spatum al loc vuoyt, e es loc de l’aygua.	And accordingly pierce the sphincter until the spatula reaches the location where the water is.
E aprop extratz aquel e entromet un instrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	And accordingly extract that and enter an instrument which has this shape:
e es semblant a canula de argent subtil; es fayt de argent o de eram o de lato leon, al qual en la partida pus bassa de lu es un petit trauc, e en les costatz de lu so tres traucs: dos de una partida e un del autra partida; e fayta es la extremitat de lu insciza segon la manieyra de pluma, ayssi cum vezes:	and it is similar to a silver tube; it is made of silver or lead or bronze, at which in the lower part of the bottom is a small hole, and on its sides are three holes: two from one side and one from the other side; and the end of it is cut off according to the manner of a feather, just as you see:
E en la extramitat de lu pus sobirana es armilla, quar quan le instrument perve al aygua, lahoras aquela tantost deysen sobre le instrument, donc evacua de l’aygua en la ora miega quantitat, quar si tu evacuas de aquela mes que no cove en la hora, fort leu mor le malaute per resolucio del sieu spirit animal, o accideys a lu cincopi que es appropinquada la mort.	And on the tip of it is a ring, for when the instrument reaches the water, then that ring will immediately be placed over the instrument, therefore evacuating from the water in the middle quantity, lest if you evacuate more than necessary at that time, soon the patient will die from resolution of their animal spirit, or else you will cause them to faint and it is approaching death.
Mays evacua de aquela segon la quantitat de la vertut de lu e segon que significan a tu las disposicios del malaute de la vertut del pols de lu e de la bontat de lu.	But evacuate from it according to the quantity of the virtue of it, and according to what signifies to you the dispositions of the patient's pulse and the goodness of it.
E aprop extrats le instrument, e rete l’aygua la qual causa es quar tantost es retenguda per la codena la qual rete le trauc que es sobre le ciphac del qual e recomtat a tu que perfores aquel segon aquela manieyra.	And accordingly extract the instrument, and retain the water which causes it to be retained by the cord that holds the hole which is above the sphincter of which I have recounted to you that you should pierce it according to this manner.
E aprop itera le instrument al autra dia si vezes le malaute tollerant aquo, e extratz de la aygua petita quantitat, e fay aquo per alcus jorns sobre temor, e guarda te de error entro que no romangua de l’aygua sino pauc.	And accordingly repeat the instrument to the other day if you find that the patient can tolerate this, and extract a small quantity of water, and do so for several days over fear, and beware of mistake until there remains only a little water.
Mays si tu temes sobre le malaute, e leyssas de l’aygua gran quantitat, lahoras cura aquel am sepultura en arena cauda, e mota suzor en banh, e al solelh espere per lonc temps; e cura aquel am medicinas dessicativas entro que sia sanat.	But if you fear for the patient and leave a great quantity of water, then accordingly cure that with burial in hot sand, and moisten with bath, and wait under the sun for a long time; and cure that with desiccative medicines until it is healed.
E cauteriza sobre le stomac, e la melsa e·l fitge aprop la extraccio de l’aygua, segon que yeu he recontat en aquo que es precedit.	And cauterize on the stomach, and the kidneys and liver accordingly with the extraction of water, according to what I have recounted earlier.
Capitol .lv.	Chapter LXV.
De la curacio dels enfants les quals so natz les locs de la urina no-perforatz.	Of the cure of children who are born with undescended kidneys that do not perforate.
Alcunas veguadas alcun dels enfantz es eyssi del ventre de la sua mayre e·l cap de la sua mixtio no es perforat (o es trauc streyt o no es en son loc).	At times, one of the children is born from the womb of its mother and the head of its mixture is not perforated (or has a very narrow hole or is not in its proper place).
Donc cove coytar am perforacio de lu tantost que es nascut am spatum mot subtil segon aquesta forma:	Therefore, it is necessary to perform an operation on the child as soon as it is born with a spatula that is very fine and subtle in this manner:
E aprop pausa en le trauc un clavil subtil de plom e ligua aquel, e te per tres jorns o per .iiii.tre.	And accordingly pause in the hole a small lead clasp and tie it up, and let it stay for three days or four.
E quant vol urinar sia remaugut e hurine; e aprop retorne aquel.	And when it wants to urinate be released and flow; and accordingly return that.
E si tu no pauses le plom, ja es possible que la urina la qual va sobre le loc, no leysa aquest claure.	And if you do not pause the lead, it is possible that the urine which flows onto the place will not close this wound.
Mays aquel del qual le trauc es streyt sia medicat am clavil de Plom, ayssi cum havem dit, per trops dias entro que sia amplificat.	But that of which the hole is narrow should be treated with a lead clasp, just as we have said, for many days until it is enlarged.
Mays aquels en les quals es le trauc no en son loc, so leditz, la qual causa es quar de aquels, aquel que es nat e·l trau es deves la fi del cap de la vergua per que no pot urinar a las partidas dedintz, entro que eleva la vergua am la sua ma a las partidas desus; e no es a lu generacio, per so quar le sperma no pot pervenir a la mayre segon rectitut, e es malautia mot laga.	But those in whom the hole is not in its place are led astray, which cause is because of them, that one who is born and the tract is twisted is due to the end of the head of the scrotum so that it cannot urinate into the parts behind, until it lifts up the scrotum with its hand to the parts above; and it is not a generation, therefore the sperm cannot reach the mother according to rectitude, and it is a disease very grievous.
E la manieyra de la operacio en lu es que·l malaute sia envessat sobre le sieu dos, e aprop exten le cap de la vergua de lu am la tua ma sinistra am vehement extraccio, e inscideys le cap del cap de la vergua del loc del perpucii am spatum agut, ayssi cum es inscizio de pluma, o que tu ne razas alcuna partida, per so que·l mieg de lu vengua semblant al cap de la vergua e que le trauc caia en le mieg loc segon que cove.	And the manner of the operation in this case is that the patient should be placed on his back, and accordingly extend the head of the scrotum with your left hand with a vehement extraction, and cut off the head of the head of the scrotum at the place of the perineum with a sharp spatula, just as one cuts off a feather or some part, so that the middle part of it becomes like the head of the scrotum, and the hole falls into the middle place according to what is necessary.
E guarda te que en la tua operacio de flux de sanc, quar motas vetz accideys aquo; e pausa te a lu am aquo que abscindeys le sanc, e cura la plagua entro que si’ sanada.	And beware that in your operation of blood flow, for many times this happens; and pause at the place where you will cut off the blood, and cure the wound until it is healed.
Capitol .lvi.	Chapter LXVI.
De albater le qual accideys en le prepucii en le cap de la vergua e de corropcio e negror e adherencia del prepucii del cap de la vergua.	Of the disease of which it occurs in the prepuce at the head of the scrotum, and of corruption and blackness and adhesion of the prepuce to the head of the scrotum.
Motas veguadas accideys aquest albater en la vergua e es eminencia de carn laga.	Many times this disease occurs in the scrotum and is a prominence of soft flesh, very grievous.
E de aquela una es maligna e autra es no-maligna.	And one of them is malignant and the other is non-malignant.
No-maligna, cove que suspendas am unci subtil e abscindas aquela entro que aquela mondes tota; e aprop pausa sobre aquela coto submirgit en enguent egipciac; e aprop aquel, cura le am enguent diafinicon entro que sia sanat.	Non-malignant, requires that you suspend it with a fine thread and cut off the part until all the excess is removed; and accordingly pause above the wound covered in Egyptian ointment; and accordingly treat it with ointment day by day until it is healed.
E si albater es maligna, de lega color, lahoras cove que tu aministres cauteri aprop la inscizio de lu e la razio de lu.	And if the disease is malignant, with dark color, then accordingly you should administer caustics around the incision and the edge of it.
Mays si albater es en le prepuci del cap de la vergua no-circumcis, e la una partida de albater es dedintz le prepucii e l’autra partida es defora, lahoras cove que tu ostes albater le qual es dedintz al comensament entro que es consolidat; e lahora tu cura aquel deforo, quar quan tu curas aquel ensemps le prepuci, no es asegurat que no sia trinquat.	But if the disease is in the prepuce of the head of the scrotum that is not circumcised, and one part of the disease is inside the prepuce and the other part is outside, then accordingly you should remove the diseased part that is inside first, until it is consolidated; and then you will cure that which is outside, for when you cure that together with the prepuce, it is not certain that it will not be torn.
E ja eysamen accideys en les genetius e en le prepuci negror e corruccio, adonc cove que tu conquavas tot aquo que ja es denigrat e que ja se vol corrompre o que ja es corrumput; e aprop lineys sobre aquel aprop aquo am mel, le qual es contusit am farina de scorsa de milgrana e de errs trissatz e crivellatz.	And thus also it occurs in the genitals and in the prepuce blackness and corruption, therefore you should conquer all that which is already corrupted and which already wishes to corrupt or has already been corrupted; and accordingly line over that with a mixture of honey and flour made from scoria of millet grain and well-crushed and well-sifted errors.
E aprop cura aquel am l’autra curacio entro que sia sana.	And accordingly cure that with the other treatment until it is healed.
Mays si endeve flux de sanc, lahoras aministra cauteri lunar segon aquesta forma:	But if there is excessive bleeding, then accordingly administer lunar caustics in this manner:
quar cauteri juvatiu es a dos disposicios ensemps, so es a flux de sanc e a la plagua quan es corrumpuda.	for lunar caustics are beneficial in two dispositions together, namely in bleeding and in the wound when it is corrupted.
E si le cap de la vergua es corrodut e es destruit tot en la hora, lahoras cove que tu intrometas en lo meat del prepucii una canula de plom per so que le malaute urina per aquela.	And if the head of the scrotum is corroded and destroyed entirely in an hour, then accordingly you should insert a lead tube into the meatus of the prepuce, so that the patient may urinate through it.
En la adherencia del prepucii am le cap de la vergua (et aquesta adherencia no accideys sino en aquel del qual le prepucii es sa, e sobre lu no es exhigida circumcizio; e quan accideys adherencia per plagua o per apostema) cove que excorjas am spatum obtus entro que sia dissolvut le liament e sia deliurat le cap de la vergua de tota partida.	In the adhesion of the prepuce to the head of the scrotum (and this adhesion only occurs in one whose prepuce is thick and no circumcision has been performed; and when adhesion occurs due to wound or abscess) you should excise with a blunt spatula until the bond is dissolved and the head of the scrotum is freed from all part.
E si es dificil desirnir aquelas exquisidament, lahoras cove que tu excorjes am spatum alcuna causa del cap de la vergua e del prepucii, e aysso es quar le prepucii, quan es subtil, fort leu es perforat per la sua subtilitat leugierament.	And if it is difficult to excise them precisely, then accordingly you should excise with a spatula some cause from the head of the scrotum and the prepuce, and thus is why the prepuce, when thin, is perforated by its own subtlety little by little.
E aprop separa entre·l prepucii e·l cap de la vergua am dra7 de li subtil, le qual ja es mulhat en l’aygua frega per que no adherescan autra veguada.	And accordingly separate between the prepuce and the head of the scrotum with a thread of fine silk, which has been moistened in water so that they do not adhere to each other again.
E aprop sia curat am vi stiptic entro que sia consolidat.	And accordingly be treated with vinegar spirits until it is consolidated.
Capitol .lvii.	Chapter LVII.
De mundificacio dels enfants e de la curacio de aquo que accideys ad aquels de circumcisio.	Of the purification of children and the treatment of that which occurs in them after circumcision.
Circumcisio no es solucio de continuitat ayssi cum las autras plaguas: mays empero cum sia de la nostra operacio e de nostra voluntat, e lus de aquela sia propriament en les enfants, es necessari que asignem en aquela milhor operacio e via pus leugiera perdusent a salut.	Circumcision is not a solution of continuity like other wounds: but rather it is a part of our operation and our will, and its purpose is properly in children. It is necessary that we assign the best possible operation and way to proceed, losing no time for the sake of health.
Donc dic que les antics no diyssero circumcisio en alcu dels lors libres, quar no n’usan en las suas leys, e no es sino quar havem aquisit per speriment, la qual causa es que yeu he atrobat la major partida dels artifexs e dels barbies usar circumcisir e mundificacio am novacula e am torores; e usan de liament am fiel e de inscizio am la ungla.	Therefore, I say that the ancients did not dictate circumcision in any of their free books, for they did not use it in their laws, and it is only because we have acquired it through experience, which is why you have found that most of the artisans and barbers use circumcision and purification with a razor and with fire; and they use a thread to bind and an incision to mark.
E yeu ja he prohadas totas aquestas manieras e no atrobegui milhor mondificacio am forfexs, am liament am fiel que en mondificacio cum la ungla, quar motas vetz efugeys la codena pus desus, quar la codena del prepucii a dos tunicas, e roman la tonica pus dejos, e fort leu es forsat ad autra inscizio e dolor sicura.	And I have already forbidden all these methods and did not find better purification with razors, with thread and fire that is like the mark of a finger, because many times the cord above has been cut off, since the cord of the prepuce has two tunics, and the tone below remains, and it is soon forced to another incision and certain pain.
E am mundificacio le qual es fayta per alphecati, e es digital, del qual usan les sabatiers, no es segurada la inscizio de la extremitat del membre viril, quar fort leu intra en le trau de lu.	And in purification made by the Alphatecians, which is digital, and used by the surgeons, it is not ensured that the incision of the extremity of the male member is secure, because soon it will enter into the tract of it.
Mays en la operacio am ungla, fort leu obazeys ferr e corromp la tua operacio.	But in the operation with a finger, iron soon causes obstruction and corrupts your operation.
E la codena del enfant es breu per natura, e motas veguadas nays en tal manieyra que no ha necessitat de mondificacio, e yeu he vist aquel.	And the cord of the child is short by nature, and many times they are born in such a way that there is no need for purification, and I have seen this.
Mays de la mondificacio que·s fa am forfexs e liamentz am fiel, la bontat, experiment descrobic a mi, quar las forfexs so de proporcional inscizio, per aquo quar la acuitat que es desus es ayssi cum la acuitat que es dejos; e donc cum tu premes la tua ma so proporcionadas dos acuitatz, e inscideysso segon una comperacio en un temps; e es fayta compressio del fiel am figura contenent la codena de la vergua de tota partida, am le qual no catz error de tot.	But from the purification that is made with razors and threads and fire, I have discovered by experience that it is not good, for the razors are of proportionate incision, so that the sharpness above is as sharp as the sharpness below; and therefore when you press your hand so proportionally two sharpnesses, and inscribe them together in a single moment; and it is made a compression of the thread with a figure containing the cord of the scrotum on all sides, with which there is no error at all.
E la manieyra de la operacio primeyra es que tu fassas estar le enfant majorment si es de aquels que entendo un petit, que no fassas sino que tu lies le fiel en la sua vergua tant solament, e que leysses aquel entro al autra dia.	And the manner of the first operation is that you should make the child as comfortable as possible, especially if it is one of those who understand little; and do not do more than simply tie the thread in its scrotum so tightly that it will not come undone until the next day.
E aprop fay aquel alegrar en tota aquela manieyra que es a tu possibla de aquo que recep la sua intelligencia.	And accordingly make the child happy in all that manner which is possible to you, according to how it receives its intelligence.
E aprop fa aquel estar entre las tuas mas estatuir preparadament, e no sia ges cezent; e occulta las forfexs en la tua ma o dejos le tieu pe, que l’enfant no veia aquelas ni degun autre dels instruments.	And accordingly make the child sit between your hands most carefully prepared, and not be at all anxious; and conceal the razors in your hand or beneath your cloak, so that the child does not see those nor any other of the instruments.
E aprop entremet la tua ma a la vergua de lu e suffla en la codena, e tira aquela entro que sia eyssit le cap de la vergua, e aprop mondifica aquel de aquo que es agregat en ela de sordicia.	And accordingly place your hand on the scrotum of him and blow into the cord, and pull it in until it is reached the head of the scrotum; and accordingly purify that which has accumulated there through impurities.
E aprop lia le loc signat am fiel dobla, e aprop ligua pus bas de aquel un petit le segon liament, e aprop te am le dit pous e endic tieu le loc del liament dejos am bona retencio, e inscideys entre dos liaments.	And accordingly tie the marked spot with double thread, and accordingly bind another small thread below that as a second ligature; and accordingly take care of the said point and indicate to yourself the location of the left ligature with good retention, and inscribe between two ligatures.
E aprop eleva la codena sus leugierament e estratz le cap de la vergua; e aprop leyssa le sanc corre petit e petit, quar es milhor ; e pausa polvera desus e sobre la polvera pausa drap en le qual es spandut mugol de huou coyt en ayguaros concosit am oli rozat recent bo; e layssa aquel sobre aquel entro al autra dia; e cura aquel am curacio entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly lift the cord slightly and extract the head of the scrotum; and accordingly let the blood flow little by little, for it is better; and pause powdered powder above and on top of the powdered powder, and pause a cloth in which is spread a yolk of hen cooked in water with roasted oil recently boiled; and lay that over that until the next day; and cure that with treatment until it is healed.
La forma de las forfexs a mondificacio, aquesta es la forma:	The form of the razors for purification, this is the form:
Sian las unas extramitatz no-talhantz e las autras sian talhant, que non sia yssit le ram del clau, e sia la longitut de las doas acuitatz ayssi cum la longitut de dos manubres engualment.	May the outer edges not be cutting and the other side be cutting, so that there is no space left at the tip of the claw, and may the length of both sharpnesses be as long as the length of two arms equally.
Mays la error en mundificacio es quar fort leu efugeys la codena intrinseca tota, o partida de lu deves la inscizio.	But the error in purification is that soon you will cut away the entire inner cord or a part of it, which should be incised.
Donc cove que tu extendas aquela de la tua hora am la tua ungla denant la apostemacio del loc e que inscidas aquela segon equalitat.	Therefore, I say that you should stretch that of your hour with your finger before the abscess of the wound and incise it according to equality.
E si no la podes tenir am la tua ungla, lahoras extratz aquela am unci e inscideys aquela.	And if you cannot hold it with your finger, then accordingly extract that with a thread and incise it.
Mays si son passatz tres dias, e roman aquo que es imflat dejos la vergua apostemat, lahoras tu leyssa aquo entro que sia cedat le apostema caut, e excorja aquel am fecilitat, e inscidex aquel segon que a tu es preparat.	But if three days have passed and the abscess has not burst open below the scrotum, then accordingly you should let it be until the abscess is fully formed, and excise that with ease, and incise that according to what is prepared for you.
E guarda te del cap de la vergua, quar no nosera a lu aquo.	And beware of the head of the scrotum, for it will not be affected by this.
E donc cura aquel am aquo que la plagua consolida de las polveras las quals havem recomtadas en le tractat de las polveras.	And thus cure that with the powder that has been consolidated, according to the recipes that we have recounted in the treatise on powders.
E si es inscidit de la codena sobre mesura, e obezeys a las partidas desus, aquo no notz a lu.	And if it is incised according to measure, and obeys the parts above, this will not be noticeable.
E mays cura aquel am aquo que havem dit entro que sia sanat.	And thus cure that with what we have said until it is healed.
Capitol .lviii.	Chapter LVIII.
De curacio de urina retenguda en la vesiqua.	Of the treatment of retained urine in the bladder.
Retencio de urina en la vesica es fayta per oppulacio fayta per peyra o per sanc congilat, o per poyre o per carnada, e semblantz ad aquels de aquo que havem dit de las manieyras de curacio en la divisio.	Retention of urine in the bladder is caused by obstruction made by a stone or by pressure or by congealed blood or by polyp or by fleshiness, and resembles those cases that we have described above in the division of methods for treating.
E si no es dissolvuda la urina, e veses retencio de lu esser per peyra le qual ja es en le col de la vesica, lahoras cove que le malaute sia encorbat sobre les sieus denolhs.	And if the urine is not dissolved and retention of it is seen to be caused by a stone which is already in the neck of the bladder, then accordingly the patient should be bent over his own knees.
E aprop conponeys les pes de aquel sobre le sieu dos e extendas le sieu ventre de la partida pus desus del sieu dos, e le malaute estrengua le sieu ale tant quant es a lu possible.	And accordingly compress the stones on that over his own back and stretch out his belly from the upper part of his back to his knees, and the patient should strain his arm as much as possible towards him.
Donc lahoras le col de la vesica es costreyt ha espulsio de la peyra a las partidas detras, per que la urina es absolta.	Therefore, the neck of the bladder is constricted to expulsion of the stone at the rear parts, so that the urine is released.
E si no es dissolvuda am aquo que havem dit he vehement es fayta la causa sobre le malaute, lahoras cove que aministres extraccio de lu am instrument le qual es apelat siringua, del qual aquesta es la forma: Sia de argent e sia subtil leon conquau, ayssi cum canula de pena de ausel am subtilitat de ray lonc en similitut d’un palm e mig, al qual sia cana subtil en le cap de lu.	And if it is not dissolved with what we have said, the cause is vehement and made to affect the patient, then accordingly you should administer extraction from him with an instrument called a syringe, of which this is the form: It should be of silver and very thin, like a quill pen, with a subtlety of length about a palm and a half, and at its tip should be a fine thread.
E la manieyra del eyssiment de la urina per aquel es que prenguas le fiel doblat e lies en la extramitat de lu lana o coto per bona liadura; e entrometas las extramitatz del fiel en la partida dejos de la ciringua, e inscideys am las forfexs si superflueys alcuna causa de la lana, mays intromet la en la canula am vehemencia E aprop enongeys la ciringua am boder e am album de huou.	And the method of extracting urine with that is to take a double thread and tie it in the extremity of the lanolin or fat for good binding; and insert the extremities of the thread into the posterior part of the syringe, and inscribe with razors if there is any superfluous cause of the fat, but introduce it into the syringe with vehemence. And accordingly fill the syringe with border and album of hen.
E fay cezer le malaute sobre la selha, e embroca la vesiqua de lu e la vergua am olis umitz, e oli de oliva e ayguaros.	And cause the patient to sit on a stool, and insert the syringe into his bladder and scrotum with olive oil and water.
E aprop entromet la ciringua am facilitat entro que pervengua a la razit de la vergua; e aprop dobla la vergua desus a la partida del embelic; e aprop empelleys la ciringua dintz aquela; e aprop empelleys aquela entro que pervengua a la vesica, e aquela centa le malaute esser pervenguda a la causa vuoda, e no es fayt asso segon aquest orde, sino le meat en le qual va a tortuositat.	And accordingly insert the syringe with ease until it reaches the root of the scrotum; and accordingly double the scrotum above at the part of the navel; and accordingly push the syringe into that; and accordingly push that in until it reaches the bladder, and let the patient be pervaded by the cause, and not made to go according to this order, but rather the way in which it goes to tortuosity.
E aprop exten le fiel am la lana petit a petit, quar la urina siec la lana.	And accordingly stretch the thread with the lanolin little by little, for the urine will absorb the lanolin.
Aprop extratz aquela e fay per curacio urina, e usa ciringua, no cesses fer aquo e usa ciringua entro que sia evacuada la vesica e le malaute atrobe alleviacio.	And accordingly extract that and make it for urine cure, and use the syringe, do not cease to do so until the bladder is evacuated and the patient attains relief.
Capitol .lix.	Chapter LIX.
De qualitat de clisterizacio de la vezica am clampcedra e am semblantz instrumentz les quals sian acordants ad aquo.	Of the quality of catharticization of the bladder with celandine and similar instruments which are suitable for this.
Quan accideys en la vesica ulceracio o apostema, o sanc congilat en aquela, o es coartat poyredura, e vols en aquela destillar ayguas e medicinas, lahoras sia fayt am instrument le qual es apelat clampcedra, e aquesta es la forma de lu:	When ulceration or abscess occurs in the bladder, or congealed blood is present in it, or the pungent juice is coagulated, and you want to make waters and medicines distill there, then accordingly use an instrument called celandine, and this is its form:
sino que en la extramitat de lu es sorda, so es clausa.	but in the extremity of it is deaf, that is to say, closed.
Et en aquela so tres traucs: dos de la una partida , ayssi quo vezes.	And in that there are three holes: two on one side, like that times.
En le comensament es loc concau, en le qual es aquo que es enpellit, e sia segon quantitat que oppile aquel, ses addicio, entro que quan alcuna causa es ab aquel tirada de las humiditatz, sia atirada, e quan es expellida, am aquo sia atirada, e quan es expellit lonc, segon que fa clampcedra am la qual es phicat naphta en las batalhas de mar.	In the beginning it is a hollowed-out place, in which is contained the water that is poured in, and it should be according to the quantity that fills it, without addition, until when some cause is pulled out by it from the humidities, it is pulled out, and when it is expelled long, the water is pulled out, as if it were a celandine, which is filled with naphtha in the battles of the sea.
Donc cum tu vols prohicir humiditatz en la vesica, entromet la extremitat de clapcedra en la humiditat, e atira am aquel aquo que es empellit a las partidas desus, quar la humiditat es atirada en la conquavitat de clapcedra.	Therefore, when you want to extract humidities from the bladder, insert the extremity of celandine into the humidity, and pull out with it the water that is poured in above, because the humidity is pulled out into the hollow of celandine.
E aprop entromet la extramitat de clapcedra en la vergua segon que havem recomtat en la ciringua; e aprop empelleys la humiditat am aquo que empelleys, quar aquela humiditat perve a la vesica tantost, e le malaute cent aquela.	And accordingly insert the extremity of celandine into the scrotum according to what we have recounted in the syringe; and accordingly pour in the humidity with water that pours in, because that humidity will reach the bladder soon, and the patient will be relieved.
Forma del cristeri subtil am le qual la vesica es cristerizada, e es aquela la forma:	Form of the subtle catheter by which the bladder is catheterized, and this is its form:
E sia fayta de argent o de lato, de la qual le cap pus aut sia semblant a petita pluma, e dejos lu cana dedintz liament.	And it should be made of silver or lead, of which the tip most up is similar to a small feather, and below it has a thread-like canal.
E aprop pren vesica de moto, e pausa en aquela la humiditat que vols cristirizar en la vesica, e aprop lia aquela entre dos am fort liguatura am fiel doble, e escalfa aquela humiditat sobre le foc.	And accordingly take the bladder in motion, and put into it the humidity that you want to catheterize in the bladder, and accordingly tie that between two with a strong ligature of double thread, and heat that humidity over the fire.
E aprop entromet la extremitat del cristeri en la vergua.	And accordingly insert the extremity of the catheter into the scrotum.
E aprop estrenh la tua ma sobre la vesica am la humiditat am strectura descent entro que·l malaute centa que aquela humiditat ja es pervenguda a la vesica.	And accordingly stretch your hand over the bladder with the humidity, and slowly descend into it until the patient feels that that humidity has already reached the bladder.
Mays si a tu no es present vesica, lahoras tu pren una pessa de parguames e fay de aquel cercle; e perfora aquel de tota la sua retonditat; e aprop entromet fiel fort en aquels traucs, ayssi quo so revolgut; e aprop agregua le cercle ayssi quo es agreguat alsofatur, pus que tu pausas en aquel aquo que tu vols de las humiditatz, e olis e ayguas.	But if the bladder is not present to you, then accordingly take a piece of parchment and make from it a circle; and perforate that all over its entire roundness; and accordingly insert a strong thread into those holes, so that they are revolved; and accordingly add the circle as it has been added before, so that you put in that which you want of humidities, oils, and waters.
E aprop tu lia aquel en le instrument e fay am aquel ayssi cum has fayt am la vesica, e exprescio am la tua ma entro que la humiditat pervengua a la vesica.	And accordingly tie that in the instrument and make it as you have made it with the bladder, and express it with your hand until the humidity reaches the bladder.
Capitol .lx.	Chapter LX.
De extraccio de peyra.	Of the extraction of stones.
Nos ja havem dit en la divisio las specias de peyra e curacio de lu am medicinas, e la diferencia entre peyra engendrada en los ronhos e peyra engendrada en la vesica, e les senhals de aquela.	We have already said in the division the species of stones and their cure with medicines, and the difference between stones generated in the lungs and stones generated in the bladder, and the signs of these.
E havem dit la peyra en la qual catz operacio am ma, e seccio.	And we have said that stone which catches operation with my hands and section.
E la peyra engendrada en la vesica propriament es aquela que es ficada en la vesica.	And the stone generated in the bladder properly is that which is formed in the bladder.
E yeu so narrant aquel am exposicio manifesta e abreviacio.	And you show it with a clear and brief explanation.
Donc dic que peyra engendrada en la vesica majorment ve als enfantz; e dels senhals de lu es que la urina que es eyssida de la vesica es semblant a aygua en la sua subtilitat, e apar en aquela arena; e le malaute fregua la sua vergua, e motas veguadas pen, e aprop es dressada; e am aquo yeys foro le cul en motz de aquels.	And I say that the stone generated in the bladder is most common among children; and one of its signs is that the urine that flows from the bladder is similar to water in subtlety, and appears in that sand; and the patient feels his scrotum, and many times pain, and accordingly is dressed; and with this, you will find the anus full of those.
E es laugiera la sanacio dels enfants de aquela entro que han conseguitz xiiii ans; e es dificil curacio en les viels.	And it is easier to cure children of that until they have reached the age of 14 years; and it is difficult to cure in the elderly.
Mays en les joves es migiera per aquo quar es entre aquels.	But in young people it is more common because it is between them.
E de aquel del qual la peyra es major e la curacio es pus leugiera; E si es pauca, es contraria ad aquela.	And of that from which the stone is greater and the cure is easier; And if it is small, it is contrary to that.
Donc cum pervenem a la curacio de aquela, cove al comensament de aquela que mondifiquem le malaute am cristeri le qual extragua tota la fenda la qual es en les sieus budels; quar aquela fenda alcunas veguadas prohibeys la envencio de la peyra deves la inquisicio de lu.	And therefore, when we come to the cure of that, it is necessary at first to purify the patient with a catheter which extracts all the crack that is in his veins; for that crack sometimes hinders the formation of the stone and makes it difficult to detect.
E aprop sia pres le malaute am les sieus pes e sia contosit e maugut enjos per so que la peyra descenda al preon de la vesica, o que saute de loc aut alcunas veguadas.	And accordingly, the patient should be placed on his knees and supported by assistants for such a reason that the stone may descend to the bottom of the bladder, or else jump from one place to another at times.
E aprop fay aquel cezer entre las tuas mas preparat, e las mas de lu sian dejos las coysas de lu, per so que la vesica tota sia fayta declinant a las partidas dejos.	And accordingly, make the patient sit between your hands that are prepared, and the things of him should be left aside, for such reason that the bladder may be made to decline towards the posterior parts.
E aprop perquier aquela e tota aquela deforo.	And accordingly, make sure that everything is done outside.
Donc si sentes la peyra en l’espazi, lahoras tu te coyta tantost am seccio sobre lu.	So if you feel the stone in space, then accordingly you should sit down quickly with section on him.
E si no catz de tot dejos le tieu tocament, lahoras cove que tu untes am oli le tieu dit indic de la ma sinistra, si malaute es enfant, o le dit miga si es jove complit, e entrometas aquel en le sieu cul.	And if you do not catch the stone completely, then accordingly it is necessary that you anoint with oil your right hand indicated by your left hand, if the patient is a child, or the middle finger if he is a young adult, and insert that into his anus.
E perquier de la peyra entro que stia dejos le tieu dit.	And accordingly, extract the stone until it comes out of your right hand.
E converteys aquela petit a petit entro al col de la vesica.	And convert that little by little into the neck of the bladder.
E aprop prem sobre aquel am lo tieu dit, e expelleys aquel a las partidas defora ves le loc del qual vos la seccio.	And accordingly press upon it with your right hand and push that out to the posterior parts outside the location where you made the incision.
E comanda al ministra que prema la vesica am la sua ma; e comanda a un autra ministra que am la sua ma dextra extenda les genetius a las partidas desus, e am la sua autra ma remaugua la codena la qual es dejos les genetius, en partida del loc en le qual se fa la seccio.	And command the assistant to press on the bladder with her right hand; and command another assistant to extend her left hand upwards towards the posterior parts, and with her other hand to hold the cord which is below the genitourinary area, in the location where the incision is being made.
E aprop entromet espatum be inscident del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And accordingly insert the spatula which is incident of this form:
e scindeys en lu aquo que es entre·l cul e·ls genetius, no en le mieg loc, abantz al latz de la coyssa sinistra; e sia la seccio sobre aquela peyra e·l tieu dit sia en le cul, e sia fayta seccio transversa, per que la seccio defora sia ampla e dedintz streyta segon la quantitat que egrecio de la peyra sia a lu possibla, e no major, quar fort leu comprem le tieu dit le qual es en le cul la peyra deves la seccio, e es foro-getada ses defacultat.	And accordingly insert the spatula which is incident of this form: and cut into it that which is between the anus and the genitourinary area, not in the middle location, but rather before the left side of the cleft; and make the incision on that stone and your right hand be in the anus, and make a transverse incision so that the incision outside is wide and straight as possible according to the amount that you have extracted from the stone, and not greater, for fear that the stone may be compressed by your right hand which is in the anus, and it will be forgotten without difficulty.
E sapias que de la peyra es alcuna a la qual so angle e margers, per que le eyssiment de lu es fayt deficil per aquo.	And know that from the stone some parts are angled and rough, for which the extraction of it is made difficult by this.
E de aquela aquo es leon semblant a glan, e es redonda, e es fayt de lu leugier eyssiment.	And from that water there comes forth something resembling a small glass, and it is rounded, and it makes the extraction of it easier.
Donc si es aquela al qual so angles e marger, ajusta en la fissura.	So if it is one with angles and roughness, adjust it in the cleft.
E si no es ayssi foro-getada, lahoras cove que tu engenes sobre aquel, o que strenguas sobre aquel am gesti decentment, la extremitat del qual sia ayssi cum lima am le qual strenguas sobre la peyra, e no evasesca de lu; o que entrometas dejos lu instrument subtil de curvada extremitat.	And if it is not so, then accordingly you should press upon it, or stretch upon it with decent gestures, the extremity of which is like a file upon which you press upon the stone, and do not let it escape from there; or that you insert below it a subtle instrument with curved extremity.
Mays si tu no podes sobre aquel, lahoras tu amplifica le trauc un petit, e si tu veus flux de sanc, abscindeys en strenh aquel am vitriol trissat.	But if you cannot press upon it, then accordingly you should widen the hole a little, and if you see a flow of blood, cut into it with great strength using vitriol mixed with vinegar.
Mays si la peyra es mays de una, lahoras al comensament tu impelleys la ma a la boca de la vesica, e aprop inscideys sobre lu; e aprop impelleys un petit aprop aquo; e semblantment fay si son motas mays de doas.	But if the stone is larger than one, then accordingly at first you should push your hand into the mouth of the bladder and inscribe upon it; and accordingly push a little further away; and similarly do so if there are many more than two.
E si es peyra mot gran, lahoras ignorancia es que tu inscidas aquel am gran seccio, quar accideys al malaute una de doas causas: o que mora o que endevengua a lu destillacio de urina continuabla, per aquo quar le loc no es de tot consolidat.	And if the stone is very large, then accordingly ignorance is that you inscribe it with a great incision, for two things will happen to the patient: either he will die or he will be afflicted with continuous urination, and therefore the location will not be fully consolidated.
Mays aministra expulcio de lu entro que sia fora-getada, o engenia en la fractura de lu am las forfexs entro que extragua aquela en pessas.	But administer expulsion from there until it is forgotten, or generate in the fracture of it with razors until that stone is extracted in pieces.
Donc cum tu auras cumplit la tua opperacio, lahoras omple la plagua de enses de aloe e de sanc de drago, e strenh aquel.	And therefore, when you have completed your operation, then accordingly fill the wound with the juice of aloe and dragon's blood, and strengthen that.
E pausa sobre aquel drap enfus en oli e vi, o en oli rozat e aygua frega, per so que apostema caut sia cedat.	And pause over that cloth soaked in oil and vinegar, or in rosated oil and water, for such reason that the abscess may be calmed.
E aprop resupina le malaute sobre le sieu col, e no deslias le liament entro al tertz dia.	And accordingly repose the patient on his back, and do not release the bandage for three days.
E cum aquel auras desliat, embroca le loc am aygua e mot oli, e aprop cura aquel am enguent diafinicon e am enguent diabazilicon entro que sia sanat.	And when you have released that, dress the wound with water and much oil, and accordingly cure it with diaphrenic ointment and diabasilic ointment until it is healed.
Mays si en la plagua accideys apostema caut, adhust e corrosiu, e de aquel semblantz ayssi cum si le sanc es en la vesica congelat, e per lu es la hurina prohibida (e aquo es conogut per la egressio del sanc am urina), a donc entromet lo tieu dit en la plagua e extratz aquel sanc, quar si roman provoca la vesica a corropcio de la vesica e de lu putrefaccio.	But if in the wound there occurs an abscess that is hot, swollen, and corrosive, and it seems as if the blood is congealed in the bladder, and by this means the urine is prevented (and this is known through the egression of blood with urine), then accordingly insert your right hand into the wound and extract that blood, for if it remains, it will provoke the bladder to corruption and putrefaction.
E aprop lava la plagua am vi agre, aygua e sal, e am opposicio a tota specia, am aquo que conveneys a lu de la curacio entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly wash the wound with vinegar, water, and salt, and with opposition to all species, with what is suitable for the cure until it is healed.
E cove en las horas de tota la curacio que tu lies amdos las coyssas e ajustes las medicinas las quals so pausadas sobre le loc.	And accordingly in all the hours of the cure, you should lie down and adjust the medicines that are paused over the wound.
E si la peyra es petita e es en le meat de la vergua, e es ficat en lu, e eyssement de urina es prohibit, lahoras cura aquel am aquo que yeu recomti denant que pervenguas a seccio, quar tropas veguadas per aquesta curacio yest acusat de seccio; e ja yeu e esproat aquo, e es que tu prenguas un perforador de ferr alfelut, del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And if the stone is small and is in the midst of the scrotum, and it is fixed there, and urine flow is prohibited, then accordingly cure that with what you have recommended before you proceed to section, for many times this cure is accused of being a section; and now I have already tried that, and it is that you take a perforator made of iron alfelut, of which this is the form:
de triangulada extramitat, agut, ficat en fust.	of triangular extremity, sharp, fixed in wood.
E aprop pren fiel, e lia am aquel la vergua dejos la peyra per so que no retorne a la vesica.	And accordingly take a thread, and tie it around the scrotum below the stone so that it does not return to the bladder.
E aprop entromet le ferr en la vergua, perforant am fecilitat entro que·l perforador vengua ad aquela peyra.	And accordingly insert the iron into the scrotum, piercing with ease until the perforator comes out to that stone.
E revolveys le perforador am la tua ma en aquela peyra petit a petit, e tu perforsa la perforacio de lu entro que fassas aquel del autra part penetrar; quar la urina tantost es absolta.	And accordingly turn the perforator with your hand in that stone little by little, and you pierce the perforation of it until you make it pass to the other side penetrate; for soon after the urine is released.
E aprop prem la tua ma sobre aquo que es romas de la peyra de la partida deforo de la vergua, quar aquela es trinquada, e es foro-getada am la urina, e le malaute es sanat.	And accordingly press your hand on the part of the stone that remains outside the scrotum, because it is stuck, and it is forgotten with the urine, and the patient is healed.
Mays si aquesta curacio no es a tu aparelhada per alcuna causa la qual prohibeys de aquela, lahoras lia un fiel dejos la peyra, e autra fiel desus la peyra.	But if this cure is not prepared for you by any cause that prohibits it, then accordingly tie a thread below the stone, and another thread above the stone.
E aprop encideys sobre la peyra en aquela vergua entre doas liaduras.	And accordingly inscribe upon the stone in that scrotum between two ligatures.
E aprop extratz aquela.	And accordingly extract that.
E aprop deslia le liament e mondifica le sanc congilat, le qual es fayt en la plagua.	And accordingly release the ligature and purify the congealed blood which is formed in the wound.
E no es necessari liament de fiel dejos la peyra, sino per que no retorne a la vesica, e l’autre liament desus sino, quar quan es desliat le fiel aprop la egrecio de la peyra, la codena retorna a son loc e cobra la plagua.	And it is not necessary to tie the thread below the stone, except that it does not return to the bladder, and the other ligature above, because when the thread is released near the extraction of the stone, the cord returns to its place and closes the wound.
E per aquo es a tu necessari quan lias le fiel desus, que tu eleves la codena a las partidas desus, o que retorne deves le tieu compliment, e cobra la plagua ayssi co havem dit.	And therefore it is necessary for you when you have tied the thread above, that you lift the cord to the upper parts, or else return with your right hand and close the wound just as we have said.
Capitol .lxi.	Chapter LXI.
De extraccio de peyra de las femnas.	Of the Extraction of Stone in Women.
Peyra en las femnas pauc es engendrada.	Stone in women is rarely generated.
Mays si ve peyra ad alcuna de aquelas, lahoras dificil es la curacio de lu, e es prohibida per tropas manieyras.	But if one does see stone in some of them, then accordingly the cure is difficult and is prohibited by many methods.
La una de lor es quar la femna fort leu es verges.	One of those reasons is that the woman herself is very stubborn.
E la segonda es quar tu no trobas femna be scient que descroba si meteyssa al metge quan es casta, o es de las femnas haventz maritz.	And the second reason is that you do not find a woman who knows how to behave herself well when she meets with a doctor, or is one of those women who have husbands.
La tersa es quar tu no hatrobas femna be sabent aquesta art, majorment la operacio am ma.	The third reason is that you do not find a woman who knows this art, especially the operation with hand.
E la quarta es que·l loc de la seccio sobre peyra en las femnas es longinc del loc de la peyra, per que indigeys de seccio preonda, e en aquela es temor.	And the fourth reason is that the location of the section on stone in women is far from the location of the stone, so you need a prolonged section, and in that there is fear.
Mays si necessitat provoca a tu ad aquo, lahoras cove que tu prenguas una femna metga be scient, e pauc es atrobada.	But if necessity demands it of you to this, then accordingly it is necessary that you take a woman who is well-behaved and not easily frightened.
Mays si tu es privat de aquela, lahoras cerca metga quast e subtil, o presenta una femna matrona be esenhada en le feyt de las femnas, o femna que en aquesta art ennueys partida del art.	But if you are deprived of that, then accordingly look for a woman who is quick and subtle, or present a mature woman well-experienced in the nature of women, or a woman who has made progress in this art.
Donc fay aquela present, e comanda a lu que fassa tot aquo que tu li mandaras, de la enquisicio sobre la peyra al comensament; la qual causa es que reguarde si la femna es verges, lahoras cove que meta lo sieu dit en le cul de lu e quiera la peyra.	Therefore present that, and command it to do all that you will tell it, from the inquiry about the stone to the beginning; which cause is that it should see if the woman is a virgin, then accordingly place your right hand in her anus and seek out the stone.
Donc si atroba aquela, coarte aquela dejos le sieu dit, e lahoras comanda a lu que inscida sobre aquela.	Therefore if you find it, cut it below your right hand, and then command it to inscribe upon that.
Mays si no es verge, lahoras comanda a la matrona que entrometa lo sieu dit en le conh de la malauta e enquiera sobre la peyra, pus que pausa la sua ma sinistra sobre la vesica, e comprem aquela am bona comprecio.	But if she is not a virgin, then accordingly command the matron to insert her right hand into the private parts of the patient and inquire about the stone, since she will place her left hand on the bladder and compress it with good compression.
Donc si atroba aquela, lahoras cove que gradantment maugua aquela de l’orrifici de la vesica a las partidas dejos am somman de la sua vertut entro que pervengua am aquel a la razit de la coyssa.	Therefore if you find it, then accordingly gradually massage that from the orifice of the bladder to the parts below with the summit of her virtue until it reaches the root of the scrotum.
E aprop inscida sobre aquela apposicio de la maytat del conh deves la razit de la coyssa de qualque part sia a lu parada e cent la peyra en aquela partida, e·l dit de lu no sia remaugut de la peyra coartan dejos lu.	And accordingly inscribe upon that apposition of the might of the private parts to the root of the scrotum of some part that is located and centered on the stone, and the right hand not be removed from the stone, cut below it.
E la seccio sia pauca al comensament; e aprop entrometa lo ray sobre aquela seccio, e si sent la peyra, lahoras ajuste en seccio segon la quantitat la qual sap que la peyra sira getada de aquela.	And the section should be small at first; and accordingly insert the forceps onto that section, and if you feel the stone, then adjust the section according to the quantity which you know will cause the stone to be extracted from there.
E sapias que las specias de peyra son motas: quar de aquelas es pauca e gran, e leon e aspra, e longua e redonda, e havent ramps.	And know that the types of stones are many: for some are small and large, and smooth and rough, and long and rounded, and having ridges.
Donc tu sapias quantas specias so de lu per aquo que tu signifiques sobre aquo que vols.	Therefore you know how many types there are of it by this which you signify about what you want.
E si tu veus flux de sanc, ajusta en le loc vetriol trissat e te aquela per una hora entro que sia abscindit le sanc, e aprop retorna a la tua operacio entro que la peyra sia fora-getada.	And if you see a flow of blood, adjust to the place vitriol mixed with vinegar and stay there for an hour until the bleeding stops, and then return to your operation until the stone is extracted.
E fay que prepares am tu dels instrumentz les quals e ditz en la extraccio de peyra en les homes, per so que sias ajudat per aquels en la tua operacio.	And make sure that you prepare with your own the instruments which are said in the extraction of stone in men, so that you may be assisted by them in your operation.
E si tu veus flux de sanc, e sabes que la expulcio del sanc es de la arceria que es insciza, lahoras tu pausa polvera sobre le loc e estrenh aquel am pulvils e strictura descent, e no iteras aquo; e layssa la peyra e no extraguas aquela, quar fort leu morira la malauta.	And if you see a flow of blood, and know that the expulsion of blood is from the wound that is inscribed, then accordingly you will pause powder on the location and strengthen it with powders and strictures descending, and do not repeat this; and leave the stone and do not extract it, for fear that the patient will soon die.
E aprop cura la plagua.	And accordingly cure the wound.
Donc cum es cedada la acuitat del sanc aprop alcus jorns, e·l loc se poyreys, lahoras tu retorna a la tua operacio entro que la peyra sia fora-getada.	And therefore when the sharpness of the blood has ceased after some days, and the location is settled, then accordingly you return to your operation until the stone is extracted.
Capitol lxii.	Chapter LXII.
De seccio sobre ernia acoza.	Of Section on Hernia in the Groin.
Hernia ayguoza no es sino agregacio de humiditat en le ciphac blanc lo qual es dejos la codena dels genetius contenent le huou, e es nompnat ciphac.	Hernia in the groin is nothing but an accumulation of moisture in the white sac which is below the cord of the testicles containing the liquor, and it is called a sac.
E alcunas veguadas es en le propri pannicol le qual a lu preparec natura en la partida del huou, entro que sia cuyat que ja es autre huou; e es la codena del genetiu entre le ciphac blanc le qual havem dit, e no es aquo sino tart.	And some times it is in the proper fold of fat which nature has prepared in the part of the liquor, until it becomes another liquor; and it is the cord of the testicles between the white sac which we have said, and not this but rather a tumor.
E la generacio de aquest hernia es per debelitat la qual accideys als genetius, per que ad aquels es efundunda aquesta materia, e alcunas vetz accideys per percuscio fayta sobre les genetius.	And the generation of this hernia is due to weakness which occurs in the testicles, because it flows into these testicles this material, and sometimes it occurs through blows made on the testicles.
E aquesta humiditat es havent motas colors, quar la color de lu o es declinant a citrina o a sanguinent, o rog, o es negra feculenta, o es ayguosa blanqua, e es aquo que es mays.	And this moisture has many colors, for the color of it is either declining to citrine or sanguine, or red, or blackish, or white watery, and it is that which is most common.
E les senhals per les quals es saubut on es aquesta agreguacio de aygua so aquestz: quar si es en le ciphac blanc le qual havem dit, lahoras le apostema es redon declinant un pauc a longitut ayssi cum figura de huou, e appar le genetiu, quar la humiditat conte aquel de tota part.	And the signs by which it is known where this accumulation of water is are these: for if it is in the white sac which we have said, then the abscess is rounded declining a little to length like the figure of a liquor, and appears the testicle, because the moisture contains that from all parts.
E si la humiditat es en le propri pannicol, lahoras le apostema es redon am partida del huou e per aysso hom estima que es autre huou.	And if the moisture is in the proper fold of fat, then the abscess is rounded with the part of the liquor and thus one estimates that it is another liquor.
E si la humiditat es entre la codena dels genetius e·l ciphac blanc, lahoras catz dejos le centiment.	And if the moisture is between the cord of the testicles and the white sac, then a swelling appears below the sensation.
E cum tu vols la cognicio de la color de la humiditat, lahoras tu esproa la color de la humiditat en le apostema am entromes cayrat del qual la forma es precedida; e segon aquo que es eyssit en le vestigi del entromes, jutga de aquo que es dedintz lu.	And when you want to know the color of the moisture, then accordingly you will inspect the color of the moisture in the abscess by entering through a channel from which the shape is preceded; and according to what it appears in the vestige of the entrance, judge from that what it is.
Donc quan nos vinem a la curacio de lu am ferr, lahoras cove que comandem al malaute que sia fleubotomat si aquo es a tu possibla, e vezes le cos de lu ple.
