Therefore when we come to the cure of it with iron, then accordingly you must command the patient to be flaccid if that is possible for you, and sometimes fill his body.
E aprop sia resupinat sobre le sieu dos sobre alcuna causa un pauc auta, e pausa dejos lu motz draps.	And accordingly it should be raised up on the patient's back for some reason a little higher, and pause below him many cloths.
E aprop setz tu sobre la part sinistra de lu, e comanda al ministra que segua a la dextra de lu, le qual extenda la sua vergua a hun de dos latz a la codena dels genetius e a la partida del mirac del ventre.	And accordingly sit you on the left side of him, and command the assistant to follow on the right side of him, which will extend his hand to one of two sides to the cord of the testicles and the part of the navel of the belly.
E aprop pren spatum lat e scindeys la codena dels genetius del mieg loc per la longitut entro prop le pentenilh.	And accordingly take a spatula and divide the cord of the testicles from the middle location by length, so that it is close to the navel.
E sia fayta la seccio segon rectetut engualment distant de la linha que deveseys la pel dels genetius, entro que pervengua al ciphac blanc comprehendent.	And accordingly make the section according to straight line evenly distant from the line that should be drawn on the skin of the testicles, until it reaches the white sac containing.
E excorja aquel, e observa, e guarda te per aysso que tu no inscidas aquel; e la tua excoriacio am la qual aquel excorjas per partida jassia que sia suspenduda am le huou mays e subtilment escruta am la excoriacio segon la quantitat a tu possibla.	And accordingly excise that, observe, and be careful not to inscribe it; and your excision with which you excise that part below, as if it were suspended in the liquor more subtly explores the excision according to the quantity that is possible for you.
E aprop perfora le ciphac ple de aygua am perforacio ampla, e extratz tota l’aygua.	And accordingly pierce the white sac full of water with a wide perforation, and extract all the water.
E aprop separa entre doas labias de la seccio am uncis, e exten le ciphac a las partidas desus; e no toques la codena les genetius comprehendent, e inscideys le ciphac en aquela manieyra que es a tu possible.	And accordingly separate between the two lips of the section with a hook, and extend the sac to the upper parts; and do not touch the cord of the testicles that contains it, and inscribe the sac in that manner which is possible for you.
E inscideys aquel am la sua totalitat o en pessas, e majorment le sieu latz subtil, quar si tu no perscrutas exquisidament la inscizio de lu, no es fayta segurtat que la aygua no retorne.	And accordingly inscribe that with its entire totality or in parts, and most particularly the subtle sides, for if you do not scrutinize the inscription of it extremely well, there is no sure guarantee that the water will not return.
Mays si le huou procezeys de aquela defora de la sua codena en la ora de la tua operacio, lahoras quan tu auras complida la seccio del ciphac, retorna dedintz aquel, e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la codena dels genetius am sutura, e aprop cura aquel ayssi cum las autras plagua, entro que sia sanat.	But if the liquor proceeds from that outside of its cord during your operation, then when you have completed the section of the sac, return inside it, and accordingly adjust the two lips of the cord of the testicles with a suture, and accordingly cure that just like the other wounds, until it is healed.
E si atrobas le huou corromput per autra malautia, lahoras cove que tu lies les vayssels les quals so sore le suspensori, e extrat le huou, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit.	And if you find the liquor corrupted by another disease, then accordingly you should open the vessels which are sore the suspensors, and extract the liquor, and accordingly cure that with what we have said.
Mays si l’aygua es agreguada en doas partidas esemps, lahoras sapias que doas son las ernias; donc inscideys aquela partida segon que has feyt en l’autra engualment; e si es a tu vist que sia una opera, lahoras tu la fay.	But if the water is accumulated in two separate parts, then you should know that there are two hernias; therefore inscribe that part according to what you have done with the other equally; and if it appears to be one operation, then you will do it.
E aprop tu abstergiys le sanc, e entramet en las seccios lana submersa en oli o en oli rozat; e pausa deforo autra lana la qual tu as submersa en vi e oli, e expandeys aquela sobre dos genetius e·l mirac del ventre; e pausa desobre draps doblatz e pulvils, e lia aquels desobre am liament le qual es segon aquesta forma:	And accordingly you will wash the blood away, and enter into the sections lamb submerged in oil or rosy oil; and pause outside another lamb which you have submerged in wine and oil, and spread it over two testicles and the navel of the belly; and pause above folded cloths and powders, and tie those above with a ligament according to this form:
e aprop sian preses dos draps e sian humplitz de lana carmenada segon aquesta semblansa; e sian faytas las extremitatz am les quals es premut de coto o de lana humida, e sian agreguatz am strectura en le braguier de las braguas, e la una de las extremitatz prengua del cul entro al dos, e la segonda prengua a la partida del pantenilh, e dos extramitatz sobre dos coyssas dejos e dos extramitatz autras sobre dos angonars, e tota extrictura sia ajustada en le braguier de las braguas.	and accordingly two cloths are pressed and filled with Carmelite wool according to this likeness; and the extremities are made with those that are wrapped in a cloth or wet wool, and are added to the structure in the breeches of the trousers, and one of the extremities takes from the backside into the crotch, and the second takes to the part of the navel, and two other extremities above two wounds below, and two other extremities above two abscesses; and all the structure is adjusted in the breeches of the trousers.
E alcunas veguadas aquesta hernia es medicada artificialment am cauteri en loc de seccio am ferr; e es que tu prenguas cauteri cutellar subtil e que inscidas am aquel la codena dels ginitius, e es ignit segon que havem recomtat entro que sia descubert le ciphac blanc contenent la aygua, e lahoras tu pren cauteri segon aquesta forma:	And sometimes this hernia is medicated artificially with a cauter in place of section with iron; and it's that you take a cauterous cutlery subtle and inscribe it on the cord of the testicles, and it is ignited according to what we have recommended until the white sac containing the water is uncovered, and then you take the cauter according to this form:
e es asemblat a letra greca.	and it's assembled in Greek letters.
E aprop perfora am aquel ciphac, e es ignit entro que tota la humiditat sia fora-gitada.	And accordingly pierce through that sac, and is ignited until all the moisture is expelled.
E aprop exten le ciphac am uncis, e excorja am uncis, e excorja am cauteri subtil ignit; e inscideys aquel segon que es a tu possible entro que eradiques tot lu; e guarda te del huou que·l foc no·l toque.	And accordingly extend the sac with hooks, and excise with hooks, and excise with a burning cauterous cutlery; and inscribe that according to what is possible for you until it is eradicated entirely; and be careful not to let the liquor touch the fire.
E sapias que aquesta operacio es pus salva e pus longinqua de flux de sanc, e milhor que operacio am seccio.	And know that this operation is more safe and less prolonged with bleeding, and better than the operation of section.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat apostema caut en la hora de seccio o en hora de cauteri, o flux de sanc, lahoras cove que tu cures qual contrarietat fa a tu per aquo, am curacio la qual conveneys a lu segon que es dit.	But if you encounter opposition, such as abscess during the time of section or cauterization, or bleeding, then accordingly you should take care to cure whatever opposition arises for you by that means, with the treatment which is suitable for him according to what is said.
Mays si le malaute es pauruc, e no spera la segonda operacio per la sua horribilitat, lahoras administra perforacio segon que yeu recomti aquo; e es quan es certificat deves tu, per aquo que havem dit de las significacios, que aquela hernia es ayguosa.	But if the patient is timid and does not expect a second operation due to its horror, then accordingly administer perforation according to what we have recommended above; and it is when you are certain, by virtue of what we have said about the signs, that this hernia is watery.
Lahoras cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute sobre alcuna cezelha elevada, aprop perfora le apostema en la partida pus bassa de lu am spatum lat, e pausa la perforacio segon la longitut del cos.	And accordingly you should make the patient sit on some elevated elevation, and pierce the abscess in the lowest part of him with a spatula, and pause the perforation according to the length of the body.
E sia la apercio ampla entro que corro tota l‘aygua.	And accordingly be the aperture wide enough that it drains all the water.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc coto e lia aquel e layssa aquel, per so que corro le romanent de l’aygua.	And accordingly pause above the location of the cut and tie that off, in order that the remaining water flows out.
E aprop cura aquel entro que la plagua sia sanada.	And accordingly cure that until the wound is healed.
Mays si contrarietat es a la egrecio de l’aygua en aquela hora tu perforas aquela: e aquo no es fayt sino per aquo quar le pannicol blanc en le orrifici de la plagua fa contrarietat e prohibeys le eyssiment de l’aygua, lahoras cove que tu metas en la plagua pena o instrument am la qual es extrayta l’aygua dels ydropitz, la forma del qual es precedida; o ajusta en la opprecio de la plagua un petit.	But if opposition is to the flow of water in that hour you pierce it: and this is not done except for that reason, because the white panniculus in the orifice of the wound causes opposition and prevents the ejection of the water; then accordingly you should put a penalty or instrument into the wound with which the water is extracted from the dropsies, the form of which is preceded; or adjust a small piece in the opposite part of the wound.
E sapias que l’aygua retorna, e es agueguada aprop vi meses o enaviro aquels; e cum es agreguada, lahoras sia perforat segon aquela meteyssa manieyra, quar le malaute ayssi passara les sieus dias.	And know that the water returns, and is again accumulated in about two months or a year after; and when it is accumulated, then accordingly be pierced according to that same manner, for the patient will thus pass his days.
Capitol .lxiii.	Chapter LXIII.
De seccio sobre hernia carnosa e la curacio de lu.	Of Section on Fleshy Hernia and its Cure.
Sapias que en la seccio sobre aquesta hernia es temor perdusent a pernicia en las majors disposicios; per que a mi es vista la dimissio de lu e esser salvat per aquela milhor.	Know that in the section on this hernia there is fear of losing one's life through perilous dispositions; for which reason it has been seen by me, to dismiss him and be saved through better means.
E yeu so rememorant la operacio en aquela e las specias dels apostemas.	And you are reminded of the operation on that and the species of abscesses.
Donc, dic que l‘apostemas natz en les cos dels quals les genetius so conponutz e es fayt aquo per motas causas: o per superfluitat aguda agra, la qual es efundida als genetius, o per percuscio.	Therefore I say that abscesses are born in the bodies of those whose testicles are composed and it is made so for many reasons: or by sudden acute superfluity, which is poured into the testicles, or by blows.
E es la color de la apostema segon la color del cos, e no es atrobat en lu dolor, e es apostema greu.	And it is the color of the abscess according to the color of the body, and it is not found in him pain, and it is a severe abscess.
E fort leu es apostema lapificada, del qual la color es fosca, e no es centiment a lu.	And very often it is a pustular abscess, of which the color is dark, and there is no sensation in him.
E alcunas veguadas es fayt per nodacio de las arcerias, e per imflacio de aquelas ayssi quo ja es perceubut la rememoracio de lu, o per imflacio de venas.	And sometimes it is made by the obstruction of arteries, and by inflammation of those vessels as well as that which is remembered of him, or by inflammation of veins.
Mays aquo que es per imflacio de arcerias es conogut per la dispercio de la apostema quan compremas aquela am les tieus ditz; e no cove que aquel toques.	But that which is due to inflammation of arteries is known by the dispersion of the abscess when you compress it with those said ties; and it is not necessary for it to touch.
Mays aquel que es fayt per imflacio de vena no es dispergut de lu alcuna causa deves la compressio am les ditz.	But that which is due to inflammation of veins is not dispersed from him for any reason, even with compression by those said ties.
E ja es possible que sobre aquesta specia sia fayta seccio e sobre les autres carns; e es que tu inscida la codena dels genetius, e aprop esten le huou a las partidas desus, e extratz aquel del ciphac blanc, e deliura le suspensori dels vaysels, e ligua les, e inscideys le suspensori pus que tu deliuras aquel de tota partida de las partidas del huou.	And it is possible that on this species a section be made and on the other flesh; and it's that you inscribe the cord of the testicles, and accordingly extend the liquor to the upper parts, and extract that from the white sac, and deliver the suspensors of the vessels, and tie them up, and inscribe the suspensor more than you deliver that from all part of the liquors.
Donc si l’huou ja es am aquelas carnadas consolida, lahoras cove que tu extraguas le huou e inscidas aquel.	Therefore if the liquor is already consolidated in those fleshed parts, then accordingly you should extract the liquor and inscribe that.
E si es adherencia entro alcuna causa del ciphac, o entre aquo que es entre les bayssels, lahoras cove que tu deliures tota aquela adherencia e inscidas aquela per inscizio redonda.	And if there is adhesion due to some cause of the sac or between what is between the vessels, then accordingly you should deliver all that adhesion and inscribe it with a rounded incision.
Mays si es nativitat de carn en le loc de la adherencia la qual es detras, lahoras cove que tu inscidas tot aquo que es de lu, e extraguas le huou ayssi cum havem dit.	But if it is a natural growth of flesh in the location of the adhesion which is behind, then accordingly you should inscribe all that is from him, and extract the liquor just as we have said.
Donc cum es complida la tua operacio, lahoras omple la plagua de lana imfuza en oli rozat e vi; e aprop cura aquela am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	Therefore when your operation is completed, then accordingly fill the wound with wool infused in rose oil and wine; and accordingly cure that with another treatment until it is healed.
Capitol .lxiv.	Chapter LXIV.
De la curacio de hernia que es de vitz.	On the Cure of Hernia that is of Veins.
Vit es apostema envolut per alcuna envolucio semblant a broto am mollificacio dels testiculs, e es fayt dificil movement exercitiu e deambulacio sobre le malaute.	Veins is an abscess wrapped in some wrapping similar to a bud in the softening of the testicles, and it is made difficult for the patient to exercise movement and walking.
E en la curacio de aquesta malautia es per temor per aquo del qual es precedida rememoracio.	And in the cure of this disease it is due to fear because of which the preceding memory is recalled.
Empero cove que diguam opperacio en aquela segon que fero les primiers.	However, I must say that the operation on that should be done according to what was done by the first ones.
E dic que cove que fassas sezer le malaute sobre una cezelha elevada; e aprop enpelleys le suspensori dels testiculs a las partidas dejos; e aprop te la codena dels genetius am les tieus ditz am les baysels que so probdas a la vergua; e tengua aquels autre ministre que tu, e extenda aquels am extencio vehement.	And I say that you should make the patient sit on an elevated elevation; and accordingly grasp the suspensors of the testicles at the left side; and accordingly tie the cord of the testicles with those said ties around the vessels which are proved to be in the sac; and have another assistant besides you, and extend them with a vehement extension.
E aprop inscideys am spatum lat agut per seccio traversa en le dreyt dels vaysels entro que sian les vayssels descubertz.	And accordingly inscribe with a spatula flat for a transverse section in the right of the vessels until the vessels are uncovered.
E aprop excorja de tota partida ayssi quo a tu havem dit en extraccio de arceria las quals so en las templas.	And accordingly excise from all parts just as we have said in the extraction of arteries which are in the temples.
E aprop fica en aquelas un’agulha en la qual sia fiel doble, e lia aquel en le primier del locs en les quals accideys vit, e lia aquel autra veguada en le derier de lor.	And accordingly put an awl in those with a double thread, and tie that in the first of the places where the veins occur, and tie it again on another occasion at the last of them.
E aprop inscideys aquels en le mieg loc per seccio dreyta segon la longuesa del cos, e extratz aquo que es agreguat de las humiditatz fetulentas e corruptas.	And accordingly inscribe those in the middle location by straight section according to the length of the body, and extract that which is accumulated with foul and corrupted humors.
E aprop cura la plagua am curacio de las autras plaguas en las quals vols sania esser engendrada per so que caian les vaysels les quals noyreysso un de dos genetius, quar no es mal per aquo.	And accordingly cure the wound with treatment of other wounds in which you wish to bring forth healing because those vessels will not nourish one of two testicles, for it is not bad for that reason.
Mays si accideys vit a totz les bayssels, lahoras cove que·ls testicols sian extragutz o que les testicols per aquo se cequo am les vayssels, per que sia privat de tot nutriment per la inscizio dels vayssels, e que sian estaborits, o que cequo per so que no sia juvament am aquels.	But if the veins are injured in all vessels, then accordingly it is necessary to remove the testicles or for the testicles to be cut off along with the vessels, so that it may be deprived of all nourishment by the incision of the vessels, and thus be destroyed, or cut off because it will not be well with those.
Capitol .lxv.	Chapter LXV.
De la cura de hernia entestinal.	On the Cure of Intestinal Hernia.
Le adveniment de aquesta hernia es per seccio que endeve en le ciphac extendut sobre le ventre de part dels angunars del mirac del ventre, per que deysendo les budels de aquela ruptura ad alcu dels budels.	The advent of this hernia is due to a section that proceeds in the sac extended over the belly on the side of the navel of the belly, so that by bursting open the bags of that rupture they come out into some of the bags.
E aquesta ruptura es o del ciphac o de excencio de lu, e accideysso aquestas doas specias per motas causas: o percussio, o per sautz, o per clamor, o per elevacio de alcuna causa greu, o per semblantz.	And this rupture is either of the sac or of excrescence from it, and occurs in these two species for many reasons: or by blows, or by salt, or by noise, or by elevation of some grave cause, or by likenesses.
E·l senhal de aquo, quan es per extencio del ciphac, es que accideys pauc a pauc en lonc temps, e no accideys soptament, e es apostema engual entro ves le preon per so quar le ciphac comprem le budel.	And the sign of this is that it occurs gradually over a long period of time, and does not occur suddenly, and it is an abscess growing equal to the prepuce on account of which the sac fills the bag.
E le senhal de lu es quan es per seccio del ciphac, quar al comensament fa accidir dolor vehement sobtament; e es apostema divers aparent dejos la codena propdana aparent, e aquo es per eyssiment del budel, e·l cos de lu a las partidas deforo del ciphac.	And the sign of this is when it occurs by section of the sac, for at first it causes sudden and vehement pain; and it is an abscess that appears different from the cord that has been torn apart, and this is due to the ejection of the bag, and the body of it in the parts outside the sac.
E alcunas veguadas es fora-getat am le budel la tela, e es apelada aquesta hernia entestinal zirbal.	And sometimes it is forgotten with the bag's skin, and this is called intestinal hernia cirrhal.
E alcunas veguadas es fayta am ventositat, e alcunas veguadas corr en le budel fenda, e aqui es retenguda, e es am aquo gran pernitia3 del malaute, e alcunas veguadas fa endevenir dolor malvada e majorment quan es premut.	And sometimes it is made with distension, and sometimes it runs in the bag's fissure, and there it is retained, and this is very great perniciousness for the patient, and sometimes it causes bad pain and mostly when it is pressed.
E en la curacio de las especias de aquesta malautia am ferr es temor, per que cove que sia esquivat le cazament en aquela.	And in the cure of the species of this disease with iron there is fear, because it is necessary to avoid the accident in that.
E la manieyra de la operacio de aquela es que comandes al malaute que redugua le budel am la sua ma a las partidas dedintz de la sua conquavitat si obezeys al sieu retornament, e aprop sia envessat sobre le sieu col entre las tuas mas, e eleva las cambas de lu.	And the manner of the operation on that is that you command the patient to draw out the bag with his own hand towards the parts outside of his conquest if he obeys his returnment, and accordingly be seated over his back between your arms, and lift up the legs of him.
E aprop sten la codena la qual siec la codena dels testicols a las partidas desus, e inscideys la codena dels testicols tota per le lonc; e aprop fiqua en doas labias de la seccio uncis segon que indigeysses a hubrir la seccio am aquels.	And accordingly tie the cord which ties the cord of the testicles to the upper parts, and inscribe the cord of the testicles all along; and accordingly place it in two lips of the section hooks according as you need to open the section with those.
E si’ la seccio segon la quantitat que a tu sia possible que de aquela le huou sia foro-getat.	And if the section is done according to the quantity that it is possible for you to forget from that, the liquor may be forgotten.
E aprop excorja aquela ciphaqueth les quals so dejos la codena dels testicols, entro que sia descubert le ciphac blanc dur de quascuna partida.	And accordingly excise those sac-like things which are left over the cord of the testicles, until the white hard sac is uncovered in each part.
Lahoras tu entromet le tieu dit en aquo que siec le testicol, en aquo que es entre ciphac blanc, le qual es dejos la codena del huou, e entre le ciphac segon, e absolve am aquel’adherencia que es en la partida detras del huou.	And accordingly insert the tie you said in that which secures the testicle, in that which is between the white sac and the sac, the latter being left over the cord of the liquor, and between the sac, and absolve with that adherence which is in the part behind the liquor.
E aprop mau am la ma la codena dels testicols a las partidas deforo, e am aysso exten le ciphac blanc en sus am la ma sinestra, e eleva le huou am le ciphac a la partida de la seccio; e comanda al ministre que extenda le huou ensus e tu dissolveys la adherencia que es detras am solucio complida.	And accordingly take hold of the cord of the testicles with your left hand, and extend the white sac in that direction with your right hand, and raise the liquor to the part of the section; and command the assistant to extend the liquor upwards and you dissolve the adherence that is behind with complete solution.
E cerqua am les tieus ditz que lay no sia alcuna causa del budel envelopat en le ciphac blanc dur.	And search for those said ties which may not be any cause of the bag being wrapped in the white hard sac.
Mays si tu atrobas de lu alcuna causa, lahoras tu enpelleys aquel al ventre dejos.	But if you find some cause from him, then accordingly you should tie that to the belly below.
E aprop tu pren una agulha en la qual sia fiel gros fayt de x fiels, e entromet aquel deves le derier del ciphac, le qual es jos la codena dels testicols, la qual siec seccio; e aprop inscideys las extremitatz las quals emineysso del fiel entro que sian quatre fiels, e aprop compausa alcus de lor sobre alcuna figura en manieyra de crotz; e lia am aquel le ciphac del qual havem dit que es dejos la codena dels testicols am fort liament de dos partz.	And accordingly take an awl with a thick thread of nine threads, and insert that from the last part of the sac, which is below the cord of the testicles, the one which you are about to section; and accordingly inscribe the extremities which protrude from the thread until there are four threads, and accordingly compose some of them into a figure in the manner of a cross; and tie with that the sac which we have said is left over the cord of the testicles with strong binding of two parts.
E aprop envolveys las extremitatz dels fiels e lia aquelas am liament vehement entro que alcu dels vayssels que noyrrisso aquels no puscan trametre alcuna causa per so que de aqui no accida apostema caut.	And accordingly envelop the extremities of the threads and tie them with strong binding until some of the vessels which nourish those are not able to transmit any cause because of this, lest a severe abscess occur.
E pausa autra veguada liament segon foro le primier liament, lonh de lu mens tres ditz; e aprop aquestz dos liaments layssa del ciphac le qual es dejos la codena dels testicols la quantitat de la grandeza del dit, e inscideys tot le romanent segon redondeza, e osta de lu le huou.	And pause another binding for a certain time after the first binding, about three times; and accordingly, these two bindings leave the sac which is left over the cord of the testicles in the amount of the great size of that, and inscribe all the remaining part according to roundness, and stop from it the liquor.
E aprop inscideys en la partida dejos de la codena dels testicols per seccio de la qual corra sanc e sania ayssi cum havem recomtat en aquo que havem dit.	And accordingly inscribe in the part left over from the cord of the testicles by section, which will bleed and heal just as we have recommended in that which we have said.
E aprop aministra lana submersa en oli, e pausa en la plagua; e aministra le liament le qual havem recomtat (e alcunas veguadas le ciphac blanc es cauterizat, le qual havem dit aprop la inscizio de lu temen de flux de sanc, quar motas veguadas accideys aquels) e leyssa le liament entro que per si caia.	And accordingly administer wool soaked in oil, and pause on the wound; and administer the binding which we have recommended (and sometimes the white sac is cauterized, which we have said should be done for fear of bleeding, because many times it occurs) and leave the binding until it falls by itself.
Mays si le cazement de lu es tardat, lahoras de aygua cauda sia embrocat, e pausa sobre aquel entro que caia segon que havem dit.	But if the bleeding is delayed, then accordingly cold water should be applied, and pause on it until it falls according to what we have said.
E aprop cura la plagua am l’autra curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly cure the wound with another treatment of wounds until it is healed.
Capitol .lxvi.	Chapter LXVI.
De hernia ventosa.	On Hernia Ventosa.
En aquesta hernia no e vist alcu que sia estat ardit sus la curacio de lu am ferr.	In this hernia, it is not seen that anyone has been bold enough to attempt the cure with iron.
E les primiers diyssero que es fayta ayssi cum havem recomtat en la hernia que es am vi; la qual es que tu lies les vayssels aprop la seccio sobre aquela am fecilitat de lu; e aprop secca en le mieg loc en enviro le apostema am aquo que obro aquel, entro que caian les vayssels.	And the first ones said that it is done just as we have recommended in the hernia which is with wine; the one which you tie the vessels accordingly to the section on that with facility of iron; and accordingly cut off in the middle location around the abscess with this which causes that, until the vessels come forth.
E cura la plagua segon que havem dit entro que sia sanada.	And cure the wound according to what we have said until it is healed.
Capitol .lxvii.	Chapter LXVII.
De la disropcio que es fayta en les anguonars.	On the Disproportion that is made in the Navels.
Alcunas veguadas endeve ruptura en les angonars ayssi cum havem dit, e emineys le loc.	Sometimes a rupture occurs in the navels just as we have said, and protrude the location.
E no deyssen als genetius alcuna causa dels budels al genetius; e si deyssen, aquo es pauc; e retorna s’en en totas horas.	And there is not any cause for the testicles in the testicles; and if there is, it is little; and returns back to all hours.
Mays si es prolonguat le temps am aquo, es ajustada fissura en le ciphac entro que deysenda le budel en le ciphac; e accideys aquo per la extencio del ciphac le qual es en le angonars ayssi cum havem dit, la qual causa es quar le ciphac es estendut, e aprop es mollificat e·l loc es apostemat e emineys.	But if the time is prolonged with this, there is an adjustment of a fissure in the sac until it descends into the sac; and it occurs because of the extension of the sac which is in the navels just as we have said, which cause is that the sac is stretched, and accordingly becomes softened and the location abscesses and protrudes.
E la cura de lu es am cauteri ayssi quo es precedida la narracio de lu.	And the cure of this is with a cauterization just as we have previously described it.
E alcunas veguadas es curada am ferr segon aquesta manieyra: e es que·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu dos entre las tuas mas, e aprop secca le loc de la ruptura dels apostemas emineys am seccio per la latitut segon la quantitat de tres ditz.	And sometimes it is cured with iron according to this manner: and it is that the patient lies on his back between your arms, and accordingly cuts off the location of the rupture of the abscesses protruding through section by the latitude according to the quantity of three fingers.
E aprop strenh le ciphac blanc que es jos la codena entro que sia descubert.	And accordingly strengthen the white sac that is below the cord until it is uncovered.
E aprop pren le ray e pausa aquel sobre le loc eminent del ciphac, e prem aquel al preon del ventre.	And accordingly take a reed and pause it on the protruding location of the sac, and press it against the belly's front.
E aprop cus le dos locs eminentz sobre la extremitat del ray del ciphac, e ajusta am la sutura un de aquels am l’autre.	And accordingly bring together the two protruding locations on the extremity of the reed of the sac, and adjust with a suture one to the other.
E aprop extratz la extremitat del ray, e no inscidas del ciphac de tot, ni no extenda le huou, ni autra causa ayssi cum yeu te fi saber en la curacio de hernia entestinal.	And accordingly extract the extremity of the reed, and do not inscribe the sac entirely, nor extend the liquor, nor any other cause just as you wish to know in the cure of intestinal hernia.
E aprop cura aquela am la curacio de las plaguas, e cum inscideyses les fiels, mundifica aquela e restaura la plagua entro que sia consolidada; quar le ciphac es contrayt e no es ajustada la eminencia de ruptura.	And accordingly cure that with the treatment of wounds, and as you inscribe the threads, purify that and restore the wound until it is consolidated; for the sac has contracted and the prominence of rupture has not been adjusted.
E cauteri es milhor en aquest loc, quar es pus propda a salut.	And cauterization is better in this location, because it is more conducive to health.
Capitol .lxviii.	Chapter LXVIII.
De mollificacio de la codena dels testiculs.	On the Softening of the Cord of the Testicles.
Motas veguadas la codena dels testiculs en alcus homes es mollificada per aysso quar las carns que so entre aquela son mollificadas, e es fedat le reguardament de lu.	Many times the cord of the testicles in some men is softened because the flesh which is between it is softened, and it is fitting for that to be observed.
Adonc necessari es ad aquel que es preguat en la curacio de lu que fassa jazer le malaute segon le sieu dos, e enscida tota la codena la qual es mollificada sobre la codena natural; e aprop que ajuste doas labias am la sutura.	Therefore it is necessary for him who is engaged in the cure of this to make the patient lie on his back between your arms, and inscribe all the softened cord which has been softened over the natural cord; and accordingly bring together two lips with a suture.
E si vols, cus en le comensament la superfluitat de la codena mollificada am tres cozeduras o quatre e am ferma sutura.	And if you wish, remove in the beginning the superfluity of the softened cord with three or four cauterizations and a firm suture.
E aprop inscideys entre las suturas; e aprop cura per curacio de las autras plaguas entro que sia sanat e caian les fiels.	And accordingly inscribe between the sutures; and accordingly cure through the treatment of other wounds until it is healed and the threads come forth.
Capitol .lxix.	Chapter LXIX.
De castracio.	On Castration.
Sapias que castratio en nostre ley es excomengada, mays per causa es legut a mi que·m remembre de lu en aquest libre; e no es necessaria la rememoracio de lu sino per doas manieyras, de las quals es la una per so que aquo sia en la sciensa del metge quan es enterroguat de aquela, que sapia la curacio de lu al qual accideys; e l’autra manieyra es que nos motas vetz havem necessitat de castracio de autras bestias per les juvamentz nostres per aquelas, ayssi cum de motos, e de bocs, e de porcs, e de semblantz a las bestias.	Know that castration in our law is excommunicated, but by reason it is allowed to me to remember of it in this book; and there is no need for the remembrance of it except for two manners, one of which is because of what I know about the science of the physician when he is required to cure of that which occurs; and the other manner is that we many times have needed castration of other beasts for our uses through those, just as with mares, oxen, and pigs, and similar to cattle.
E donc dic que castracio es fayta en dos manieyras: o per atrissio, o per fissura a seccio.	And therefore I say that castration is done in two manners: either by castration, or by incision at section.
Mays en aquela que es fayta per atrissio, la via de la opera es que nos fassam cezer la bestia en aygua cauda entro que·ls genetius de lu sian mollificatz e sian linhitz e que pendan.	But in that which is done by castration, the way of the operation is that we make the beast lie down in cold water until its testicles are softened and relaxed and hang.
E aprop pren aquels am la tua ma entro que sian resols e no apparescan dejos le tocament.	And accordingly take those with your hand into which they are resolved and do not appear to be left behind by the touch.
Mays en castracio fayta per fissura e seccio, cove que tu tenguas la bestia e premas la codena dels testicols de lu am la ma senestra.	But in castration done by incision and section, it is necessary that you hold the beast and press the cord of the testicles with your left hand.
E aprop lia le suspensori, e inscideys sobre quascun huou am una seccio entro que dos huous proceseysso.	And accordingly tie the suspenders, and inscribe on each liquor with one section until two liquors process.
E aprop inscideys aquels pus que auras quascu excorjat.	And accordingly inscribe those more than you will have excised.
E no leysses sobre aquels del ciphac alcuna causa, sino le ciphac subtil le qual es sobre les vazes.	And do not leave on those any cause from the sac, but only the subtle sac which is over the veins.
E aquesta manieyra de castracio es milhor la qual es fayta per atrissio, quar atrissio fort leu layssa alcuna causa dels testicols per que la bestia desira coyt.	And this manner of castration is better which is done by castration, because castration leaves no cause for the testicles so that the beast does not desire to copulate.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly cure the wound until it is healed.
Capitol .lxx.	Chapter LXX.
De la cura de hermafrodozia.	On the Cure of Hermaphrodites.
Hermafrodozia en les homes es segon dos manieyras: la una es quar o appar en aquo que siec l’espazi en la codena de testiculs, en aquel que es entre dos testiculs figura quar cunh de femna en la qual so pels.	Hermaphrodites in men are according to two manners: one is when there appears in that which is the space in the cord of testicles, between two testicles a figure as if a female were in it, with breasts.
E alcunas veguadas de aquel corr urina le qual es en la codena dels testiculs.	And sometimes from that there comes urine which is in the cord of the testicles.
Mays en las femnas es una specia: e es que·l conh de la femna sobre le pentenilh es ayssi cum dos testiculs de home un pauc de tot yminiheys a la partida deforo ayssi cum le perpucii de home e dos testicols.	But in women it is one species: and it is that the female's vulva on the pubis is as if two male testicles, with only a small part of the outer skin resembling the perineum of a man and two testicles.
E la curacio es de tres specias: de dos dels homes e de una specia de las femnas.	And the cure is of three species: of two of men and one species of women.
E es que cove que tu inscidas aquelas carns ajustadas entro que efuga la emprecio de aquela, e aprop que cures aquelas am curacio de las autras plaguas.	And it is that you need to inscribe those adjusted flesh into which the pressure of that one is escaped, and accordingly cure those with the treatment of other wounds.
E en la segonda specia dels homes de la qual yeys urina la qual es en la codena dels testiculs, no es curacio ni opperacio en lu.	And in the second species of men from which urine comes that is in the cord of the testicles, there is no cure nor operation for it.
Capitol .xxi.	Chapter XXI.
De lentinge e de carn eminent per causas de las femnas.	On Lumps and Flesh that protrudes due to causes of women.
Lentige fort leu es ajustada sobre causas naturals entro que es etressat e es fayt leg le reguardament; e alcunas veguadas es magnificada en alcunas femnas en tant entro que es spandit ayssi cum en les homes e perve entro al coito.	Lump is very little adjusted over natural causes until it is estranged and made to be a legible sign; and sometimes it is magnified in certain women to such an extent that it spreads just like in men, and extends as far as to the act of copulation.
Adonc cove que tu tenguas la superfluitat de lentinge am la tua ma o am unci e inscidas.	Therefore it is necessary that you take the excess lumpiness with your hand or with a tool and inscribe.
E no ultimes en inscizio, majorment en le preon de la razit, per so que no endevengua flux de sanc.	And do not stop until you have inscribed, especially in the belly of the rational part, so that it may not engender a flow of blood.
E aprop cura aquela am curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly cure that with the treatment of wounds until it is healed.
Mays carn nascuda es carn que nays en le horrifici de la mayre entro que umple aquel, e fort leu es eyssit a las partidas deforo segon semblansa de coa (e per aquo alscus primiers appelero aquo “malautia caudada”); donc cove que nos inscidam ayssi cum inscidem lentinge, e curem aquela entro que sia sanada.	But born flesh is flesh that grows in the horror of the womb until it fills it, and very little is emitted to the outer parts according to the shape of a tail (and therefore we will also call this one "malautia caudata"); therefore it is necessary that we inscribe as we inscribe lumpiness, and cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .lxxii.	Chapter LXXII.
De curacio de alratica.	On the Cure of Rickets.
Alratica es que le conh de la femna no sia perforat, o sia le trauc petit.	Rickets is when the female's vulva is not perforated, or if it is pierced with a small hole.
E es o natural o accidental.	And it is either natural or accidental.
Accidental es per malautia la qual ha precedit, e aquela es fayta o per carn nada ajustada o per ciphac subtil o espes.	Accidental is due to disease which has preceded, and that is caused either by flesh not properly adjusted or by subtle or thick sac.
E es fayt o en le preon de la mayre, o en les costatz de lu, o en le pus sobira de lu, o en le pus bas de lu, e prohibeys de cuoyt e de enprenguacio e de enfantament, e fort leu prohibeys las mestruas.	And it is caused either in the womb of the mother, or in the ribs of the child, or in the topmost part of the child, or in the lowest part of the child, and prohibits coition, pregnancy, and childbirth, and very little prohibits menstruation.
E la cognicio de aquela es fayta per reguardament de la metrona, si la oppilacio es apparent, propdana; mays si no es apparent, lahoras tu cerqua aquela am les tieus ditz o am le ray.	And the knowledge of that is made by observing the pulse of the metrona, if the obstruction is apparent, palpable; but if it is not apparent, then you must search for it with the fingers or with a reed.
Mays si oppilacio es per ciphac subtil, e es propda a las doas labias, lahoras tu coyta e disromp aquela.	But if obstruction is due to subtle sac, and is palpable in the two lips, then you must cut and disrupt that.
E es que pauses sobre las doas labias pulvils, e aprop pausa les tieus ditz indicz de amdoas las mas encemps.	And it is that you pause on the two lips of the pulse, and accordingly pause the fingers on both sides simultaneously.
E la femna sia sobre le sieu dos, las sieuas coyssas extendudas, e aprop exten las doas labias am forsa entro que aquel ciphac subtil sia romput e la oppilacio sia uberta.	And the woman should lie on her back, with her legs extended, and accordingly stretch out the two lips with force until that subtle sac is broken and the obstruction is open.
E aprop pren lana e enbeu le4 en oli e pausa aquela sobre·l loc, e jagua am home le dia per so que·l loc inscis no sia consolidat.	And accordingly take wool and wet it with oil and pause that on the location, and make the patient lie down at home for a day in order that the inscribed location may not be consolidated.
Mays si le ciphac es gros e espes, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquel am spatum lat o am fuelha de mirta.	But if the sac is large and thick, it is necessary that you inscribe that with lard or with myrtle leaves.
Mays si la oppilacio es per carnada, lahoras suspen aquela am unci, e inscideys aquela.	But if the obstruction is due to fleshiness, then suspend it with a tool and inscribe that.
E sian am tu las medicinas que fan cessar flux de sanc ses mordicacio, ayssi cum ahacatia, e sanc de drago, e enses, ajustat am album de huou.	And you will have medicines that cause the blood to cease flowing without scratching, such as hiccups, dragon's blood, and gallbladder, adjusted with album of egg.
E aprop aministra una canulha de plom ampla per so que la plagua no sia consolidada leugierament.	And accordingly administer a leaden catheter wide enough to prevent the wound from being consolidated slightly.
E tengua aquela per alcus jorns e aministra calgua de li sec.	And keep that for some days and administer lukewarm water.
E aprop sia curada am l’autra curacio de consolidacio entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly be cured with another cure of consolidation until it is healed.
E alcunas vetz accideys en la mayre nativitat de autres carns, e lahoras cove que inscidas segon aquesta manieyra.	And sometimes it happens in the natural birth of other flesh, and accordingly it is necessary to inscribe according to this manner.
Mays si aysso es per apostema crancos, a l’apostema crancos le qual es en la mayre no sia fayta contrarietat am ferr en deguna manieyra.	But if it is due to gangrenous abscess, then let there be no contradiction with iron in any manner against the gangrenous abscess that is in the mother.
Capitol .lxxiii.	Chapter LXXIII.
De la cura de emorroydas e de tayl e de botor roja que accideysso en le conh de las femnas.	On the Cure of Hemorrhoids, Tail, and Red Bottom that occurs in the vulva of women.
Emorroydas so apprecio dels orificis de motas venas entro que de aquelas corro mot sanc continuadament; e cum so antiquadas emorroydas e son fayts theyls.	Hemorrhoids are a swelling of the outlets of many veins, until those veins flow continuously with blood; and as old hemorrhoids become, they form excrescences.
E ja yeu he dit en la divisio las specias de aquelas e les senhals de aquelas, e diyre ayssi aquelas que recebo curacio e aquelas que no recebo curacio.	And now I have said in the division the species of those and their signs, and will say also which ones receive cure and which ones do not receive cure.
Donc dic que emorroydas e theyls quan so en le preon de la mayre e no apparo al sentiment, lahoras en aquelas no sia fayta curacio am ferr.	Therefore I say that hemorrhoids and excrescences when they are in the womb of the mother and do not appear to the sense, then in those there should not be made cure with iron.
Mays aquelas las quals so en le orrifici de la mayre sobre las quals catz sentiment, so aquelas que so curadas.	But those which are in the outlet of the mother and on which one can sense something, are those which are cured.
E cove que tu metas la femna en mayso frega e aprop exten atheyl am les forfexs, o am drap aspre, e inscideys aquelas am las razitz.	And it is necessary that you put the woman in a warm bath and accordingly stretch out her excrescence with forceps or with rough cloth, and inscribe those on the roots.
E aprop pulveriza sobre aquelas deves le fluxs del sanc de una de las polveras insciscivas ses mordicacio, ayssi cum acassia e semblant ad aquels.	And accordingly powder is to be spread over those with the flows of blood from one of the inscribed powders without scratching, such as ash tree and similar to those.
E aprop enpellesca les sieus pes per una hora, e aprop pausa aquela en aygua freja.	And accordingly press her feet with your own for an hour, and accordingly pause that in cold water.
E si persevera le fluxs del sanc, lahoras fay aquela sezer en decoccio de sumat e de scorsas de milgranas e de gualas e de semblantz.	And if the blood flows persistently, then let that be stopped in a decoction of sumac and scorched mulberries and gauls and similar things.
E aprop pren farina de ordi e comfiys aquela am miel e vi agre e fay emplastre am aquo sobre le dos de lu.	And accordingly take barley flour and mix it with honey and vinegar and make an poultice with water on the back of her.
E si le sanc es abscindit, bo es; e sino, fay adherir am dos ventozas, e a las mamilhas ses escarificatio.	And if the blood is absolved, it is good; and otherwise, let it adhere to two poultices, and on the nipples without scarification.
E aprop pren lana e submergeys aquela am suc de coliandre o am suc de arnagloza o am suc de guarravier am vi pentit e fay adherir al loc; e aprop cura le loc am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly take wool and submerge it in the juice of colicandra or in the juice of Arnagluz or in the juice of Gurravera with vinegar, and make it adhere to the location; and accordingly cure the location with a poultice until it is healed.
Mays athyl rog le qual es de aspre reguardament, cove que tu inscidas aquo que a tu appar de aquel segon que he dit en theyl engualment.	But the excrescence that is of hard regard, it is necessary that you inscribe on that which appears to you according to what I have said in the equal part.
E cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .lxxiv.	Chapter LXXIV.
De perforacio de eyssedura accident en la mayre.	On the Perforation of Accidental Hernia in the Mother.
Motas specias de apostemas accideysso en la mayre, ayssi cum cranc e apostema lapident e ulceracios e adhubelat e erpetromens e fistulas emorroyas e raguarrias e thyl e autres apostemas.	Many species of accidental hernias occur in the mother, such as gangrenous and lapidary abscesses, ulcers, adhesions, herpes, hemorrhoids, and red bottoms, and other abscesses.
E yeu ja he dit aquestas malautias e las specias de aquelas e les senhals de aquelas, e las curacios de lor en la divisio.	And now I have said these illnesses and the species of those and their signs, and the cures for them in the division.
E cove que yeu digua en aquest tractat de apostema caut le qual ve en la mayre quan es dels apostemas que collegeysso sania, e si vols saber en qual manieyra se fa la opperacio de lu am ferr.	And it is necessary that you say in this treatise on gangrenous abscesses which occur in the mother when they are among those that can be cured, and if you wish to know how the operation is done with iron.
Adonc cove que tu consideres si la dolor de la apostema en le sieu comensament es aguda am percussio e flecma e febre, e vezes aquel enrogezir e si catz sobre aquel le sentiment, lahoras no·t coytes am perforacio de lu, e cura aquel am aquo que ajuda sobre la maturacio entro que cesse la acuitat dels accidentz.	Therefore it is necessary that you consider whether the pain of the gangrenous abscess in its beginning is acute with percussion and flux and fever, and if it becomes more inflamed and if there is a sensation on it, then do not cut with perforation, and cure that with water that helps with maturation until the acuity of the accident ceases.
E lahoras cove que tu fassas cezer la femna sobre una cezelha que aia doas cezelhas; e recline sobre le sieu dos e ajusta les sieus pes a la partida pus dejos del ventre, e las sieus coyssas sian expandudas, e pausa les sieus brasses dejos les sieus denols, e lia quascus am liament ad aquo convenient.	And accordingly it is necessary that you make the woman lie on a bed with two pillows; and recline her on her back and adjust her feet to the part most distant from the belly, and her legs be expanded, and pause her arms below her knuckles, and tie each one with a ligation suitable for water.
E aprop la matrona segua del latz dreyt e aministre le instrument am le qual es ubert le orrifici de la mayre, la forma del qual vindra en aquelas causas que·s faran aprop.	And accordingly the midwife will follow the right hand and administer the instrument with which the outlet of the mother is opened, in the form that will come about in those causes that are to be done accordingly.
E cove quan vols ministrar aquest instrument que tu fiques am lo ray le preon de la mayre de la femna, e aquo que del instrument es intrat en la mayre no sia mays que·l preon de la mayre e leda le malaute.	And accordingly when you wish to administer this instrument, you must make it with a reed the womb of the mother of the woman, and that which is entered into the mother's womb should not be more than the mother's womb and lead the patient.
Mays si l’estrument es major que·l preon de la mayre, lahoras cove que tu pauses pulvils sobre la textura del preon de la mayre per sso que sia prohibit l’intrament de tot instrument en le preon de la mayre.	But if the instrument is greater than the womb of the mother, then it is necessary that you powder with powder on the texture of the womb of the mother so that it may be prohibited for any instrument to enter into the womb of the mother.
E cove que tu pauses le vertitge que corr en le strument del latz pus desus e que le ministre tengua le strument e revolva le vertitge entro que sia ubert le orrifici de la mayre.	And accordingly it is necessary that you pause the turning that runs in the instrument from the right hand and above, and that the minister holds the instrument and turns the handle until the outlet of the mother's womb is opened.
E cum appar la excitura, e es tocada am la ma e es leon e molh, lahoras cove que tu secces aquela deves le cap de lu am spatum lat.	And when the excitation appears, and is touched with the hand and is hot and moist, then it is necessary that you stopper that with the head of it with lard.
E cum la sania es evacuada, lahoras cove que tu pauses en la plagua una meca submersa en oli rozat o oli vert en le qual sia alcuna stiptisitat; e pausa la calca7 en la seccio en le preon de la mayre.	And when the pus is evacuated, then it is necessary that you pause in the wound a poultice submerged in rose oil or green oil which has some purgative properties; and pause the pressure in the section within the womb of the mother.
E pause deforo la mayre e sobre le pentenilh lana munda submersa en aygua en la qual sian bulidas malvas.	And pause outside the mother, and on the pentinent wool clean, submerged in water in which blueberries have been boiled.
E aprop sia curada aprop dos dias am enguent le qual conveneys ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly it is cured within two days with an ointment that corresponds to the condition until it is healed.
E alcunas veguadas es lavada la mayre e la plagua enayssi que es cristerisat am aygua e mel, e aprop am aygua en la qual es bulhida razit de liri o de aristologia longua, e aprop retorna al enguent.	And sometimes the mother is washed and the wound is cleansed in this way that it is anointed with water and honey, and accordingly with water in which rye or long aristology has been boiled, and accordingly returns to the ointment.
E si la plagua es dedintz en la mayre ameguada, lahoras cove que tu sias prohibit de la curacio de lu am ferr, habantz cura aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio.	And if the wound is deep in the mother's flesh, then it is necessary that you be prohibited from curing it with iron, having cured it with water as we have said in the division.
Capitol .lxxv.	Chapter LXXV.
A ensenhar las matronas en qual manieyre les enbrios bius sian medicatz quan yeysso segon figura no-natural.	To teach midwives in what manner the living beings should be medicated when they are sick according to a non-natural figure.
Necessaria causa es que la matrona conogua en le comensament la figura del enfantament natural per senhals de lu, e es que quan tu vezas la femna expremar a las partidas dejos e desira odorar le ayre, e sobre aquo es enleujada per aquo que sobre ela es del part, e festina le eyssiment del enbrio, lahoras sapias que aquest part es segon figura natural, e es l’eyssiment de lu sobre le sieu cap, e la segondina am aquel o suspensa o pendent del ombelic.	A necessary cause is that the midwife should know in the beginning the figure of natural childbirth by signs of it, and this is because when you see the woman expelling at the partings and desires to smell the air, and on top of that she is lifted by what is above her part, and hastens the exit of the living being, then you will understand that this part is according to a natural figure, and it is the exit of the child over its head, and the second birth with that or suspended or pendant from the navel.
Donc cum tu vezes aquels senhals, lahoras cove que·l ventre de lu sia compremut per so que l’embrio deysenda leugerament quar quan deyssen sobre le sieu cap, deysen a lu la segondina, e es mondada de aquelas superfluitatz am bona mondificacio.	Therefore, since you see those signs, then it is necessary that the belly of the child be compressed in order that the living being may descend slightly when they are on its head, and then give birth to the second one, and it is cleansed of those superfluities with good cleansing.
Mays aquel que es otra aquest part es no-natural e no-lausable, quar quan le enbrio es eyssit sobre sos pes e·l cos de lu es eyssit devant le cap de lu e·ls pes de lu, e la ma de lu una, o al pe de lu .i., o es eyssit le cap de lu e la ma de lu, o al ventre de lu, e fort leu es convertit sobre le sieu col, e semblant de las figuras de lu no-lausablas.	But that which is another this part is non-natural and not to be tolerated, because when the living being is born on its feet and the body of it is born before its head and its feet, and one hand or at the foot .i., or is born the head of it and one hand or at the belly of it, and very little is turned over its neck, and similar to the figures that are non-tolerable.
Don necessaria causa es a la matrona que sia savia e subtil en totas aquelas causas, e que·s guarde de error e de decepcio.	Therefore, it is a necessary cause for the midwife to be wise and subtle in all these causes, and to beware of error and deception.
E yeu so mostrant tota figura de aquelas, e qual engen es en aquelas per so que sia significat per aquo e sia stat sobre aquo.	And you will show the entire figure of those, and which art is in them so that it may be signified by that and has been established on top.
Quan le feyt es eyssit sobre le sieu cap per egrecio natural, e aquel es vehement sobre la femna e es fayt a lu part dificil, e vezes la vertut de lu ja debelitada, lahoras fay aquela sezer , o que las femnas tenguan lu, e evapora le conh de lu am fenugrec coyt e am olis humitz.	When the child is born on its head by natural expulsion, and that is violent against the woman and is made a difficult part, and times the virtue of it already debilitated, then let that be stopped, or what women have in them, and evaporate the vulva with fenugreek cooked and with sweet olive oil.
E aprop entrometa la metrona entre les sieus ditz espatum petit e fenda am aquel la segondina, o secce aquela am la sua ungla entro que corro aquo que es en ela de humiditat.	And accordingly let the metrona enter between the two said spatula and slit with that which is the second birth, or cut it with its own nail until it runs through what is in it of humidity.
E preme le ventre de la femna entro que deyssenda le fet.	And press the belly of the woman until it descends the afterbirth.
Mays si no deyssen, lahoras cove que la femna sia cristirizada de mucellage de ptilli e mucellage de fenugrec am cizami.	But if it does not descend, then it is necessary that the woman be anointed with a poultice of papyrus and a poultice of fenugreek with camomile.
E aprop comanda a lu, aprop le cristeri, que sia compremuda e fay aquela stornudar am condisi; e te la boca de lu e·l nas de lu per huna hora, quar le fet sira foro-getat tantost.	And accordingly command it to be compressed and make that afterbirth snore with condensation; and tie the mouth of it and the nose of it for one hour, because the afterbirth will soon be forgotten.
E si las doas mas del fet so foro-getadas al comensament, lahoras cove que tu redusiscas aquelas am fecilitat petit a petit.	And if the two more of the afterbirth are forgotten at the beginning, then it is necessary that you reduce those with small ease little by little.
Mays si no obezeys al intrament, lahoras pausa la femna sobre una cezelha e leva les pes de lu sus, e aprop concuceys la cezelha sobre la terra; e la femna sia tenguda que no caia deves la concussio.	But if it does not obey the instrument, then let the woman be paused on a bed and lift her feet up, and accordingly conceive the bed on the earth; and the woman is to be held so that she may not fall with the concussion.
E si las mas no son dedintz tornadas e morr le fet, lahoras inscideys aquelas e extratz le romament del fet o lia le cors a la ma de lu am drap e extratz aquel am equalitat, quar aquel sira foro-getat.	And if the afterbirth is not returned and the child dies, then let those be inscribed and extract the remains of the child or tie its body to the hand with cloth and extract that with equality, because it will soon be forgotten.
De eyssiment del embrio sobre les sieus pes.	On the Exit of the Embryo over its Feet.
Quan le fet yeys sobre les sieus pes, lahoras cove que tu impelliscas aquels en sus, e aprop convertas le fet petit, e aprop que engualhes aquel, e aprop que prenguas un pe de lu e extendas aquels petit a petit.	When the child is born over its feet, then it is necessary that you push those in, and accordingly transform the small child, and accordingly make it equal, and accordingly take one foot of it and stretch those little by little.
Mays cum son eyssit entro a las coyssas, lahoras tu comanda a lu que se exprema, e fay aquela extornudar am condizi, quar sira foro-getat si Deus lo vol.	But when they are born into the legs, then it is necessary that you command them to exit, and make that afterbirth snore with condensation, because it will soon be forgotten if God so wills.
E si no es foro-getat am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras tu retorna le fet petit a petit entro que pauses aquel segon figura natural, quar aquel sira lahoras foro-getat am leugier eyssiment.	And if it is not forgotten with what we have recounted, then you must return the small child little by little until it pauses in the second figure of nature, because that will soon be forgotten with a lighter exit.
E si es prohibit am tot aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras pren de musellage de altea e de goma dissolvuda, e percuteys tot en le mortier per bona percussio, e aprop linieys am aquo le conh de la femna, el pus bas del ventre de lu.	And if it is prohibited by all that we have recounted, then take a poultice of altor and dissolved gum, and pound it all in the mortar with good pounding, and accordingly line it with water on the vulva of the woman, at the lowest part of her belly.
E aprop fay aquela cezer en aygua tebeza, entro que consegua les ypocondias.	And accordingly make that poultice cease in warm water, until it reaches the hypochondria.
E cum vezes que las partidas dejos de lu so lenificadas, lahoras fay a lu subfumiguacio de mirta e sub-pausa aquela a lu.	And when the parts that are left of it are relaxed, then make it sub-fumigate with myrtle and sub-pause it for.
E quan te la sub-fumiguacio per una hora, lahoras tu la fay sezer sobre una cezelha, e aprop fay aquela stornudar e extrenh la boca de lu, e levas de aquela, e prem la partida pus bassa del ventre de lu am leugiera compressio, quar le fet sira tantost foro-getat.	And when the sub-fumigation has taken place for one hour, then make it cease on a bed, and accordingly make that afterbirth snore and stretch out its mouth, and take away from that, and press the lowest part of her belly with gentle compression, because the child will soon be forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet sobre les sieus denols e las suas mas.	Exit of the Child over its Fingers and Toes.
Quan le fet eyssira segon aquesta forma, lahoras tu engenies en entrometen las suas mas petit a petit; e aprop la femna stia evessada sobre le sieu col, e les pes de lu pengo en jos, e aquelas sia jasent sobre le lieyt, e complegua las suas mas.	When the child is born in this form, then you must entwine its toes little by little; and accordingly the woman should be elevated on her neck, and her feet hanging down, and those should be placed on the lyre, and complete its toes.
E aprop prem sobre le ventre de lu petit a petit, e aprop extratz aquo que es dejos les pes de lu de las aurelhas entro que sia preparada en la partida pus dejos.	And accordingly press on her belly little by little, and accordingly extract what is left of her feet from the ears until it is prepared at the lowest part.
E si le fet no es fora-getat, lahoras pren les pes de lu e mau aquels am movement vehement, e aprop prem aquo que es sobre les ypocondres petit a petit entro que le fet puege a las partidas desus.	And if the child is not forgotten, then take her feet and move them with violent motion, and accordingly press that which is on the hypochondria little by little until the child can push against the parts above.
E aprop entrometa las suas mas e engualhe le fet petit a petit, e comanda a la femna que se exprema entro que le fet sia foro-getat.	And accordingly entwine its toes and equalize the child little by little, and command the woman to exit until the child is forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet latutidinalment pendent una de las suas mas.	Exit of the Child laterally hanging from one of its toes.
Sia engeniat en reduccio de la ma de lu, mays si no podes aquela reduzir, lahoras eleva la femna e fe aquela anar.	Be entwined in the reduction of the hand of it, but if you cannot reduce that, then lift the woman and make her go.
E si anar no pot, lahoras fay la jazer sobre le lieyt, e concuteys las coyssas de lu am concussio vehement, e aprop aministra liamentz les quals yeu e recomtatz de mucillages.	And if she cannot go, then make her lie down on the lyre, and pound her legs with strong concussion, and accordingly administer those which I have recounted as poultices.
E si es vengut le enfantament, lahoras fay aquela sezer sobre cezelha, e aprop studia sobre la reduccio de la ma, e enguala le fet segon figura natural, e fay stornudar la femna e comanda a lu que comprema a si entro que sia foro-getat.	And if the childbearing is done, then make her cease on a bed, and accordingly study on the reduction of the hand, and equalize the child according to natural figure, and make the woman snore and command it to compress itself until it is forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet sobre·l col expandudas las suas mas e la fassia de lu es al dos de la sua mayre.	Exit of the Child over its neck, with its toes expanded and the fold of it at the two sides of its mother.
Cove que la matrona tengua la ma del fet e aprop revolva aquel petit a petit, e eque aquel am facilitat.	It is necessary that the midwife take the hand of the child and accordingly revolve it little by little, and make it easy.
E cum es e quant so es engualhat, e lahoras pausa sobre le conh de lu aquo que havem recomtat de oli e de mucellages.	And when it is equalized and as much as is equalized, then pause on the vulva of her that which we have recounted of oil and poultices.
E aprop comandas a lu que·s maugua petit a petit, e quan auras feyt aquo, lahoras fay aquela cezer sobre una cezelha e comanda li que sia inclinada sobre le latz dreyt, e aprop comanda a lu que sia compremuda; e fay aquela stornudar am condizi.	And accordingly command it to be compressed little by little, and when you have done that, then make her cease on a bed and command it to be inclined over the right side, and accordingly command it to be compressed; and make it snore with condensation.
Exitus foetus praeparati super latus.	Exit of the prepared fetus onto its side.
Quan deyssen a horrifici de la mayre segon aquesta manieyra, considera, e lahoras tu inscideys la segondina am la tua ungla entro que sia evacuada de la humiditat.	When it is delivered to the horror of the mother in this manner, consider, and accordingly you inscribe the afterbirth with your nail until it is evacuated of its humidity.
E si le fet es suspendut sobre la cara e·l col de lu, lahoras tu inscideys aquela del embelic, per so que no sia retengut e mora.	And if the child is suspended over the face and neck of it, then you must inscribe that from the navel, for so that it may not be retained and die.
E aprop empelleys le fet a las partidas dedintz entro que pauses aquel segon que cove, e manda a la femna que comprema a si alcunas veguadas, e el sira fora-getat am eyssiment leugier, si Dieus o vol.	And accordingly push the child into the afterbirth until it pauses according to what is necessary, and command the woman to compress herself several times, and if God so wills, it will soon be forgotten with a lighter exit.
Exitus geminorum aut foetuum multorum.	Exit of twins or multiple fetuses.
Sapias que gemels motas veguadas so natz, e alcunas vetz naysso tres o quatre , mays aquo es estranh e tart s’endeve; mays v so causas foro natura, e no vivo.	Know that sometimes twins are born, and some times three or four, but this is strange and does not befit nature; but five causes are natural, and none live.
E conte aquelas, ja sia que sian montiplicatz, una segondina, e son seperatz per ciphac, distingen aquels enter le liguament en l’ombilic de cascun de aquels E alcunas veguadas so foro-getatz ayssi cum es un fet per eyssiment natural leugier, e so eysitz alcunas veguadas per eyssiment no-lausabla ayssi cum havem recomtat.	And in those cases, whether they are multiplied or not, one afterbirth, and they are separated by a ciphac, distinguish each from the others within the navel of each of them. And sometimes they are forgotten thus as if it were one child born naturally with a lighter exit, and sometimes they are born with an unnatural exit just as we have recounted.
E si son dificils alcus de lor deves le enfantament e perveno ad aquo que havem dit de las figuras no-naturals, lahoras tu cura aquels ayssi cum havem recontat.	And if some of them are difficult to deliver and persevere until they reach what we have said about unnatural figures, then you must cure those just as we have recounted.
E si’ la matrona subtil e fassa aquo que fa am facilitat e subtilitat, e am tarditat, e sia ingeniat segon tota figura segon que es a lu preparat de l’engen amenant a salut.	And if the midwife is subtle and does what she does with ease and subtlety, and in delay, and is ingenious according to all figure, according to what is prepared by nature leading to salvation.
Rememoratio eius quod formatur in matrice ex embrionibus et Abortiuntur.	Recollection of what is formed in the womb from embryos and those that are aborted.
Alcunas veguadas son formatz en la mayre un, e dos, e tres, e quatre, e v, e vi, e vii, e mays x, e ja es deves mi verificat que una femna abortem ne getet vi, e una autra x totz formatz, la qual causa fo fayta per mensuracio dels glorios savis.	Certain ages are formed in the mother's womb, one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, and up to ten, and you should verify with me that a woman aborts at the sixth or tenth stage, while another may have all of them formed, which is caused by measurement according to the wise and glorious.
E tot aysso cove que sia en la sciencia de la matrona quar fort leu ad aquela parve semblant de aquo, e donc opause se ad aquo am so que cove.	And all this must be in the science of the midwife because very little is like that to her, and therefore pause at that with such as is necessary.
Capitol .lxxvi.	Chapter LXXVI.
De extraccio del fet quan es mort.	On the Extraction of the Fetus when it is Dead.
Quan tu curas le fet mort am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la medicacio e no es defora eyssit, e tu yest forsat usar de opperacio am ma, lahoras cove que consideras si la femna es de sana vertut e no es am alcu dels accidentz per les quals sobre ela es temuda perdicio.	When you cure the dead fetus with what we have said in the division of medicine and it is not born outside, and you are forced to use an operation on her, then it is necessary that you consider whether the woman has a sound virtue and is not affected by any of the accidents for which upon her there is feared destruction.
Lahoras cove que la femna sia envessada sobre le lieyt sobre le sieu dos, e sia le cap de lu enclinat enjos e las coyssas de lu sian elevadas.	Then it is necessary that the woman be elevated on the lyre over her backside, and have her head inclined downwards, and her legs raised.
E·l ministre tengua aquela de doas partz o sia liada en le lieyt per so que·l cos de lu no se extenda deves la extraccio del fet.	And the minister should hold that with two parts or be tied to the lyre in such a way that the body of it does not extend excessively during the extraction of the fetus.
E aprop tu humecta la boca de la mayre de lu am olis humitz e am mucellage de altea e de fenugrec e de semensa de li.	And accordingly, you should moisten the mouth of her with oil and sweet olive oil and poultice of altor and fenugreek and seed of lily.
E aprop unte la matrona la sua ma am aquels olis e mucellages, e aprop entrometa la sua ma am fecilitat en la mayre, e aprop cerque am la ma loc en le qual fique les uncis en le fet.	And accordingly, the midwife should take her hand with those oils and poultices, and accordingly entwine her hand with ease in the mother, and accordingly search for the precise location where the nails are stuck to the fetus.
E locs convenient en aquo: adonc tu considera si le fet es preparat que deysenda sobre le sieu cap, e lahoras tu fique les uncis en les huels de lu, o en le col, o en la boca, o en le palat, o dejos la barba, o en la furcula de lu, o en les locs propdas de las costas, o dejos les ypocondres.	And find the suitable location there: then you should consider if the fetus is prepared to descend onto its head, and accordingly fix the nails in the hollows of it, or on the neck, or in the mouth, or on the palate, or below the beard, or in the furcula of it, or in the appropriate places on the chest, or below the hypochondria.
Mays si le deysendiment es sobre les pes de lu, lahoras en le pentenilh, o en le mieg de las costas.	But if the descent is onto the feet of it, then in the pubis, or in the middle of the chest.
E cove que tengua le unci am la ma dreyta, e pausa la curvitat de lu en aquel loc le qual es entre les ditz de la ma senestra, e entrometa la ma am facilitat e fique le unci en alcu de aquels locs les quals havem ditz, entro que pervengua a la causa boyda.	And it is necessary to hold the nail with the right hand, and pause the curvature of it in that location which is between the fingers of the left hand, and entwine the hand with ease and fix the nail in some of those locations which we have said, until one reaches the cause of the boyd.
E aprop pause e fique en la apposicio de lu un autre unci, o le tertz si es necessitat, per so que sia atraccio engual, e no sia extencio segon la sua rectetut tant solament.	And accordingly, pause and fix in the apposition of it another nail or the third if necessary, for so that there may be an equal attraction, and not an extension according to its straightness only.
Ans sia maugut a tota partida, per so que l’eyssiment de lu sia alleujat ayssi cum es fayt en dent deves la eradicacio de lu.	And thus it is good for all parts, for so that the exit of it may be alleviated just as it is done in the way of the eradication of it.
E cove en lu aquo que es entre lor que la extencio sia mollificada; e si alcuna partida de lu es retenguda, lahoras cove que la matrona unte alcus sieus ditz am oli e entrometa aquels espertament e revolva am aquels aquo que es retengut.	And it is necessary in that which is between them for the extension to be mollified; and if some part of it is retained, then it is necessary that the midwife take certain fingers with oil and entwine those expertly and revolve with what is retained.
Donc si la partida del fet es fora-getada, lahoras les uncis sian permudatz entra loc le qual sia pus aut; e fay aysso entro que tot le fet sia fora-getat.	Therefore, if the part of the fetus is forgotten, then the nails should be permitted to enter that location where it is more uppermost; and do so until all the fetus is forgotten.
Mays si la ma es eyssida denant l’autra, e no es possible reduzir aquela per la coartacio de lu, lahoras cove que drap sia envolopat sobre aquela; e aprop extratz aquela entro que tota sia fora-getada, e inscideys aquela o en la junctura de la ma o en le coyde.	But if the hand is gone before the other, and it is not possible to reduce that by the contraction of it, then it is necessary that a cloth be wrapped around that; and accordingly extract that until all is forgotten, and inscribe that either in the juncture of the hand or in the armpit.
E ayssi cove que fassas en l’autra ma e en les dos pes.	And thus it is necessary to do the same for the other hand and both feet.
Mays si le cap del fet es gran, o accideys a lu coartacio en le eyssiment, o es en le cap de lu aygua ajustada, lahoras cove que entrometa entre les ditz espatum spinos e fenda le cap e extragua la aygua, o que discroba aquel am un instrument le qual es nompnat “alundat”, la forma del qual vindra am las formas dels autres instruments en le capitol le qual es aprop aquest.	But if the head of the fetus is large, or if there is contriction in the exit, or if there is water adjusted in the head of it, then it is necessary that the midwife entwine between the fingers the spatula with spines and split the head and extract the water, or that she dissects that with a instrument which is called "alundat", the form of which will come from the forms of the other instruments in the chapter which is appropriate to this.
E semblantment fassa si·l fet es de gran cap per natura: e lahoras cove que inscida aquel am algematu, o que prengua aquel am alunda ayssi cum havem dit; e aprop extra les osses am les forceps.	And similarly do so if the fetus is naturally large-headed: and then it is necessary that you inscribe that with an algemate, or take that with an alundat as we have said; and accordingly extract the bones with forceps.
E si le cap es eyssit e es coartat deves la furcula, lahoras sia fendut entro que la humiditat la qual es en le pietz sia efunduda.	And if the head is extracted and constricted at the furcula, then it should be split open until the humidity which is in the feet is poured out.
Mays si no es complicat, ni obezeys a eyssiment, lahoras tu inscideys le cap tantost segon que a tu sira possible.	But if it is not complicated, nor obeys the exit, then you should inscribe the head at once according to what is possible for you.
E si le dejos del ventre es apostemat o es en lu ydropici, lahoras cove que tu perfores aquel entro que corro la humiditat que es en lu.	And if the remaining part of the belly is apostemated or is in a liquid state, then it is necessary that you perforate it until the humidity which is in it runs out.
Mays si le fet es sobre les sieus pes, lahoras la atraccio de lu es leugiera e la direccio de lu a la boca de la mayre es leugiera.	But if the fetus is on its feet, then the attraction of it is light and the direction of it to the mouth of the mother is light.
Mays si es coartat deves le ventre e·l pietz, lahoras cove que tu extraguas aquel am drap le qual auras envolopat sobre la tua ma, e que fendes le ventre e·l pietz entro que corra aquo que es en aquels.	But if it is constricted at the belly and feet, then it is necessary that you extract that with cloth which you will have wrapped around your hand, and that you split open the belly and feet until the water which is in them runs out.
Mays si les autres membres so ostatz e torna le cap, lahoras la metrona entrometa la ma senestra; mays si la boca de la mayre es huberta, lahoras intrometa la ma en le preon de layre, e cerque am aquela le cap, e atira aquel am les ditz entro a la boca de la mayre, e aprop entrometa en lu un unci, o dos uncis, e atire lu am aquels.	But if the other members are still and return to the head, then take it with your left hand; but if the mouth of the mother is swollen, then insert your hand into the preeon of layre, and seek out that head, and draw it with those fingers into the mouth of the mother, and accordingly entwine in it one nail, or two nails, and pull it with them.
