E si la boca de la mayre es coartada per apostema caut le qual accideys a l’u, lahoras cove que no sia trebelhat sobre lu; abantz cove lahoras aministrar efusio de causas humidas grassas.	And if the mouth of the mother is constricted by an apostemal swelling that occurs in it, then it is necessary not to trouble about it; instead, it is necessary to administer an effusion of humid and greasy causes.
E aministre emplastres; e segua le pacient en ayguas que mollifican e humectan.	And minister plasters; and follow the patient in waters that soften and moisten.
E si le fet es sobre le sieu costat, lahoras si possible es, sia agulat: e sia aministrat aquo que havem dit en le fet viu.	And if the fetus is on its own chest, then it is necessary to pierce it as much as possible; and administer water that we have said for the living fetus.
E si aquo no es possible, lahoras sia inscidit en pessas, e sia extrayt.	And if this is not possible, then it is necessary to inscribe in membranes, and extract.
E cove que non layssas alcuna causa dedintz de la segondina.	And it is necessary that you do not leave any cause behind the afterbirth.
E cum tu auras complida tota la tua opperacio, lahoras aministra aquo que havem dit de la curacio en les apostemas cautz les quals accideysso de la mayre.	And when you have completed all your operation, then administer water that we have said for the cure of apostemal swellings which occur in the mother.
E si accideys flux de sanc, lahoras deyssendas en ayguas stipticas e aministra l’autra curacio.	And if there occurs a flow of blood, then you should descend into stiptic waters and administer the other cure.
E yeu ja e vist una femna en le ventre de la qual era fet mort, e aprop sobre aquel foc autra veguada emprenhada, e aprop foc mort es le fet autre.	And I have already seen a woman in whose belly was a dead fetus, and accordingly above that same focus another pregnancy begun, and accordingly dead heat is the other fetus.
Accidit al u aprop lonc temps apostema en le sieu embelic; e inflat es entro que foc ubert, e comensec a getar brac.	An accident befell me at a long time ago, an apostemal swelling in my own navel; and it swelled up to the point of being like a hot fever, and I began to discharge pus.
E yeu fu appelhat a la cura de lu, e medicat a lu per lonc temps, e la plagua no es consolidada.	And you were summoned to his cure, and treated him for a long time, and the wound did not consolidate.
Adonc yeu pausegui sobre lu de alscunas causas emplastra de forta atraccio, e eyssic de lu un os, e aprop passero alcus jorns, e eyssic un autre os; e yeu fu trop meravilhat, cum en le ventre no sia os.	Then I applied to him some plaster of strong attraction, and extracted from him a bone, and after passing certain days, I extracted another bone; and I was too amazed, as in the belly there should not be bones.
E adonc yeu cogitegui que eran dels osses del fet mort.	And then I thought that they were the bones of the dead fetus.
Donc yeu enguisigui la plagua, e extrayssi de lu motz osses , la femna existent en las sieuas milhos disposicios, e ja visquec en tal manieyra per lonc temps, correc de lu un petit de brac.	Therefore I dressed the wound, and extracted from him several bones, the woman existing in her own milk-disposing vessels, and already living in such a way for a long time, corrected by him a small amount of pus.
E yeu no afermegui asso esser stranh, sino quar en aquo es sciensa e ajutori ad aquo que le metge artifec am la ma per curacio aministra.	And I did not consider it strange, but rather because in that is science and assistance to that which the physician artist administers with his hand for cure.
De las formas dels instrumentz que so necessaris a extrayre le fet.	On the forms of the instruments that are necessary to extract the fetus.
Forma de vertitge am la qual es uberta la mayre:	Form of a veritable uterus, in which is opened the mother:
Aquesta es la forma de strenhedor en le qual so engualhatz les libres, al qual engualhament sian dos virtitges en doas extremitatz de dos futz.	This is the form of strength in which are equalized the liberties, to which equalization are two virtues at two extremities of two feet.
May empero aquesta virtitge cove que sia pus subtil de strictori, e sia fayt o de eba o de fust de boys.	But however this virtue must be more subtle in the strictor, and made of ebony or of boxwood.
E sia la latitut de quascun fust quays dos ditz e le marge de quascu amdos quays un dit, e la longitut de quascu es un palm e mig; e en le mieg loc de dos fustz so dos ajustaments de aquel meteys fustz les quals ja son fermatz, dels quals la longitut es la maytat de un palm e un pauc mes, e la latitut de quascu es quay dos ditz, o un pauc mes.	And the latitude of each foot is two fingers and the edge of both feet is one finger; and the longitude of each is one palm and a half; and in the middle location between the two woods are two adjustments of those very woods which are already fixed, the length of which is almost equal to one palm and a little more, and the latitude of each is two fingers or a little more.
E aquestz dos additamentz sian entromeses en la boca de la mayre per que sia uberta am aquels quan tu revolves las doas prescriptas virtigges.	And these two adjustments are entwined in the mouth of the mother so that it is opened to them when you revolve the two prescribed virtues.
Forma autra semblant de aquela pus subtil e pus leugiera:	Another similar form, but more subtle and lighter:
Sia fayta de fustz de eba o de boys segon la semblansa de forceps.	It is made of ebony or boxwood wood, according to the shape of forceps.
Mays empero en la extremitat de lu so dos additament ayssi cum vezes, e la longitut de aquels additament es quays un palm, e la latitut de quascu es dos ditz.	But however in the extremity of it there are two adjustments like times, and the length of those adjustments is one palm, and the latitude of each is two fingers.
E cum tu vols am aquels ubrir la mayre, lahoras tu fay cezer la femna sobre le lieyt les pes pendentz, ubert aquo que es entre las coyssas de lu.	And when you want to open the mother with those, then you must cause the woman to cease sitting on the lyre, and let her feet hang down, so that what is between her thighs may be opened.
E aprop obre la tua ma am le instrument ayssi cum fas am forfexs engualment segon la quantitat que vols de la aprecio de la boca de la mayre entro que la metrona fassa so que vols.	And accordingly work with your hand on the instrument just as you would with forceps equalization according to the quantity that you want of the appreciation of the mouth of the mother until she makes it in the way that you want.
La forma de vertitge la qual diysero les antics:	The form of uterus which they called the ancients:
Forma de impellent am le qual es empellit le fet:	Form of impulsion, in which the fetus is propelled.
Forma de amisidat2 am le qual es conterit le cap gran	Form of amenorrhea, in which the large head is contained.
E es asemblat a forceps al qual so dentz en la extremitat, ayssi cum vezes, e alcunas veguadas es fayt lonc ayssi cum forceps segon aquesta forma, ayssi cum vezes, al qual so dentz ayssi cum dentz de ressegua am le qual es inscidit e conterit.	And it is assembled with forceps which have teeth at the end, like times, and sometimes it is made long like forceps according to this form, like times, which has teeth like teeth of a reaping hook with which it is inscribed and contained.
Forma de amesidat pauc:	Form of amenorrhea little:
Forma de unci havent una spina:	Form of nail having a spine:
Forma de unci havent doas spinas:	Form of nail having two spines:
Forma de forceps a la qual so dentz de cerra am le qual le cap del fet sia conterit:	Form of forceps to which are teeth like saws with which the head of the fetus is contained.
Forma de spatum havent dos extremitatz am le qual le cap es abscindit:	Form of spatula having two extremities at which the head is cut off:
Forma de dos espatums latz:	Form of two broad spatulas:
Totz aquels instrumentz so excersitatz, e quan mes so multiplicadas las specias de aquel e so preparadas deves le artifexs, quant es pus leugier a la sua opperacio e pus aut deves les homes per la sua quantitat.	All those instruments are exercised, and when more species of them are multiplied and prepared, the artisans must be as skilled in their operation and as expert as they can be, for it is easier to perform their operation.
E no obres de aquels instrumentz ja sia qua sia deves tu aparalhat, quar la necessitat de aquels no es excusabla.	And you must not neglect those instruments in any way, for the necessity of them is irrepressible.
De extraccio de la segondina.	On the extraction of the afterbirth.
Quan la segondina es retenguda deves le enfantament, lahoras cove que tu comandes a la malautae que retengua le sieu ale, e aprop fay aquela stornudar am condizi, e strenh la tua ma sobre la boca de lu e sobre las nars de lu, e si per aysso es defora eyssit, bo es.	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, then it is necessary that you order the patient to strain her own belly, and accordingly make her fart with conditions, and strengthen your hand over the mouth of her and on her nostrils, and if through this it has come out, all is well.
E sino, lahoras tu pren una ola e perfora en la cuberta un trauc e pausa en aquela erbas ubrent la boca de la mayre, ayssi cum calament e ruda e anet e camamilla e scicados arabic e cassia lignea e santaurea.	And if not, then you take a cloth and perforate it in the covering of a wound and pause in that herb which opens the mouth of the mother, like calamus, rough thistle, anise, camomile, Arabic balm, cassia lignea, and St. John's Wort.
Totas aquestas erbas o alcunas de lor sian submersas en aygua en la ola, e pausa aquela sobre le foc.	All these herbs or some of them are submerged in water in the cloth, and then pause it on the fire.
E aprop pausa una canula de canaviera en la boca de la mayre, e tengua aquela entro que la evapor vengua a la concavitat de la mayre.	And accordingly, place a reed cane in the mouth of the mother, and keep it until the vapor comes to the concavity of the mother.
E aprop fay aquela stornudar ayssi cum havem dit, e la segondina sira fora-getada am velocitat.	And accordingly, make her fart as we have said, and the afterbirth will be expelled with speed.
Mays si roman aprop aquesta curacio e no es eyssida, lahoras tu comanda a la matrona que submerge la sua ma sinistra en oli sizami o en micellage de altea, e aprop entrometa aquela en le conh e queresca am aquela la segondina, e cum aquela auras trobada, lahoras pren la e exten aquela pauc a pauc Mays si es annexsa en le preon de la mayre, lahoras entrometa la sua ma segon que havem recomtat, e quan aura trobat la segondina, extragua aquela petit a petit segon rectetut per so que la mayre no caja deves la atraccio vehement.	But if the cure does not take effect and the afterbirth remains, then you command the midwife to submerge her left hand in sesame oil or in an emulsion of aloes, and accordingly entwine it with a cord and seek out the afterbirth, and when you find it, then take it and stretch it little by little. But if it is attached in the womb of the mother, then entwine your hand as we have recounted, and when you find the afterbirth, extract it slowly and carefully so that the mother does not suffocate from the vehement attraction.
Abantz cove que sia permudada als costatz dreyt e sinestre am facilitat.	Above all, it is necessary to be skilled on both right and left sides with ease.
E aprop sia ajustat en la quantitat de atraccio, quar ela obedira e evasira de adhirencia.	And accordingly, adjust in the quantity of attraction, for she will obey and evade adherence.
E si la boca de la mayre es coartada, nos ja havem recomtat la curacio am sturnutacio e am medicacio de la ola am erbas.	And if the mouth of the mother is constricted, we have already recounted the cure with farting and medication of the cloth with herbs.
Mays si no es fora-getada am totas las causas las quals havem recomtadas, lahoras guarda te que no fetigues sobre aquela en iteracio de abstracio, mays empero cove que aquo que es eyssit de lu a la boca de la mayre lies a la coyssa de la femna, e aprop cristeriza aquela am enguent e tetrafarmacon; quar aquel fara poyrir aquela aprop alcus dias e sira dissolvuda e sira fora-getada.	But if it is not expelled with all the causes which we have recounted, then be careful that you do not tire over it in iteration of abstraction, but rather let what has come out from it to the mouth of the mother lie in the vagina of the woman, and accordingly encrust it with a poultice and tetra-pharmacopoeia; for that will make it rot away slowly and dissolve and be expelled.
Mays quan se poyreys, es de lu elevada mala audor al cap, e al estomac, e aquo ledeys la malauta; e adonc cove que sian aministradas sub-fumiguacios e convenientz ad aquo.	But when it rots, it is elevated to bad authority in the head and stomach, and accordingly leads the patient into suffering; and then it is necessary that sub-fumigations and conveniences be administered according to this.
Mays alcus dels Antics ja so esproatz sub-fumigacio de nazitort e de figuas seccas.	But some of the Ancients have already been experimented with sub-fumigation of hazelnuts and dried figs.
Forma de instrument am le qual la femna es sub-fumiguada deves la retentio de mestruas e de la segondina:	Form of instrument with which the woman is sub-fumigated in order to retain menstruation and afterbirth:
Sia fayta de veyre o de eram.	It is made of yew or horn.
E sia pausada la extremitat subtil en le conh e la extremitat ampla sobre le foc, e la sub-fumiguacio sia pausada sobre las brazas del foc.	And it is paused with the subtle extremity in the womb and the wide extremity over the fire, and the sub-fumigation is paused over the arms of the fire.
E tengua aquela entro que sia consumida aquela sub-fumiguacio e itera·n autra.	And keep that in until that sub-fumigation is consumed and iterate with another.
De curacio del cul del enfant no-perforat.	On the cure of the unbroken navel of the child.
Motz enfantz naysso e les culs de lu no so perforatz, les quals ya ciphac subtil e opilat.	Many children are born with navels that are not perforated, which already have a subtle and opaque cicatrice.
Adonc cove a la matrona que perfore am le sieu dit aquel ciphac; e sino, perfora aquel am spatum agut, e guarda se que no toque le lacert.	Then have the midwife pierce with her own finger that cicatrice; and if not, pierce it with a sharp spatula, and be careful not to touch the lactation.
E aprop pause sobre aquel lana enfusa en vi e oli; e aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia senat.	And accordingly, place on that a layer of lanolin infused in wine and oil; and accordingly cure it with a poultice until it is healed.
Mays si temes que sia opilat, lahoras pausa en le trauc una canula per motz dias, e osta la quan le enfant voldra degerir.	But if you fear that it may be opilated, then place a reed cane in the wound for several days, and stop when the child will desire to defecate.
E ja accideys oppilacio del cul per consolidacio de plagua o de apostema; adonc cove que aquela consolidacio sia inscidida, e aprop sia curada am aquo que avem dit de la curacio e del plom.	And if there occurs an opilation of the navel due to consolidation of wound or apostemal swelling; then it is necessary that this consolidation be inscribed, and accordingly cured with the water we have said for the cure and lead.
De curacio de las fistulas que endeveno dejos.	On the cure of fistulas that were left over.
Las fistulas que endeveno en la partida dejos pus bassa so nodacio e grossetut las quals endeveno prop del cul defora o en l’espazi de la una partida.	The fistulas which remain after the departure, being lower down in the navel and thicker than those which are located near the anus outside or in the space of one part.
E es una fistula o motas.	And it is a single fistula or several.
E cum aquela nodacio es antiquada e corr de la humiditat aygosa blanca o poyridura subtil, e alcunas veguadas so de aquestas fistulas alcunas penetrantz.	And since this nodule is aged and flows with white or subtle pus, and sometimes some of these fistulas are penetrating.
E aquelas penetrantz so conogudas per aquo que es eyssit de aquelas per la egressio e per ventosetat; e alcunas vetz use le malaute de egressio, e fort leu es eyssit de aquelas verm.	And those that are penetrating are known by what comes out of them through the egress and windiness; and sometimes the patient uses the egress, and very little comes out from those vermin.
E so de aquelas fistulas alcunas veguadas en l’espazi penetrantz entro a la vesica, e entro al meat de la vergua; e so de aquelas penetrantz entro la junctura de la coyssa e entro al notz de la coeta.	And some of those fistulas sometimes penetrate into the space between the bladder and the urethra, and into the glans of the penis; and some also penetrate into the junction of the vagina and into the notch of the clitoris.
E aquo en que es conoguda fistula penetrant entro al cul e no-penetrant, es que tu metas le tieu dit endic en le cul, e entrometas tenta subtil de eram o de ferr en la fistula quan no y es turtuositat.	And the way to know if a fistula is penetrating into the anus or not-penetrating, is that you insert your finger into the anus and entwine a subtle thread of horn or iron in the fistula when there is no turbulence.
Mays si en aquela es turtuositat, lahoras entromet en aquela tenta subtil de plom o de pels de caval entro que tu sentas la tenta o le pel en le tieu dit.	But if there is turbulence in that, then you insert into it a subtle thread of lead or horsehair until you feel the thread or hair in your finger.
E si no sentas aquela de tot ni no procezeys del trauc alcuna causa de egestio ni verm ni ventositat, ayssi cum havem dit, lahoras sapias que es no-penetrant, e lahoras coyta te a la curacio.	And if you don't feel that at all or there is no process of the tract at all nor any cause of egestion, vermin, or windiness, as we have said, then you know it is not-penetrating, and accordingly turn to the cure.
E quan la fistula es penetrant entro a la vesica o entro al meat de la vergua, lahoras la significacio de lu es eyssiment de urina de aquela e prohibicio de lu ad aysso que·l loc am medicina sia consolidat.	And when the fistula is penetrating into the bladder or into the glans of the penis, then the significance of it is to be cleansed with urine from that place and prohibition of further passage so that the location may be consolidated through medicine.
Mays si es penetrant entro la junctura de la coyssa o entro al os e envencio de dolor en le circuit, lahoras senhal de lu es que la tenta perve entro aqui si en lu no es turtuositat entro al os, e envencio de dolor en le circuit de la partida; e que de lu yeys poyredura tostemps; e que no val en aquela medicacio, ni es consolidada am enguent.	But if it is penetrating into the junction of the vagina or into the bone and causing pain in the circuit, then the sign of it is that the thread will pass through here if there is no turbulence in the bone, and pain in the circuit of the part; and that from here there is pus everywhere; and that it does not hold with medicine, nor is it consolidated by poultice.
E en totas aquelas fistulas penetrant no es curacio de tot, e la curacio de aquelas es trebalh e vanetat dels folyls metges sobre·l qual so fermatz.	And in all those penetrating fistulas there is no complete cure, and the cure of these is the toil and vanity of foolish physicians who are fixed.
Mays en aquela que no es penetrant e no antiqua, sanacio am ferr es sperada segon que yeu a tu recomtare, e aquo que ja yeu e proat.	But in that which is not penetrating and not aged, the healing with iron is expected according to what you have recounted, and what has been tried.
E es que le malaute jagua entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos e eleva las cambas de lu entro sus, las coyssas sian enclinadas al ventre de lu, e aprop entromet tenta de plom, o de eram si es en la fistula turtuositat, entro que sapias le loc on perve la tenta.	And it is that the patient lies between your thighs over his own back and raises his knees to yours, so that the woman's legs are inclined towards her belly, and accordingly you insert a thread of lead or horn into the fistula if there is turbulence, until you know the place where the thread passes.
E si aquela sent le malaute entorn le cuol, lahora cove que tu entrometas le tieu dit endic en le cuol.	And if that patient feels pain around the navel, then you must insert your finger into the navel.
E si sentas en le tieu dit la tenta ja per si meteyssa descuberta penetrar, otra aquo que sentas entre le tieu dit e aquela siphac o carn, lahoras sapias certanament que aquela es penetrant; e adonc no trebalhes en aquela, quar no es en aquela sanacio, ayssi cum havem dit.	And if you feel the thread already inserted and having passed through, or between your finger and that siphac or flesh, then you know certainly that it is penetrating; and accordingly do not intervene in that, for there is no healing in that, as we have said.
Mays empero diyssero alcus que es sana en alcus homes tart.	But however, some may say that it is healed in some men's hearts.
E de la medicacio per la qual es sperat juvament en lu es que tu ignes cauteri subtil segon le ample de la fistula, ayssi cum es precedit, e intrometas aquel ignit en la fistula entro que pervengua entorn le cuol; e aprop itera aquel doas o tres vetz entro que sapias que ja son adhustas totas aquelas carns ajustadas fistuladas que so semblantz a cana de pluma de ausel.	And the medicine by which healing is expected in that place is that you ignite a subtle cauter, according to the size of the fistula, just as it has been preceded, and insert that ignited into the fistula until it comes around the navel; and accordingly iterate that two or three times until you know that all those fleshed-adjusted fistulas that are like reeds of swan's plumage have become adjusted.
E aprop cura aquela am calguas envolopadas en boder entro que en yescan totas aquelas carns que so adhustas, e aprop cura aquela am medicinas la carn engendrantz e consolidantz, e si es sanada, bo es; e sino, lahoras no es sana en degun temps per autra curacio.	And accordingly, cure that with cloth wraps in butter until all those adjusted fleshed-adjusted fistulas are healed; and accordingly, cure that with medicines promoting and consolidating the skin, and if it is healed, well; and otherwise, there will be no healing at any time through another cure.
E si la tenta intra, e no penetra entro·l tieu dit le qual es en le cul, e entre aquel e la tenta que es velament spes de carn o de ciphac, e vezes la fistula en aquo que siec la superficia de la codena, lahoras secca la codena del comensament de la fistula, e tu ve seccan am la tenta, e sia en la fistula entro que la seccio pervengua al loc en le qual perve la extremitat de la tenta, e per la tenta es liberat e catz.	And if the thread goes in and does not penetrate into the navel which is in the anus, but instead enters between that and the thread which is a velamen of flesh or cicatrix, and the fistula opens up to the surface of the skin, then dry the skin from the beginning of the fistula, and you see it drying with the thread, and it is in the fistula until the drying reaches the location where the end of the thread emerges, and through the thread it is liberated and cut.
E aprop mundifiqua aquelas carns fistuladas las quals so asembladas a canula de pena de ausel e no romangua de aquelas alcuna causa.	And accordingly, cleanse those fleshed-adjusted fistulas which are assembled like a reed of swan's plumage and do not remain any cause.
Mays si flux de sanc vezes que vengua entre tu e la tua opperacio quan ensideysses aquelas carns, lahoras le milh que sia e del pus leugier instrument es cauterizar am foc o am medicina acuta, quar cauteri am foc ajusta bonas doas habitutz: so es adhustio de aquelas carns ajustadas, e abscizio del sanc exseccacio de las humiditatz.	But if there is a flow of pus which comes between you and your operation when you are cleansing those fleshed-adjusted fistulas, then the most excellent instrument to use is cauterization with fire or acute medicine, because cauterization with fire adjusts good two habits: so it adjusts those adjusted fleshed-adjusted fistulas, and abscesses the pus by excising excess humors.
E aprop cura aquela am calguas envolopadas en boder o en caus trissat entro que·l loc geta brac, e aprop lahoras cura la plagua am enguentz carn dura engendran e consolidan.	And accordingly, cure that with cloth wraps in butter or in threefold fabric until the place gets firm, and accordingly, cure the wound with poultices of hard flesh which generate and consolidate.
E so medicinas en las quals so stipticitat e exseccio; quan lahoras es restaurada ja es sanada e no temes iteracio.	And these medicines, in which there is purification and excision; when accordingly it is restored, it is already healed and you do not fear relapse.
Mays si la fistula ja perve entro al preon del cul e es elonguada de lu superficia del cos, lahoras entromet le tieu dit en le cul e inquireys am aquel.	But if the fistula has already penetrated into the perineum of the anus and is elongated from the surface of the body, then insert your finger into the anus and investigate that.
E donc si centes la tenta e entre tu e ela es velament de ciphac o de carn, e es propda a la penetracio, lahora no es operacio en lu sino segon via di fiducia e de speransa.	And therefore, if the thread is inserted and between you and it is a velamen of cicatrix or flesh, and it is prepared for penetration, then there is no operation in that place except through the way of faith and hope.
La qual causa es aministrar en lu una de tres manieyras: o que cauterize aquela ayssi cum havem dit; o que secces aquela entro que consieguas la conquavitat de lu per que sia a tu possible entrometre las qualcas e la curacio propdana; e no procesiscas mot am seccio per so que no inscidas le lacert contenent le cuol, e que accidisque sobre le malaute eyssiment de la egistio ses voluntat; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit quar fort leu sira sanat; o que elongues aquel velament e mondes aquel pus que seccas aquel entro prop le cul, ayssi cum havem dit, o am tenta o am autre instrument de aguda extremitat, e aprop mondifique aquelas carns fistuladas las quals so en la seccio entro la on podes am percrustacio; e aprop esforsa te a far la restauracio de tota la plagua am seccio, e si le orrifici pus desus no es consolidat, e romangua la fistula uberta en la partida del cul, e sira pus leugier per le malaute.	The cause is to administer in that place one of three ways: either to cauterize it as we have said; or to dry it until you achieve the conquest of the place so that you can insert the threads and the propounded cure, and do not process anything else except drying because you do not want to inscribe the lacerta contained in the navel, and what happens is that it occurs on the patient's own accord through their desire; or to elongate the velamen and remove the pus that dries out that place until it reaches the prop of the anus, as we have said, either with a thread or with another instrument of acute extremity, and accordingly cleanse those fleshed-adjusted fistulas which are in the drying process, and accordingly strive to make the restoration of the entire wound through drying, and if the orifice above is not consolidated and the fistula remains open on one side of the anus, it will be even more difficult for the patient.
E alscunas veguadas la fistula es finida segon aquesta manieyra: es quan tu entrometas la tenta en la fistula, e es en le latz del cul entorn la superficia del cos am la codena e en le marge del cul, lahoras pren tenta de perforada extremitat, que es ayssi cum agulha de preparantz les coers segon aquesta forma:	And sometimes the fistula is finished in this way: when you insert the thread into the fistula, and it is on the edge of the anus around the surface of the body with the skin and on the margin of the anus, then take the thread of perforated extremity, which is like a needle preparing the vessels according to this form:
e entromet en aquela fiel envolopat de v fiels o entorn aquels; e aprop entromet tenta am fiel en la fistula entro que consiegua la conquavitat de lu.	and insert it into that faithful wrap of V-folds or around those, and accordingly insert the thread into the fistula until you achieve the conquest of that place.
Mays si es penetrant en le marge del cul prop dedintz, lahoras tu extratz le fiel de aquel trauc ayssi que tu intrometas le tieu dit en le cul; e extraguas la extremitat del fiel e ajustes las duas extremitatz essemps, e estrenh cascuna, e leyssa aquo per un dia o per dos, e quan mays inscideys le fiel en la carn, estrenh be aquel entro que aquelas carns sian inscididas las quals so entre doas extremitatz del fiel e que cajan.	But if it is penetrating in the margin of the anus, then you extract the thread from that tract as if you were inserting your finger into the anus; and extract the extremity of the thread and adjust the two ends to be equal, and strengthen each one, and leave it like that for a day or two, and when you insert the thread more deeply into the flesh, strengthen it well until those fleshed-adjusted parts are inserted between the two ends of the thread and they fall apart.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia consolidada e sanada.	And accordingly, cure the wound so that it is consolidated and healed.
Mays si le orrifici de la fistula no es penetrant, lahoras fay aquel penetrar, en qualque manieyre sia a tu preparat, sino que sia mot en le preon, quar no es a tu que fassas aquo per que no inscidas le lacert; e aprop fay am aquela entro que sia sanada.	But if the orifice of the fistula is not penetrating, then make it penetrate in any way that you have prepared, except not to make it too narrow, for it is not up to you to do so; and accordingly, make it so that it is healed.
La forma de spatum spinos am lo qual es fenduda la fistula: la curvitat del qual es mot aguda e l’autra partida es no-aguda, per so que no inscidas aquo que no es necessari, ayssi cum vezes.	The form of the spatula with which the fistula is split open: its curvature is very sharp and the other part is not sharp, so that you do not insert anything that is unnecessary, as sometimes happens.
De sutura de emorroydas en las quals corra sanc en la inscizio de aquelas.	On the suturing of hemorrhoids in which there is bleeding in the incision of those.
Emorroydas so segon dos manieyras, quar o so entre le cul semblantz aysi que es de carbos, o quays aquelas sian cum a gras de rasim.	Hemorrhoids are according to two ways, for either they are between the anus like carbon, or those that are like grass on rye.
E de aquelas so petitas e grans, e que le sanc corr de aquelas tostemps e es una, e so motas, e so fora·l cul, e en las extremitatz de lu.	And of those there are small and large ones, and the blood flows from them at all times and is one, and many, and outside the anus, and in the extremities of it.
Mays empero aquelas que so foro le cul so segon las mes de pauca humiditat, de las quals corr aygua citrina o un petit de sanc am cos continuabla, e so segon la color del cos.	But however, those that are outside the anus are according to the months of little humidity, from which yellow water or a small amount of blood flows with continuous flow, and according to the color of the body.
E la curacio de aquela que es dedintz le cuol es que comandes al malaute que se assela e que se exprema entro que le cuol yesca e las emoroydas apparescan a tu.	And the cure for that which is outside the anus is that you command the patient to sit down and to stretch out until the anus is relaxed and the hemorrhoids appear to you.
Adonc tu te coyte e suspen am uncis o que tenguas aquelas am la tua ungla, e aprop incideys aquelas deves las suas razitz.	Then you take hold and suspend with the hooks or whatever you have those at your finger's end, and accordingly insert those into the patient's rectum.
Mays si les uncis no so tengutz en aquelas per la humiditat de lor e mollificacio de aquelas, lahoras pren aquelas am drap aspre o am coto o am flassada de lana, e extratz aquelas am les tieus ditz, e aprop inscideys aquelas e polveriza sobre lor alcunas polveras caudas aprop la inscizio, per que sian ad aquelas en loc de cauteri; o cauteriza aquelas segon que es precedit en le capitol de cauterizar.	But if the hooks are not grasped in those due to the moisture of their surface and softening of those, then take those with a rough cloth or a piece of cotton or wool, and extract them with your fingers, and accordingly insert them and powder some powders over them around the incision, so that they are adapted to those places where cauterization is needed; or cauterize those according to what has been preceded in the chapter on cauterization.
E aprop cura aquelas am l’autra curacio entro que sian sanadas.	And accordingly, cure those with the other cure until they are healed.
E si le cul no obezeys a egressio, lahoras cristerisa le malaute am cristeri en le qual sia mordicacio petita, e sia lavat am aquel aquo que es en le cuol e que obezesca a egressio leugierament quan le malaute s’esprem.	And if the anus does not obey evacuation, then cause the patient to sit on a cristeri with a little bit of mordicacio, and be washed with that water which is in the navel and which will obey evacuation slightly when the patient presses.
Mays si las emorroydas so defora le cul, lahoras la causa de lor es leugiera, e es que tu prenguas aquelas am la tua ungla, o que prenguas aquelas am unci, e inscidas aquelas, e aprop cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit entro que sian sanadas.	But if the hemorrhoids are outside the anus, then the cause of theirs is slight, and it is that you take those with your finger or with hooks and insert them, and accordingly cure those with the water we have said until they are healed.
E aquel que avoreys inscizio, cove que aministres sutura de lor segon aquesta manieyra: pren fiel envolopat e entromet aquel en agulha e aprop extratz las emorroydas a las partidas dessus, e fay aquel penetrar am la agulha en la razit del autra part, e envolveys las doas extramitatz del fiel en la partida pus dejos de la agulha, e so latitudinalment; e estrenh la emorroyda am strectura fort, e aprop noza le fiel e extratz la agulha.	And he who will make the incision must administer suturing to them in this manner: take a thread wrapped around and insert it into a needle and accordingly extract the hemorrhoids from the upper parts, and make that penetrate with the needle into the root of the other part, and wrap the two ends of the thread around the most distant part from the needle, and so latitudinally; and strengthen the hemorrhoid with strong stricture, and accordingly pull out the thread and extract the needle.
E fay aquo a totas, e layssa de aquelas una e no la cozes, per so que la superfluitat del sanc corra de aquela.	And do this to all of them, and leave one and don't close it, so that the superfluity of blood will flow from that one.
E aprop pausa sobre le cul drap enfus en oli rozat o en cerot; e pausa aquel sobre·l cuol e comanda al malaute que·s repause.	And accordingly, pause on the anus with a cloth dipped in rose oil or cerote; and pause that on the navel and command the patient to rest.
E aprop layssa aquela entro que caja; e quan es casuda, cura aquelas am enguentz o am autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, leave that until it forms a scab; and when it has formed, cure those with poultices or other cures until they are healed.
De curacio de fistulas.	On the Cure of Fistulas.
Motas veguadas accideys per exseccacio de fenda o per costriccio de natura.	Many times accidents happen through excision of a fissure or constriction of nature.
E cum so antiquadas e no val en aquela medicina, lahoras cove que tu razas aquelas am la puncta de spatum o am la tua ungla entro que sian faytas humidas e sia hostada de aquelas la escorsa pus desus, la qual prohibeys aquelas de consolidacio; e aprop cura aquelas entro que sian consolidadas.	And since they are so old and no longer good with that medicine, then you must take those away with the point of a spatula or your finger until they are made humid and there is no more scabbing above, which prevents them from consolidating; and accordingly, cure those until they are consolidated.
Lahoras tu osta aquelas am razio pus vehement que la primieyra entro que mot sancno e sian excoriadas; e aprop cura aquelas entro que sian sanadas.	Then you must take those away with the reason more violent than the first, until there is no more bleeding and they are exfoliated; and accordingly, cure those until they are healed.
De curacio de almesamir, so es clau.	On the Cure of Hemorrhoids, that is the key.
Sapias que alamermar, so es clau, e no es si no notz redon segon la color del cors semblant a cap de claviel, e es fayt en tot le cors e majorment en las partidas dejos les pes e als ditz, e endeve per aquels dolor deves le anament.	Know that hemorrhoids, that is the key, and not just notes in red according to the color of the body like a cap of claviel, and it is done throughout the entire body and most especially in the lower parts and the right side, and thus it can be inferred by those pains that one should take heed.
E adonc cove que sia inscidit aquo que es en le circuit del clau, e sia tengut am les forfexs o am unci, e sia eradicat de la sua razit; e aprop cura aquel.	And then it is necessary to incise that which is in the circuit of the key, and to take hold with forceps or hooks, and to eradicate its root; and accordingly, cure that.
E si vols, cauteriza le segont que es precedit en le sieu capitol.	And if you wish, cauterize it according to what is preceded in the chapter on cauterization.
Mays de veruca es eminencia petita aspre fistulada redonda sobre la superficia del cos, e motas veguadas veno en las mas dels enfantz.	But a verruca is a small, hard, rounded, and fistula-like prominence on the surface of the body, and many times it appears in children.
E curacio de lu es que estendas e inscidas aquela, o que estrenhas aquela am fiel o am pel entro que caja.	And the cure for that is to stretch and incise it, or to strengthen it with a thread or with wool until it forms a scab.
E si vols, cauteriza aquo, segon que havem dit, am foc o am medicina acuta.	And if you wish, cauterize that too, according to what we have said, with fire or acute medicine.
E ja so eradicadas enversas e no-enversas am le instrument le qual yeu diyre.	And then they are eradicated, both inward and outward, with the instrument which you will dictate.
Mays formica es eminencia petita feutrada o fistulada grossa sobre la superficia del cos anant mot en le preon, e quan le freg atroba aquela es centit en lu semblant de mordificacio de formigua, e es fayta entorn le cos.	But a formica is a small, fatty or fistula-like prominence on the surface of the body, going forward and when the finger touches that it seems to be bitten by a formicula, and it is made around the body.
E curacio de lu es que prenguas una canula de pena de auca o de pena de voltor, e sia fort, e pausa aquela sobre la formigua entro que la contengua le cercle de la canula de las partidas de lu; e aprop revolveys la tua ma am la canula entro que inscidas aquo que es en le circuit de la formigua, e pauses aquela en le preon de la carn, e que eradiques la formigua de la sua razit.	And the cure for that is to take a needle made of swan's quill or vulture's quill, and be strong, and place it on the formica so that it contains the circle of the needle in its parts; and accordingly, revolve your hand with the needle until you incise what is in the circuit of the formica, and place it in the navel of the flesh, and eradicate the formica from its root.
E si vols, fay aquo am canula de eram o de ferr segon aquesta forma:	And if you wish, do this with a needle made of iron or steel according to this form:
Sia la partida desus de la canulha trahent a subtilitat, sorda (so es no-perforada), envolopada per so que sobre le dit la aprencio de lu sia ablaviada e la revolucio de aquela.	Be the upper part of the needle thin, subtle (so it is not perforated), wrapped in order that over the said place there may be a gentle ablation and a rotation of it.
E si vols cauteriza la formiga segon que es denant dit en la cauterizacio de atheyl en le capitol de cauteri.	And if you wish, cauterize the formica according to what is said before in the chapter on cauterization.
De forma dels instrumentz que so aministratz a dar cristeri.	On the Form of the Instruments that are administered to give Cristeria.
Alcunas veguadas es fayt cristeri de argent o de lato o de eram fondut o malleat; e alcunas veguadas es fayt de aquels instrumentz petit e gran segon aquels als quals so aministratz, quar aquel que es aministrat en la curacio dels petitz enfants sia petit; e de aquel dels quals los culs son freuls o doloyrozes, les cristeris de aquels sian petitz.	Sometimes it is made Cristeria of silver or lead or iron melted or pounded; and sometimes it is made with those instruments small and great according to what they are administered, for that which is administered in the cure of little children is small; and for those whose backsides are fat or troubled, their Cristerias are small.
La forma de cristeri gran e pauc:	The Form of Cristeria Great and Small:
Le cap de la canula de lu desus en le qual es liada la borsa sia ampla segon aquesta manieyra; e sia a lu distinacio la on la borsa es liada ayssi cum vezes.	The head of the needle of you above, in which the pouch is tied, should be broad according to this manner; and there should be a distinction at the point where the pouch is tied just like it happens sometimes.
E la extremitat de lu pus dejus, la qual es entromesa en le cul, sia sorda (so es no-uberta) mot leon, atrasent a subtilita; e en la un del latz de lu sian dos traucs, e en l’autre costat un trauc, e sia la amplesa del trauc segon la groseza dels rays e pus gros un petit.	And the extremity of you below, which is inserted into the anus, should be blunt (so it is not open) just like a lion's, and should bend back slightly; and on one side of you there should be two holes, and on the other side one hole, and the width of the hole should be according to the thickness of the rays and a little thicker than thin.
E sia la borsa en la qual sian pausadas las medicinas de vesica de bestia o de pel de ovelha, e la razit de lu sia un palm.	And the pouch in which the medicines of the vesica of animal or sheep's wool are placed, and the root of you should be one palm.
E sia perforada per motz traucs ayssi cum es revolvuda; e si l’espazi le qual es entre les traucs la grossetut del dit.	And it should be pierced with many holes just like it is revolved; and if the space which is between the holes is as wide as the said.
E aprop entromet en aquels traucs fiel fort de fiel cru le qual sia de detz fiels, o enviro aquels; e ajusta am aquel la borsa; e quan es pausada en lu la borsa, sia streyt en le cap del cristeri entre dos distingentz am fort costriccio, e aprop cristeriza am aquel quascun trauc: Mays la qualitat de cristerizar am aquel es que tu omples la borsa de la medicina, que sia escalfada segon la quantitat de la tolleransa del malaute; e guarda te que no sia trop cauda ni trop freja.	And accordingly, insert the thread into those holes strong thread of raw thread which is of ten threads or around them; and adjust that with the pouch; and when it is placed in you, the pouch should be tightened at the head of the cristeria between two distinguished points with a firm constriction, and accordingly cauterize each hole: But the quality of cauterizing that is that you fill the pouch with medicine, which should be warmed according to the quantity of the tolerance of the patient; and take care not to make it too hot or too cold.
E aprop le malaute sia resupinat sobre le sieu dos, e eleva las suas cambas en sus e pausa dejos lu un cuer sobre le qual ja so les homes o un lansol; e aprop unta la extramitat del cauteri am oli o am album de huou o am mucellage de fenugrec o de semblantz; e aprop entromet aquel en le cul am facilitat, e aprop le ministre prengua la borsa e exprema aquel am doas mas e essemps am vehemencia entro que sia evacuat en le budelh tot aquo que es en le cristeri; e aprop extra le cristeri e le malaute leva las suas cambas a la paret.	And accordingly, the patient should be raised up on his back, and lift his legs upwards and place one foot above the other, with a cloth or a lanolin over it; and accordingly, apply some oil or albumen of honey or mucilage of fenugreek or similar substance to the extremity of the cauterized area; and accordingly, insert that into the anus with ease, and accordingly, have the nurse take the pouch and express everything out of it with two fingers and samples with vehemence until everything is evacuated from the poultice; and accordingly, extract the poultice and the patient should lower his legs to the floor.
E si la medicina forsa aquel a eyssiment, tengua le tant quant poyra; e si dorm am aquel per tota una nueyt, es mays derier en juvament.	And if the medicine makes him sleep that deeply, hold it as long as he can tolerate; and if he sleeps with that for an entire night, it is more effective in healing.
Mays si tu cristerizas aquel en las malautias de solucio de ventre e l’eyssiment de lu le coyta, lahoras tu itera le cauteri entro que sia sanat.	But if you cauterize that in the diseases of bowel evacuation and the appearance of blood, then you must repeat the cauterization until it is healed.
E si en le cul so emorroydas o apostemas ledens, lahoras sia le cristeri mot subtil e leon, dels cristeris am les quals les enfantz so criterisatz.	And if there are hemorrhoids or abscesses in the anus, then make the poultice very subtle and like a lion's, one of those poultices with which children are treated.
De curacio de las plaguas.	On the Cure of Plagues.
Yeu ja e dit en la divisio de la curacio de las plaguas aquo que convenia al libre, e yeu dic assi la curacio de aquelas am ma e am medicinas segon le conpliment.	And I have already said in the division of the cure of plagues that which is suitable for the free man, and I will say thus the cure of those with me and with medicines according to their complement.
Donc dic que las plaguas son diversificadas segon aquo en que son faytas las plaguas e segon le loc sobre le qual cazo las plaquas.	Therefore, I say that plagues are diversified according to the way in which they are made and according to the place on which they fall.
E las causas per que motas vetz son faytas las plaguas so ayssi cum getament de peyra, o inscisio d’espaza o de cotel, o percussio am lansa, o am fustz, o am sageta, o semblantz ad aquels de motas causas.	And the causes by which many times plagues are made are just like a blow of iron, or incision with a sword or with a knife, or percussion with a lance, or with a club, or with an arrow, or similar to those from many causes.
Mays las plaguas que so en les locz del cos so ayssi cum plagua la qual catz sobre le cap, o·l col, o·l pietz, o·l ventre, o·l fitge, e semblantz ad aquels dels membres.	But the plagues that are on the parts of the body are just like a plague which falls on the head, or the neck, or the feet, or the belly, or the thigh, and similar to those of the members.
E yeu so recomtant la curacio de alcunas plaguas per que pauses aquela ratiocinacio e regla sobre las autras plaguas.	And I will recommend the cure for some plagues, by which you may pause and reason about the other plagues.
E yeu comensare de las plaguas del cap simplas, quar la rememoracio de las compostas vindra al comensament del tertz capitol.	And I will begin with the simple plagues of the head, because the remembrance of the complex ones will come at the beginning of the third chapter.
Donc dic que quan accideys en le cap plagua simpla e no es fractura, lahoras considera: si es per getament de peyra o de semblant, e ja ha trinquada la codena tant solament e es gran plagla e temes sobre aquel malaute havinement de apostema caut, lahoras tu te coyta e fleubotoma la cephalica tantost, e no tardas aquo; e extrats ad aquel del sanc segon la quantitat de la vertut de lu si no mes alcuna causa prohibent de fleubotomia, majorment si·l sanc que es eyssit de la plagua es pauc.	Therefore I say that when a simple plague occurs on the head and is not a fracture, then consider: if it is due to a blow of iron or similar, and the wound has already opened so much and is large and you fear on that patient having an abscess caught, then take care and bleed the cephalic vein at once, and do not delay; and extract from that blood according to the quantity of the virtue of it, unless some other cause prohibits bleeding, especially if the blood which has come out of the plague is little.
E sia la flaubotomia del contrari de la partida plaguada; e guardase le malaute de replecio e de vi e de viandas grossas.	And be the bleeding from the opposite side of the wounded part; and take care that the patient is not filled with blood, nor fed with wine or heavy food.
Mays si de la minuicio prohibeys alcuna causa, lahoras sia aminorat de la vianda e no apropinque a carn ni a vi.	But if some cause prohibits from the beginning, then reduce the food and do not approach meat or wine.
E pausa sobre la plagua, si a lu accideys apostema caut, coto enfus en oli rozat solet o en vi en le qual es stipticat.	And pause on the wound, if an abscess is caught, apply hot oil or wine which is sterilized.
Mays si est segur de apostema caut, lahoras pausa sobre la plagua, si es recent am le sieu sanc e le ayre no ha mudat aquela la polvera la qual yeu recomtare aprop petit.	But if it is sure of an abscess, then pause on the wound, if it is recent with its own blood and the air has not changed that powder which I recommend in due small proportion.
E si le ayre ja ha mudada aquela, lahoras pausa sobre alscus enguentz entro que sia sanada.	And if the air has already changed it, then pause on another poultice until it is healed.
Mays si la plagua es gran o es per inscizio d’espaza e de semblantz, e no so ajustadas las labias de lu per puvils, lahoras ajusta aquelas am sutura segon que yeu recomtare de la sutura de lor.	But if the wound is great or is due to incision with a sword and similar, and the lips of it are not adjusted by powders, then adjust those with suture according to what I recommend on the suturing of them.
Mays si la plagua ja es discuberta del os e pen, e no es retencio de lu sino un petit suspensori, lahoras inscideys aquela e aprop cura la plagua am medicinas e restaura la carn aprop en loc de codena, e comanda al malaute que sia pescut de viandas en las quals es groceza: caps e formen coyt e semblantz a lor, entro que sia compost.	But if the wound is already uncovered of bone and skin, and there is no retention of it except for a small suspender, then incise that and accordingly cure the wound with medicines and restore the flesh to its natural place, and command the patient to be fed with food in which there is grease: caps and forms like those, similar to their own, until it is composed.
E si atrobas en la codena putrefaccio e no adhereys al os, lahoras tu inscideys tot aquo poyrit e geta aquo, e aprop cura aquo.	And if you find in the wound putrefaction and it does not adhere to the bone, then you must incise all that is rotten and cut it out, and accordingly cure that.
Mays si en aquestas plaguas es arteria o vena de la qual fluxs de sanc pot evenir, e no es abscindida per medicinas, lahoras tu inquier sobre la arteria, e si atrobas aquela no-inscidida, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am spatum, o lia aquela; e si necessitat te provoca que aquo que havem dit no comfereys, lahoras tu cauteriza entro que·l sanc sia abscidit.	But if in these wounds there is an artery or vein from which bleeding can occur, and it is not closed by medicines, then you must inquire about the artery, and if you find that one which is not incised, then you must incise it with a spatula or tie it off; and if necessary, take steps to ensure that what we have said does not come to pass, then you must cauterize until the bleeding is stopped.
E si aquestas plaguas son simplas e petitas, lahoras la causa de lor es leugiere; enayssi que tu polverizas sobre aquelas aquesta polvera, quar consolidada aquela denant que l’ayre mude aquelas.	And if these wounds are simple and small, then the cause of them is light; therefore, you must powderize on those this powder, since it will consolidate before the air changes those.
E la manieyra de la polvera es aquesta: recipe oli de enses partida una, de sanc de drago partida doas, de caus no-extincta partidas tres; sia tot mot trissat e crivellat, e de lu sia la plagua omplida, e sia constrengida per bona constriccio entro que be sobre aquela aderesca, e sia coagulada am le sanc.	And the method of the powder is this: take oil of dragon's blood one part, blood of dragon two parts, and caus no-extincta three parts; mix all well and finely powdered, and fill the wound with it, and compress it with good constriction until it adheres well to that, and coagulates with the blood.
E aprop strengeys aquela desus am pulvils e leyssa aquela, e no la deslias mentre esta ayssi que no es apostemada, quar no es eredicada de lu la medicina entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, strengthen that above with powders and loosen it, and do not remove it until it is in this state, for the medicine will not be absorbed from it until it is healed.
E alcuna vetz fa aquo sola cautz, quan no es a tu en present enses e sanc de drago.	And sometimes make this powder alone, when you do not have oil of dragon's blood and blood of dragon in front of you.
E ja fa aquesta meteyssa operacio en las grans plaguas quan conveneys que sia pausada sobre aquelas e sian streytas, e so plaguas recentz am le lor sanc, las quals le ayre no ha alteradas.	And already perform this kind of operation on great wounds when it is necessary to pause over them and be tightened, and on recent wounds with their own blood, which the air has not altered.
E si le ayre las ha alteradas, e majorment quan es en temps d’estiu, lahoras no es entencio a la posicio de aquesta polvera, mays adonc cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit, enayssi que tu pauses sobre aquelas alcus enguents degistius, o que pauses sobre aquelas pols de la farina del ordi am aygua e mel entro que getan poyredura; e aprop cura aquelas am l’autra curacio entro que sian sanadas.	And if the air has altered them, and especially when it is in the summer, then it is not suitable to apply this powder, but instead cure those with what we have said, by applying certain poultices or by applying powders of barley flour mixed with water and honey until they become purulent; and accordingly, cure those with other remedies until they are healed.
Mays si accideys am la plagua fractura en os, e es petita, lahoras tu extratz aquo am gesti.	But if it occurs by a fracture in bone, and is small, then you must extract that with forceps.
E yeu diyre la cura de las fracturas del cap en aquo que es envenidor.	And I will say the cure for fractures of the head in this way which is venomous.
De las plaguas del col.	On the Wounds of the Neck.
Mays si la plagua accideys en le col, lahoras no es en lu differencia en medicacio, e entre la plagua del cap quan es simpla.	But if the wound occurs on the neck, then there is no difference in treatment, and it is similar to a simple wound of the head.
Mays si ja le nervi del col es inscis o arteria, lahoras si es nervi, no es en lu engen sino que sia evitada curacio de lu am aquo que fa vehement stipticitat, ayssi cum ziniar e zegi que es vetriol e semblantz a lor quar nozo als nervis e contrazo aquel.	But if the nerves of the neck are cut or an artery is involved, then if it is a nerve, do not apply any further treatment to it, but rather avoid applying anything that would cause vehement stiptication, such as ziniar and zegi which are like vitriol and similar to them, which can harm the nerves and contract them.
E no pauses sobre la plagua alcuna causa de tot freja, quar la sustancia dels nervis es freja e la continuacio de lu es am le cervel, le qual es le pus aut de totz les membres.	And do not apply anything to the wound that could cause total numbness, because the substance of the nerves is numb and the continuation of it is in the brain, which is the most noble part of all the members.
E si’ aquo am que es curat de medicinas leugieras, ayssi cum es caus lavada am aygua dousa, alcuna veguada enfusa en oli rozat o no-rozat, e thucia quan es lavada am aygua dousa e las autras peyras minarantz segon aquesta manieyra, e enguentz humitz.	And if that is treated with light medicines, just as it is cleansed with double water, and some of it infused in hot or not hot oil, and when it is cleansed with double water and the other parts are reduced according to this method, and poultices moistened.
Mays si la plagua es gran, lahoras aministra sutura, o coarta las labias de lu, e aprop cura aquela am pulvils entro que sia sanada.	But if the wound is great, then apply suture, or tighten the lips of it, and accordingly cure that with powders until it is healed.
Mays si a la plagua es profunditat o accideys en lu a la pus bassa partida poyredura, lahoras perfora aquela en le loc mays depremegut.	But if the wound is deep or occurs at the lowest part of the poultice, then perforate that in the most depressed location.
Mays si en la plagua ja es inscisa arteria e es conseguit flux de sanc, lahoras separa o secca aquela, o lia aquela, o cauteriza aquela si necessitat te provoca ad aquo.	But if the wound has already been incised and an artery is cut and bleeding occurs, then separate or dry it off, or tie it off, or cauterize it if necessary to stop the bleeding.
Mays si ja ha insciditz les spondils del golayro o tot, e so salvadas las venas del col, lahoras tu ajusta las labias de la codena am sutura sobre la cana del golayro e no toques aquel; abantz egala aquel e reduzeys aquel sobre la sua figura natural, e aprop strenh aquel am strectura decent, e leyssa aquela per alcus jorns; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz en les quals es stipticitat e excitacio entro que sia sanat.	But if the vertebrae of the neck or all of it have been incised and the veins of the neck are saved, then you must adjust the lips of the wound with suture over the canal of the neck and do not touch that; above equalize that and reduce it to its natural shape, and accordingly strengthen it with decent tension, and loosen it for a few days; and accordingly cure that with poultices in which there is stiptication and excitement until it is healed.
Mays si la plagua ja en le os a fayta enprecio, lahoras percuireys aquela, e lahoras si en lu ha fragmentz de hos, extratz totz aquels que podes de lor; e aquo que a tu no es apparelhat, leyssa aquo entro que la plagua se poyrisca, e sia separat e la egrecio de lu sia alleujada.	But if the wound has made an impression on the bone, then pierce that and then, if there are fragments of bone in it, extract all those which you can; and what is not dressed by you, leave it until the wound is purulent, and be separate from it and the excretion of it be alleviated.
E si la plagua es recent lahoras polveriza sobre aquela polvera la qual t’e recomtada.	And if the wound is recent, then powderize on that the powder which I have recommended to you.
Mays si en la plagua es fayta fistula, lahoras cura aquela am aquo del qual la rememoracio vindra aprop en le sieu capitol.	But if the wound has made a fistula, then cure that with what will be remembered in its own chapter.
De las plaguas del col o de semblantz quan fayta entre las spallas e es fayta am spaza o am cotel o am lansa o am semblantz.	On the Wounds of the Neck or Similar Ones When Made Between the Shoulders and is Made with a Sword or Knife or Lance or Similar.
Si es percussio de lansa o de cotel, e vezes de lu la profunditat, lahoras considera mays si de la plagua yeys ventositat quan le malaute elena; lahoras sapias que la plagua es mortal.	If it is a blow from a lance or knife and pierces the depth of the wound, then consider more whether the wound has ventilation when the patient breathes; know that the wound is mortal.
E si en lu no es profunditat e la plagua es recent am le sieu sanc, lahoras tu pauses en lu de la primieyra horo polvera, e no strenhas aquel per que no sia le sanc retengut en la profunditat de lu e que retorne al cor e que aucigua le malaute, mays pausa en lu enguent atractiu, e deslia aquela doas veguadas le dia.	And if there is no depth to it and the wound is recent with its own blood, then you must pause on it in the first hour with powder, and not strengthen that so that the blood does not become retained in the depth of it and return to the heart and kill the patient, but rather pause on it an attractive poultice, and remove it two times a day.
E si l’enguent no es a tu present, lahoras tu pausa en le orrifici de la plagua coto viel per que sucque aquo que yeys de las humiditatz; e fay que le malaute dorma sobre la plagua per que corra aquo que es en lu ajustat.	And if the poultice is not at your present, then you must pause on the orifice of the wound with a small amount of vinegar so that it sucks out what comes from the humidities; and make sure the patient sleeps over the wound so that water flows in there and adjusts itself.
Mays si ja de la plagua son passatz tres dias o mays e no accideys al malaute spasme ni tremor de cor mal ni strictura de ale, e vezes las autras dispozicios bonas de lu, lahoras sapias que plagua es salva; e adonc cura aquela am calguas e am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanada.	But if three days or more have passed since the wound occurred and there is no spasmodic movement nor tremor of the heart, nor constriction of the artery, and other good dispositions are seen in him, then know that the wound is saved; and accordingly cure it with caustics and other remedies until it is healed.
Mays si la sanacio de lu es excusada, e ja tot temps es uberta, lahoras sapias que ja es fayta fistula; cura donc aquela per le sieu capitol.	But if the healing of him is excused, and it has already been open for a long time, then know that a fistula has formed; cure therefore that according to its own chapter.
E si la plagua es per inscisio de spaza o de cotel, e es simpla en la superficia del pietz o del dos, lahoras cura aquela am aquo que es precedit de sutura, si es gran, o am polvera, si es petita.	And if the wound is due to incision with a sword or knife, and is simple on the surface of the foot or hand, then cure that with what precedes suture, if it is great, or with powder, if it is small.
Mays si ja ha fayta enprecio en le os, e so ja de lu inscizas pessas, lahoras tu torqua la plagua e coyta ad extrayre aquelas pessas, si so separadas.	But if it has already made an impression on the bone, and you have already incised those fragments, then twist the wound and pull out those fragments, if they are separated.
Mays si no so separadas, lahoras leyssa las entro que se poyresca la plagua, que la extraccio de lor es alleujada.	But if they are not separated, then loosen them until the wound purifies, and the extraction of them is alleviated.
E de las autras plaguas accidentz en les autres membres le juvament en curacio es le juvament de aquo que havem dit.	And for other wounds that occur in other members, the treatment is the same as what we have said.
De las plaguas del ventre.	On Wounds of the Abdomen.
L’indisposicio la qual accideys en le ventre es o gran, o pauc, o migiera.	The indisposition that occurs in the abdomen is either great, small, or medium-sized.
De la gran alcunas veguadas yeys le budel o nervi del budel, per que es fayta intromissio de lor e la sutura de lor esser pus vehement e pus subtil.	On the Great Wounds Some Times You Will Find the Bladder or Nerve of the Bladder, So That There Is Intrusion Of Them And The Suture Of Them To Be More Vehement and Subtle.
E disrupcio petita es fayta dificil per autra manieyra, e siec se que la reduccio de lor es pus dificil, si no te coytes de la intromissio de lor al sieu loc tantost, quar se ubre e es engrossat per que le intrament de lu es fayt difficil.	And a small disruption is made difficult by another method, and it is seen that the reduction of them is more difficult, if you do not take care to insert them into their place at once, for they swell and become engorged, making the instrument of it difficult.
E donc la milhor disrupcio es migiera, quar en aquela no es dificil la reduccio del budel, ayssi cum es dificil en las doas specias denant ditas.	And therefore the best disruption is medium-sized, because in that one it is not difficult to reduce the bladder, just as it is difficult in the two species mentioned earlier.
E sapias que sutura del ventre es segon quatre manieyras, mays doas suturas son comunas que conveneysso en suturas de las autras plaguas del cors.	And know that the suture of the abdomen is according to four methods, but two sutures are common that are used in sutures of other wounds of the body.
E duas autras suturas proprias comunican a las autras plaguas, mays empero so mays proprias en la sutura del ventre.	And two other specific sutures communicate with the others, but however they are more proper for the suture of the abdomen.
E yeu recomti a tu quascuna am exposicio e declaracio.	And I recommend to you any exposition and declaration.
Donc dic que quan la plagua es petita e es eyssit alcuna causa del budel per aquela, e es fayt dificil a reduzir aquel, lahoras aquo es en una de doas manieyras: o per parvitat de la disrupcio ayssi cum havem dit, o quan al budel es venguda inflacio per la frigiditat de l’ayre.	So I say that when the wound is small and there is some cause of the bladder due to it, and it is made difficult to reduce it, then this is done in one of two ways: either by the parvity of the disruption just as we have said, or when the bladder has become inflamed due to the coldness of the air.
E donc quan aquo es ayssi, lahora cove que tu scalfes aquel enayssi que tu submerges una sponga ho drap humit en aygua tebeza sola, o que coguas en aygua squinant, e cyperum, e spic, e embroques am aquela le budel entro que la imflacio sia resolvuda.	And so when this is the case, then it is necessary that you scrape off that part and immerse a sponge or wet cloth in hot water only, or that you soak it in warm water with cyperum, spic, and embrocate, and apply it to the bladder until the inflammation is resolved.
E alcunas veguadas fa aquo vi en le qual ha stipticitat, e es milhor que la aygua sola en resolucio de la imflacio.	And sometimes this remedy is seen in which there is stiptitation, and it is better than hot water alone for the resolution of the inflammation.
E donc cum tu vezes la imflacio esser resolvuda, lahoras tu humecta le budel am aygua en la qual es coyta altea e malvas, quar per aquo es alleujat le intrament de lu am pauca causa.	And so when you see the inflammation be resolved, then you moisten the bladder with water in which there is a high and bitter extract, because by this it is alleviated the instrument of it with little cause.
Mays si es escusat le intrament de lu aprop aquesta curacio, lahoras scindeys la disrupcio un petit am strument am le qual so inscididas emorroydas.	But if the instrument is excused for this cure, then divide the disruption into small parts with an instrument by which it is incised and bloodless.
E la curacio primieyra es milhor, quan es propriada que no es seccio, e no sia occupacio a seccar aprop necessitat e defaliment.	And the first cure is better when it is proper and not a section, and there is no occupation to cut into what is necessary and inevitable.
Del instrument, sec se la forma de lu:	Of the instrument, see how its form is:
La una partida de lu torta aguda, e l’autra partida no-acuta, e la extremitat subtil, e no sia am la subtilitat de spatum, abantz sia obtusa un pauc.	One part of it is sharp and acute, and the other part not acute, and the extremity subtle, and not like the subtlety of a spatula, but rather obtuse to some extent.
E donc cum la plagua es amplificada e yeys fora le budel, lahoras cove que la sua reduccio sia segon la forma de lu natural, en le sieu loc propri, si es possible sobre aquo, quar milhor es.	And so when the wound is amplified and extends outside the bladder, then it is necessary that its reduction be according to the form of nature, in its own proper place, if possible above it, for it is better.
Mays quan la disrupcio es ampla, e es en la partida pu bassa del ventre, lahoras cove que tu fassas jazer le malaute sobre le sieu dos, e pausa las suas cambas pus autas que·l sieu cap; e si es en la partida pus desus del ventre, lahoras tu pause le cap de lu e·l pietz pus autz que las partidas dejos.	But when the disruption is large and is in the lower part of the abdomen, then it is necessary that you make the patient lie on his back with his knees higher than his head; and if it is in the upper part of the abdomen, then you should elevate the patient's head and feet above the remaining parts.
E semblantment si la disrupcio es en una de las doas partz del ventre, lahoras pausa la tua entencio e la tua consideracio tostemps en aysso per que la partida en la qual es la plagua sia pus auta que l’autra.	And similarly if the disruption is in one of the two parts of the abdomen, then pause your intention and consideration at that point for some time, so that the part where the wound is may be higher than the other.
E ayssi cove que tu aministres aquo en las plaguas grans e en las plaguas migieras.	And thus it is necessary that you administer this in great wounds and medium-sized wounds.
E en las plaguas petitas, pausa aquo que es a tu preparat, e aprop fay que·l ministre sia entre las tuas mas pyatados, le qual tengua la disrupcio tota am la sua ma e ajusta las labias de lu, e aprop descuebre de aquela ad aquel que siec la sutura alcuna causa aprop autra.	And in small wounds, pause on what is prepared for you, and accordingly make sure that the minister be between your most trusted advisors, who have the disruption entirely under their hand and adjust the lips of it, and accordingly uncover from that to this one who sees some other cause to propose suturing.
E aquesta es la manieyra de sutura comuna: una que prenguas la agula, o comte de agula segon la cantitat de la amplitut de la plagua; e aprop layssa de la extremitat de la disrupcio del dit anular, e strenh la agula una, otre que tu no metas fiel en las doas extremitatz de la codena, am doas extremitatz del ciphac que es dejos la codena de las partidas dedintz, entro que fassas aquela penetrar de aquela partida; e tu ja has agreguadas doas extremitatz de la codena e doas extremitatz del ciphac, e so faytas quatre ordes.	And this is the common method of suturing: first take a needle, or count of needles according to the size of the wound; and accordingly leave from the end of the disruption on the little finger, and strengthen the needle one by one, so that you do not put faith in both ends of the thread at once, with two ends of the ciphac that is left over from the parts inside, until it makes that penetrate from this part; and you have already added two ends of the thread and two ends of the ciphac, making four orders.
E aprop strenh am fiel doble en le circuit de la agula, e alcunas veguadas de doas partz ensemps, e aprop agregua las doas labias e la plagua per agreguacio decent; e aprop layssa la grossitut del dit e fiqua una autra agulha en aquela, e aprop lia aquela am fiel ayssi cum fiest am la primieyra agulha; e no cesses far aquo si es necessitat am las agulhas entro que ajas complida tota la contriccio de la plagua.	And accordingly strengthen with double thread in the circuit of the needle, and sometimes from two parts together, and accordingly add the two lips and the wound by decent addition; and accordingly leave the thickness of the finger and place another needle in that, and accordingly tie it with thread just as you tied the first needle; and do not cease to do so if necessary with the needles until you have completed all the contraction of the wound.
E sian las agulhas migieras entre groceza e subtilitat, quar las agulhas subtils mot leugierament insciden la carn; e las grossas so de dificil intrament en la codena, e donc per aquo cove que sian migieras en subtilitat e grosseza.	And the needles should be of medium size between grossness and subtlety, because the fine needles barely cut into the flesh; and the coarse ones are of difficult instrument in the thread, and therefore it is necessary that they be of medium size in subtlety and coarseness.
E no cove que la agulha sia ficada en doas extremitatz de la codena propdana mot, per so que la carn no sia inscidida leugierament e que la plagua se huebra devant la sua consolidacio.	And it is not necessary that the needle be inserted in both ends of the thread at once, because then the flesh would not be cut slightly and the wound would be healed before its consolidation.
E no sian prolonguadas de sutura per que la plagua no sia prohibida de consolidacio.	And do not prolong the suturing for fear that the wound will be prohibited from consolidation.
E aprop inscideys las extremitatz de las agulhas per so que no ledescan le malaute deves le sieu dormier; e pausaras sobre la sutura pulvils expanduts de tota partida, les quals tenguan las extremitatz de las agulhas; e layssa aquelas entro que sapias que la plagua ja es consolidada.	And accordingly insert the ends of the needles so that they do not disturb the patient's sleep; and pause on the suturing with poultices spread out from all parts, which have the ends of the needles; and leave them in until you know that the wound is already consolidated.
E aquestas specias de sutura am agulhas en cal manieyra es pus convenient en las plaguas petitas, quar habasta en la sutura de lor una agulha o doas o entorn aquelas.	And this species of suture with needles in that manner is more suitable for small wounds, because it is sufficient to use one needle or two or around those.
Mays la segonda sutura es cominal: e es que tu aministres am sutura las quatre extremitatz, de la codena e doas extremitatz del ciphac, en una veguada, am agulha en la qual sia fiel envolopat engual en subtilitat e grosseza.	But the second suture is common: and it is that you administer with suturing the four ends, of the thread and two ends of the ciphac, in one go, with a needle in which the thread is wrapped in subtlety and coarseness.
E aprop quan am la agulha auras penetrat aquestas quatre extremitatz, reduzeys la agulha de aquela meteyssa partida de la qual comensest, per so que le fiel retrayt caja de la pus subirana partida a la plagua, per so que la sutura sia segon sutura de drap am la qual les draps so strengutz.	And accordingly when you have the needle penetrate these four ends, reduce the needle to that middle part from which you began, in order that the thread may withdraw from the most superior part to the wound, so that the suture be according to a cloth suture with which the cloths are strengthened.
E pausa entre quascuna sutura la quantitat del gros del dit mendre.	And pause between each suture the quantity of the thickness of the finger, smaller.
E aquesta sutura sabo les homes.	And this suture knows men.
E am tal sutura yeu cozegui la plagua la qual era accidida a un home en le sieu ventre le qual era stat plaguat am un cotel, e era la disrrumpcio de la plagua major de un palm, e era eyssit dels budels entorn dos palms del budel del mieg loc e era la disrupcio en le mieg del membre; e adonc yeu reduzegui aquel depus que le budel havia stat foro la plagua per xxiiii horas.	And with such a suture, I treated the wound which had occurred to a man in his belly, which was wounded by a knife, and the disruption of the wound was greater than one palm, and it was surrounded by bladders around two palms from the bladder of the middle part, and there was a disruption in the middle of the member; and then I reduced that since the bladder had been pierced through the wound for 24 hours.
E la plagua fo consolidada en le spazi de xv dias o entorn, e curegui aquel e es sanat; e aprop aquo visquec per motz ans, e es conversat en las suas disposicios.	And the wound was consolidated in the space of 15 days or around, and cured that man, and he is sane; and accordingly, I saw him for many years, and he was converted to his former dispositions.
E les autres metges havian jutgat que no fora sanat; e per miracle foc, quar yeu no curegui aquel am enguent, quar era en loc en le qual enguent no era atrobat ni deguna medicina, mays pausegui sobre la plagua coto viel dos veguadas lo dia e ablucio assiduo am aygua de mel entro que foc sanat.	And the other doctors had judged that he would not be cured; and by a miracle it was so, because you did not treat him with poultice, since there was no remedy or medicine available in that place, but instead you paused over the wound cutting twice a day and ablution with water of honey until it was cured.
Mays yeu diyre dos specias de sutura proprias segon narracio de Paraula.	But I will tell you two species of suture proper according to the narration of Paraula.
E es que tu comenses am sutura de la codena, e entrometas agulha de la partida deforo a la partida dedintz.	And it is that you begin with the suture of the thread, and insert needle from the outside part to the inside part.
E donc cum la agulha penetra en la codena e en aquel meteys lacertz segon rectetut e en longetut de tot le cos, e layssa la extremita del ciphac en le qual has entromesa la agulha; e fay penetrar en la autra extremitat la agulha de la partida dedintz a la partida deforo en l’autra extremitat del mihat.	And therefore, as the needle penetrates the thread and inserts itself into the lacertus according to rectitude and in length throughout the entire body, and leaves the end of the ciphac in which you inserted the needle; and make the needle penetrate into the other extremity from the inside part to the outside part in the other extremity of the arm.
E don cum tu auras fayta aquela penetrar, lahoras tu fay aquela penetrar autra veguada en aquela meteyssa extremitat del mihat de la partida deforo a la partida dedintz; e leyssa la extramitat del ciphac que es en aquest latz, e fay penetrar la agulha en l’autra extremitat de la partida dedintz a la partida deforo.	And then when you have made it penetrate once, then you make it penetrate again in the same extremity of the arm from the outside part to the inside part; and leave the end of the ciphac that is on this side, and make the needle penetrate into the other extremity from the inside part to the outside part.
E fay penetrar am aquela la tua penetracio am la qual fas aquela penetrar en le ciphac en la extremitat del mirat la qual es en la partida de lu entro que tot aquel penetre.
